Chapter 1383: The Annihilation Tribulation Descends

The Nameless Monument appeared, and the universe stabilized!

In that moment, time seemed to come to a standstill.

In the silence of all things, a majestic aura was born. It was a power so vast and magnificent that it froze even Li Fan's thoughts, the closest observer.

If the Nameless Monument had merely existed silently without any intention of attacking, and stood within the Immortal Domain, Li Fan would have been torn to shreds by this aura.

Even with his strength capable of traversing the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, facing the Nameless Monument in the Immortal Domain, Li Fan was truly like an ant in a storm, his life and death beyond his control!

Li Fan's expression changed drastically, wanting to summon the Wooden Sword Phantom to escape. But he was horrified to find that the laws constituting the Wooden Sword were all affected by the Nameless Monument and could not function at all.

Even the 'Transformation Between True and False' was the same!

The Nameless Monument stood there as if it were the center of all worlds. Everything else, except for the gradually stabilizing Immortal Domain, all rushed towards the Nameless Monument and were drawn into it!

The descent of all things formed a swift waterfall flow. Only the strongest beings at the peak of the Star Sea could barely hold their ground outside the small vortex.

From the edge of the Star Sea, rumbling sounds could be faintly heard. It was the sign of the continuous artifact ruins and the Great Wall of Remaining Realms disintegrating. Countless boundless ruins were rolling towards the Immortal Domain.

Even the invisible High Wall seemed to be affected.

Amidst violent tremors, inexplicable changes occurred. Like dark clouds pressing down, countless images descended upon the border of the Star Sea.

……

Various terrifying anomalies occurred one after another. A crisp female voice, filled with surprise and terror, suddenly sounded. It was so out of place.

But it could pierce through the storm caused by the Nameless Monument and reach everyone's ears, which was enough to show the terror of her power.

"Southern Immortal Pillar? How could it be here!"

Before her words were finished, her owner had already transformed into a streak of light, rushing towards the center of the storm. It seemed she wanted to enter the Immortal Domain to investigate.

But the Immortal Domain emitted a faint glow, actually pushing the figure back several feet.

"This is..."

"Tai Li Star Domain, Cang Sheng Ancient Realm!"

The slightly slender figure finally revealed her true appearance. She looked pale, as if she had just recovered from a serious illness. Her eyes were deep, as if containing infinite mysteries, making any observer fall into them. Her appearance was not particularly beautiful, and could even be called ordinary.

But she possessed a unique charm that made people unforgettable.

"She is..."

The appearance of this figure caused Li Fan to slightly regain his senses.

Thinking about what she said, looking at the somewhat familiar figure, Li Fan's heart stirred: "Immortal Ruins True Immortal? I only saw her skeletal remains and phantom avatars before, but I didn't expect her to be a woman!"

As if sensing the thoughts related to her in the surroundings, the True Immortal frowned slightly and swept her gaze left and right.

Li Fan couldn't help but be startled.

But perhaps because of the influence of the Nameless Monument, the True Immortal could not pinpoint her target accurately. And after confirming that everyone around was just a mortal, the True Immortal's attention returned to the Immortal Domain.

Her figure rippled like waves, and she seemed to be trying to merge into the Immortal Domain.

But the Immortal Domain seemed to have a natural repulsion towards True Immortals. A more intense burst of light suddenly erupted, pushing the True Immortal back several feet in an instant.

The True Immortal's expression immediately turned grim.

Her aura suddenly changed. Her figure also disappeared from everyone's sight.

Li Fan only vaguely saw a transparent bulge in the distorted space, seemingly moving towards the Immortal Domain.

The light of the Immortal Domain's periphery was suddenly pushed aside in a large area.

After a few breaths, the True Immortal successfully entered the Immortal Domain.

Her goal was clear: the Nameless Monument in the center.

The Immortal Domain seemed small from the outside, but the Immortal Ruins True Immortal flew for a long time, only covering a small distance. In fact, the closer she got to the Nameless Monument, the slower her speed became, as if there was an infinite distance between them.

The events within the Immortal Domain did not affect the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

The continuous Great Wall of Remaining Realms and the sea of artifact ruins inevitably fell towards the Nameless Monument.

Before they could even approach the Immortal Domain, they transformed into streams of light.

After being absorbed by the Nameless Monument, they only added a few smudges to it.

Not even a shallow mark was left.

The "waterfall flow" became more intense. Li Fan found it increasingly difficult to maintain his stance.

With every stream of light that passed by him, Li Fan felt as if the original object had smashed into him, pushing him step by step towards the Immortal Domain.

In the Star Sea, nothing could escape this fate.

Even the Xuanhuang Realm was no exception.

Li Fan saw two figures, one large and one small, standing side-by-side, attracting Li Fan's attention. It was Chu Fa and Tian Yi. They had actually broken free from the temptation of the Nameless Monument and were doing their best to prevent the Xuanhuang Realm from falling.

But it was futile, like trying to hold back a tide. It only delayed the inevitable.

Besides them, another pair of large and small figures, side-by-side, caught Li Fan's attention.

"Dao, Su Gu. Xin, Jue Mie. Xing Nian Xiu, Tong Yi, Wang Shen. Qian Xing Hun Yi, Bai Zhe Po Zhuan."

"...Wu Jiu."

A faint, mysterious voice emanated continuously from the larger figure. The smaller figure, meanwhile, looked at the Nameless Monument not far away with greed mixed with a hint of fear.

"Grand Master Tian Du!" Li Fan's heart trembled.

"What the phantom was chanting seemed to have appeared when I faced the Calamity of Wind Annihilation in my previous life."

"Is there some profound mystery?"

This time, the distance was much closer, allowing Li Fan to hear the phantom's incantation completely. Li Fan memorized the entire Celestial Scripture.

With a thought, an invisible force enveloped Li Fan. It felt like a giant hand pressing down, stabilizing him amidst the storm caused by the Nameless Monument.

"This seems to be useful for avoiding calamities?" Li Fan was filled with doubt.

The young Taoist companion next to the phantom looked at Li Fan with a hint of mockery.

However, he didn't say anything, his attention quickly returning to the Nameless Monument.

Li Fan glanced at 'Returning to True,' whose charging progress was still decreasing. With a thought, he summoned Tian Yang and Qiu Shui.

The two figures traversed space and arrived beside Li Fan, standing guard on his left and right.

The power of the two Supreme beings did not even draw the attention of the phantom Taoist.

Li Fan also had no intention of provoking the Grand Master. He shifted his gaze back to the Immortal Domain.

He did not know what method the Immortal Ruins True Immortal had used, but she had unexpectedly moved much closer to the Nameless Monument.

The blurry scene within the Immortal Domain was gradually becoming clearer. Mountains and rivers began to appear.

Li Fan keenly sensed that the aura from the Grand Master had become somewhat unstable, as if unwilling, and was showing signs of restless movement.

At this moment...

The rolling black energy from the center of the Star Sea finally arrived like a flood.

As if possessing sentience, it bypassed Li Fan and headed straight for the Immortal Domain.

The Grand Master's phantom suddenly seemed to wake up as if he had seen a ghost, his face filled with extreme terror. He instantly fled, disappearing without a trace.

The Immortal Domain's light could not block the black energy at all.

Instead, due to the attraction of the Nameless Monument, the surging black energy became even more condensed.

What was originally a boundless sea of black energy, after being infused into the Immortal Domain.

It transformed into a long, flowing rope, descending from the heavens!

The sky of the Immortal Domain was like a collapsing city wall, about to crumble.

The mountains and rivers that had just appeared began to disintegrate inch by inch, instantly turning into nothingness.

Moments later, endless black energy surged forth.

A black avalanche swept from the surroundings, engulfing everything, swallowing everything.

The sky of the Immortal Domain continuously collapsed.

The scope of the Immortal Domain also shrank continuously.

At the critical moment, the Immortal Ruins True Immortal finally reached the Nameless Monument.

She struck out with a brilliant ray of light, hitting the Nameless Monument.

The Nameless Monument seemed to suddenly gain several characters. A pillar of light, connecting heaven and earth, erupted from the top of the Nameless Monument moments later.

It forcefully resisted the approaching tide of black energy and the oppressive storm from the heavens!

Like a pillar supporting the sky, it propped up the collapsing heavens!

"Calamity of Dao Annihilation..."

"Southern Immortal Pillar..."

Witnessing all this, Li Fan vaguely began to understand the meaning of the Immortal Ruins True Immortal's words.

But one pillar alone could not stand.

The power of the Immortal Ruins True Immortal alone, stimulated by the Nameless Monument, did not seem to be able to stop the descent of the Calamity of Dao Annihilation.

The tide of black energy, though slow, was relentlessly pressing down.

The True Immortal's face showed despair.

And after swallowing the Immortal Domain, the black energy seemed somewhat different from before.

Vague figures seemed to flicker within it.

Li Fan's sense of crisis increased dramatically.

He looked back and saw that in the remaining regions of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, countless black energies were emerging from every corner.

In an instant, they spread throughout the entire Star Sea.

Moreover, the black energy was not the original version from the Star Sea, but rather a sublimation after devouring the Immortal Domain.

In the Star Sea, ghostly figures flickered like a hundred ghosts walking at night.

The figures within the black energy seemed to contain some great terror, causing Li Fan's heart to race and his scalp to tingle.

Even 'Returning to True' issued a rare warning.

It urged him to escape quickly.

"It's time to use 'Returning to True'."

Looking at the terrifying scene of the black energy raging, Li Fan had this thought.

But just as the light screen of 'Returning to True' enveloped him, Li Fan suddenly had an epiphany.

He threw out a white circle, which instantly flew towards the Nameless Monument in the Immortal Domain.

It was precisely the white circle, "Falling Mortal."

It did not encounter the obstruction that the Immortal Ruins True Immortal had, but directly entered, breaking through the siege of the surging black energy tide.

It collided with the Nameless Monument.

There was no earth-shattering explosion.

A dazzling light erupted from the white circle.

Then it disappeared from sight.

At the same time, a character, precisely representing the principle of the Great Dao, a True Immortal Character Script, appeared completely on the Nameless Monument!

The appearance of this True Immortal Character Script seemed to inject powerful energy into the Southern Immortal Pillar.

The pillar of light erupted, expanding by a circle.

It forcefully pushed back the encroaching black tide.

The somewhat desperate Immortal Ruins True Immortal reacted at this moment.

Without any reservation, she poured all her energy into the Nameless Monument before her.

Flesh and blood, hair, disappeared from the Immortal Ruins True Immortal's body.

She transformed back into the skeletal form that Li Fan had seen in the Immortal Ruins before.

Within the Nameless Monument, a second True Immortal Character Script slowly appeared.

The pillar of light grew stronger again, finally breaking through the black tide.

A giant ring of light formed in the sky.

The Immortal Ruins True Immortal, carrying the Nameless Monument, broke through the blockade of the black energy.

Perhaps sensing Li Fan's intervention, perhaps wanting to take him along, she flew towards Li Fan's location.

However, to her utter astonishment, Li Fan retreated rapidly.

At the same time, Tian Yang and Qiu Shui stepped forward to intercept.

"'Returning to True'!"

Li Fan thought silently.

Chapter 1384: The Bone of the Nameless Immortal

"Returning to True!"

As Li Fan murmured in his heart, a layer of mist instantly enveloped everything around. However, Li Fan was shocked to find that the Nameless Monument not far away, also known as the Southern Immortal Pillar, seemed to retain its color even through the Returning to True's mist! It remained as radiant as ever.

Along with it, the True Immortal of the Immortal Ruins beside the Nameless Monument was also vaguely visible within the mist. Tian Yang and Qiu Shui's interception seemed to have not delayed her for long. The mist surrounding her was getting closer and closer to Li Fan. But just as she had approached the Nameless Monument in the Immortal Domain, her speed of approaching Li Fan slowed down, as if there was an infinite distance between them. Until she completely stopped. Thick fog completely obscured the True Immortal of the Immortal Ruins. Even the Nameless Monument became indistinct.

"That is..." Li Fan couldn't help but cast his gaze towards the Nameless Monument. He could vaguely see that on the monument, besides the two True Immortal Character Scripts formed by the Immortal Ruins True Immortal and the white circle Falling Mortal previously, a third character was beginning to manifest. Or rather, it was countless characters, appearing on the Nameless Monument simultaneously, densely packed!

A terrifying impact that was difficult to describe erupted from the Southern Immortal Pillar. Even though the scene in the Star Sea was no longer clear, from the ripples of the Returning to True's white mist, one could discern the power of this impact.

"Pfft!" Even with the protection of the Returning to True's white mist, the moment the countless symbols entered Li Fan's eyes, his brain felt as if it had been struck hundreds of times by a heavy hammer. His soul trembled and churned, his consciousness almost torn to shreds. Fortunately, at this very moment, the Southern Immortal Pillar itself could not withstand such pressure.

With a boom, it exploded into countless fragments! Perhaps it was a coincidence, or perhaps other factors were at play. In any case, the largest fragment flew straight towards Li Fan. It pierced through ordinary space a thousand times faster than the pursuit of the Immortal Ruins True Immortal, arriving within the Returning to True's white mist!

At the same time, the Returning to True's white mist completely engulfed the world. The moment the shattered stone entered the white mist, it lost all its speed and luster, merely floating quietly at the edge of the mist.

Dazed and disoriented, Li Fan, upon regaining his senses, looked around at the surrounding mist-shrouded area. Facing the situation where the anchor point had not returned to its predetermined state, he fell into deep thought. After carefully sensing the fluctuations from Returning to True, Li Fan cautiously beckoned and brought the fragment of the stone monument to his side.

A familiar light screen suddenly burst open, and the interrupted Returning to True process resumed. Scenes from his previous life flashed one after another. Before Li Fan's consciousness plunged into darkness, he noticed that the fragment of the Nameless Monument in his hand had disappeared when he didn't know when.

...

One year after anchoring, at the peak of Jieli Mountain! Li Fan, who was 20 years old, opened his eyes again. "Hoo!" This time, the simulation ended and he returned to the beginning, but it did not give Li Fan a feeling of having experienced millennia. The thrilling, bizarre, and unbelievable events at the end of his previous life were still vivid in his memory. It was as if they had happened in this life as well.

Li Fan instinctively glanced at the Returning to True panel. The charging progress remained at 31%. It was worth noting that at the beginning of Returning to True, the charging progress was the highest at 400%. This was enough to show how dangerous the end of his previous life was. Although he had successfully returned to the predetermined anchor point, Li Fan still felt somewhat uneasy. He walked out of the thatched cottage and came to the cliff edge of the mountain peak, facing the vast sea of clouds.

Staring intently at the Returning to True panel, he noticed a new item added to his retained items.

[...Leg bone]

Before the words "leg bone," there were twisted, blurry symbols. Li Fan could not discern their meaning. But Li Fan naturally knew where this bone came from. "Nameless Monument, Southern Immortal Pillar?" "This Immortal Pillar is actually forged from the leg bone of some unknown existence?"

Li Fan was extremely shocked. The indecipherable, twisted, and blurry symbols immediately made Li Fan associate it with the legendary Nameless True Immortal. This bold guess, in turn, sparked countless thoughts in Li Fan's mind.

"But the most important thing now is..." "To ensure my own safety." Casually picking up a stone at his feet, he clenched it in his hand and murmured in his heart. The prompt from Returning to True followed. "Do you wish to consume one available anchor point and replace the bound item... leg bone."

The moment the prompt appeared, Li Fan inexplicably breathed a sigh of relief. Returning to True had not gone out of control. He still possessed the highest control authority over Returning to True. The appearance of this leg bone simply meant that he had brought an additional stowaway during his last Returning to True process.

"Even so, this Nameless True Immortal leg bone is indeed extraordinary." Li Fan secretly marveled in his heart. Since the true origin of the leg bone could not be known for now, he could only refer to it as the Nameless True Immortal for the time being. He first used "No" to continue retaining the Nameless True Immortal leg bone.

Staring at the fragment of the stone monument in the Returning to True panel, Li Fan's expression became solemn. Recalling all the events that happened at the end of his previous life. "The Nameless Monument, also known as the Southern Immortal Pillar. It can resist the Calamity of Dao Annihilation to a certain extent."

"Since it is named Southern Immortal Pillar, it implies that there were definitely more than one such pillar in the Immortal Realm back then." "Leg bone... could it be that other Immortal Pillars were also forged from the bones of other parts of Nameless True Immortals? Or perhaps, from other Nameless True Immortals?" Li Fan felt a lingering chill in his heart.

"At the beginning, the Southern Immortal Pillar was basically indifferent to the Calamity of Dao Annihilation. It was only after the Hungry Immortal infused it with his [Hunger] character art that a sky-supporting pillar of light was formed, which then successfully resisted the Calamity of Dao Annihilation. The Nameless Monument seems to possess the supreme divine ability of revealing all things in the universe as their original Great Dao laws, and manifesting them as True Immortal Character Scripts on the monument."

"It was precisely because I saw this that I had a flash of inspiration and unleashed the White Circle Falling Mortal. Of course, it wasn't to save the Hungry Immortal's life, as I was already preparing for Returning to True at that time. It was to investigate the origin of the White Circle Falling Mortal." "As expected, Falling Mortal represents some extremely powerful law in the mortal world..."

Li Fan carefully recalled the character that appeared on the Nameless Monument in his previous life. "[Innate]." "It is of almost the same caliber as [Creation]." "In the past, the Dao Inscriber Immortal could reveal the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth as True Immortal Character Scripts. Yet now, beyond the High Wall, they can solidify the power of laws and forge them into objects?"

Li Fan's shock was even greater than when he first learned about the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone.

"However, whether the White Circle Falling Mortal is a product from beyond the High Wall is still uncertain..." Li Fan pressed his throbbing temples and took a deep breath. His thoughts returned to the main topic. "The Nameless Monument has appeared, absorbing everything from the outer Star Sea, as if to reveal the laws of heaven and earth on the monument and restore the true body of the Southern Immortal Pillar." "What I saw, and everything in the Star Sea, all transformed into threads of light, adding shadows to the Nameless Monument. This confirms this point." "And then..."

Thinking to this point, a strange color suddenly flashed in Li Fan's eyes. "Returning to True was activated, the Nameless Monument sensed it, and thousands of characters manifested on it!" In that instant, the characters that appeared on the monument were too numerous and too complex. Even with the help of the Dao Dissolving Stone, Li Fan could not remember them. He couldn't even leave a basic impression. He only vaguely remembered seeing dozens of familiar, but more complete and pure, True Immortal Character Scripts on it.

However, Li Fan did not feel regret or tiếc nuối. He had a premonition that if he were greedy and disregarded the consequences, trying to forcibly remember the entire monument of True Immortal Character Scripts... his fate would be the same as the Nameless Monument in his previous life. He would be shattered to pieces in an instant!

"Although forged from the leg bone of a Nameless True Immortal, and hailed as the Southern Immortal Pillar. It still could not withstand the thousands of characters manifested by Returning to True..." "It survived the Calamity of Immortal Realm's Destruction, yet was buried by its own characteristics." Li Fan secretly shook his head and warned himself, while also having new thoughts about [Returning to True].

"Since the Nameless Monument is called an Immortal Pillar, it might have once been inscribed with multiple True Immortal Character Scripts to resist the Calamity of Dao Annihilation in the Immortal Realm." "This is why, the moment I saw it, countless insights continuously emerged in my mind. Although the True Immortal Character Scripts on the monument have disappeared for unknown reasons, some faint imprints remain..." "All things in the world are derivations of the Dao. If one can master all the Daos, one can manifest everything in the world with a single thought. This is the so-called, Transformation Between True and False!"

At this moment, Li Fan had not yet chosen the inheritance option for Returning to True, and was still an undeniable mortal. However, he stood with his hands behind his back, his eyes slightly narrowed. A powerful pressure surged onto his body. In this instant, Li Fan's cultivation returned to the peak of the Nascent Soul stage, based on the Xuanhuang World Destruction Transformation. With a flick of his finger, a meteor shot upwards from the mountain peak against the flow of gravity. It tore through the sky curtain of the Great Xuan small world, revealing the dark void outside.

After completing all this, the mysterious aura on Li Fan's body slowly disappeared. "My understanding of the Transformation Between True and False has reached a higher level." "Without the assistance of Returning to True, I can momentarily restore my past cultivation. And in that instant, I can unleash my full power." "Although this transformation cannot last, it is of extraordinary significance to me."

After opening the Returning to True panel, Li Fan chose to inherit his cultivation. In an instant, Li Fan transformed from an ordinary person back to the peak of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. It was as if he had experienced hundreds of lifetimes of vicissitudes. "Transformation Between True and False..." Li Fan did not stop, but instead savored the entire process of Returning to True being activated, simulated, and undergoing reincarnation.

In a flash, another full cultivation of Li Fan descended! It was as if he had suddenly merged with another him. At this moment, the spiritual energy within Li Fan surged and boiled. The Wooden Sword Phantom was unsheathed, and in an instant, he arrived in the void of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. All his strength was unleashed. Ten thousand formidable transformations descended and evolved in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. It continued for a long time. The other layer of cultivation that appeared on Li Fan quietly receded. He returned to his normal state.

"I had already touched the limit of the Star Sea, but now I can temporarily achieve a double increase in strength through the Transformation Between True and False..." "And this increase has no side effects. Moreover, I can borrow all the operating costs from nowhere, achieving a certain meaning of perpetual motion." Li Fan looked at his hands, feeling incredibly incredulous. Even though he was the creator of this divine ability, he was shocked by its actual performance, which completely defied common sense.

"Returning to True, Returning to True..." Murmuring in his heart, Li Fan's gaze slowly became unfathomably deep. "What exactly is Returning to True?" "The Nameless Monument only sensed from the periphery and manifested thousands of True Immortal Character Scripts that it couldn't even bear itself. Its origin..." Even in his imagination, Li Fan could not fathom the origin of Returning to True. Li Fan only knew that possessing Returning to True was definitely his greatest fortune.

"In fact, I don't need to cultivate any new techniques at all. As long as I deepen my understanding of Returning to True, I can achieve true destruction and creation with a flip of my hand." "What True Immortals, what Nameless True Immortals. Life and death are all within my single thought." Li Fan's heart surged with emotion, filled with longing. But eventually, fantasies had to return to reality.

After a long while, Li Fan, who had a sufficient understanding of himself, shook his head slightly: "But this also has a paradox. If I don't cultivate first and improve my own strength and understanding, how can I truly understand [Returning to True]?" "When my strength was low, even if I held onto Returning to True for thousands or tens of thousands of lifetimes, I could not achieve the temporary Transformation Between True and False as I do now. Even if it's just my past cultivation." "And as my understanding of True Immortal Character Scripts and the Great Dao deepens, my deconstruction of Returning to True also gradually increases." Returning to True is too profound, mysterious, and complex. Even the laws of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth are merely tools for its interpretation. "The height of Returning to True is above the heavens. To touch Returning to True, one must first ascend to the Nine Heavens."

Li Fan had some restless thoughts in his heart, but they were quickly suppressed the moment they appeared. "It's still necessary to cultivate step by step, with solid foundations." Li Fan mused, and then thought of the reason why he had decided to unfold the Immortal Domain in his previous life. "Looking back now, the reason why I died prematurely in the simulation of my death was probably due to the combined effect of Mo Sha and the Nameless Monument." "It is very likely that Mo Sha, a weakened version of the Calamity of Dao Annihilation, returned to the Dao Annihilation realm after sublimation. When the Immortal Domain unfolded, the Nameless Monument also appeared instantly..."

Recalling the scene, Li Fan couldn't help but feel his skin crawl. "It was still too wishful thinking." "It could be harbored by ancient True Immortals to escape the Calamity of Dao Annihilation. I should have known that the Immortal Domain would never be simple." Li Fan sighed inwardly. But Li Fan did not give up on absorbing the Mo Sha Heavenly Immortal Soul because of this. Instead, the characteristic of Mo Sha, which could pose a great threat to Immortal-level beings, further strengthened Li Fan's resolve to use it as a material for Dao integration. After all, in the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea today, only Mo Sha Heavenly Immortal Soul could capture Li Fan's interest.

"Anchor the Xuanhuang Realm for sublimation..." "The Nameless Monument is too terrifying, so I cannot consider it for now." "But... a fragment of the Nameless Monument might be enough." The Wooden Sword Phantom was ready, and Li Fan, having made sufficient preparations, took out the Nameless True Immortal's bone, which had also returned with him through Returning to True.

Chapter 1385

If it were before Returning to True in the previous life, Li Fan would never have dared to risk his life to take out the stone fragment that flew out from the Nameless Monument himself before Returning to True was fully charged. However, now, the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone had become a bound item of Returning to True. Li Fan had personally witnessed the leg bone losing its spiritual essence and becoming motionless after entering the white mist of Returning to True. Li Fan was confident that the subsidiary items of Returning to True would absolutely not harm him.

He carefully examined the object that appeared before him. If it weren't for the prompt from Returning to True, Li Fan would never have thought that this fist-sized round stone fragment was the leg bone of an unknown, powerful being. "Unlike the complete Southern Immortal Pillar, looking at its surface, there are no philosophical insights surging in my mind. It seems to be just an ordinary stone..." Li Fan observed from a distance, without getting too close.

"The Nameless True Immortal is a being beyond True Immortals, who has completely mastered a certain Dao and transcended. Mortals cannot know or see it." "However, there are no traces of the Great Dao on this leg bone..." "Could it be that the Dao mastered by this Nameless True Immortal has been stripped away? Was He Himself slaughtered, and His bones refined into an Immortal Pillar that supports the heavens?" Li Fan's mind raced with speculation.

But even when facing an unremarkable leg bone, Li Fan did not lower his guard. The True Immortal's skeletal remains beneath the dark sea could give birth to [The Will to Survive]. Who knew what horrors the Nameless True Immortal's remains could evolve into? However, the reason Li Fan was so eager to take it out and study it was naturally to verify a certain guess in his heart.

In his previous life, after he threw the White Circle Falling Mortal at the Nameless Monument, and the monument manifested the [Innate] character. Li Fan's understanding of the details of the [Innate] character was magnified countless times, presented perfectly. It should be known that True Immortal Character Scripts are actually alternative manifestations of the Great Dao, and not something that can be easily comprehended. Even the True Immortal of the Immortal Ruins had to meditate for tens of thousands of years to comprehend a single character [Hunger].

As for the peerless prodigies among mortals, like the elders of the Immortal Boat throughout the generations, even to merely replicate the original appearance of True Immortal Character Scripts, they had to pass down their knowledge generation after generation through collective wisdom. There was a natural chasm between True Immortal Character Scripts and mortal existence, preventing mortals from investigating them.

Li Fan, with his great fortuitous encounters, had seen quite a few True Immortal Character Scripts. However, most of them were imitations from the "He Gan Immortal" who had caused the catastrophe in the Star Sea back then. Originally, Li Fan thought that his knowledge had already captured eighty to ninety percent of the true essence. But at the end of his previous life, a mere stroke on the Nameless Monument inscribed with True Immortal Character Scripts made Li Fan suddenly realize. "The True Immortal Character Scripts that I know now, namely [Innate] and [Hunger], are the closest to the fundamental. In fact, my understanding of Innate is even superior to Hunger! Because Hunger was seen by me observing from outside the Immortal Realm, while [Innate]... was directly projected into my mind!" A faint light flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"The Nameless Monument is like an analytical machine, breaking down all things into their most original state and manifesting them as True Immortal Character Scripts. Furthermore, when an object is personally thrown into it, there seems to be an additional bonus..." "Isn't this a perfect, natural artifact for learning True Immortal Character Scripts?" Thinking of this, Li Fan couldn't help but become somewhat excited. Even though he considered himself usually calm, he found it difficult to contain his excitement at this moment.

"Even if it's just a fragment of the Nameless Monument, this leg bone's ability to deduce True Immortal Character Scripts far surpasses that of the entire Immortal Boat!" "It will be of great help to me in mastering as many True Immortal Character Scripts as possible!" Li Fan stared intently at the leg bone not far away, his eyes shining, his heart surging with emotion.

True Immortal Character Scripts were not merely significant in the mortal realm. Even after ascending to True Immortal, they remained so. To progress further, True Immortals had to continue studying them, choosing a suitable path to seek the realm of [Namelessness]. "Of course, what is manifested on this Nameless Monument might not necessarily be pure True Immortal Character Scripts representing the original laws of the Great Dao." "It's more like..." "The insights of that Nameless True Immortal into all the Great Daos in the mortal world." "Unless this Nameless True Immortal is the legendary [Dao Inscriber Immortal]..." Li Fan's thoughts suddenly paused. After careful consideration, if this were truly the case, the implications were too profound for Li Fan. He silently buried this thought deep in his heart for now.

"The vision of a Nameless True Immortal is naturally far superior to ours. What He inscribed, even if not the Great Dao itself, is almost indistinguishable from it. It is sufficient to serve as my teacher for a long time to come." "Although my idea is good, manifesting True Immortal Character Scripts on the Nameless Monument is not an easy task. "The White Circle Falling Mortal itself is mysterious and unpredictable. Manifesting characters individually was as expected." "As for the Hungry Immortal. He gave his all, and only managed to manifest the character [Hunger] on the stone monument..." Li Fan frowned slightly: "With ordinary methods, even if the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea were to be buried, it might not be enough to manifest many effective characters."

"But it doesn't matter, I took out this leg bone precisely to deal with those strange and unusual things." A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. In his past two lifetimes, Li Fan had experienced two great upheavals in the Star Sea. One was when Mao Bao attracted external forces from beyond the High Wall, and the other was when the Immortal Domain descended, carrying the Immortal Pillar. Under the overwhelming crisis of annihilation, all hidden existences in the Star Sea were exposed. With all means employed, Li Fan saw clearly.

"Now, in the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea, besides those few, there are only a few others who can pose a threat to me." "Before achieving Dao Integration, it is estimated that even if I explore and research again, the result will be the same as in my previous life. But now that I have the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone, it's different." "No matter how strong or mysterious, can it surpass the Nameless True Immortal?!" Scenes from Li Fan's previous life flashed before his eyes.

"Then let's take them one by one!" The Nameless True Immortal's leg bone descended, and after a long time without any abnormality, Li Fan felt reassured. With a thought, he returned it to the Returning to True's bound space. Then, he returned to the Xuanhuang Realm and arrived at the small world inhabited by the You clan.

In his previous life, Li Fan discovered that the You clan, as descendants of the first Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, seemed to have True Immortal Character Scripts related to the power of [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] sealed within their bloodline. However, with his strength at that time, he couldn't glimpse it completely. But in this life, with the Nameless Monument, Li Fan didn't need to act personally. "As long as enough You clan members are sacrificed, the True Immortal Character Script of [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] can truly be manifested!"

Looking at the not very numerous, and physically weak You clan population below, Li Fan's expression was indifferent. "The current number is not enough. A portion also needs to be allocated to provide me with Origin Energy Essence." "As the saying goes, 'To take something, one must first give something'..." Li Fan waved his hand gently, just as he had done in his previous life. The apocalyptic images related to the Immortal-Mortal Transformation appeared in the minds of a few You clan members below. They turned into dust for touching the forbidden, but the physical constitution of the entire You clan gradually became stronger due to a certain degree of ancestral return.

"Governing a large country is like cooking a small fish. Patience is key." Li Fan murmured in his heart, leaving behind a strand of divine sense to supervise. He himself returned to the Great Xuan small world. The White Circle Falling Mortal appeared, turning Jieli Mountain into nothingness. The Lecture Platform stood between heaven and earth, attracting mortals from all over Great Xuan like moths to a flame.

"In this life, the plan remains unchanged. Promote the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation, and achieve Dao Integration with Heavenly Souls." "Only some minor details need to be refined and modified." "It is still necessary to play the role of the Teacher of Heaven and Earth, allowing all living beings to perceive the flaws in the High Wall and explore the carefree paradise for me." "Carefree..." Li Fan's gaze turned towards the territory of the Five Elder Council, his expression inexplicably changing.

In his previous life, when the Nameless Monument appeared, the Five Elder Council members, including the Longevity Heavenly Venerable, did not show up. It seemed they hadn't noticed it at all. But later, when the Returning to True's white mist enveloped everything, and only the Nameless Monument shone, some anomalies were revealed. "Besides the Hungry Immortal, there were other observers at that time. Although they had no physical form, their thoughts reached them undetectably. Within the Star Sea, only a few could achieve this level." "However, it was enough to make the Hungry Immortal and a group of Grand Elders unable to notice. It's hard to say what the specific combat power of this person is. But this life-saving technique is truly uncanny."

... "However, with the experience of the beings exploring in the previous life, the speed of exploring the dreamland in this life will definitely accelerate further." "No matter how deep the dream is, it cannot withstand my incessant probing through reincarnation." "Hmph... Carefree!" Strands of divine sense flew towards various small worlds in Xuanhuang, manifesting grand Lecture Platforms that reached the heavens. Under Li Fan's control, simulated Heavenly Dao were gradually created. Where small worlds already had Heavenly Dao consciousness, they were replaced. Where they didn't, they served as their Heavenly Dao.

In Li Fan's sea of consciousness, points of light gradually lit up. Each point of light represented a small world in Xuanhuang. Li Fan, like a deity from above, looked down upon billions of living beings. At the same time, Li Fan did not forget Wuyou from the Thirteen Peaks World. Under Li Fan's guidance, he also generated the idea of going out and exploring a larger world. However, after the upheaval, Li Fan needed more time to prepare in this life. Wuyou was currently still comprehending the Heavenly Dao of the small world in the Thirteen Peaks World. But Li Fan had secretly connected this small world with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

Before Returning to True was fully charged, Li Fan did not dare to act rashly, proceeding step by step, almost exactly following the trajectory of his previous life. In the blink of an eye, three years had passed since anchoring. In these three years, Li Fan's focus was on the You clan. He descended heavenly revelations almost every few days. The You clan's overall comprehension of the Immortal-Mortal Transformation had even almost caught up with Li Fan.

The You clan members who further unlocked their seals and reverted to their ancestral bloodline showed a terrifying rate of reproduction. Fetuses grew from birth to adulthood in only twenty to thirty days. Moreover, every You clan member was almost robust and immune to all diseases. In just three years, their figures had filled and occupied the entire small world. Seeing the world's ecosystem struggling to cope, Li Fan felt it was time to harvest.

Dark clouds suddenly gathered in the sky. Amidst the swirling vortex of oppressive clouds, a stone monument crashed to the ground. Its immense power instantly crushed tens of thousands of You clan members. Blood flowed like water, surging towards the stone monument. Their corpses also turned into streams of light, flying into the stone monument. As Li Fan had predicted, the stone monument began to manifest faint illusory figures. However, the materials absorbed so far were too scarce, and it was still far from manifesting the complete True Immortal Character Script.

The appearance of the stone monument shocked the entire You clan. After several attempts to confirm its danger, all the You clan members chose to flee from the area covered by the stone monument. But how could Li Fan let them have their way? The formation, as if breathing in and out, absorbed most of the You clan members into the stone monument. They became the fuel for deducing the True Immortal Character Scripts. The formation's range continued to expand, almost engulfing the entire You clan completely. Soon, only a corner of the small world was left with surviving You clan members, numbering around eight thousand.

The inexplicable arrival of this doom made these You clan members tremble with fear. And just then, Li Fan sent out a dark illusionary shadow, blocking the expanding formation. The dark illusionary shadow emitted wisps of darkness. It forced the ravenous formation to retreat. The You clan members who survived the disaster rejoiced, spontaneously kneeling and praying. The illusionary shadow seemed to sense their piety, and once again forced the formation to retreat, creating enough space for the You clan to survive. Then, as if exhausted, it transformed into a stone statue, falling into the You clan's settlement. The You clan members quickly gathered around, protecting the stone statue.

Li Fan, positioned above the small world, saw this scene and nodded slightly. "Every time the You clan multiplies to a certain extent, the formation harvests a batch." "This way, not only do I satisfy my consumption of Origin Energy Essence; but I also have enough material for the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone to deduce the [Immortal-Mortal Transformation]." With this thought, Li Fan couldn't help but glance at the stone monument standing in the center of this small world. The Nameless True Immortal's leg bone was naturally not that large; it was merely covered by a formation on the outer layer as a disguise.

After absorbing ninety percent of the You clan, the changes on the leg bone were also very obvious. Continuous golden patterns emerged. "These characters seem more complex than [Creation] and [Innate]." "Moreover, besides complexity..." Li Fan mused, his expression inexplicable. "There is also a sense of sacredness, a majestic aura within it." Comparing it to his experiences in his previous life, Li Fan estimated that at the current pace, it would take about another hundred years to manifest the complete True Immortal Character Script. "This is too slow." "Do I need to unlock more of the You clan's bloodline seals?"

Chapter 1386: Mortal Peeks into the Immortal Realm

In the small world, stimulated by the impending possibility of extinction brought about by the stone tablet, the You clan's desire for reproduction reached a new peak.

Once their subjective initiative was fully ignited, their reproductive speed was predictable to at least double.

"The factors limiting their clan's expansion are resources and time."

"This physique..."

Li Fan's eyes flickered. He casually grabbed a You clan member for research, comparing him to his previous life.

"As the seals are gradually unlocked, the efficiency of returning to the ancestral state does not grow linearly; rather, the further back one goes, the greater the enhancement."

Li Fan controlled the energy output level, constantly testing.

He discovered that the vitality of these You clan members was terrifyingly abundant.

They could now withstand the attacks of ordinary late-stage Qi Refining cultivators with their flesh and blood.

"Moreover, a strong adult You clan member can withstand a blow from a Core Formation stage cultivator without dying. With their physical quality, as long as they are not killed on the spot, they can quickly become vigorous and alive again..."

Li Fan shook his head slightly, and the thought that had just emerged in his mind was immediately extinguished: "The current level is already the limit."

"It's not that I fear these You clan members becoming uncontrollable. No matter how strong they become, they are utterly powerless against the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone. It's just a concern about the first Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate..."

"The revival of descendants from the bloodline is not impossible. It is still best to be cautious."

"As for how to ensure that I can use the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone to deduce the complete [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] in this lifetime..."

Li Fan glanced at the blurry imprints on the stone tablet.

"True Immortal Transformation, once lost, is lost forever. If it's not fully comprehended during the first encounter, there will be no opportunity to understand its mysteries in this lifetime..."

"Once the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone has deduced more than half of the progress, I will personally comprehend its mysteries within the You clan's bloodline."

"While comprehending, I will directly inject everything I see and feel into the stone tablet. I cannot remember it, but the Nameless True Immortal should not be subject to this limitation."

Li Fan made a tentative plan in his heart.

Below, the stone statue that the You clan regarded as their savior was continuously transmitting Origin Energy Essence to Li Fan.

As the You clan members' physique improved, the quantity and quality of Origin Energy Essence produced by each of their prayers far surpassed previous levels.

In this lifetime, Li Fan no longer had to worry about insufficient Origin Energy Essence.

Golden light flowed, and Li Fan, outside the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone, set up another layer of immortal formation protection.

At the same time, using the [Artifact Creation, Thousand Forms of Living Beings] formation, he generated a heavenly authority to monitor all actions in this small world.

After making thorough preparations, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction and left.

Over the next six months, Li Fan used the inexhaustible Origin Energy Essence to set up immortal formations in the majority of the Profound Yellow Realm's small worlds.

Firstly, to promote the return of the small worlds to the Profound Yellow, preparing for the future sublimation into an Immortal Domain.

Secondly, to better control the myriad realms and search for "embryos" suitable for refining Eternal Remnant Thoughts.

In his previous life, Li Fan attempted to use Kou Hong, a sincere Dao seeker, to catalyze the birth of artificial Eternal Remnant Thoughts. Although the result ultimately failed, it gave Li Fan some inspiration.

In fact, judging from the fact that [Returning to True] could barely swallow Kou Hong's remnant thought, it was not far from the formation of a true Eternal Remnant Thought.

Perhaps it was only a final push.

Li Fan pondered, perhaps it was due to the insufficient refining time and insufficient heat.

"Profound emotions that do not fade with the passage of time, and react with renewed brilliance. The more the river of time washes over them, the more crystalline and radiant they become." Li Fan's eyes showed contemplation.

"I do not yet control the power of distorted time, but I can use illusion formations to achieve the effect of 'approaching reality'."

"In this lifetime, I will collect enough seeds and then throw them all into the [Bewildering, Profound Yellow Beings] grand formation!"

"If there are enough seeds, I don't believe not one will ripen!"

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes: "If not for the scenes from my previous life that flashed back after swallowing Kou Hong's remnant thought, with my temperament, I would probably still have stubbornly sought harmonization with the Dao."

"Eternal Remnant Thoughts can stimulate the unknown potential of [Returning to True], which is indeed too important."

"Equally important are the Three-Pronged Tree and the puppet from the Immortal Boat, these relics left by Sun Piaomiao. I wonder if these items can still be useful to [Returning to True] in this lifetime..."

The Immortal Boat possessed the power of True Immortal Character Scripts, and its treasure trove within the Hundred Question Immortal Records was even more inexhaustible. It could even control an ancient Desolate God.

Before [Returning to True] was fully charged, Li Fan would not risk provoking it rashly.

"Now that Origin Energy Essence is abundant, I can set up immortal formations to kill enemies at any time."

"But in terms of my strongest killing divine ability, it is still [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger]."

On the Great Xuan Dao Lecture Platform, three figures were in slumber.

One large and two small, two males and one female.

The young figure was naturally Ou Shangtian.

As for the other two, they were like Ou Shangtian. The miraculous items within their bodies were suspected to originate from the True Immortal's skeletal remains.

"In my previous life, I glimpsed many scenes from the True Immortal's flesh and blood."

"I wonder if I can see more this time."

The miraculous item within Ou Shangtian was the Qian Gan Bone Hand.

As for the man and woman, they were the Stepping Wind Foot and the Illusory Vision Divine Eye, respectively.

The Stepping Wind Foot not only allowed for rapid travel by wind but also enabled the absorption of the luck and destiny of every person it killed. By using all beings as steps, one could ascend step by step, gazing down from high above.

The Illusory Vision Divine Eye could not only see through all illusions in the world but also, at crucial moments, spontaneously generate illusions. Whether it was a warning of the future or the perception of hidden treasures in the vicinity, its uses were endless.

Li Fan had even captured the female cultivator with the Illusory Vision Divine Eye before he even made a move; she seemed to have sensed it beforehand and her expression changed dramatically. However, the power gap between her and Li Fan was too vast. Even though she sensed it, she had no time to react and was captured by Li Fan.

The three supreme artifact bearers floated quietly in the air.

Li Fan, finally ready, made his move.

With brushstrokes like flying dragons and snakes, the character [Ancient] suddenly appeared in the arena.

The mystical power to trace back to the past shone upon the True Immortal's skeletal remains within the three figures.

The True Immortal's flesh and blood began to emerge from them.

It was as if the True Immortal who had died long ago was about to be resurrected.

Golden threads served as ropes, and Li Fan manipulated them, bringing the three masses of flesh and blood closer to each other.

They were still some distance apart, but they instantly attracted each other.

Li Fan looked at the writhing, deformed mass of flesh and blood not far away. He had already prepared a character, which floated and formed.

This character was not some True Immortal Character Script, but an array formation carved by Li Fan himself.

The formation connected to the You clan's small world.

The simulated Heavenly Authority that was suppressed there was responsible for channeling everything affected here into the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone.

The formation had not been fully deployed, only a hint of its aura was leaking out.

That mass of flesh and blood, as if encountering some terrifying monster, trembled violently and rapidly retreated backward, trying to escape.

How could Li Fan let it have its way? He manipulated the character, and with a gentle press, it was suppressed upon the True Immortal's flesh and blood.

Even though the formation was not fully connected, this character still held the True Immortal's flesh and blood tightly.

It was as if it had instantly lost its spirituality, becoming a pile of dead meat, utterly incapable of moving.

Li Fan, holding another character, then slowly approached.

Drawn by the deterrence of the aura, which was possibly from the Nameless True Immortal, even though Li Fan was a mortal below the Immortal level, after approaching, the True Immortal's flesh and blood showed no abnormalities.

It was as if all its strange properties had vanished.

It allowed Li Fan to grope and examine it freely.

Li Fan nodded slightly, separating a wisp of his divine sense and probing into the True Immortal's flesh and blood.

Boom!

After all, Li Fan was not the Nameless True Immortal himself.

He was merely borrowing power, only able to suppress the True Immortal's flesh and blood superficially. When he tried to truly act as a mortal, the backlash he should have received still descended.

But this time, perhaps because Li Fan had already peeked into it, the backlash he suffered was much less severe than the first time he encountered it.

His hair did not turn white instantly, only his lifespan was consumed at about two to three times the normal aging speed.

This was completely within Li Fan's acceptable range.

Li Fan's expression was indifferent as he watched the scenes unfolding before him.

At first, it was related scenes similar to what he had seen in his previous life.

"...Qionglang Star Domain... Annihilation... Guarding..."

"...Target found."

"Your subordinate, accepts the order."

Still conversations within the Immortal Realm.

However, this time, with the last gaze of longing from that True Immortal before leaving the Immortal Realm, Li Fan was able to truly witness the legendary Immortal Realm with his own eyes.

It was like a sea with countless waves appearing simultaneously. Each wave was a star domain within the Immortal Realm.

Within the star domains, True Immortals were as rare as stars. Most were creations of True Immortals themselves.

Images of magnificent and sacred palaces simultaneously appeared in each wave.

Seated in the palaces were figures who seemed to command a region of the immortal domain.

Even that descending True Immortal dared not look directly at them.

He only saw a phantom figure from memory.

The sea of stars surged, and all the waves disappeared beneath the horizon.

The True Immortal descended to the lower realm, Profound Yellow.

...

Even though it was just a fleeting glimpse, the vibrant and boundless Immortal Realm scenes he spied upon still stirred Li Fan's heart.

"It is rumored that the Immortal Realm is a supreme holy land with infinite resources. It seems it is indeed true."

"That ocean is truly too vast! Each wave encompassing a star domain could be considered an endless expanse!"

"It's simply unimaginable!"

Li Fan's heart trembled, his brow furrowed. The glimpse of the Immortal Realm completely surpassed his understanding.

The memory of the True Immortal from the Immortal Realm continued.

He was guarding Profound Yellow, seemingly waiting for something.

The stars floated and sank, and time passed, though he knew not how long.

Even these True Immortals could not avoid having their emotions fluctuate.

"Five hundred years have passed since the calculated time."

"It still hasn't appeared..."

The constant shaking of the image was enough to illustrate the True Immortal's inner turmoil at that time.

"Let's wait a bit longer."

Within the Profound Yellow Realm, the sun rose and set. Who knew how much time passed.

"Fifteen hundred years."

"It has completely exceeded the scope of error..."

"The worst has happened. That thing..."

"It probably won't come."

As this thought emerged, the entire world instantly turned gray, as if the last straw of hope had been lost. The True Immortal closed his eyes, and endless despair surged within his heart.

But he didn't know why, as he thought of something, the despair in his consciousness gradually subsided.

"The Great One has great plans."

"Ants also have their own ways of survival."

"..."

The True Immortal's gaze swept across the Profound Yellow Realm of that time and the entire sea of stars.

Boom! The image shattered abruptly.

...

"Even as a True Immortal, one is still an ant?"

"Then what kind of existence could the 'Great One' he spoke of be?"

"Nameless True Immortal?"

"Is the gap truly so vast between being nameless and not?" Li Fan's heart trembled again.

The True Immortal's personal memories were naturally far more credible than unfounded speculation.

Li Fan, therefore, established a preliminary understanding of the Immortal Realm.

As Li Fan spied on these memories, the speed at which his lifespan flowed was two to three times faster than before.

His hair began to show streaks of white, but Li Fan still did not give up on continuing to spy.

He had a premonition that the most important intelligence was about to appear.

...

The images flowed again, and the True Immortal was no longer overlooking the Profound Yellow Realm.

Instead, he was sitting at a stone table by a pool of water, drinking tea with someone.

That figure was blurry.

But judging by the True Immortal's attitude, the other party was definitely an extraordinary figure.

What shook Li Fan even more was that the pool of water by the stone table where the True Immortal sat was also very familiar to him.

It was the fishing pond!

From the figure opposite him, a voice emerged.

The True Immortal nodded respectfully, but in Li Fan's memory, no imprint was left behind.

After finishing a cup of tea, the figure opposite disappeared mysteriously. The True Immortal's extremely tense emotions also relaxed.

The stone table, the stone chair, and even the cup of tea they had just drunk vanished.

It was as if it had all been a dream, having never happened.

But Li Fan could feel the excitement of the True Immortal's emotions in his memory.

He looked at the calm pool of water not far away.

With a flick of his finger, he threw a light cluster into it.

The light cluster entered the water without causing any ripples, and was instantly swallowed and disappeared.

The True Immortal closed his eyes, sensing something.

After a long time, He slowly walked to the edge of the pool.

He looked down at his reflection in the water.

Boom!

A face appeared in Li Fan's mind.

The True Immortal's flesh and blood, which had been suppressed by the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone, suddenly became violent.

Li Fan's hair instantly turned completely white.

He suddenly withdrew from spying on the memory.

"It's just the aging of the body. I still have over three hundred years of lifespan, which is not a big deal."

"The True Immortal's flesh and blood also quickly calmed down. It should just be a brief resonance caused by the True Immortal's face appearing in the memory."

Li Fan quickly made a judgment.

The mass of flesh and blood was still obediently suppressed by the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone.

Li Fan, however, had not yet recovered from what he had just seen, his expression somewhat dazed.

In the reflection of the fishing pond water, he saw the True Immortal's face.

However, what made him confused and terrified was that the face was exactly the same as his own!

Chapter 1387: Infinite Return

The moment Li Fan saw his own face in the water of the fishing pond, myriad thoughts instantly flashed through his mind.

"Could the body I transmigrated into and possessed actually be the reincarnation of that True Immortal who descended to the mortal realm back then?"

"Did I not awaken [Returning to True] through [Transmigration], but rather by [Possessing] and taking the treasures of the original body?"

Against his will, this thought spread wildly in Li Fan's mind.

But...

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, [Returning to True] surprisingly emitted a faint, mocking laugh.

This made Li Fan pause, then suddenly come to his senses.

"No. The original body I replaced was too ordinary. Where was there any hint of a True Immortal's demeanor?"

"If I hadn't intervened, he would have likely remained an unremarkable scholar his entire life, dying without having mastered any martial arts."

"And even I, without [Returning to True]."

Li Fan recalled the end of his first life.

"Although I had children and grandchildren, I was ultimately just a mortal, dying of old age."

"I could use a part of [Returning to True] as my foundation, and coupled with the sensing and interaction between me and it over so many reincarnations..."

"I am absolutely not the reincarnation of a True Immortal, nor was [Returning to True] captured by a True Immortal's contingency plan."

"Only one possibility remains..."

"Even in memory, the fishing pond reflected my original appearance?"

After ruling out the answer that could have sent chills down his spine, Li Fan not only did not feel better but still felt even colder.

He suddenly looked up at the real fishing pond.

"To achieve Namelessness, and merge with the Dao. The fishing pond, regardless of when and where, represents that True Immortal."

"Did the Nameless True Immortal see me through the fishing pond just now?"

Li Fan's heart leaped.

The more he thought about it, the more terrified he became.

For example, was this a trap set by that True Immortal in conjunction with Nameless? Had his possession of [Returning to True] been exposed?

Even worse, his [Returning to True] had not finished charging. If that Nameless True Immortal attacked, even with his supreme escape techniques, he might not be able to escape.

Li Fan couldn't help but curse inwardly.

He had originally thought that he had basically explored the Star Sea within the High Wall, and as long as he did not proactively provoke those few existences, there would be no danger. Who would have thought that merely studying True Immortal flesh and blood could lead to so many complications!

Even though his previous life's experience seemed to indicate that even if Li Fan died, [Returning to True] could still be activated.

But firstly, Li Fan had never truly died and experienced the self-activation of [Returning to True]. Secondly, Li Fan was not sure if [Returning to True] would still be effective if its charging was not yet complete.

Cold sweat broke out.

As if facing the greatest crisis in his life, Li Fan did not choose to wait for death.

In a flash, Li Fan thought of various possible countermeasures.

"Go to the center of the Star Sea, and by falling into it, trigger the black energy of the Calamity of Dao Annihilation..."

"Go to the breach in the High Wall, strike the High Wall, and attract the attention from outside the High Wall."

"If captured into the fishing pond, then find Mao Bao."

...

But no matter which method, facing the realm of a Nameless True Immortal, it seemed like futile struggles.

"If it were just a True Immortal, these clever tactics might still work."

"The realm of Namelessness..."

Thinking of the True Immortal's fear and reverence for [Namelessness] in the memory of descending to the mortal realm, Li Fan felt a sense of powerlessness.

"It still has to be [Returning to True]."

In the end, Li Fan did only one thing. The phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed, and he flew towards the Xuan Immortal Boat at the edge of the Star Sea.

He infiltrated it silently and retrieved the puppet from the first level of the secret treasury.

This puppet had assisted in rebuilding the Immortal Boat in his previous life. Li Fan entered as if it were his own home, without alarming anyone on the Xuan Immortal Boat, and successfully retrieved the puppet, one of Sun Piaomiao's relics.

To Li Fan's surprise, even though [Returning to True] had already absorbed it once, it still showed a desire to consume the puppet.

Eagerly feeding it to Returning to True, Li Fan let out a sigh of relief as he saw the charging progress reach 150%.

"The effect has weakened, but judging by [Returning to True]'s reaction, it can still be consumed one more time."

"This implies that the Three-pronged Tree might be the same."

"Items that can allow Returning to True to be consumed three times consecutively..."

"What is the origin of these items left by Sun Piaomiao?"

Li Fan's brow furrowed.

Suddenly, an idea flashed through Li Fan's mind.

"The Three-pronged Tree can inexplicably simulate one more time for [Returning to True]."

"And this puppet might also be related to the power of simulation."

In front of Li Fan, the Immortal Realm scene glimpsed not long ago reappeared.

"Before I transmigrated, I once heard that on an immeasurable long timescale, the smallest particles that make up all things, through countless combinations, will recreate everything that has ever happened. This is returning, and also destiny."

"True is false, false is true. Each simulation of Returning to True can be seen as another return of all things."

"Infinite timescale implies infinite energy..."

Li Fan's thoughts drifted to the unfathomable depths beneath the ocean of the Immortal Realm.

"Perhaps this puppet is the key to unlocking that infinite power."

"Or perhaps, it is a projection of the Great Dao related to infinite power."

At this moment, Li Fan was completely immersed in his thoughts, unable to extricate himself.

It wasn't that he had forgotten the fatal crisis of being pursued by the Nameless True Immortal.

But when Li Fan was arduously flying towards the Xuan Immortal Boat, and the Nameless True Immortal had not yet descended.

Then, it meant He would not come again.

It was just a false alarm, and nothing had happened.

When Li Fan slowly emerged from his contemplation, he did not feel much relief from surviving the disaster.

"The power of a True Immortal is immense, as if they were present themselves."

"The realm of Namelessness is likely even more so."

"In the memory of that True Immortal descending to the mortal realm, when facing me, He did not react."

"Either the Nameless True Immortal cannot perceive or detect [Returning to True] within me. Or..."

"That Nameless Angler's situation is probably not good."

Li Fan's heart leaped.

In his previous life, at the end of Mao Bao's appearance and easily capturing the Hungry Immortal, Li Fan had two speculations.

One was that Mao Bao was the work of the Nameless Angler, used to capture the True Immortal on the verge of achieving Namelessness, and achieve some form of eating.

Or, the angler was also being fished. Mao Bao was thrown into the fishing pond by an unknown force outside the High Wall, specifically to track down the Nameless Angler when the Nameless Angler revealed any traces.

Combining the current events, it seemed that Li Fan's second speculation was developing.

Even though Li Fan had exposed such a flaw, the Nameless Angler still had not appeared. This was like stirring up grass and startling a snake!

Li Fan took a deep breath.

In this short period, the True Immortal's blood had led to too many events.

It was all far beyond Li Fan's current control.

Whether it was a True Immortal or a Nameless True Immortal. They were not something he could contend with.

Li Fan's desire to achieve Dao Integration grew stronger.

"After merging with the Celestial Immortal Soul, at the very least, from an ant who cannot resist at all, I will become a wolf that can bite back fiercely."

"Moreover, I have a premonition. When I reach the level of [Immortal], [Returning to True] will also undergo an unprecedented transformation!" Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp light.

This premonition was also a form of comfort that [Returning to True] had conveyed after sensing his random thoughts. Or perhaps it was some encouragement or assurance.

It made Li Fan feel a little more at ease.

"It seems that this life should try to avoid any more complications."

"Achieving Dao Integration as soon as possible is the best course!"

While contemplating, Li Fan had already made up his mind.

"The second level of the secret treasury is protected by Heavenly Star Light Lotus. I haven't found a way to break it yet, so I won't force it."

"Let's clear out the first level of the secret treasury first."

As the saying goes, "A thief never leaves empty-handed."

Since he was already in the Hundred Tales Immortal Record's secret treasury, how could Li Fan leave empty-handed?

After carefully selecting again, he took away all the useful items.

Before the Xuan Immortal Boat's crew discovered it, he left quietly.

Not to mention that shortly after, the Xuan Immortal Boat fell into chaos again due to the discovery of the theft from the secret treasury, almost splitting into two for the second time.

Li Fan, on the other hand, returned to the Xuanhuang Realm laden with spoils. The first thing he did was to reforge his two "Supreme" combatants.

He arrived at the edge of the Star Sea, holding the liquid long sword, and performed the [Tai Jia Divine Art] improved by the elders of the Xuan Immortal Boat.

This time, due to the passage of tens of thousands of years and no cultivators having contacted the Star Sea's consciousness, coupled with the goodwill accumulated from the Tai Jia Realm, Li Fan's communication with the Star Sea was far smoother than in his previous life.

Not only did it not feel any anger about its power being taken, but it was also surprised that such an ant could perform such a divine ability.

Coincidentally, the power of the Star Sea infused this time was slightly different from before.

Under the combined power of the Unity Character Script and the Life Form Shape, the new Qiu Shui was slowly born.

"Thank you, Great Master, for bestowing life!"

The sword spirit, still naked, knelt respectfully before Li Fan.

This time, Qiu Shui's eyes were full of life and intelligence. Li Fan had already decided on a name for him long ago.

"From now on, I shall call you... [Autumn Water]!"

After accepting the name "Autumn Water," Li Fan immediately rushed back to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Eternal Remnant Thought, True Immortal flesh and blood, Black Star Stone, Copper Immortal Crane...

Coupled with the combat memories of [Ancestor].

The key materials were all ready.

During the forging of Tian Yang, Li Fan also had Qiu Shui continuously infuse the infinite power of the Star Sea.

The puppet's body surged with energy. If Li Fan hadn't used immortal formations to conceal it, the cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm would have surely noticed the commotion.

After a period of hard work, [Supreme] Tian Yang emerged once more.

This time, although he did not gain combat insights from the ancient Desolate God, he was infused with the infinite power of the Star Sea.

Like the Qiu Shui Sword, Tian Yang also became adorned with starlight, appearing divine.

With the two Supreme protectors in place, Li Fan could finally breathe a sigh of relief.

"Even if a True Immortal were to reappear, I would have no fear."

After observing the sparring match between Tian Yang and Qiu Shui, Li Fan thought so.

Li Fan sat at the Great Xuan Lecture Platform.

Treasures obtained from the Xuan Immortal Boat's secret treasury were arranged like stars in the sky.

"Some treasures that nourish small worlds can be integrated into the small worlds."

"When the small worlds return to Xuanhuang, they can serve as supplements for Xuanhuang's sublimation."

"As for those divine weapons and sharp swords, they can be distributed to the beings exploring the carefree dreamlands. They are almost all realm artifacts, which can greatly speed up their exploration."

...

With a thought from Li Fan, strands of starlight flew towards the various small worlds.

Feeling the increasingly brilliant points of light in his sea of consciousness.

Waves of enlightenment surged into Li Fan's heart.

"The Dan, is the transformation of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth; the Medicine, is to cure all diseases in the world. The Great Dao is formless, independent and unchanging, traversing all things endlessly. Combining with Dan, manifesting with Medicine. Heaven and Earth? It's just a Dan recipe..."

"The Alchemy King Scripture is indeed extraordinary!"

If in his previous life, Li Fan's promotion of Xuanhuang's sublimation was like carrying out a routine task.

Then now, Li Fan felt as if he were refining an unparalleled Dan medicine with the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth.

"First, use low heat to slowly bake it."

"The current auxiliary materials are still insufficient."

Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he revisited some preparatory tasks he had done in his previous life.

In addition, he secretly diverted some of the vitality from the terrestrial fissure depressions into the Xuanhuang Realm.

Controlling the flow of the surging vitality, Xuanhuang Realm's inexplicable transformation was only vaguely perceived by a few.

But how could they possibly find the mastermind behind Li Fan?

Of course, Li Fan did not forget to sow seeds in the Xuanhuang Realm before its sublimation.

For example, the ancient Immortal-Mortal miasma.

It was hidden in an underground cavity in Flag Ridge Prefecture.

In his previous life, Li Fan had already verified that this Immortal-Mortal miasma, as part of Xuanhuang's laws, would continuously strengthen as Xuanhuang Realm's power increased.

However, due to the hasty Returning to True, he had hardly seen the true Immortal-Mortal Miasma of the Immortal level. This life was meant to rectify that regret.

Besides the Immortal-Mortal Miasma, Li Fan also drew inferences and collected some other items in the Xuanhuang Realm that could cause great damage to cultivators, and even to Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao itself.

For example, the Sky-Shattering Arrow, created with a bizarre power.

It first appeared in the life when Xuanwu replaced the Heavenly Dao, capable of affecting and distorting the perception of the Heavenly Dao over a large area.

Another example was the Myriad Xuanhuang World Destruction Transformations.

In his previous life, Li Fan had already confirmed that the World Destruction Transformations were extremely effective against Mo Sha.

To hunt Mo Sha as much as possible this time, naturally, he had to be prepared.

Various powers of planetary transformation were mixed into the ball of light and secretly channeled into the Xuanhuang Realm by Li Fan, similar to how the Heavenly Physician had transplanted other ruined immortal cultivation realms.

Under normal circumstances, grafting and merging foreign objects like this would inevitably trigger rejection from Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao.

Natural disasters would descend, and through the evolution of destruction and rebirth, they would slowly fuse.

But the ingenious part was that the Xuanhuang World Destruction Transformations Li Fan infused originated from Xuanhuang Realm itself.

Therefore, Xuanhuang Realm would not perceive this suddenly appearing "fat meat" on its body.

As if it were its own.

Chapter 1388: Refining the Mysterious Yellow World

The Xuanhuang Realm entered its fifteenth year since anchoring.

On this day, Li Fan, following his old routine, captured the Medicine King Cauldron that had returned from beyond the heavens.

As always, he subdued the Medicine King Sect members to serve him.

At the same time, he quietly brought Ruan Tianxiao back to the former site of the Medicine King Sect and had him swallow the "Stone Pill" again.

Just like in his previous life.

Ruan Tianxiao's appearance and temperament became ethereal and detached, like a celestial being descending from the heavens, after swallowing the elixir.

At the same time, he began to lecture on the [Alchemy King Scripture] to the surroundings.

The profound verses echoed endlessly.

Even though it was not the first time Li Fan had heard this peerless scripture, he still felt various profound insights emerging.

It was as if his alchemy path had unknowingly taken another step forward.

The lingering resonance echoed, and Li Fan, combining his new understanding of the Medicine King Scripture, fine-tuned his plan for Xuanhuang's sublimation.

"After nearly ten years of nurturing, with various hidden methods of nourishment, the Xuanhuang Realm has gradually recovered from its decline."

"The time is ripe; it is time to begin the first step of alchemy."

A faint light flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he looked past the Xuanhuang Realm's firmament, seeing the countless connected small worlds.

"Myriad realms, all returning to Xuanhuang."

"All laws converge into one, universal harmony!"

With a somewhat eerie tone, Li Fan's whisper determined the fate of those myriad small worlds.

At this moment, the simulated Heavenly Dao in these small worlds began to mobilize the power of their worlds.

They autonomously expanded their world forms, as if extending tentacles along the channels Li Fan had already laid out.

Touching and connecting to the Xuanhuang Realm.

First, a single star in the darkness, tinged with Xuanhuang's color.

Then, soon, hundreds, thousands of golden stars lit up, surrounding the Xuanhuang Realm, shining brilliantly and magnificently!

"Shifting the Heavenly Principles and Earthly Laws..."

Li Fan, at this moment, split off a figure and floated towards the sky.

Simultaneously, he chanted.

The return of so many small worlds naturally required Xuanhuang Realm's cooperation.

Otherwise, it might be perceived as an attack by an unknown external enemy by Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao.
