"Although the power of a single small world is negligible compared to the Xuanhuang Realm, there are simply too many small worlds surrounding Xuanhuang Realm, and the quantitative change is enough to turn into a qualitative one."

"Injecting it directly into the Xuanhuang Realm like a rolling torrent might cause backlash."

"The same approach is needed, requiring a [medicinal guide]."

As Li Fan's thoughts churned, strands of hazy figures of Heavenly Souls descended.

They paused for a moment at their location, then quickly flew towards various parts of the Xuanhuang Realm.

They were carrying out the "heavenly duty" of absorbing the returning small worlds.

Li Fan roughly divided their responsibilities, assigning them areas to be responsible for. With the carrying capacity of Heavenly Souls

Chapter 1389: Guest from the High Wall

Once, twice.

Li Fan scanned with his divine sense repeatedly, but couldn't find the reason for the immortal formation's misjudgment on the storyteller.

"Perhaps it's not his fault..."

Frowning, Li Fan carefully searched the nearby items.

Finally, his gaze fell upon the wooden clapper the storyteller used.

"This thing..."

It appeared unremarkable, just a piece of black wood.

But when Li Fan held it, the moment he made contact, his soul felt a hint of coolness.

"Huh?"

Since comprehending the "Infinite Void Method," Li Fan's soul had always been in a "perfected" state, operating within its limits. Even if there was any damage, it could be instantly healed through the circulation of five-elemental power and primordial chaos.

His soul had reached a certain level of strength; only by breaking through his major realm could it grow. In fact, since advancing to the Soul Transformation stage, Li Fan's soul strength had not increased for a long time.

But now, as this coolness integrated, Li Fan felt his soul gradually consolidating, its bottleneck loosening!

"Hiss... What kind of treasure is this awakening wood?" Li Fan was surprised and delighted, but more so, he was vigilant.

One must know that Li Fan's current soul strength was already comparable to the Profound Yellow Longevity stage.

After reaching the limit, any further progress was not something that could be achieved through effort alone.

"The Immortal Boat's secret treasury holds countless treasures. None of them were useful to me, yet the Profound Yellow Realm actually hides one..."

Li Fan cautiously set up an immortal formation to isolate this black awakening wood.

Then, he searched the storyteller's mind for the origin of the awakening wood.

It wasn't some coveted heirloom. It was made by him, chopped from a tree in his courtyard and processed.

Li Fan took the storyteller, named Ge Daoquan, to his home.

In the courtyard, the verdant green tree still stood tall.

As soon as he entered the yard, Li Fan felt something different.

It was like walking in the scorching sun on a hot summer day, and suddenly entering a cool shade.

There were only two words for it:

Comfort!

If it were an ordinary cultivator, the contrast between the outside and inside would likely make them groan.

Li Fan took a deep breath, his vigilance not diminishing, and gradually approached the tree.

The leaves suddenly rustled without wind, making soft sounds.

Li Fan had encountered many peculiar trees in his countless reincarnations.

In the Profound Yellow Realm, there were the Myriad Spirits, the Heavenly Splendor, the Earth Veins—these three ancient Profound Yellow trees, and the Source of All Life, the Ruo Wood.

In the Immortal Boat, there was a divine tree from the Ancient Divine Wood Sect.

But all of these were different from the one before him.

Whether it was the Three Ancient Trees or the Ruo Wood.

They all had their own consciousness, giving Li Fan a sense of cunning and strangeness, like spirits of plants that had gained sentience.

But this one in the courtyard...

It was purely a tree.

Pure, yet extraordinary.

The crisp rustling of the leaves colliding eased Li Fan's always-tense heart.

Li Fan didn't know the name of this tree.

He no longer had the desire to get to the bottom of it. He simply sat cross-legged under the tree, meditating like he was on the verge of enlightenment.

Another gentle breeze passed, and dozens of emerald green leaves drifted down from the tree.

Like flowing light, they flew into Li Fan's body.

Li Fan's eyes slowly closed.

When he opened them again, ten days had passed.

The struggles and desperation in his hundreds of lifetimes of reincarnation, the constant worry of being ambushed by monsters of unparalleled cultivation appearing out of nowhere, the near-death experiences...

All the accumulated fatigue in his heart was eliminated.

It was as if he had slept soundly.

Body and mind were refreshed.

Li Fan stood up again, feeling unprecedentedly refreshed.

He gazed at the tree in the courtyard.

All its splendor had faded; in his eyes, it was no longer special.

It was just like any other ordinary tree.

Li Fan recalled the scenes that had flashed through his mind during his ten days of deep sleep.

Memories originating from the tree itself.

A streak of light cut through the sky, falling near the tree.

It seemed to have lost its life force, lying there motionless like an inanimate object. It looked like a scorched, blood-stained sphere, half-burned.

As time slowly passed, the decaying outer layer of the sphere gradually peeled off.

A baby crawled out from within.

The baby did not cry incessantly upon birth, but merely looked around, then chose a direction and began to crawl with unwavering determination.

Soon, it disappeared from the tree's sight.

As for the outer layer of the sphere, it slowly dissolved under the sun, rain, wind, and frost, turning into nutrients absorbed by the tree...

...

In the sky, there were terrifying tremors and flashes of fire, as if a brutal war was underway.

A figure quietly approached the tree.

"How could it be just a tree?"

"Did the lock-on go wrong?"

"This godforsaken place..."

In the man's hand stood a robot, made of metal, with a single eye. The eye emitted a golden light, pointing towards the tree ahead.

The man's expression was one of confusion and anxiety. He fiddled with the robot again, but its gaze remained fixed on the tree.

The man cursed angrily and threw the mechanical doll to the ground.

In the sky, it seemed some cultivators had noticed the man below.

The man's expression shifted slightly, and he fled as a golden light.

Another unknown number of days passed. The mechanical doll had already been buried deep underground.

As the sun rose and set, the traces of the earth-shattering battle were gradually smoothed over by time.

Occasionally, mortals passing by would feel an inexplicable sense of peace.

So, people began to choose to settle down, and a mortal town gradually emerged.

For ten generations, people lived near this tree. Their moods were unusually good. Although they lived ordinary lives, they were content and happy. Even when encountering difficulties, they would just smile and move on.

Until the eleventh generation, his descendant chose to become a storyteller to make a living. He happened to be short of a good awakening wood, so he chopped a piece from the tree in his home.

...

With thoughts churning, the first thing Li Fan did was to start digging around the tree.

Knowing that divine sense searches were ineffective, Li Fan had to do it himself.

Not long after, he indeed found the mechanical doll that the man had carelessly discarded hundreds of years ago.

Buried for years, it was still like new when retrieved.

Untouched by the passage of time.

However, the third eye of the mechanical doll was inexplicably closed.

No matter how he activated it, there was no reaction at all.

Li Fan played with this mechanical artifact, feeling a familiar aura.

"Falling Mortal..."

Li Fan's heart became solemn.

After pondering for a moment, Li Fan made a decision.

He took out the white circle, [Falling Mortal], and shone it towards the mechanical doll.

Falling Mortal was the physical manifestation of the Great Dao Law, [Innate].

For the past ten years, Li Fan had been holding the white circle, recalling the inscriptions on the Nameless Monument from his previous life.

He wanted to comprehend this Great Dao.

But he was somewhat disappointed. No matter how he pondered, he couldn't form his own understanding, unlike other True Immortal Character Scripts.

It was as if...

The principle of [Innate] in the world had already converged into one place, and no one else could meddle with it.

Li Fan didn't force it. Anyway, [Returning to True] had already bound the White Circle Falling Mortal, and at present, being able to summon and comprehend it anytime and anywhere, the difference wasn't too significant.

At this moment, the white circle's light locked onto the mechanical doll.

Under the white light's illumination, the doll, which should have been decomposed into nothingness, was miraculously unharmed!

It wasn't that its status was still above Falling Mortal, making it immune to its decomposition effect.

But the light released by the white circle, upon sensing the mechanical doll, suddenly turned green.

Because of this, the mechanical doll was spared from decomposition.

Under the illumination of the white circle, the mechanical doll, originally in slumber, came back to life.

It flew, standing on Li Fan's palm, and opened its third eye.

It seemed to be searching for something, constantly turning.

But for some reason, the doll's rotation speed increased faster and faster.

It turned into a spinning top, as if out of control.

"Is it broken?"

Li Fan frowned slightly.

He didn't stop it for now, letting the doll continue to spin.

Li Fan first looked at the green tree in the courtyard.

"A hundred years ago, the doll pointed to this tree because it absorbed the outer layer of the sphere, which included the infant."

"That layer of substance should have had a mind-awakening and enlightening effect."

"But with the passage of time, especially after I absorbed it, and now, the effect has become very weak, which is why the doll started pointing elsewhere."

"Even though its effect has weakened considerably, it still had such a miraculous effect on me. It's hard to imagine what it was like at the beginning."

Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he continued to ponder: "The White Circle Falling Mortal can sense the mechanical doll, proving they originated from the same source..."

"This means my guess from my previous life was correct. That person suppressed in the deepest part of the Nether Prison also came from beyond the High Wall."

Li Fan's expression immediately became serious.

Yes, the figure of the man that appeared in the tree's memory was precisely the skeleton Li Fan had seen in the deepest part of the Nether Prison in his previous life.

The cultivator who called himself Qin Zhuang!

"I soul-searched him, but I didn't get this recent memory."

"Clearly, he used secret methods to conceal and fabricate his experiences. What skillful means!"

Li Fan secretly praised him. He wasn't angry at being tricked, but rather felt a sliver of excitement.

"He thought he acted flawlessly, but didn't realize that everything leaves a trace."

"Under normal circumstances, these traces are hard to find. But under the Profound Yellow Myriad Beings Illusory Formation, they finally revealed themselves!"

Li Fan recalled the infant crawling out of the sphere in the tree's memory.

"Qin Zhuang... I'll call him that for now."

"He came inside the High Wall, seemingly to search for that infant's whereabouts."

"So, is this infant also from beyond the High Wall?"

"Qin Zhuang is related to the Heavenly Sword Sect, could this infant also be a descendant of the Heavenly Sword Sect?"

In an instant, countless questions flooded Li Fan's mind.

This lifetime, the Immortal Alliance's Nether Prison had already been enveloped by the Profound Yellow Myriad Beings Illusory Formation. Qin Zhuang would inevitably fall into the illusory formation.

But judging from the results of his previous life's probing, Qin Zhuang would not reveal any flaws.

"Failed twice in a row..."

"It seems that the means to counter the illusory formation from beyond the High Wall are already very widespread."

Li Fan pondered for a moment, and did not rush to capture and interrogate Qin Zhuang.

"Since it can bypass the immortal formation, other physical punishments should also be useless."

"We need to use more specialized methods. Perhaps after I achieve Dao Integration, I will have new methods."

...

Recalling his thoughts, Li Fan looked again at the continuously spinning mechanical doll.

It still showed no signs of stopping.

Li Fan pondered and observed carefully.

"It seems to be rotating, but there are different intervals between each rotation."

"This appearance is like..."

"Having found many different targets simultaneously. And these targets are distributed throughout the Profound Yellow Realm?"

Li Fan drew an incredible conclusion.

"Wait, could it be..."

In an instant, a thought flashed through Li Fan's mind like lightning.

To verify his guess, Li Fan flew towards a certain direction with the mechanical doll in hand.

As he got closer, the frequency of the doll turning towards Li Fan's direction of travel indeed increased.

Finally, Li Fan arrived at his destination.

Looking at the previously stopped doll, Li Fan smiled meaningfully.

On the plaque of the wooden house, three large characters were written.

Thousand Miles Hall!

The mechanical doll's third eye stared directly at Jiao Xiuyuan, who was sleeping inside the hall.

Then, as if it had run out of energy again, it slowly closed.

"The infant from back then turned out to be him."

"Jiao Xiuyuan, from beyond the High Wall?"

"But unlike Qin Zhuang, he couldn't immune the illusory formation..."

Li Fan's thoughts churned.

Then, Li Fan closed his eyes, and holding the mechanical doll, entered the [Profound Yellow Myriad Beings] grand formation.

Within the illusory formation, Jiao Xiuyuan was still his normal self, constantly shouting and conducting business.

The moment Li Fan appeared before him, Jiao Xiuyuan seemed to sense something. His shouting stopped, and his gaze fell upon the mechanical doll in Li Fan's hand.

Li Fan pretended to turn and leave.

"Fellow Daoist, please stay!" Jiao Xiuyuan repeatedly called out, blocking Li Fan.

"Since you've come, why not come in? Come and sit." Jiao Xiuyuan said with a smile, his dark face revealing a hint of憨厚.

With the absolute professionalism of a merchant, he didn't glance at the doll in Li Fan's hand again.

Li Fan put away the doll and sighed, "It's an ancestral item. I originally wanted to sell it. But after repeated consideration, I thought better of it."

"Farewell!" Li Fan cupped his hands and was about to leave again.

"Don't rush off, Daoist friend. I find your face familiar. If you have any difficulties, just say the word. If it's within my ability, I will definitely help you." Jiao Xiuyuan patted his chest vigorously, acting as if he were righteous and honorable.

Li Fan hesitated for a moment, then finally sat down.

Jiao Xiuyuan quietly closed the Thousand Miles Hall and shut the doors.

He focused his attention solely on Li Fan.

"To be honest, Daoist friend, ever since I was born, I've been having the same recurring dream."

Li Fan pondered for a moment and then spoke, immediately capturing Jiao Xiuyuan's attention.

"In my dream, I saw a ray of light descending from the sky. An infant crawled out of a sphere..."

Li Fan spoke, carefully observing Jiao Xiuyuan's reaction.

Jiao Xiuyuan listened with great interest, but unlike Li Fan's expectations, he showed no abnormality.

"I suspect this dream might be related to the doll passed down in my family," Li Fan said again.

Chapter 1390: The Way of Life and Death in Dust Abyss

"Fellow Daoist," Li Fan said with a grim expression, gritting his teeth, "do you know what a terrifying experience it is to have the same dream your entire life?"

"It's all this peculiar little person's fault! I want to completely escape these nightmares, so I came to your Thousand Miles Hall."

"But after all, it's an ancestral item. The ancestral instruction is to keep this item well... " Li Fan showed a conflicted expression.

Jiao Xiuyuan frowned and agreed, "Ancestral instructions are important, but one's own life is more important."

"This thing is indeed eerily powerful and an ominous object. But rest assured, fellow Daoist, my Thousand Miles Hall has always been fair; I won't offer a lower price because of this."

Li Fan hesitated for a moment, then slowly said, "I can sell it, but it would be best if I could figure out what secrets lie behind this little person. Otherwise, it will be difficult to explain to my family."

"May I take a close look?" Jiao Xiuyuan asked tentatively.

Li Fan was somewhat hesitant but finally handed over the mechanical puppet.

The previous search had exhausted the puppet's energy, so even when it fell into Jiao Xiuyuan's hands, it showed no reaction.

Jiao Xiuyuan examined it up and down, frowning from time to time.

"Can you tell anything?" Li Fan asked.

"Looking at the puppet's appearance, it seems to be from the ancient immortal cultivation realm of [Dust Abyss]. It is said that the cultivators of this realm all have true immortal bloodlines, are born with three eyes, and possess many innate divine abilities..."

"But strangely, I've never seen the material of this puppet," Jiao Xiuyuan said with a peculiar expression.

"Dust Abyss Realm?" Li Fan feigned complete unfamiliarity.

"An ancient secret, moreover, this realm has long since been destroyed. It is normal that you don't know, fellow Daoist," Jiao Xiuyuan waved his hand, showing no intention of elaborating, his attention still focused on the mechanical puppet.

At this moment, Li Fan secretly manipulated the illusory formation.

The mechanical puppet seemed to suddenly open its third eye, emitting a beam of light that shot straight towards Jiao Xiuyuan.

Both Li Fan and Jiao Xiuyuan exclaimed in unison.

By the time they reacted, the golden light had already disappeared, as if it were an illusion.

"Fellow... Fellow Daoist, are you alright? Was that golden light not an illusion?" Li Fan asked with feigned shock and uncertainty.

Jiao Xiuyuan nodded with a solemn expression, "I saw it too. Did it come towards me...?"

Jiao Xiuyuan's words seemed to serve as a reminder.

Li Fan suddenly remembered something and said, "That's right! Before, whenever I had the thought of selling this mechanical puppet, I always felt uneasy and couldn't make up my mind. Only when I came near your Thousand Miles Hall did my resolve finally strengthen."

Li Fan's expression turned somewhat horrified, "Could it be that you, fellow Daoist, have some inexplicable connection with this mechanical puppet?"

Jiao Xiuyuan did not answer this time, instead meticulously examining the three-eyed puppet.

Uncertain about what he discovered, his expression became increasingly serious.

"This thing... might be alive."

After a long silence, Jiao Xiuyuan suddenly spoke, a bombshell.

"Ah?" Li Fan seemed startled, staring at the puppet in disbelief.

"It seems that it was sealed and crafted from a living cultivator of the Dust Abyss Realm using some incredibly extraordinary method."

"Although transformed into an object, it still retains all the magical powers and abilities of a powerful cultivator with true immortal bloodlines!" Jiao Xiuyuan judged.

"This... This is impossible, right? To transform a person into an object, even the Revered Heavenly Preacher himself might not be able to achieve such a feat. Moreover, didn't you say that the Dust Abyss Realm has already been destroyed?" Li Fan asked with disbelief.

"Beyond Profound Yellow?" Jiao Xiuyuan muttered first.

Then, as if to verify his claim, he took out a green bottle from somewhere.

With great reluctance, he poured out a drop of thick green liquid and fed it to the mechanical puppet.

"This bottle contains pure life essence. If it were a dead object, it definitely wouldn't react to it."

"But if it still possesses the attribute of [life], it will instinctively absorb it."

As if to confirm Jiao Xiuyuan's words, the moment the green liquid approached, the mechanical puppet's normal two eyes suddenly opened, quickly absorbing the liquid.

Li Fan still didn't sense any aura of a living being from it, but he watched as the puppet, little by little, came to life.

The puppet's target was indeed Jiao Xiuyuan.

The third eye shot out a golden light, like a chain, tightly binding Jiao Xiuyuan.

"Fellow Daoist, are you alright!" Li Fan asked with great tension, but without any intention of intervening, merely observing from a distance.

Bound by the golden chain, Jiao Xiuyuan couldn't move, and his expression seemed frozen, showing no response.

"Don't worry, it's just a small trick; how could it possibly harm me!" It was still Jiao Xiuyuan speaking, but his voice came from another corner.

Li Fan followed the direction of the voice and saw that a withered yellow branch had grown from the ground in the corner, seemingly appearing out of nowhere.

The branch continuously extended and transformed.

Soon, another Jiao Xiuyuan emerged from it!

"You... Are you a person or a ghost!" Li Fan shivered in fear, his face showing terror.

"Hehehe, it's just a minor splitting technique," Jiao Xiuyuan soothed.

After saying only this, the Dust Abyss Realm mechanical puppet shot another beam of golden light from its third eye.

It locked onto Jiao Xiuyuan.

Still without any ability to resist, Jiao Xiuyuan was captured again.

"Fellow Daoist!" Li Fan trembled, his legs shaking, on the verge of fleeing.

"Don't panic!" Another voice suddenly appeared.

A third Jiao Xiuyuan appeared within the Thousand Miles Hall.

His fate was the same, bound again by golden chains.

"Let's see how many times you can shoot!"

Filled with anger, ten voices appeared simultaneously.

Branches sprouted everywhere within the Thousand Miles Hall. Ten identical Jiao Xiuyuans appeared one after another.

Faced with such a bizarre scene, the three-eyed puppet was momentarily dazed.

After a moment, it shot out golden chains to attack, but only managed to emit three before it seemed to be its limit.

As if drained, it returned to its dormant state.

"You want to capture me, Old Jiao? You're still too green!" Jiao Xiuyuan snorted triumphantly.

Seven voices spoke one after another.

Afterward, six of them transformed back into withered branches, withered and retracted into the ground.

Only one remained, staring at the six bound Jiao Yuans in the field.

He slowly approached and touched the golden chain.

"This thing..."

As if it were an illusion, Jiao Xiuyuan's hand passed directly through it.

Li Fan, also out of curiosity, tried to do the same.

He, too, could not touch it.

"It seems to be an innate divine ability of the Dust Abyss Realm cultivators."

"Truly remarkable," Jiao Xiuyuan exclaimed after trying for a long time without being able to touch its physical form.

"Fellow Daoist Jiao... It seems that the mechanical puppet's target is truly you?"

"Could it be that the infant from our ancestors' dreams is you? Did the mechanical puppet come to our world to hunt down Fellow Daoist Jiao?" Li Fan's expression became increasingly horrified, his tone more alarmed.

"But that doesn't make sense either. Fellow Daoist, you don't look that old. The timeline doesn't match. Could it be the infant's descendant?" Li Fan scrutinized Jiao Xiuyuan, his eyes filled with doubt.

"I should be that infant myself," Jiao Xiuyuan said frankly.

"Ah?" Li Fan's eyes widened in astonishment.

"Old Jiao here has lived much longer than ordinary people. It's just that for most of the time, I was unconscious and acted purely on instinct," Jiao Xiuyuan said indifferently.

"In fact, I have some vague memories of my childhood experiences, which were sealed deep in my mind and almost forgotten. After this incident, I've remembered some of them." Jiao Xiuyuan's tone became somewhat dreamy.

"Fellow Daoist Jiao, are you truly an extraterrestrial cultivator?" Li Fan stared intently at Jiao Xiuyuan, as if trying to see through him, his expression filled with curiosity and excitement.

"I should... be," Jiao Xiuyuan hesitated for a moment, then finally nodded.

"I have no memory of what happened before I crawled out of that sphere. But since the puppet tracking me comes from outside Profound Yellow, it's likely my homeland is also like that."

"No wonder I instinctively wanted to cultivate techniques that allow for body transformation into myriad forms, all to evade pursuit?" Jiao Xiuyuan spoke enigmatically.

Li Fan marveled, full of disbelief, "It's truly hard to imagine how you, fellow Daoist, managed to survive all alone from infancy to the present and even establish the Thousand Miles Hall business."

Jiao Xiuyuan waved his hand, "It's not that difficult, actually. In fact, since I can remember, as long as I acted according to my desires, I've rarely encountered any major difficulties. All obstacles would naturally be resolved. Of course, except for doing business."

"Making money is truly difficult!" Jiao Xiuyuan suddenly sighed, somewhat out of place.

"I intended to resolve my own calamity, but I didn't expect to implicate you, fellow Daoist Jiao. If it weren't for me, this puppet wouldn't have lost its motive and come knocking on your door." Li Fan showed remorse.

Jiao Xiuyuan, however, took it lightly, "What is destined cannot be avoided. Moreover, for me, this might be a blessing in disguise."

Li Fan expressed some surprise, "How so?"

"Living in the Profound Yellow Realm for too long, being influenced by my surroundings, I inevitably followed the path of defying heavenly principles."

"It has been a great help, and if not for the Heavenly Venerate's new methods, I might have lost my life when I was young."

"But some of my homeland's techniques have also been sealed because of it, making it hard to recall them."

"If not for today's incident..."

Jiao Xiuyuan's expression became somewhat dazed.

As if recalling some important information deep in his mind, he occasionally frowned.

His eyes became brighter and brighter.

Li Fan faintly sensed a profound and unusual aura emanating from Jiao Xiuyuan, fluctuating unstably.

Jiao Xiuyuan seemed to have discovered something and looked around.

There was a hint of astonishment in his eyes.

"Stop!"

Just as he was about to break through the illusory formation, Li Fan spoke indifferently.

The scene before Jiao Xiuyuan's eyes shattered violently.

"Fellow Daoist Jiao, Fellow Daoist Jiao!"

"Why are you stunned! Are you selling this promised minor Medicine King Cauldron or not!"

An impatient urging voice echoed in his ears.

Jiao Xiuyuan was slightly stunned, and a torrent of information instantly flooded his mind.

It turned out that he had painstakingly dug up some high-quality minor Medicine King Cauldrons from the ruins of the former Medicine King Sect. Not only could they be used as storage artifacts, but they also contained spiritual energy spaces capable of cultivating various spirit herbs and plants, making them incredibly valuable.

"Sell, of course I'll sell..." Jiao Xiuyuan instinctively replied.

Just then, he suddenly remembered that he had learned from a cultivator who was skilled in deduction that a meteor would soon fall back to Profound Yellow.

The essence of that meteor was very likely the true Medicine King Cauldron that had carried the entire Medicine King Sect away back then.

At that time, the remaining minor Medicine King Cauldrons would become the key to entering the true Cauldron. The true Medicine King Cauldron contained the essence of what the Medicine King Sect had taken away.

As keys, the value of the minor Medicine King Cauldrons would inevitably skyrocket!

"I won't sell!" Upon realizing the immense future profits, Jiao Xiuyuan's heart skipped a beat, and he immediately changed his mind.

"Fellow Daoist Jiao, why are you going back on your word?" The opposing cultivator became anxious.

Jiao Xiuyuan, however, directly collected all the minor Medicine King Cauldrons and closed the door, refusing all guests.

He was calculating how to inflate the price of the minor Medicine King Cauldrons as much as possible.

"Hmm?"

Jiao Xiuyuan vaguely felt that he had forgotten something extremely important.

But in the face of immense commercial profits, he decided to put it aside for now.

...

Outside the illusory formation, in the real Profound Yellow Realm.

Li Fan looked at the golden chains before him, his expression somber.

Everything that had just happened, although within the illusory formation,

was real in its manifestation on the three-eyed puppet. It had truly received a large amount of life force and briefly come alive. However, the life force did not come from the green bottle Jiao Xiuyuan had taken out but was derived from the immortal formation's power.

The stimulation was real, and the golden chains emitted from the three-eyed puppet's third eye were also real. They were now solidified in the air, seemingly similar to the golden threads cast by the Heavenly Physician.

However, they were fundamentally different.

The Heavenly Physician's golden threads were the "power to drive and alter laws" cultivated by the Heavenly Physician's comprehension and understanding of the laws of heaven and earth.

But this golden light from the puppet's third eye...

"Is a law itself."

"It seems to indeed originate from the abilities of the Dust Abyss Realm cultivators."

Li Fan was not very interested in this mysterious three-eyed race. Even if they were once powerful, they had now been reduced to mere puppets.

Li Fan was more interested in the heaven-defying method of transforming life into objects and the forces behind it.

"Mao Bao, Falling Mortal, and this three-eyed puppet."

"Beyond the Wall, the transformation of life into objects, and laws into objects..."

"It truly is the ultimate utilization of external things," Li Fan's heart felt heavy, yet he was full of awe for this unknown civilization beyond the Wall.

"Compared to the white circle, the method of forging this puppet is relatively crude, perhaps a breakthrough point."

Chapter 1391: Stone Tablet Displays Immortal Characters

"Crude" was a descriptor relative to the flawless and seamless white circle, [Falling Mortal]. In truth, the method of refining life into an object employed by the three-eyed figurine had completely surpassed Li Fan's understanding. Even with the physical object before him, Li Fan was at a loss on how to begin researching it. Among all the theories he had encountered, only the [Alchemy King Scripture], personally passed down by Sun Piaomiao, bore even a slight resemblance. But not much.

"Transforming life into an object, yet retaining the inherent attributes of life."

"And possessing the attributes of an 'object'."

"..."

Li Fan conducted a series of experiments on the acquired three-eyed figurine. First and foremost, he confirmed that the figurine's self-awareness had been erased; it could only act according to predetermined rules. He then tested the figurine's resistance to damage. After the three-eyed figurine failed, it was casually discarded by Qin Zhuang, indicating that outside the high wall, it was not considered a particularly valuable item. Yet, for such a small object, Li Fan had to employ his ultimate skill, the [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger], to inflict significant damage.

"If they were merely cultivators from the Dust Abyss Realm, even with their rumored True Immortal bloodline, they could not achieve such a feat. By adding the attribute of being an 'object,' and perfectly fusing the two without any flaws, their defensive capabilities have been greatly enhanced..."

Beings from outside the high wall seemed to have an extraordinary resistance to illusion formations. Li Fan used the three-eyed figurine to test nearly all the immortal formations he possessed. He found that the figurine, even in its unconscious state, could consistently evade the fatal blows of the immortal formations, moving within them with ease.

"Besides 'life' and 'object,' there seems to be a third superimposed attribute."

Li Fan observed while adjusting the immortal formations in response to the three-eyed figurine's evasive maneuvers. He then used new formations, optimized by the Ultimate Dissolution Disc, for further testing. The result remained unchanged; the figurine effortlessly dodged them. Li Fan did not become agitated. He continued with a new round of iterations. After improving the formations for the fiftieth time, the three-eyed figurine's flawless evasion finally showed a flaw, occasionally being caught by the circulating immortal formations.

A bright light flashed in Li Fan's eyes. "My immortal formations are like a large net woven together. Although seemingly invincible within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, capable of encompassing all beings when deployed, to these creations from outside the high wall, the gaps within the net are all perceived as weaknesses!" "However, as I patch these gaps one by one, and the net becomes denser and its holes smaller..." "It will become much harder for it to resist formations solely by instinct!" "In simple terms, my mastery of formations hasn't improved qualitatively, but it has become increasingly impenetrable!"

Li Fan intently watched the dust abyss race figurine within the immortal formation, his thoughts churning. He applied all the detailed modifications from the upgraded formations to all his major formations. It was as if a hastily sketched outline had become an increasingly refined portrait with the addition of continuous details. "Such refinement of formation details cannot be achieved by one person or in a short period. It requires the collective wisdom passed down through generations, like the disciples of the Immortal Boat, diligently researching without end!"

Li Fan seemed to glimpse scenes of countless figures, tirelessly working day and night, delving into the study of formations. "My completion can be so rapid only because I can directly utilize existing resources. In fact, without the help of the Dissolution Disc, I wouldn't be able to iterate formations so quickly!"

"The three-eyed figurine was brought by Qin Zhuang from outside the wall five hundred years ago."

"As for the white circle and Mao Bao, they are creations from the recent period."

"Five hundred years have passed with no progress, has the technology outside the high wall advanced so much?"

Li Fan's thoughts stirred, and he took out [Falling Mortal] and threw it towards the evolving formation. He wanted to compare its reaction to that of the three-eyed figurine when facing the shifting formations. However, as Li Fan had expected, [Falling Mortal] proved immune to all applied formation techniques. His observation plan failed before it even began.

"I didn't even get to see it exhibit evasive maneuvers like the three-eyed figurine within the formations."

"It's as if they operate on completely different planes of existence..."

Li Fan's gaze flickered, deep in thought: "It seems that over the past five hundred years, the technology outside the high wall has seen a qualitative leap." Previously inspired by the uneven time flow within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, Li Fan speculated that the time flow outside the high wall might be much faster than inside. Tens of thousands of years had passed within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea since the Immortal Realm's Great Calamity. Outside the high wall, perhaps millions of years had elapsed. "The difference between the creations from outside the high wall, such as the three-eyed figurine and others that arrived later, seems to support my theory from another perspective." "Of course, it's also possible that Mao Bao and [Falling Mortal] are extremely rare existences outside the high wall. It's simply a matter of disparity in general value..."

However, since both Mao Bao and the white circle were reeled in from the fishing pond, Li Fan instinctively believed that such 'bait' wouldn't be particularly rare.

"With the three-eyed figurine helping me calibrate and reduce the flaws in my immortal formations, perhaps in this lifetime, I will have the opportunity to perfect the formations."

"And extract useful intelligence from Qin Zhuang's mind."

The experiment was on the right track, with little chance of further deviation. The subsequent process was purely mechanical repetition. Li Fan created a simulated persona and began refining complex formations. Afterwards, he started researching the golden beams that the three-eyed figurine shot out to capture Jiao Xiuyuan. It had been confirmed earlier that these golden beams were innate divine abilities of the Chen Yuan Realm cultivators, representing laws themselves. And what could be better for deciphering laws than the leg bone of the Nameless True Immortal?

Carrying the golden beams, Li Fan teleported to the small world of the You clan. Protected by Li Fan's illusory statue, the You clan, who were on the verge of extinction, had reclaimed most of their territory. However, periodically, the terrifying stone stele in the center of the world would unleash boundless calamity, claiming the lives of nearly half the You clan. The presence of the stone stele and the illusory statue kept the You clan in a perpetual state of fear and devout prayer.

Arriving before the leg bone of the Nameless True Immortal, Li Fan first checked the progress of the True Immortal Script manifestation on the stele. Perhaps due to a qualitative change from amassed quantity, the nameless stele, which had absorbed a large amount of You clan flesh and blood, was manifesting characters at a much faster rate than Li Fan had anticipated. The mysterious characters, currently less than one-fifth manifested, already emanated a unique power. Unlike [Hunger] and [Innate], this True Immortal Script of [Immortal-Mortal Transformation], as it manifested on the stele, could partially penetrate the stele's restraint and project its power outwards. It was precisely this faint influence that, even without Li Fan's direct intervention, was slowly advancing the You clan's ancestral reversion process. This occurred silently, unnoticed even by the simulated persona constantly overseeing the operations. Only Li Fan, upon his personal arrival, keenly perceived this subtle change.

Li Fan frowned slightly and decisively set up numerous immortal formations around the stone stele to isolate the True Immortal Script's influence on the outside world. "This doesn't mean that the rank of this [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] Script is higher than the Nameless True Immortal's." "Rather, this particular Script possesses a certain special quality. The Great Dao it relates to even influenced the Nameless True Immortal during his lifetime." "And this stele is not the complete Southern Immortal Pillar, merely a shattered leg bone." "Such anomalies are not unexpected." "True immortals are indeed full of hidden perils. One cannot be too careful!" Li Fan inwardly warned himself. He then proceeded with his primary task. He projected a beam of stationary golden light towards the stele. Upon contact, the stele immediately absorbed it. A new True Immortal Script imprint began appearing at the corner of the stele. However, Li Fan found it somewhat strange. Both [Hunger] and [Innate], as well as the nascent [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] Script, had appeared in the central area of the stele. Yet, this new Script, instead of occupying the vast central space, had squeezed itself into the corner. Li Fan tried to recall which True Immortal Scripts had appeared in the corresponding area of the nameless monument in his previous life. It was unfortunate that his memory was a fleeting glimpse, leaving no lasting impression. Thus, after much deliberation, he found no clues.

He decided not to dwell on it and continued to input the golden light. As expected of a pure manifestation of law, it was far more efficient than inputting material objects and then deciphering them. With one more beam of golden light yet to be absorbed, the True Immortal Script on the stele was fully manifested.

"This is..."

"Detain?"

Like all True Immortal Scripts, the moment Li Fan saw it, its true meaning flooded his mind. This Script was not particularly complex. Yet, in Li Fan's eyes, it held a different kind of significance. Having encountered numerous True Immortal Scripts, Li Fan had previously made a simple classification based on their function. Most True Immortal Scripts were annotations of the Great Dao laws of heaven and earth. However, a select few were derivatives of Immortal Realm edicts! Such as the [Return] Script, which had caused the inexplicable disappearance of the Nine Star Red Pearl, the core of the ancient immortal formation, not long ago. The [Detain] Script that had now appeared before Li Fan belonged to this latter category.

"The Dust Abyss Realm cultivators, possessing True Immortal bloodlines. This perhaps is not mere hearsay."

"True Immortals descending to the mortal realm comes at a great cost. The Immortal Realm must also find representatives in the lower realm to execute their will. It is likely that the Dust Abyss Realm cultivators served as the Immortal Realm's pawns in the lower realms..." Li Fan suddenly recalled that the Dust Abyss Realm was rumored to be among the first cultivation realms affected by the Great Calamity of the Immortal Realm, and should have long been annihilated. Yet, years later, survivors were still seemingly being refined into objects by powers outside the high wall.

"There are several possibilities."

"First, the entire lower realm is not just the Dust Abyss Realm. The Utmost Darkness Star Sea might be just one of them."

"Second, some Dust Abyss Realm cultivators survived and escaped the Utmost Darkness Star Sea before the high wall was established. They then prospered outside the high wall. However, looking at the current situation, their circumstances might not be favorable."

Li Fan collected his thoughts and began experimenting with the newly acquired [Detain] Script. It bore a striking resemblance to the [Insect Binding] divine ability he had acquired long ago, perhaps even a superior replacement. [Insect Binding] required the caster's strength to be greater than the target's. However, with the [Detain] Script, as long as the target could not immune itself to True Immortal Scripts' power, it would be instantly apprehended. Body, soul, and consciousness would enter a state of frozen stillness, rendered completely vulnerable!

Li Fan summoned Qiu Shui and Tian Yang for experimentation. Both were at the Supreme stage. However, perhaps due to Tian Yang having absorbed the combat experiences of an immortal puppet and thus inheriting some of its characteristics, it fared extremely poorly under the [Detain] Script. It had to exert its full strength just to barely break free. Qiu Shui's response was much better, utilizing the boundless power of the Star Sea to minimize the [Detain] Script's influence.

"Immortal Realm edicts derived from True Immortal Scripts seem to originate from a different source than those transcribed from the Great Dao laws."

As Li Fan personally experienced the power of the [Detain] Script, a thought flashed through his mind. "Beyond its general potency, it also possesses a special suppressive effect on certain existences."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes. He had previously glimpsed the entirety of the Immortal Realm. Within the boundless sea, True Immortals were but a minority. Most regions of the Immortal Realm were populated by creations of True Immortals, such as immortal puppets and servants. Magnificent and sacred palace imagery appeared simultaneously in each region. Seated within these palaces seemed to be supreme beings ruling their respective Immortal Domains. Even the True Immortal who descended to the mortal realm dared not look directly at them. His memory only retained a phantom image. The Star Sea surged, and all the regions disappeared below the horizon. The True Immortal arrived in the lower realm, Xuanhuang.

... Although it was just a fleeting glimpse, the vibrant and boundless scenery of the Immortal Realm he witnessed still stirred Li Fan's heart. "Legends say the Immortal Realm is a holy land with infinite resources. It seems the rumors are true." "That ocean is truly vast! Each region contains countless star domains!" "It's simply unbelievable!"

Li Fan's heart was greatly stirred, and his brows furrowed. The memory fragments from the True Immortal's descent completely surpassed his understanding. The True Immortal's memories continued. He was guarding Xuanhuang, seemingly waiting for something. The Star Sea ebbed and flowed, and an unknown amount of time passed. The True Immortal could not help but feel emotions amidst the passage of time.

"Five hundred years have passed since the calculated time."

"It hasn't appeared yet..."

The continuous shaking of the images was enough to show the True Immortal's inner turmoil at that time. "Let's wait a little longer."

In the Xuanhuang Realm, the sun rose and set, and an unknown amount of time passed. "It's been fifteen hundred years."

"It has completely exceeded the margin of error..."

"The worst has happened. That thing..."

"It probably won't come."

As this thought arose, the entire world instantly turned dim, as if it had lost its final lifeline. The True Immortal closed his eyes, and infinite despair surged in his heart. But inexplicably, after thinking of something, the despair in his consciousness gradually receded. "Great beings have great beings' intentions." "Ants have ants' ways of survival." "..." The True Immortal's gaze swept across the Xuanhuang Realm and the entire Star Sea at that time.

Boom! The image suddenly shattered.

... "Even as a True Immortal, one is still an ant?" "Then what kind of existence is the 'Great Being' he spoke of?" "Nameless True Immortal?" "Is the gap between achieving Namelessness and not so vast?"

Li Fan's heart trembled again. The True Immortal's own memories were naturally far more credible than baseless speculation. Because of this, Li Fan initially formed some understanding of the Immortal Realm. The speed of life expenditure while spying on this memory was two to three times faster than before. His hair began to show threads of white, but Li Fan still did not give up on further exploration. He had a premonition that the most important intelligence was about to emerge.

... The images flowed again, and the True Immortal was no longer looking down at the Xuanhuang Realm. Instead, he was sitting at a stone table by a pool of water, drinking tea with someone. That figure was indistinct. But from the True Immortal's attitude, the other party must be an extraordinary great being. What shocked Li Fan even more was that the pool of water by the stone table where the True Immortal was sitting was very familiar to him. It was the fishing pond!

From the figure opposite, a voice came out. The True Immortal nodded respectfully. However, in the memory, no imprints were left behind. After finishing a cup of tea, the figure opposite mysteriously disappeared. The stone table, stone chair, and even the cup of tea they had just drunk disappeared, just like the figure. It was as if it had been a dream from the beginning, and nothing had happened. But Li Fan could feel the True Immortal's excitement in his memory. He looked at the calm pool of water not far away. With a flick of his finger, he threw a ball of light into it. The ball of light entered the water without causing any ripples, and was swallowed and disappeared in the blink of an eye. The True Immortal closed his eyes and sensed something. After a long time, He slowly walked to the edge of the pool. He looked down at his reflection in the water.

Boom! A face appeared in Li Fan's mind. The mass of True Immortal flesh and blood suppressed by the Nameless True Immortal leg bone suddenly became violent! Li Fan's hair instantly turned completely white. He suddenly withdrew from the memory spying.

"It's just bodily aging, and I still have over three hundred years of lifespan. It's no big deal."

"The agitation of the True Immortal flesh and blood also subsided quickly. It should just be a momentary resonance caused by the True Immortal's face appearing in the memory." Li Fan quickly made a judgment. The mass of flesh and blood was still honestly suppressed by the Nameless True Immortal leg bone. Li Fan, still trying to recover from the scene he had just witnessed, appeared somewhat dazed. In the reflection of the fishing pond, he saw the True Immortal's face. However, what made him confused and terrified was that the face was exactly the same as his own!

Chapter 1392: Xuanhuang Serves the Heart

Li Fan suppressed the thought for a moment, though it lingered: "There will be a day for that, but not now. This lifetime, the goal of merging with the Dao through the Profound Yellow Realm's Celestial Soul will override all else."

"Besides the Star Sea's Starving Immortal, I can also experiment with that watcher and even the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate. Theoretically, as they hold Immortal Realm posts, the restrictions on them should be deeper."

Li Fan was very satisfied with his gains this time. Not only had he greatly compensated for the deficiencies in his immortal formations, but he had also mastered a True Immortal Character Script representing an Immortal Realm decree. All of this was merely a glimpse into the secrets beyond the wall. He could hardly imagine what the world outside the wall had become by now.

"As for Jiao Xiuyuan's identity..." Li Fan had truly not expected that Jiao Xiuyuan was likely an orphan from beyond the wall. "When Jiao Xiuyuan was first brought into the wall, he must have been recently born. In such a situation, to be separated from his hometown and family..." "A major upheaval must have occurred. The faction represented by Qin Zhuang also tracked down clues and followed years later."

Li Fan's expression was unreadable. "Why would they entrust the life of a young bloodline to be sent into the wall and the Profound Yellow Realm?" "To them, was the Profound Yellow Realm a sanctuary to escape conflict? Or is there some treasure hidden in this land that even those beyond the wall covet?" "And more importantly, beyond the high wall, it seems they can observe the situation within the wall to some extent. At the very least, they could ascertain that the Profound Yellow Realm had not been devoured and destroyed by the Star Sea. Otherwise, sending Jiao Xiuyuan would be no different from sending him to his death."

The substance within the sphere that encased the young Jiao Xiuyuan, if even a small drop were to fall, could cultivate a miraculous tree capable of evading the influence of immortal formations. It was conceivable that Jiao Xiuyuan himself, having absorbed most of that substance, would be even more extraordinary. This was why Li Fan did not immediately resort to soul-searching, but instead used immortal formation illusions to test him. "It's just that Jiao Xiuyuan has been in the Profound Yellow Realm for so many years, it's entirely justified to call him indigenous. That special ability seems to have been dormant..."

Li Fan's divine sense swept over Jiao Xiuyuan, who was still lost within the Profound Yellow All Beings Grand Formation. Li Fan temporarily abandoned the idea of helping him awaken his potential. The aura emanating from Jiao Xiuyuan when he was on the verge of awakening had made Li Fan feel uneasy. This uneasiness was not due to crushing power, but rather a primal premonition, like detecting a danger signal.

"Since Jiao Xiuyuan originally came from beyond the high wall, perhaps when I explore beyond the wall in the future, I can consider letting Jiao Xiuyuan take the lead." "His special identity will stir up sufficiently turbulent currents, allowing me to glimpse more secrets." "Of course, the final decision will still be made based on the information obtained from Qin Zhuang's mind."

"Celestial Sword Sect..." Thinking of this former top ten immortal sect that had escaped using a world-splitting divine weapon, Li Fan's heart suddenly stirred. "Could it be that Jiao Xiuyuan's bloodline origin is also from a faction that fled the Profound Yellow Realm in history?" "Even if not, it is definitely related to the Profound Yellow Realm." "When the timescale is stretched, those immortal sects that fled back then have likely developed to astonishing levels. I wonder if they still recognize these old relatives of the Profound Yellow Realm..."

Thoughts churned, lingering endlessly. The more information Li Fan knew about the outside of the wall, the more eager he became to go there. But first, he had to increase his self-preservation capabilities.

"Soon."

"After fifteen years of slow simmering, it's time to switch to rapid boiling!"

Li Fan's gaze fell upon the Profound Yellow Realm. When the vast majority of living beings in the Profound Yellow Realm fell into the ultimate illusion formation, the Profound Yellow Realm became empty. Without the influence of humans and cultivators, the Profound Yellow Realm's speed of rest and recovery was nearly a hundred or even a thousand times faster than usual. Especially in the illusion formation, cultivators were dying all the time. The deaths of cultivators returning their essence to heaven were akin to potent tonics, each one a supplement. Although weak individually, their sheer numbers and continuous supply made up for it. Moreover, what cultivators absorbed was a part of the world's power. The Profound Yellow Realm absorbed it without any hindrance.

The feedback from cultivators, the return of the myriad small worlds, the influx of vitality from the fissures and dark rivers, and the nourishment from the boundless power of the Star Sea. The Profound Yellow Realm became increasingly "solid" and "strong" at a visible rate. "The foundation has become sufficiently thick, far exceeding my preparations in my previous life. It is enough to withstand the drastic changes to come."

A faint light flashed in Li Fan's eyes. Dozens of figures suddenly flew out from the illusion formation. These were all the Dao Integration cultivators of the Profound Yellow Realm. Li Fan's plan was not significantly different from his previous life. When the colossal power to sublimate the entire Profound Yellow Realm was infused, some 'medicinal guides' were still needed to buffer it. And these Dao Integration cultivators were the perfect choice.

Glimmers of golden light flashed. Even Dao Integration cultivators were no match for Li Fan, offering no resistance. They fell into a deep sleep, dormant in the illusionary dream, manipulated by Li Fan like insects. "The Immortal Domain was not unfolded in this lifetime. The mere Immortal Spiritual Qi from the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate's legacy would definitely not be enough to support the qualitative transformation of the Profound Yellow Realm." "Fortunately, I can now communicate with the Star Sea and draw upon its boundless power, which is enough to support the long period of quantitative change before the critical point of transformation." "What I need to do is, at the crucial moment, unleash the Immortal Spiritual Qi and merge it into the Profound Yellow Realm, pushing it over the final threshold." "Then, use the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone to temporarily anchor the 'momentum' of the Profound Yellow Realm." "After the Profound Yellow Immortal Domain descends, with my great contribution in promoting its sublimation, it should not be difficult to summon Mo Sha through reverse reasoning." "Then, use the 'Myriad Profound Yellow World Destruction Transformations' prepared in advance and implanted into the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth, which have undergone transformation along with it, to kill Mo Sha's Heavenly Immortal Soul!"

As Li Fan manipulated these Dao Integration cultivators, he quickly reviewed the overall Dao Integration process in his mind. He confirmed that there were no major flaws. Looking at the Dao Integration cultivators, each wrapped tightly in golden threads like cocoons, Li Fan levitated one and re-infused it into the immortal formation spread across the Profound Yellow Realm. Merging with the formation nodes, their presence was completely concealed by the immortal formation's aura, making it impossible for others to detect. In fact, as long as the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth had not transformed and sublimated into an Immortal Domain, they would not be able to detect the existence of these Dao Integration cultivators.

"As the Profound Yellow All Beings Grand Formation absorbs cultivators and feeds their energy back to the Profound Yellow Realm, its connection with the Profound Yellow Realm grows increasingly strong." "These 'medicinal guides' can be quietly implanted into the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth precisely through these connections." "Firstly, to aid its sublimation on the path to becoming an Immortal Domain." "Secondly..." "The illusion formation can instantly transform into an annihilation immortal formation when necessary. With these 'medicinal guides' acting as pre-implanted formation nodes, it's akin to directly activating the immortal formation within the Profound Yellow Realm." "At that time, even if the Profound Yellow has become an Immortal Domain, it will have quite a lot to deal with!"

Li Fan's heart stirred with excitement. During the preparation for Dao Integration, his understanding of formations and alchemy had improved considerably through practical application, leading to a sense of mastery. Numerous brilliant ideas surged in his mind. It had to be said that this perspective of using all things in heaven and earth and all living beings as formations and medicines was perfectly suited to Li Fan, who possessed [Returning to True]. His actions completely resonated with his thoughts, giving him a feeling of unbridled exhilaration.

Of course, Li Fan did not let this go to his head and become reckless. He was well aware that the reason the immortal formations and the Alchemy King Scripture passed down by Sun Piaomiao allowed for such a detached attitude towards sentient beings, viewing them as ants, was entirely due to their transcended strength. True Immortals, indeed, belonged to a different caliber than ordinary mortals. Li Fan could only achieve this by borrowing the extraordinary power of [Returning to True]. Therefore, Li Fan's desire for Dao Integration became even more urgent. "Even if I can only achieve the status of a quasi-immortal, I should be completely different from a mortal!"

After implanting all the Dao Integration 'medicinal guides' into the Profound Yellow Grand Formation, Li Fan nodded slightly, deploying the formation to conceal all traces. He then turned his gaze to the Thirteen Peaks World, one of the few remaining small worlds in the Profound Yellow Realm. Over ten years had passed, and Wuyou still appeared as a child. He stood alone on the mountaintop, motionless for a long time, as if he had turned into a statue. The other beings in the Thirteen Peaks regarded him as a deity, daring not approach, only kneeling in distant worship.

But today, following an unspoken suggestion from Li Fan, Wuyou, who had been in enlightenment for a long time, finally opened his eyes. With a single step, he left the Thirteen Peaks small world and truly entered the Profound Yellow Realm. In fact, under Li Fan's secret guidance, Wuyou had already gained insight into the principles of the Profound Yellow Realm's Heaven and Earth. But when the young man, who had lived his entire life in a tiny world composed of only thirteen peaks, suddenly arrived in the vast Profound Yellow Great World, Wuyou's heart was still filled with immense shock. He looked up at the sky, down at the earth, his gaze seemingly traversing the entire Profound Yellow Realm. When he saw the sleeping beings within the world, due to Li Fan's prior hints and guidance, Wuyou was not overly surprised. He barely paid them any attention. Wuyou's true focus was solely on this Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth.

Wuyou stood still for seven days and seven nights, observing the Profound Yellow Realm. Only then did he open his eyes and begin his journey. This Great Heavenly Venerate of Profound Yellow, handpicked by Li Fan, did not immediately perform the ritual and enter the trial illusion. Instead, his figure drifted, wandering across the Profound Yellow land. He observed the mountains, rivers, plants, and gentle breezes of Profound Yellow. Although Wuyou's realm was still that of a mortal, and he had not embarked on the path of the new cultivation method, his compatibility with the Profound Yellow Realm's principles of Heaven and Earth grew with his travels. With two steps, he did not need the art of shrinking the ground into an inch; the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth actively cooperated, shortening the distance between them. He did not need to ride the wind; with a gentle spread of his arms, a gentle breeze would come, lifting him...

New cultivators needed to devour the essence of heaven and earth to master the power of its principles. But Wuyou, with the active cooperation of the Profound Yellow Realm, could perform acts of Dao Integration as a mortal. He could even draw upon not just a single heavenly law, but all that he could see. It was somewhat reminiscent of the time when Heavenly Dao Bai appeared, and the essence of heaven and earth swiftly came to his aid, responding to his call. Anyone in the world would be treated with such favor. They would gradually and unconditionally believe that they were the chosen sons of destiny, destined to become the Great Heavenly Venerate of Profound Yellow. But only Li Fan, who was behind the scenes and orchestrating everything, knew that the Profound Yellow Realm's cooperation was solely due to sensing Li Fan behind Wuyou. If Li Fan wished for such treatment, the Profound Yellow Realm's cooperation could be tens of times more spectacular! After all, considering the Profound Yellow Realm's current recovery speed, Li Fan's contribution was so immense that calling it 'recreated' would not be an exaggeration! Watching Wuyou joyfully exploring the Profound Yellow Realm, Li Fan smiled slightly. Wuyou was indeed an excellent puppet chess piece. He had almost no independent consciousness, acting purely on instinct. Unlike Sun Tianci before, even if Wuyou inherited the position of Great Heavenly Venerate of Profound Yellow, he would not take any proactive or excessive actions. He would naturally allow the Profound Yellow Realm to continue developing in a beneficial direction. Consequently, there would be no reason to obstruct Li Fan's plans. "And when the time comes to need that ball of Immortal Spiritual Qi, without me needing to guide him, the Profound Yellow Realm's urging will make him contribute it very willingly. After all, this is the mission of the Great Heavenly Venerate of Profound Yellow..." Li Fan mused as he waited for Wuyou to emerge from the illusion formation. With Sun Tianci's precedent, there were no further complications this time. A peculiar rhythm descended upon heaven and earth. The new Great Heavenly Venerate of Profound Yellow was born. Wuyou still appeared as the same pure, innocent child with clear eyes. After manifesting in reality, he stood still for a moment, then began to act. Li Fan secretly followed and observed. He discovered that Wuyou's first destination was precisely the great spatial rift in the far south of Profound Yellow. This was a scar left by the Southern Nether demonic beasts when they broke through the world and departed. Unhealed after ten thousand years, it had become a terrifying forbidden zone that most cultivators feared. Wuyou drifted to the front of the great vortex, looking at the scene of storms and thunder before him. He gently sent out a beam of white light. This warm radiance, like a clear string sound that could soothe internal anger, gradually reduced the tempestuous winds and rains of the great vortex. Wave after wave of white light descended, continuously. This ten-thousand-year-old wound of the Profound Yellow Realm was also slowly healing. Li Fan watched clearly from the side. The white light emitted by Wuyou was drawing upon the Profound Yellow Realm's vitality. However, under normal circumstances, the world's vitality was generally distributed, not concentrated in one place. But after being summoned by the Great Heavenly Venerate of Profound Yellow, it could be gathered in one spot. Under the effect of concentrated vitality, the wound rapidly healed.

Chapter 1393: Heavenly Beast Dies and Revives

The Xuanhuang Realm's unique path of self-evolution was quite extraordinary.

The [Law Cannot Coexist] calamity, which led to the mutual slaughter of ancient cultivators and the demise of countless sects, was Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao's counterattack against new-law cultivators who devoured everything.

It was indeed effective, eliminating over ninety percent of the cultivator population at the time and plunging the Xuanhuang Realm into a millennium-long era of cultivation wasteland.

Only when the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable returned and powers beyond the Heavenly Dao intervened did cultivators begin to flourish again.

It could be said that in the struggle against cultivators, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao had ultimately won.

However, the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable's later interference reversed the outcome.

Since the [Law Cannot Coexist] calamity, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao had not produced any targeted changes.

For a long time, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao's subservient state led most cultivators to lose their reverence for it.

Now, witnessing the dramatic changes within the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan sighed: "From today onwards, the tables have turned! Perhaps in future confrontations, cultivators will be on the losing end."

"If they even have a future."

Perhaps only Li Fan knew why, after the [Law Cannot Coexist] calamity, no new changes had occurred in the Xuanhuang Realm for millennia.

It was precisely because Mr. Bai had sealed a portion of Xuanhuang's malevolent thoughts back then, leaving Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao incomplete and thus losing a certain 'characteristic.'

This lifetime, Li Fan returned all of Xuanhuang's malevolent thoughts to heaven and earth, coupled with nourishment from various methods.

Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao's long-standing deficiency was gradually remedied.

Now, it was finally beginning to reveal its true prowess.

Li Fan's gaze flickered, rapidly deducing within his sea of consciousness: "Without the intervention of super external forces, Xuanhuang will naturally evolve strange changes to suppress cultivators."

"Perhaps the 'anomalies' that originally existed only in certain regions will now engulf the entire Xuanhuang Realm. More uniquely formed life forms similar to flowing colored clouds might even appear..."

The adaptive capabilities of a complete Xuanhuang Realm did not particularly exceed Li Fan's expectations.

After all, it was suspected to be an experimental ground created by the Immortal Realm; it would be illogical if it were just like any ordinary cultivation world.

Li Fan was more curious about the mechanism of these changes.

The great formations left behind by the Immortal Realm in the past had long since lost their effectiveness.

Even the core of the formation, the Nine Star Red Pearl, was nowhere to be found.

"It seems that Xuanhuang's ability to manifest these changes relies entirely on its inherent characteristics."

Li Fan squinted upwards, observing with great interest.

Due to the sufficient goodwill, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao did not conceal anything, allowing Li Fan to observe to his heart's content.

The fusion of the [True-False Transformation] and the power of immortal formations allowed Li Fan to simulate various virtual personas.

From being his loyal consciousness avatars, executing his commands flawlessly, to replacing the consciousness of various half-immortal artifacts and even nascent small worlds, serving as extensions of Li Fan's control.

It was incredibly versatile.

However, Li Fan had experimented nearly a hundred million times, and there was one bottleneck he had never broken through.

And with the current outlook, there seemed to be no prospect of progress.

That was, all created simulated personas could only execute Li Fan's initial instructions step by step.

This was not to say the situation was bad; at least it ensured these creations would not go out of control.

However, Li Fan was not particularly concerned about 'losing control.'

He even hoped these simulated personas might bring him some pleasant surprises.

Regrettably, none had achieved this so far.

"Like Xuanhuang Realm, which naturally generates adaptive changes based on real-time situations while maintaining its inherent characteristics..."

"This is what I desire."

Li Fan's thoughts connected with Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao, attempting to decipher the source of this transformation power.

He was certain that this mysterious power must have originated from the Immortal Realm's methods in the past.

If he could thoroughly comprehend it...

"Even if there are no living beings in the Star Sea, I will have inexhaustible subordinates, willing to explore beyond the high wall through successive sacrifices!"

Thinking of this, Li Fan's heart grew somewhat fervent.

However, after careful examination, Li Fan discovered that even Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao itself did not understand the meaning of this transformative power.

It only knew it possessed it from birth and could not ascertain its origin.

"To thoroughly study it would require a complete dissection of Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao. It seems impossible in this lifetime; perhaps in the next."

Li Fan nodded slightly with some regret.

Unaware that it had narrowly escaped disaster, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao, through the continuous efforts of the Great Celestial Venerable Wu Ming in clearing and repairing damages, was becoming increasingly vibrant.

It was like a stubborn stone, constantly polished by various forces, gradually revealing its hidden beauty.

"The Great Celestial Venerable is in place, and the next step can commence."

"The slow baking has lasted for fifteen years; it is time to add the medicinal auxiliaries..."

Li Fan flew to the center of the Xuanhuang Realm, standing with his hands behind his back, suspended in the void.

With a thought, spiritual energy surged towards him, at his command.

Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao now trusted Li Fan implicitly, and with the slightest greeting, Xuanhuang wholeheartedly supported him.

The spiritual energy currents of the entire Xuanhuang Realm converged towards Li Fan's location.

A phantom grand brush appeared before Li Fan.

Like a giant whale drinking water, it absorbed all the world's spiritual energy.

The phantom brush gradually solidified.

Then, guided by Li Fan's will, a second sun suddenly rose in the Xuanhuang Realm.

The moment this sun appeared, the Xuanhuang Realm seemed to transition from winter to spring.

A unique vitality emerged from the mysterious characters, silently flowing to all parts of the Xuanhuang Realm.

It was precisely the [Sun] Character Script, learned by Li Fan from the Immortal Boat!

Like the rising sun, its energy radiated, and all things began to revive!

Under Li Fan's precise control, the Script's power was perfectly modulated.

It was like a potent elixir for the Xuanhuang Realm, causing various auspicious phenomena of vibrant life to emerge across the world.

Li Fan did not stop.

He then channeled vitality from the Star Sea's earth fissure depressions.

Although both were forms of vitality, their natures differed.

The Script's vitality was externally stimulated and passively absorbed, potentially causing self-harm if not controlled.

The vitality from the earth fissure depressions, however, originated from within and permeated silently.

Even if absorbed beyond one's limit, it would only be stored and would not cause harm.

Its drawback was its slow effect, requiring gradual accumulation.

These two types of vitality, yin and yang, complemented each other.

Under Li Fan's secret coordination, they gradually merged into the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth.

The Xuanhuang Realm's sky seemed to become even clearer.

As the Script in the sky gradually dissipated and the spiritual energy attracted by Li Fan dispersed, the Xuanhuang Realm's deficiencies created over millennia by cultivators were completely replenished.

Life boomed everywhere, with myriad things competing in beauty!

However, Li Fan's alchemy was not yet complete.

"Seizing the opportune moment, striking while the iron is hot!"

With the surging life force in the Xuanhuang Realm, various transformations naturally emerged.

The birth of life within the realm was insignificant.

The crucial aspect was the gradual evolution of numerous grotto-heavens.

With abundant vitality, new grotto-heavens began to form, as if bearing fruit.

But the formation of each grotto-heaven naturally siphoned off some of Xuanhuang Realm's own power.

How could Li Fan, who sought to refine the Xuanhuang Realm into a great pill, allow such a thing to happen?

Just like he had severed the newborn five-element grotto-heavens previously.

Li Fan's gaze swept over everything, and all the grotto-heavens in sight turned to dust, rejoining Xuanhuang's essence.

Sounds of destruction echoed incessantly.

Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao did not show the slightest bit of blame for Li Fan's actions of annihilating the grotto-heavens.

Instead, it emanated sentiments of joy.

It was evident that it was dissatisfied with the countless grotto-heavens that had evolved from its own being, but was limited by its own constraints and could only allow it.

Li Fan's deliberate intervention, helping it eliminate these 'parasites,' was something it ardently desired!

Disregarding Xuanhuang's increasingly fawning intentions, Li Fan calmly observed the world.

Things were not as rosy as Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao perceived.

The sudden surge of vitality within the Xuanhuang Realm, leading to the formation of grotto-heavens, was a form of energy release.

But now, this release channel had been ruthlessly severed by Li Fan.

The result was that the Xuanhuang Realm had to forcibly absorb all the vital energy.

It grew fuller and fuller, and eventually...

With a 'boom,' it exploded!

It was akin to a pill-refining process where the alchemist kept adding ingredients without controlling the heat, leading to a furnace explosion.

Of course, Li Fan would not stand by and watch such a thing happen.

Before the Xuanhuang Realm could explode from the sheer volume of vitality, he would decisively initiate the sublimation plan.

Although there was abundant vitality now, as soon as Xuanhuang Realm's 'momentum' began to ascend, this vitality would be rapidly consumed, proving insufficient!

"When pressure is high, add auxiliary materials."

Li Fan observed for a while, ensuring the Xuanhuang Realm had reached a temporary equilibrium.

Then, he teleported to Luoyan State.

This was once a Celestial Law Realm, now subtly implanted within the Xuanhuang Realm by the Heavenly Physician.

The world's rejection reaction had subsided, and the fusion of the two realms was nearing completion.

Li Fan lightly stepped on the ground, and from beneath, a figure flew out of the Xuanhuang All Beings Grand Formation.

It was one of the chosen cultivators to serve as a medicinal guide.

"Deteriorated realms are like medicine; inject them into Xuanhuang."

Li Fan whispered, his figure seemingly stretching infinitely upwards.

He had erected a 'Ascension Formation.'

However, instead of using the [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger] divine ability, he took out a world fragment obtained from the remnant Great Wall.

From Li Fan's current perspective, the Xuanhuang Realm appeared only the size of an ordinary person.

The remnant world fragment, however, was shaped like a medicinal pill.

Gently holding it, he slowly pressed it into the Xuanhuang Realm's 'body.'

With his elevated stance, Li Fan's aura exerted immense pressure.

Under Li Fan's aura, the life forms within the Xuanhuang Realm, even in their sleep, trembled.

Even Xuanhuang Realm itself dared not transmit even a fawning thought, compelled to cooperate.

It was as if ancient memories had been reawakled.

Carefully implanting the remnant world, Li Fan's momentum suddenly waned.

"Go!"

He lightly gestured towards the compliant cultivator.

The cultivator exploded uncontrollably, not into flesh and blood, but into a phantom resembling the Heaven and Earth Essence, expanding exponentially in an instant.

It formed a film, enveloping the remnant world Li Fan had implanted.

"Rotate!"

Li Fan uttered another low command.

Streams of illusory light rapidly circulated within the film.

It was Li Fan, using the power of the immortal formation, assisting the phantom in consuming and digesting the enveloped remnant world!

The remnant world fragment, having survived millennia of calamity, was now transforming into streams of light, flowing into the phantom film.

However, this was not its final destination.

It was merely an intermediate step.

Above, the phenomenon of the Dao Integration cultivator's death began to manifest.

However, compared to the normal situation, this celestial phenomenon not only appeared extremely slowly but also lasted for an exceptionally long time.

As the phenomenon persisted, the Dao Integration cultivator's process of returning to heaven and earth proceeded in parallel.

When the phenomenon completely vanished, it signified the complete integration of the remnant world into the Xuanhuang Realm.

This was Li Fan's method of using Dao Integration cultivators as medicinal guides and buffers, using remnant worlds as medicine, to nourish the Xuanhuang Realm!

His methodology, learned from the Heavenly Physician, had undoubtedly surpassed it.

Although a Dao Integration cultivator served as a buffer, this method was still far too aggressive for the previously frail Xuanhuang Realm.

Only with the enhancements from Li Fan's various measures in this lifetime, making Xuanhuang's constitution sufficiently robust, could this prescription be applied!

This was just the preliminary condition.

Not to mention the compatibility of the remnant world with Xuanhuang, obtaining suitable remnant worlds from the remnant Great Wall was no easy feat.

The arbitrary removal of remnant worlds could trigger turmoil in the entire Star Sea, including the remnant Great Wall.

It was crucial to act at the right time.

Li Fan's success in this lifetime was also due to the experience gained in his previous life.

More importantly, treating remnant worlds as mere pills, such a seemingly effortless method could hardly be achieved even by Star Sea Supreme Beings.

Only with the assistance of True Immortal flesh and blood and immortal formations could Li Fan accomplish it with such apparent ease.

After completing one instance, Li Fan did not rest.

He continuously implanted the prepared remnant worlds into various locations within the Xuanhuang Realm.
