Even before Xuanhuang Realm began absorbing their power, Li Fan could vaguely sense the impending transformations within the world.

"The Xuanhuang Realm is unique within the Star Sea, but that does not mean it possesses all the laws."

"Compared to the laws pervading the Star Sea, it still has some deficiencies."

"But these deficiencies can be compensated by consuming the remnant worlds I provide."

"The principle is the same as its absorption of immortal artifacts."

Li Fan's eyes gleamed, and he continued his work.

He only stopped when he felt the Xuanhuang Realm had reached its limit.

"Hmm, as it continues to strengthen, it can still be 'fed' again after some time."

"This process will repeat until it reaches its absolute limit."

"At that point, it will undergo transformation."

Chapter 1394: Primordial Yellow Regeneration Change

However, it also understood who was in control of the situation. It rubbed against Li Fan's palm, showing deference.

"The Qilin beast is a creation of the Immortal Realm. Judging by its eagerness, it seems capable of devouring Immortal Realm chess pieces..."

"The stones that Xuanhuang couldn't fully digest can be processed through this little 'rascal'!"

"When the little fellow is well-fed, I'll kill it and offer it to the heavens!"

Li Fan's eyes flashed. He immediately withdrew the protection from the Immortal Realm chess piece. The Qilin beast, ecstatic, began gnawing at it with loud crunching sounds. The sound of brittle bones being crushed echoed endlessly.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, capturing the dramatic changes occurring within the Immortal Realm chess piece. According to previous observations, an Immortal Realm chess piece was composed of countless True Immortal Scripts representing the laws of the Immortal Realm. When the chess piece was damaged or stimulated, the True Immortal Scripts within would unfold, revealing a glimpse of the Immortal Realm. However, a single chess piece contained incomplete True Immortal Scripts, merely fragments. Therefore, when unfolded, it did not depict the Immortal Realm of the past, but only when all the chess pieces were gathered and the fragments pieced together to form complete True Immortal Scripts. Only then would the true Immortal Realm, containing the Southern Immortal Pillar, descend.

But after all, it was a part of the Immortal Realm. Even unfolding and transforming its form required vast amounts of energy, let alone its destruction. It was certainly not something ordinary individuals could achieve.

Now, under the Qilin beast's chewing, the True Immortal Script fragments composing the Immortal Realm chess piece disintegrated further, turning into minuscule energy fragments that the Qilin beast happily swallowed.

Although it had just been born, the Qilin beast was already stuffed after eating. But seeing the nearly untouched Immortal Realm chess piece, the little creature was reluctant to let go and continued to gnaw for a while longer. Finally, unable to eat more, it reluctantly lay down on the chess piece, fearing Li Fan would take it back.

Having had its fill, the Qilin beast fell into a deep slumber. The Immortal Realm law fragments swallowed within its belly were quietly transforming its body. Its shell became even harder, and its body grew more robust.

The most significant change was in the Qilin beast's eyes. Though not yet open, Li Fan could already sense the extraordinary power hidden within. Even while sleeping, its eyes seemed to be vigilantly observing its surroundings, concentrating most of the time on Li Fan, as if it had already sensed Li Fan's ulterior motives!

"The Qilin beast's eyes are quite interesting."

"The Heavenly King Xuan, fleeing from the Immortal Realm, gained countless treasures. But what he fed the Qilin beast, I cannot say for sure compared to what I feed it. After all, I am feeding it genuine Immortal Realm fragments. Even True Immortals might hesitate to do so."

Li Fan eagerly anticipated the Qilin beast's performance when it fully matured in this lifetime. It wasn't that he needed the Qilin beast's combat power. According to Mo Ruobin, a fully grown Qilin beast was comparable to the Twelve Law Kings, which was of little use to Li Fan.

What Li Fan truly cared about were the Qilin beast's eyes. In his previous life, Li Fan, following Mo Ruobin, entered the Qilin beast's eyes and, amidst countless illusory worlds, saw the humanoid characters hidden within. This character was not the work of the Dao Inscriber Immortal but an attempt at 'inscribing Dao' by someone else. Although the inscriptions were less refined and beautiful than the Dao Inscriber Immortal's, the inherent quality of the Dao law it depicted was extremely high. Thus, the humanoid character gave Li Fan a feeling comparable to the power of [Immortal-Mortal Transformation].

"The Qilin beast is formed from a jade pendant, yet it is lifelike, indistinguishable from a true sentient being. Such a technique..."

Li Fan vaguely guessed while caressing the Qilin beast. He had always suspected that the pattern engraved at the very bottom of the Star Sea originated from this humanoid character. Now, as he gently stroked the Qilin beast and compared the faint aura emanating from it with Qiu Shui, his suspicion was further confirmed.

"It seems the [Form of Life], which was a simplified version, is still incredibly complex... The methods of the Immortal Realm are beyond what mortals can comprehend."

"Even the simplified version is so intricate... "

Li Fan frowned slightly, recalling the scene he witnessed in the earth fissure depression.

"[Immortal-Mortal Transformation] and [Form of Life]..."

"The Spiritual Gathering and Immortal Ascension Formation in the Dark Sea contains [Immortal-Mortal Transformation]."

"[Form of Life] is hidden within the Qilin beast's eyes."

"Are the other two formations in the Star Crossing Great Formation also hiding corresponding True Immortal Scripts?"

A thought suddenly flashed in Li Fan's mind.

"[Golden Lock Dangling Formation], the Root of Heaven and Earth."

Li Fan had visited the Root of Heaven and Earth space more than once but found no trace of True Immortal Scripts. It utilized the power of ancient immortal formations born alongside the Xuanhuang Realm. As for the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, it was completely destroyed during the era of the Ten Great Immortal Sects and no longer existed in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"I might be overthinking it. [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] and [Form of Life] are high-tier True Immortal Scripts among many. Even with Heavenly King Xuan's extensive gains in the Immortal Realm, obtaining these two Scripts might have been his limit..."

Li Fan mused inwardly. Returning his attention to the juvenile Qilin beast,

"The [Form of Life] engraved in the Star Sea is too vast. Detecting it takes a great deal of time."

"And the one within the Qilin beast's eyes was poorly inscribed and within Heavenly King Xuan's formation, making it too distorted..."

"Moreover, this little creature's manifestation is likely the closest to its original form."

Thinking this, Li Fan couldn't help but touch the Qilin beast again. With Li Fan's well-intentioned emanations of power, the Qilin beast's eyes did not accept it. Instead, it grew increasingly nervous, even showing signs of waking the slumbering young beast. It had to be said that as a creation of the Immortal Realm, its senses were indeed acute. Even though Li Fan had already glimpsed it in his previous life, the Qilin beast still showed such a reaction.

Li Fan did not push too hard; he had plenty of time to deal with this little creature. Regardless of whether it was mere objects or true sentient beings, Li Fan had ways to control them.

With a thought, Qiu Shui appeared beside Li Fan, shimmering with blue light. It immediately sensed the Qilin beast's presence. Perhaps due to being of the same origin, the Qilin beast's vigilance towards Qiu Shui significantly decreased.

"Leave this little one to you for now. Take good care of it," Li Fan instructed.

"As you command, Great Master!"

Qiu Shui did not dare to delay, approaching and picking up the Qilin beast. It also noticed the Immortal Realm chess piece being crushed by the Qilin beast. As it was not a creation of the Immortal Realm, Qiu Shui did not perceive the chess piece's extraordinary nature. Furthermore, wielding the boundless power of the Star Sea, it had no interest in any single world, only faithfully executing Li Fan's orders.

Noticing the Qilin beast's lack of interest in its boundless Star Sea power, Qiu Shui appeared somewhat distressed.

"It has the Immortal Realm chess piece to gnaw on, so you don't need to feed it further."

"Take it and tour the Xuanhuang Realm and the Star Sea. That would be sufficient," Li Fan said calmly.

Qiu Shui breathed a sigh of relief and, carrying the Qilin beast, departed according to his orders.

"Given the little creature's sensitivity, perhaps it might discover some unexpected things."

With Qiu Shui's Supreme stage power and its ability to commune with the origin of the Star Sea, Li Fan was not worried about their safety.

Returning his attention to the transparent Heaven and Earth Essence, after five conveyances (three, two, three, two, three), the transparent Heaven and Earth Essence had finally integrated all the half-immortal artifacts into the Xuanhuang Realm.

On the Xuanhuang land, besides the Qilin beast, four other peculiar life forms emerged: the Human-faced Snow Mountain, the Thousand-Mile Dragon Worm, the Flowing Colored Cloud, and the Galloping Giant Tree.

Among these, the most noteworthy was the strange cloud floating in the sky, emitting multicolored light. The cloud spontaneously generated illusions, constantly shifting, mostly displaying scenes from the Xuanhuang Realm. However, at intermittent moments, it would also reflect scenes from the Immortal Realm of the past!

It was precisely because Li Fan had glimpsed the Immortal Realm's appearance in the True Immortal's memory that he could recognize it.

"This should be the result of devouring three half-immortal artifacts."

When the illusory scene of the Immortal Realm appeared, even for a fleeting moment, it caused the cloud to boil and churn. The seven-colored light flickered incessantly, and the entire cloud seemed on the verge of evaporating and vanishing. After returning to its normal form, the flowing colored cloud had shrunk by a tenth. Yet, inexplicably, it did not cease reflecting scenes from the Immortal Realm. Instead, it began to do so more frequently.

Each reflection consumed its own life force. After eight such cycles, the flowing colored cloud completely dissipated. Li Fan vaguely saw the laws contained within the half-immortal artifacts it had devoured, flowing into the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao. It had only been slightly more than half a month since the manifestation of the flowing colored cloud.

"Vanished like smoke, having only existed for half a month. For a cloud, this is a long life, but for a transcendent creation, it's practically a premature death."

Li Fan looked at the other three creations. The Heaven and Earth Essence, like a scarlet sun suspended above their heads, the Human-faced Snow Mountain was transforming into a Flame Mountain. The Thousand-Mile Dragon Worm was continuously splitting itself, one into two, two into four. After half a month, it had become billions of small worms. However, these small worms lacked any survival capabilities; they only ate and split again. When the size of the split bodies could no longer support them in finding food, the worm swarm was nearing its end.

As for the Galloping Giant Tree, it continued to run forward ceaselessly. Its leaves withered, and its branches cracked during its sprint, also signaling its impending demise.

Among the four creations, only the juvenile Qilin beast remained in sweet slumber.

"This is Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao acting intentionally..."

"Perhaps it discovered that the Qilin beast's lifespan was too long, making the process of devouring and integrating the Immortal Artifact laws take too much time. So, it created such a unique change!"

Li Fan discerned the underlying pattern.

"It seems it has found a new path. In the future, Xuanhuang's internal cycle will likely accelerate significantly."

"Correspondingly, strange creatures will emerge more frequently within the Xuanhuang Realm."

This was a peculiar change that had not occurred even when the Xuanhuang Realm faced the world-ending crisis. Li Fan recorded it with great interest.

Chapter 1395: The Great Medicine of Heaven and Earth Refining

The Xuanhuang Realm's unique path of self-evolution is quite special.

The "Law Cannot Coexist" calamity, which led to the mutual slaughter of ancient cultivators and the demise of countless sects, was Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao's counterattack against new-law cultivators who devoured everything.

It was indeed effective, eliminating over ninety percent of the cultivator population at the time and plunging the Xuanhuang Realm into a millennium-long era of cultivation wasteland. Only when the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable returned and powers beyond the Heavenly Dao intervened did cultivators begin to flourish again.

It could be said that in the struggle against cultivators, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao had ultimately won. However, the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable's later interference reversed the outcome.

Since the "Law Cannot Coexist" calamity, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao had not produced any targeted changes. For a long time, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao's subservient state led most cultivators to lose their reverence for it.

Now, witnessing the dramatic changes within the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan sighed: "From today onwards, the tables have turned! Perhaps in future confrontations, cultivators will be on the losing end."

"If they even have a future."

Perhaps only Li Fan knew why, after the "Law Cannot Coexist" calamity, no new changes had occurred in the Xuanhuang Realm for millennia. It was precisely because Mr. Bai had sealed a portion of Xuanhuang's malevolent thoughts back then, leaving Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao incomplete and thus losing a certain 'characteristic.'

This lifetime, Li Fan had already returned all of Xuanhuang's malevolent thoughts to heaven and earth, coupled with nourishment from various methods. Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao's long-standing deficiency was gradually remedied. Now, it was finally beginning to reveal its true prowess.

Li Fan's gaze flickered, rapidly deducing within his sea of consciousness: "Without the intervention of super external forces, Xuanhuang will naturally evolve strange changes to suppress cultivators."

"Perhaps the 'anomalies' that originally existed only in certain regions will now engulf the entire Xuanhuang Realm. More uniquely formed life forms similar to flowing colored clouds might even appear..."

The adaptive capabilities of a complete Xuanhuang Realm did not particularly exceed Li Fan's expectations. After all, it was suspected to be an experimental ground created by the Immortal Realm; it would be illogical if it were just like any ordinary cultivation world.

Li Fan was more curious about the mechanism of these changes. The great formations left behind by the Immortal Realm in the past had long since lost their effectiveness. Even the core of the formation, the Nine Star Red Pearl, was nowhere to be found.

"It seems that Xuanhuang's ability to manifest these changes relies entirely on its inherent characteristics."

Li Fan looked up and squinted, observing with great interest. Due to the sufficient goodwill, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao did not conceal anything, allowing Li Fan to observe to his heart's content.

The fusion of the "True-False Transformation" and the power of immortal formations allowed Li Fan to simulate various virtual personas. From being his loyal consciousness avatars, executing his commands flawlessly, to replacing the consciousness of various half-immortal artifacts and even nascent small worlds, serving as extensions of Li Fan's control. It was incredibly versatile.

However, Li Fan had experimented nearly a hundred million times, and there was one bottleneck he had never broken through. And with the current outlook, there seemed to be no prospect of progress. That was, all created simulated personas could only execute Li Fan's initial instructions step by step.

This was not to say the situation was bad; at least it ensured these creations would not go out of control. But Li Fan was not particularly concerned about 'losing control.' He even hoped these simulated personas might bring him some pleasant surprises. Regrettably, none had achieved this so far.

"Like Xuanhuang Realm, which naturally generates adaptive changes based on real-time situations while maintaining its inherent characteristics..."

"This is what I desire."

Li Fan's thoughts connected with Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao, attempting to decipher the source of this transformative power. He was certain that this mysterious power must have originated from the Immortal Realm's methods in the past. If he could thoroughly comprehend it...

"Even if there are no living beings in the Star Sea, I will have inexhaustible subordinates, willing to explore beyond the high wall through successive sacrifices!" Thinking of this, Li Fan's heart grew somewhat fervent.

However, after careful examination, Li Fan discovered that even Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao itself did not understand the meaning of this transformative power. It only knew it possessed it from birth and could not ascertain its origin.

"To thoroughly study it would require a complete dissection of Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao. It seems impossible in this lifetime; perhaps in the next."

Li Fan nodded slightly with some regret. Unaware that it had narrowly escaped disaster, Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao, through the continuous efforts of the Great Celestial Venerable Wu Ming in clearing and repairing damages, was becoming increasingly vibrant. It was like a stubborn stone, constantly polished by various forces, gradually revealing its hidden beauty.

"The Great Celestial Venerable is in place, and the next step can commence."

"The slow baking has lasted for fifteen years; it is time to add the medicinal auxiliaries..."

Li Fan flew to the center of the Xuanhuang Realm, standing with his hands behind his back, suspended in the void. With a thought, spiritual energy surged towards him, at his command. Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao now trusted Li Fan implicitly, and with the slightest greeting, Xuanhuang wholeheartedly supported him. The spiritual energy currents of the entire Xuanhuang Realm converged towards Li Fan's location. A phantom grand brush appeared before Li Fan. Like a giant whale drinking water, it absorbed all the world's spiritual energy. The phantom brush gradually solidified.

Then, guided by Li Fan's will, a second sun suddenly rose in the Xuanhuang Realm. The moment this sun appeared, the Xuanhuang Realm seemed to transition from winter to spring. A unique vitality emerged from the mysterious characters, silently flowing to all parts of the Xuanhuang Realm. It was precisely the "Sun" Character Script, learned by Li Fan from the Immortal Boat! Like the rising sun, its energy radiated, and all things began to revive!

Under Li Fan's precise control, the Script's power was perfectly modulated. It was like a potent elixir for the Xuanhuang Realm, causing various auspicious phenomena of vibrant life to emerge across the world. Li Fan did not stop. He then channeled vitality from the Star Sea's earth fissure depressions. Although both were forms of vitality, their natures differed. The Script's vitality was externally stimulated and passively absorbed, potentially causing self-harm if not controlled. The vitality from the earth fissure depressions, however, originated from within and permeated silently. Even if absorbed beyond one's limit, it would only be stored and would not cause harm. Its drawback was its slow effect, requiring gradual accumulation.

These two types of vitality, yin and yang, complemented each other. Under Li Fan's secret coordination, they gradually merged into the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth. The Xuanhuang Realm's sky seemed to become even clearer. As the Script in the sky gradually dissipated and the spiritual energy attracted by Li Fan dispersed, the Xuanhuang Realm's deficiencies created over millennia by cultivators were completely replenished. Life boomed everywhere, with myriad things competing in beauty!

However, Li Fan's alchemy was not yet complete.

"Seizing the opportune moment, striking while the iron is hot!"

With the surging life force in the Xuanhuang Realm, various transformations naturally emerged. The birth of life within the realm was insignificant. The crucial aspect was the gradual evolution of numerous grotto-heavens. With abundant vitality, new grotto-heavens began to form, as if bearing fruit. But the formation of each grotto-heaven naturally siphoned off some of Xuanhuang Realm's own power. How could Li Fan, who sought to refine the Xuanhuang Realm into a great pill, allow such a thing to happen? Just like he had severed the newborn five-element grotto-heavens previously. Li Fan's gaze swept over everything, and all the grotto-heavens in sight turned to dust, rejoining Xuanhuang's essence. Sounds of destruction echoed incessantly.

Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao did not show the slightest bit of blame for Li Fan's actions of annihilating the grotto-heavens. Instead, it emanated sentiments of joy. It was evident that it was dissatisfied with the countless grotto-heavens that had evolved from its own being, but was limited by its own constraints and could only allow it. Li Fan's deliberate intervention, helping it eliminate these 'parasites,' was something it ardently desired!

Disregarding Xuanhuang's increasingly fawning intentions, Li Fan calmly observed the world. Things were not as rosy as Xuanhuang's Heavenly Dao perceived. The sudden surge of vitality within the Xuanhuang Realm, leading to the formation of grotto-heavens, was a form of energy release. But now, this release channel had been ruthlessly severed by Li Fan. The result was that the Xuanhuang Realm had to forcibly absorb all the vital energy. It grew fuller and fuller, and eventually... With a 'boom,' it exploded! It was akin to a pill-refining process where the alchemist kept adding ingredients without controlling the heat, leading to a furnace explosion.

Of course, Li Fan would not stand by and watch such a thing happen. Before the Xuanhuang Realm could explode from the sheer volume of vitality, he would decisively initiate the sublimation plan. Although there was abundant vitality now, as soon as Xuanhuang Realm's 'momentum' began to ascend, this vitality would be rapidly consumed, proving insufficient!

"When pressure is high, add auxiliary materials."

Li Fan observed for a while, ensuring the Xuanhuang Realm had reached a temporary equilibrium. Then, he teleported to Luoyan State. This was once a Celestial Law Realm, now subtly implanted within the Xuanhuang Realm by the Heavenly Physician. The world's rejection reaction had subsided, and the fusion of the two realms was nearing completion. Li Fan lightly stepped on the ground, and from beneath, a figure flew out of the Xuanhuang All Beings Grand Formation. It was one of the chosen cultivators to serve as a medicinal guide.

"Deteriorated realms are like medicine; inject them into Xuanhuang."

Li Fan whispered, his figure seemingly stretching infinitely upwards. He had erected an 'Ascension Formation.' However, instead of using the "Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger" divine ability, he took out a world fragment obtained from the remnant Great Wall. From Li Fan's current perspective, the Xuanhuang Realm appeared only the size of an ordinary person. The remnant world fragment, however, was shaped like a medicinal pill. Gently holding it, he slowly pressed it into the Xuanhuang Realm's 'body.' With his elevated stance, Li Fan's aura exerted immense pressure. Under Li Fan's aura, the life forms within the Xuanhuang Realm, even in their sleep, trembled. Even Xuanhuang Realm itself dared not transmit even a fawning thought, compelled to cooperate. It was as if ancient memories had been reawakled. Carefully implanting the remnant world, Li Fan's momentum suddenly waned.

"Go!"

He lightly gestured towards the compliant cultivator. The cultivator exploded uncontrollably, not into flesh and blood, but into a phantom resembling the Heaven and Earth Essence, expanding exponentially in an instant. It formed a film, enveloping the remnant world Li Fan had implanted.

"Rotate!"

Li Fan uttered another low command. Streams of illusory light rapidly circulated within the film. It was Li Fan, using the power of the immortal formation, assisting the phantom in consuming and digesting the enveloped remnant world! The remnant world fragment, having survived millennia of calamity, was now transforming into streams of light, flowing into the phantom film. However, this was not its final destination. It was merely an intermediate step.

Above, the phenomenon of the Dao Integration cultivator's death began to manifest. However, compared to the normal situation, this celestial phenomenon not only appeared extremely slowly but also lasted for an exceptionally long time. As the phenomenon persisted, the Dao Integration cultivator's process of returning to heaven and earth proceeded in parallel. When the phenomenon completely vanished, it signified the complete integration of the remnant world into the Xuanhuang Realm. This was Li Fan's method of using Dao Integration cultivators as medicinal guides and buffers, using remnant worlds as medicine, to nourish the Xuanhuang Realm! His methodology, learned from the Heavenly Physician, had undoubtedly surpassed it. Although a Dao Integration cultivator served as a buffer, this method was still far too aggressive for the previously frail Xuanhuang Realm. Only with the enhancements from Li Fan's various measures in this lifetime, making Xuanhuang's constitution sufficiently robust, could this prescription be applied! This was just the preliminary condition. Not to mention the compatibility of the remnant world with Xuanhuang, obtaining suitable remnant worlds from the remnant Great Wall was no easy feat. The arbitrary removal of remnant worlds could trigger turmoil in the entire Star Sea, including the remnant Great Wall. It was crucial to act at the right time. Li Fan's success in this lifetime was also due to the experience gained in his previous life. More importantly, treating remnant worlds as mere pills, such a seemingly effortless method could hardly be achieved even by Star Sea Supreme Beings. Only with the assistance of True Immortal flesh and blood and immortal formations could Li Fan accomplish it with such apparent ease.

After completing one instance, Li Fan did not rest. He continuously implanted the prepared remnant worlds into various locations within the Xuanhuang Realm. Even before Xuanhuang Realm began absorbing their power, Li Fan could vaguely sense the impending transformations within the world.

"The Xuanhuang Realm is unique within the Star Sea, but that does not mean it possesses all the laws."

"Compared to the laws pervading the Star Sea, it still has some deficiencies."

"But these deficiencies can be compensated by consuming the remnant worlds I provide."

"The principle is the same as its absorption of immortal artifacts."

Li Fan's eyes gleamed, and he continued his work. He only stopped when he felt the Xuanhuang Realm had reached its limit.

"Hmm, as it continues to strengthen, it can still be 'fed' again after some time."

"This process will repeat until it reaches its absolute limit."

"At that point, it will undergo transformation."

Chapter 1396: About to Overturn the Star Sea

Up to this point, the preparatory work for refining Xuanhuang into an elixir of ascension has been mostly completed.

What Li Fan needs to do next is to wait.

Wait for the Nameless One to truly inherit the authority of the Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang, and wait for the Xuanhuang Realm to absorb various essences and reach its limit.

"At most three years, or as little as one year."

Whether it succeeds or fails, the remaining time in this life will not be much.

The plan Li Fan had previously drafted should now be implemented.

With a flash, he arrived at the small world of the You Clan.

The [Detain] character script was out of place, residing in a corner of the stone tablet. The characters for the transformation between immortal and mortal gradually spread. It was uncertain how many had already appeared.

But Li Fan had a vague premonition that the complete manifestation of these mysterious characters was not far off.

Li Fan scanned the small world with his divine sense. As expected, during the period he did not supervise, the physique of the You Clan members continued to strengthen.

After carefully examining the body of each You Clan member, he selected the strongest one.

He split off a strand of his divine sense and possessed its body using the [Dao Pill] method.

Then, Li Fan avoided other You Clan members and slowly walked through the immortal formation, arriving before the stone tablet.

Using the You Clan member's body, he gazed from afar at the few characters revealed on the leg bone of the Nameless True Immortal. Li Fan sensed his own bloodline churning within him.

It was as if some scorching spring was constantly beating and roasting, wanting to boil all the blood in this body.

Li Fan couldn't help but avert his gaze.

The abnormality within his body continued, like the unceasing beating of war drums.

"It seems I have glimpsed that True Immortal script and touched some kind of taboo..."

"But I will try it nonetheless!"

Li Fan let out a cold snort. While he was attached to the You Clan's body, his eyes became even more devout.

He kowtowed, sensing the subtle changes within him.

With the experience of glimpsing the characters of the Immortal-Mortal Transformation in his previous life, Li Fan was incredibly smooth this time, sensing that trace of profound mystery.

The You Clan's body seemed to be suffering a heavenly curse.

Time flowed rapidly upon it, its hair turning white in an instant, its life being rapidly burned away.

Li Fan remained unmoved, focusing his spirit instead on probing the traces of the Immortal-Mortal Transformation.

With the portion already displayed on the stone tablet as a reference, Li Fan excluded it and only needed to probe the remaining character traces.

Having made full psychological preparations, Li Fan's speed in probing these endless True Immortal script characters in this life was a bit faster than in his previous life.

But it was almost as fleeting as before.

This short period was not enough for Li Fan to glimpse the full appearance of this character.

The possessed You Clan body, as if consumed by fire, turned into ashes.

At the same time, Li Fan's true self flashed to the front of the stone tablet and imprinted all his insights.

Just as the Star Sea Hungry Immortal did in his previous life.

On the stone tablet, that mysterious character rapidly extended. In an instant, it expanded by more than double its original size.

Li Fan sensed that after all his insights regarding the Immortal-Mortal Transformation were completely devoured.

The stone tablet actually wanted to absorb him as well!

Having witnessed the power of the true Southern Immortal Pillar, how could Li Fan not be prepared?

The phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed, helping Li Fan successfully evade the stone tablet's absorption.

But in that brief moment of contact, Li Fan was shocked to discover that his original peak Deity Transformation realm had actually fallen to the middle stage of Deity Transformation.

If he had hesitated for another moment, he might have been directly drained into a mortal!

"Everything related to the Nameless True Immortal is indeed terrifying and not to be underestimated!"

Li Fan took a deep breath and calmed himself.

He carefully observed the appearance on the stone tablet.

In addition to the Immortal-Mortal Transformation character, which had doubled its progress, there were also some mottled shadows.

These shadows connected to form a ring, which was precisely the appearance of the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven.

"The Way of the Five Elements..."

Unfortunately, the trace was too shallow, and nothing could be discerned from it.

Li Fan's gaze then turned to his target.

"The True Immortal character scripts I know are [Hunger] and [Chaos], on the first tier."

"Next are [Innate] and [Creation], on a higher tier."

"Above those are this [Immortal-Mortal Transformation] and [Form of Life]."

Li Fan compared these two known scripts, and under cross-verification, he felt slightly at ease.

"I have already deduced eighty percent. Based on the current rate of life input from the You Clan, it should be enough."

"If, in the end, there is still a shortage. I can also sacrifice all the You Clan members together."

Li Fan nodded to himself.

"Conversely, the complete [Form of Life]..." Li Fan frowned slightly.

If his guess was correct, these two were of the same grade. Then the shape Li Fan had currently comprehended was probably less than one-fifth of the complete form!

"Just glimpsing its full appearance is already so strenuous. Let alone comprehending the Dao contained within."

However, Li Fan did not seek to understand its principles now. Just being able to use it like the Xuan Heavenly King was enough!

"The little 'bá' was transformed from a jade pendant. I wonder if throwing it directly to this stone tablet can manifest its principles?" Li Fan's heart suddenly fluttered.

But narrowing his eyes and after careful consideration, Li Fan suppressed this budding idea.

"Let's raise the little 'bá' a bit bigger first. If that doesn't work, then rely on the stone tablet."

It wasn't that Li Fan had grown benevolent, but that in this lifetime, caution was paramount.

Mortal objects could be swallowed by the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone. It was fine.

The 'bá' beast, after all, was a creation of the Immortal Realm, containing immeasurable energy. If this leg bone were to eat its fill all at once...

Who knew what changes might occur.

Li Fan did not forget the scene from the end of his previous life, where the leg bone inexplicably flew towards him after the Nameless Stele exploded.

"One must guard against it."

"One cannot be blinded by momentary profit."

In fact, there were many things Li Fan wanted the stone tablet to devour and then manifest its principles.

Including the Qingming Pearl, still buried at the end of the ground fissure depression.

Although in his previous life, according to Xu Ke's description, the moment he touched the Qingming Pearl, this supreme treasure had vanished into smoke due to energy depletion.

But Li Fan was certain that at this point in time, the Qingming Pearl was still maintaining its final indestructible form.

Mortals could not collect it.

The Nameless True Immortal's leg bone, however, most likely could!

"This stele is a natural auxiliary Dao enlightenment machine."

"Anything dangerous can be fed to it, and then its principles can be sensed through a mediating step."

"Even..."

Li Fan's gaze left the stone tablet and looked towards the depths of the starry sky.

"Destroying the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea, and even the High Wall, would be acceptable."

"The entirety of a star sea should be enough to manifest many laws on the stone tablet!"

The thought of that scene made Li Fan's heart pound with excitement.

"There will be such a day, but not now."

"At the very least, I must first have the power to protect myself. Only then can I undertake such a grand undertaking!"

Chapter 1397: New Era of the Tridents

The Nameless True Immortal's leg bone continued, as per plan, to analyze the Immortal-Mortal Transformation script using the flesh and blood of the You Clan members.

Li Fan first made specific improvements to the simulated persona supervising this area, ensuring it had a detailed understanding of the You Clan's bloodline's unsealing degree. After confirming that the You Clan members would not lose control even in the final moments of this life, Li Fan then teleported away.

Returning to the Great Xuan Lecture Platform, he first reviewed the overall progress of the beings exploring the Carefree Dreamlands over the past dozen years.

The complexity of the dreamland was indeed beyond imagination.

Nearly a million people had been invested so far, yet there had been no qualitative breakthroughs.

The most deeply exploring individual, surnamed Hou Mingwu, had reached Level 7 in dreamland experience. Within the dream, he could already destroy a world with a mere wave of his hand. Such terrifying destructive power was comparable to the Longevity stage in the Xuanhuang Realm, even surpassing it.

This Level 7 explorer, Hou Mingwu, did not have high cultivation talent in reality. After listening to the lecture phantom for over a month, he barely broke through the Qi Refining stage. Unexpectedly, after being dispatched by Li Fan into the dreamland, within his first dream world, he fortuitously acquired a heaven-defying treasure called the "Mirror of Restoration," capable of reshaping shattered, defunct magical treasures. In the dreamland, almost all powerful magical treasures had limited uses. Once depleted, recharging them required either a large amount of dreamland currency or feeding them with lower-tier magical treasures.

The price for reactivation was too high, sometimes not worth the cost.

Therefore, some chose to sell these defunct treasures at a low price, at least to recoup some of their expenses.

Hou Mingwu used the heaven-defying properties of the Mirror of Restoration to repair treasures and then resell them.

After several transactions, he amassed a fortune.

The dreamland was vast, and after each transaction, Hou Mingwu would change his usual dreamland region, so for a long time, nobody discovered his secret.

By the time the news of him possessing the Mirror of Restoration finally got out, Hou Mingwu had already grown strong enough.

He was laden with treasures, and the number of items he carried alone could rival top teams in the dreamland. During dreamland missions, Hou Mingwu could use his treasures indiscriminately, regardless of the cost. Even in treacherous worlds where brute force was ineffective, he could always escape danger with the help of his numerous magical treasures. Thus, Hou Mingwu's efficiency in conquering dreamland worlds was far beyond ordinary individuals.

Despite endless greed from others, Hou Mingwu always acted alone, refusing all invitations for cooperation or team-ups. They had no way to deal with him.

Once, several major teams joined forces, using a tracking magical treasure to forcibly follow Hou Mingwu during a mission, intending to conspire and seize the Mirror of Restoration.

However, Hou Mingwu seemed to have detected their tracking in advance and laid an ambush in the world. Before they could act, the entire world plunged into a terrifying doomsday scenario of destruction.

Pursuit was out of the question. The major teams scattered like startled birds, suffering heavy casualties. Afterward, they first suspected a mole within their ranks, then speculated that Hou Mingwu must possess a supreme treasure capable of predicting the future and averting misfortune.

After this incident, the schemes against Hou Mingwu in the dreamland temporarily ceased.

In truth, their guesses were not entirely wrong; besides the Mirror of Restoration, Hou Mingwu did indeed possess a supreme treasure. This treasure was not from the dreamland; it was Li Fan's attention!

As the vanguard exploring the Carefree Dreamlands, how could Li Fan allow Hou Mingwu to be harmed so easily?

The million individuals dispatched to the dreamland were like Li Fan's eyes. Some were even within the major teams targeting Hou Mingwu. They just didn't realize they were traitors.

Protected by Li Fan, Hou Mingwu had virtually no mortal danger in the Carefree Dreamlands.

And Hou Mingwu did not disappoint Li Fan.

The several worlds he experienced in the deep dreamland verified Li Fan's judgment.

The scope of the Carefree Dreamlands had long since left the Xuanhuang Realm and extended into the starry sky.

Because Li Fan clearly saw the shadow of the Mystic Immortal Boat in those worlds!

Not merely abstract representations of the immortal boat, but individual concepts like the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God, the Heavenly Star Light Lotus, the Duan Divine Arm, and the Dao-Chasing Giant.

"The Immortal Boat should be unaware of this matter. The Carefree Dreamlands did not forcibly pull the Immortal Boat's people into the illusion. It merely used snippets of their subconscious thoughts as a basis for constructing the dream."

"The Immortal Boat's crew are no ordinary individuals. Yet, they were so easily captured by Wu You's thoughts. Wu You... is this strong?" Li Fan couldn't help but frown slightly.

"However, it can be confirmed that it truly exists and has not been sensed by him. Perhaps the Mystic Immortal Boat fell prey to Wu You at some point."

Li Fan gazed into the distance, his sight seemingly piercing through the boundless starry sky and arriving at the foot of the high wall.

"It has already enveloped the Immortal Boat, perhaps not far from breaking through the wall's blockade."

"No wonder Wu You seems to have never cared much about the affairs within the Xuanhuang Realm. Even during several world-ending crises in Xuanhuang, he merely lay low without intervening. Was he trying to achieve his goal through an alternative route, a different method to pass through the high wall?"

The previous discovery had almost confirmed that the high wall's blockade seemed to have a weaker effect on consciousness and mental energy. Li Fan had long ago vaguely suspected Wu You's subtle actions, merely confirming it now.

"If my true body were to leave the wall, it would be too dangerous. It would be better to use the power of Wu You's dreamland to test the waters first..." This thought flashed through Li Fan's mind.

"My hope, Sun Erlang and the others, their exploration progress cannot keep up with this unknown person named Hou Mingwu. I should indeed make the best use of everything and have them do what they are good at."

Shaking his head slightly, Li Fan further divided a wisp of his divine sense to monitor Hou Mingwu's every move.

In this lifetime, Li Fan did not intend to interact with Wu You yet.

Although Li Fan was certain that Wu You had definitely discovered him, the orchestrator behind dispatching millions of beings to invade the dreamland, through the actions of the Xuanhuang formation master.

But for some reason, Wu You, despite having the ability to instantly expel everyone from the dreamland, had not acted yet.

"It seems a certain level of detachment means not caring at all."

"Quite interesting."

"It's a pity that with his current strength, his consciousness cannot exist solely in the void. If I were to destroy him in the real world, Wu You's dreamland would also vanish!" Li Fan also felt a sense of condescension.

Wu You didn't care about the intruders in the dreamland; Li Fan didn't care about him either.

"I only need to proceed step by step, steadily merging with the Dao."

Recalling his thoughts, Li Fan's gaze became profound and deep.

Fortunately, in this lifetime, when he envisioned and deduced the scene of merging with the Dao soon, the fatal sense of crisis from the Mists of Oblivion did not appear again.

"There shouldn't be any major mishaps."

However, for safety's sake, Li Fan still needed to make a trip to the Mystic Immortal Boat.

"Since the puppet can still be somewhat effective, perhaps the Tri-pronged Tree is also similar."

Being able to unofficially simulate for free once, even Li Fan was tempted. After all, from the situation in his previous life, the simulation process did not seem to involve Li Fan personally experiencing it but would flash in his mind like a slideshow.

Under the augmentation of the wooden sword's phantom, Li Fan quickly arrived outside the Mystic Immortal Boat.

"The Tri-pronged Tree is on the second level of the Immortal Boat's secret treasury, guarded by the Heavenly Star Light Lotus. If I forcibly take it, I will inevitably clash with the Immortal Boat head-on..."

"Let's see the current situation inside the Immortal Boat first."

Thinking thus, Li Fan, like a ghost, silently infiltrated the Mystic Immortal Boat.

Compared to more than ten years ago, the defensive measures had improved somewhat. But not too much. At least for Li Fan, they were still like empty props.

After investigating within the Immortal Boat, Li Fan basically understood the current situation.

Since the last time he plundered the Immortal Boat's secret treasury, taking away most of the useful treasures from the first level of the Hundred Tales Immortal Record.

The Immortal Boat first went through an internal strife, narrowly splitting.

After the turmoil finally subsided, the high-pressure atmosphere within the Immortal Boat had not eased. Because of the immense loss of resources, the survival of the Immortal Boat's people became a major issue. Even though the population had decreased after the internal strife, they were still living in great hardship.

The scarcity of resources did not eliminate the conflict between the Duan Immortal Tower and the Immortal Axis Institute; on the contrary, the struggle between them became more intense. Although no elders died, many disciples perished.

In the previous life, due to Li Fan's sudden appearance as an outsider, the internal conflict of the Immortal Boat was redirected. Facing the fact that there were still other civilizations in the starry sea, the Immortal Boat appeared extremely united. In fact, most elders were willing to sacrifice their lives for the future of the Immortal Boat.

But in this lifetime, without external factors redirecting attention, and even with internal conflicts intensifying, the Immortal Boat displayed the darkness of human nature, rather than the good. Of course, to Li Fan, "good" and "evil" made no difference. He only cared about the treasures in the Immortal Boat's secret treasury.

The treasures on the second level of the secret treasury were all preserved within the lotus seeds of the Heavenly Star Light Lotus. The Heavenly Star Light Lotus was a strange treasure collected by the Immortal Boat since ancient times. It parasitized the starry sea, having survived countless calamities and still possessing life. With Li Fan's current strength, destroying it would not be difficult. However, to destroy it while simultaneously retrieving the treasures stored in nearly a hundred lotus seeds... was quite difficult.

Li Fan hid in the second level and observed the Heavenly Star Light Lotus from close proximity for a long time, finally determining a strategy to overcome it. Although the Heavenly Star Light Lotus appeared incredibly divine, at its peak, its本体 alone was larger than a hundred cultivation realms combined. But it was still within the category of "living beings." Since it was alive, it must have its weaknesses. Li Fan did not need to find the weakness himself. Li Fan had the Dao One Worm.

The Dao One Worm was a peculiar symbiotic beast capable of generating spiritual energy. Extending his hand, a vague shadow slowly approached, attempting to invade the dreamy colors of the light lotus. Li Fan released a variant of the Dao One Worm this time. Its ability to produce spiritual energy was halved, but in exchange, its adaptability and survival capabilities became astonishingly strong. However, the moment it got close, the faint light emitted by the Heavenly Star Light Lotus evaporated the Dao One Worm without a trace.

Li Fan was unconcerned and released two more Dao One Worms. Their fate remained unchanged. Compared to the Heavenly Star Light Lotus, the Dao One Worm was too insignificant. The demise of their lives did not cause any ripples. Li Fan relentlessly released four more Dao One Worms at once. Although they vanished in an instant, Li Fan alone noticed that the Dao One Worms lasted a fraction longer. The successive Dao One Worms did not die in vain; they fed back information about the Heavenly Star Light Lotus to the swarm. The subsequent ones would then alter themselves based on this information, seeking to adapt and survive within the radiance of the Heavenly Star Light Lotus.

The number of Dao One Worms grew exponentially. When the entire swarm reached one million, the Dao One Worms were able to evolve and merge themselves into the dreamlike radiance of the Heavenly Star Light Lotus.

"It seems that although it has developed self-awareness, this creation of the starry sea has not escaped the scope of spiritual energy after all. After tens of millions of generations of evolution, the Dao One Worm can complete its analysis." Li Fan nodded with some satisfaction, watching the continuous shadows of ink-like substances invading the Heavenly Star Light Lotus.

"Perhaps, only celestial spiritual energy, a power that completely transcends and belongs to a different category, can completely prevent the erosion of the Dao One Worm." The efficacy of the Dao One Worm was undeniable. It could create spiritual energy from nothing, and even invade and replace entire cave-heavens and worlds with its swarm. However, as Li Fan's strength grew, the infinitely useful Dao One Worm gradually became redundant. It was only in special circumstances like this that it could be deployed. Li Fan had once considered cultivating a more advanced Dao One Worm.

Unfortunately, after being infused with Source Energy essence, the Dao One Worm lost its original characteristics. And the next level up, celestial spiritual energy... Li Fan himself did not possess it and had to rely on the legacy of the Great Celestial Venerate.

"When I merge with the Dao, perhaps I can provide the Dao One Worm with a suitable breeding environment." Besides True Immortals, the Immortal Realm also had countless creations and servants. Li Fan believed that after achieving enlightenment, he could bring his followers along. The erosion of the Dao One Worm was like spring rain, silently nourishing everything. When the entire lotus seed was quietly transformed into Dao One Worms, the Heavenly Star Light Lotus itself did not notice. It only vaguely sensed an unease, its lotus-like radiance flickering unstably.

The protection of the lotus seed was completely removed. Li Fan first obtained the Tri-pronged Tree, his primary target. Sensing the reaction from the Still True, Li Fan's heart stirred: "It's still effective." "However, it's not enough to support an entire lifetime of simulation." "Only twelve hours?" Li Fan's eyes flashed, feeling a rare surge of excitement in his heart. "If my guess is correct, after simulating with the Tri-pronged Tree, my life won't end directly." "Instead, everything that happens in the next twelve hours of the simulation will appear in my mind, as if I personally experienced it." "I just don't know if I can bring back any gains?" "Even if not, this is equivalent to a life-saving insurance!" Li Fan suppressed the urge to use the Tri-pronged Tree immediately. He continued to manipulate the Dao One Worms, eroding and stealing the items preserved within the Heavenly Star Light Lotus seeds. As expected of a Star Sea treasure entrusted with important tasks by the Immortal Boat. When Li Fan consecutively stole three items, driven by instinct, the Heavenly Star Light Lotus spontaneously curled up. The second level of the secret treasury instantly turned dark, its dreamy radiance extinguished. Even Li Fan could no longer sense the aura of the Heavenly Star Light Lotus, as if it had completely vanished! The anomaly of the Heavenly Star Light Lotus also alerted the Immortal Boat's crew. Li Fan vaguely sensed several familiar auras rapidly approaching, namely the Immortal Boat elders led by Jian Dao Sheng and Zhong Dao Gong. "There's still the aura of the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God." "It seems that prolonged internal strife has kept their nerves perpetually taut." Li Fan smiled slightly, and under the flash of the dim sword phantom, he escaped the scene of the crime. Treasures in the second level of the secret treasury were stolen again, causing another bloody storm in the Immortal Boat. The Duan Immortal Tower and the Immortal Axis Institute accused each other, igniting the conflicts accumulated over a decade. Fierce battles unfolded within the Mystic Immortal Boat. At this moment, the instigator Li Fan had already returned to the Great Xuan small world within the Xuanhuang Realm. Besides the Tri-pronged Tree, the other two items Li Fan took were the Small Medicine King Cauldron and the Broken-winged Gray Bird. These three items were all relics of Sun Piaomiao. The treasures in the second level of the secret treasury were all concealed by the Heavenly Star Light Lotus, their specific effects unobservable. As for the actual value of these three items, except for the Broken-winged Gray Bird, their effects were verified in his previous life. It was a rational choice to take them out within the limited time. "The Tri-pronged Tree and the Small Medicine King Cauldron are both extraordinary items." "The Broken-winged Gray Bird likely holds hidden uses, although I haven't discovered them yet." Li Fan planned to use the Tri-pronged Tree for further deduction at the critical moment before merging with the Dao. As for the Small Medicine King Cauldron, Li Fan still intended to feed it to the little Qilin, if it could still eat it. Li Fan's attention was now focused on the Broken-winged Gray Bird. In his previous life, Li Fan and the people on the Immortal Boat had tried many methods but found no special properties in this item; it seemed to be an ordinary object. Li Fan observed it for a short while but found nothing unusual. Therefore, he adopted the simplest and most brutal method. Extending his palm, within a small area, the World Destroying Immortal Formation enveloped it. Like sharp blades, they hacked at the Broken-winged Gray Bird. To Li Fan's surprise, almost instantly, the Broken-winged Gray Bird vanished into nothingness under the power of the Immortal Formation. It completely disappeared from the world. This caught Li Fan, who had prepared himself, somewhat off guard. "Could it be that it was just a trick left by Sun Piaomiao?" Li Fan carefully observed the space in front of him, confirming that no fragments remained. The Broken-winged Gray Bird had vanished. "It seems I was overthinking it." Li Fan chuckled self-mockingly. But moments later, his expression suddenly changed. A faint ethereal voice suddenly came from beyond the heavens!

Chapter 1398: Finger Flicking High Wall

Li Fan did not have time to react, and the voice appeared clearly in his mind.

It seemed to have precisely locked onto Li Fan.

Then it quickly faded, like snow melting into water, leaving no trace.

Only after all this happened did Li Fan's body begin to stiffen slightly, and his breath caught.

He looked around, observing vigilantly.

Staring at the [True Return] interface that had been exhaled before him, after a long while, Li Fan let out a long sigh and silently closed it.

"Fortunately, it was just a false alarm!"

"The target of the transmission seemed to be just the person who destroyed this bronze immortal crane."

"But this transmission..."

"It seems to have come from outside the High Wall?!" Li Fan was filled with suspicion and uncertainty.

Narrowing his eyes, he carefully recalled the voice he had just heard.

"Tianluo Era, 213th year. Starting with Shangzhang Dayuanxian, Zuò'è Èrpéng, ending with Yānmào Xuánmào..."

"..."

"What does this mean?" Li Fan frowned tightly.

It seemed to be just a chaotic jumble of words, without any practical meaning.

But given that the transmission crossed the High Wall and had a clear target.

There must be a deep meaning behind it.

"It seems to be a designation for a certain year."

"But it is compounded again. What does that mean?"

"Could it be the unique dating method of the Immortal Realm?"

Li Fan pondered for a long time but could not figure it out.

The concepts involved in this transmission were something Li Fan had never encountered in his previous reincarnations.

"This transmission was triggered only after destroying the bronze immortal crane."

"The bronze immortal crane was kept together with the Immortal Realm chess pieces..."

"Perhaps it is important information left by Sun Piaomiao for the person who will complete the reconstruction of the Immortal Realm."

Li Fan could only guess at this point.

There was simply too little related information; further speculation was useless. Li Fan had no choice but to firmly memorize this message.

What Li Fan was more concerned about now was the meaning of this transmission coming from outside the wall.

"Sun Piaomiao disappeared without a trace later because he was already outside the wall?"

"At the time of his disappearance, the Great Tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction had not yet occurred, and the High Wall did not exist. Later, the formless High Wall rose up, encircling the Star Sea, and Sun Piaomiao never returned..."

"What exactly does the High Wall signify?" Li Fan's thoughts raced.

This transmission from outside the High Wall reignited his strong interest in this unknown realm.

"No matter what, the Immortal Realm left by Sun Piaomiao must be an important clue."

"My current strength is insufficient to explore it."

"Achieve Dao Integration! Ascend to the Immortal Realm!"

As Li Fan continued to explore, the more he encountered, the more he felt endless mysteries and unknowns.

His desire to become stronger became unprecedentedly intense.

...

In the Xuanhuang Realm, time flowed second by second.

The Great Celestial Venerable, Nameless, remained ignorant. Following the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's self-operation, it continuously repaired the damages accumulated over millennia.

Coupled with Li Fan's continuous secret nourishment through various methods.

Three years passed, and the Xuanhuang Realm had become immensely prosperous to its limits.

It had reached the critical point where a quantitative change catalyzed a qualitative one.

The beings in the entire world, even those within the illusion formation, were still infected by this grand momentum naturally born between heaven and earth, filled with anticipation and endless fear.

The three-year period had arrived.

Li Fan sensed that the restriction on the Nameless One had begun to dissipate on its own.

The true Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang, after an empty millennium, reappeared in the world!

As if a heavy invisible weight was suddenly placed on his shoulders.

This was the might and authority originating from the Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang!

Sensing the restraint on his body, Li Fan frowned slightly. This situation was not within his expectations, but after careful consideration, Li Fan quickly felt relieved.

The Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang was appointed by the Immortal Realm, in charge of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao and all sentient beings in the world.

Although it had been empty for millennia since Mr. Bai, its position still existed.

The Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable spread the new law of devouring heaven and earth to all beings. From absorbing the spiritual energy of heaven and earth to reversing the principles of heaven and earth, the higher the cultivation realm, the deeper the connection with the world.

Up to the present day, cultivators of the new law and the Xuanhuang Realm had become inseparable, becoming a part of heaven and earth.

The Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth must strictly obey the Great Celestial Venerable's commands and could not disobey.

This also led to the situation where, when the new Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang appeared, all cultivators practicing the new law also felt the power of this restraint.

However, conversely, although cultivators were a part of heaven and earth. The overall strength of Xuanhuang Realm cultivators was too great. Even without considering the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable above all beings, the remaining cultivators combined would not be much weaker than the Xuanhuang Realm.

The restrictions from the ancient era of the Xuanhuang Realm, although they could affect cultivators.

Their effect was limited.

"This is what is called the 'balance of power.' There are no fixed rules. The strong rule the weak, and the weak cannot rule."

The burden on his shoulders was even lighter than that of a chess piece carrying fragments of the Immortal Realm. For Li Fan, it did not affect his actions at all.

"However, with such drastic changes in the Xuanhuang Realm, it cannot be concealed from the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable and the Heavenly Physician. They will definitely return to the Xuanhuang Realm immediately."

"Fortunately, during these three years, I have also made thorough preparations."

Li Fan's gaze turned towards the outside of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Golden threads enveloped the boundary of the Xuanhuang Realm's sky, like a formless high wall, separating the Xuanhuang Realm from the outer void!

Within the condensed golden light, countless different fleeting images seemed to evolve incessantly.

Li Fan looked at his meticulously prepared creation with great satisfaction.

"The improved Great Xuanhuang Beings Formation. Plus the imitation formless High Wall..."

"And most importantly, the deterrent of the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone!"

"With the support of the boundless Star Sea power, trapping the Heavenly Physician and the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable for a period of time is not a problem!"

In his previous life, the Heavenly Physician was able to break free so quickly.

It was because Li Fan was, after all, only at the mortal realm, and the immortal formation was only operating and lowered in grade using Origin Energy Essence. It could not truly simulate the might of an "immortal."

Therefore, when the Heavenly Physician vaguely sensed something within the illusion formation and chose to confront the True Immortal directly, the immense gap caused him to immediately discover the flaw in the formation.

But this lifetime was different.

Li Fan connected the core of the formation with the leg bone of the Nameless True Immortal.

Even though it was just a remnant bone of a deceased Nameless True Immortal, the faint aura it emitted was not much weaker than that of a True Immortal!

The performance of the Star Sea Hungry Immortal appearing simultaneously with the Southern Immortal Pillar in the previous life confirmed this point.

An aura suppression comparable to that of a True Immortal would mean that the Heavenly Physician would certainly not seek death without reason.

If he still insisted on trying...

Even at the Grand Supreme realm, he could only turn into a character on the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone without any resistance!

It could be said that the Great Xuanhuang Beings Formation, overseen by the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone, had also undergone a qualitative transformation to some extent. It was not an iterative improvement of the formation itself, but a sublimation brought about by the extraordinary nature of the formation materials!

This was only Li Fan's first layer of defense.

In addition to the illusion formation, Li Fan also used the technique of drawing a circle on the ground to create a prison, erecting another layer of a High Wall outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

This High Wall, although incomparable to the formless High Wall that encircled the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

It was still an imitation created through the insights of Mo Rubin into the flaws of the High Wall in his previous life, and the contemplation of countless beings towards the High Wall in this lifetime. Then, after Li Fan's improvement.

Li Fan had personally experimented.

To surpass this wall, even without needing the True Immortal realm, one's momentum needed to reach the critical point of ninety-nine percent.

Without a large amount of True Immortal flesh and blood as fuel, and without the assistance of ascension formations.

With their current realm alone, the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable and the Heavenly Physician could not cross the High Wall in a short time!

"My High Wall, although it appears to be separated from the true formless High Wall by just a sliver."

"That slight difference translates into a world of difference."

"The Heavenly Physician's strength, the Grand Supreme realm at the limit of the Star Sea, is truly not to be underestimated. I also cannot expect this High Wall to hold them back for too long."

"I still have a third method!"

Li Fan's gaze retracted from the sky.

He looked towards various parts of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Once the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm begins, the various qualitative changes within it can serve as my weapons. The Super Immortal-Mortal Miasma, countless Heavenly and Earth Immortal Souls..."

"As long as I do not show any intention of refining Mo Sha, they can all be used by me! After all, I am the greatest benefactor promoting Xuanhuang's ascension to the Immortal Domain. If successful, I can certainly be called the reborn parent of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"The power of the Immortal Domain's laws should be sufficient to counter the Awakened Hungry Immortal."

"Everything is ready, it is time to begin."

Li Fan sneered inwardly.

His gaze then locked onto the Great Celestial Venerable, Nameless.

Since the test restriction three years prior was lifted, Nameless had entered a state of stillness.

As if formally accepting the position of Great Celestial Venerable.

However, his characteristic of being ignorant and unknowing made his expression very indifferent, without joy or sorrow.

The decree from the Immortal Realm no longer existed. Now, the Great Celestial Venerable's every action was based on the highest interests of the Xuanhuang Realm.

In the current situation, using the Immortal Spiritual Energy from the Great Celestial Venerable's legacy to help Xuanhuang Realm sublimate became an inevitable choice.

Under the urgent urging of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, a large amount of Immortal Spiritual Energy rapidly surged from Nameless.

Like a raging fire boiling oil, it propelled the Xuanhuang Realm into the final path of sublimation.

Either ascend to the Immortal Domain successfully, or be utterly destroyed and turn into dust!

With the thorough preparations made by Li Fan, if there were no external interference, success was almost certain.

Therefore, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao did not hesitate at all.

Amidst rising winds and surging clouds, it blew and dispersed the Immortal Spiritual Energy to every corner of the heaven and earth.

Even though it was not the first time Li Fan had seen true Immortal Spiritual Energy, he was still deeply intoxicated by this extremely wondrous and mysterious power.

Even if Immortal Spiritual Energy appeared before him, Li Fan still could not understand its form of existence.

Let alone utilize it.

Perhaps, as Li Fan had predicted, only by ascending to the Immortal Realm, even if only half-immortal, could one wield this transcendent power.

But just because Li Fan could not use it did not mean that other objects around him could not.

"Dissolution Disc! Little 'bá'!"

Li Fan thought, and two balls of light appeared on his shoulders, one on the left and one on the right.

The Ultimate Dissolution Disc had accompanied Li Fan throughout his growth. Its characteristic of infinitely deducing formations had greatly assisted Li Fan. For a long time, the formations deduced by the Dissolution Disc were Li Fan's strongest trump cards.

However, it was ultimately a mortal creation. Limited by its innate material, the Ultimate Dissolution Disc had reached its limit long ago. Even though Li Fan constantly fed it immortal formation data, it had only achieved theoretical breakthroughs between immortal and mortal. It could smoothly deduce immortal formations, but in reality, it could only substitute them by downgrading immortal formations.

And now, sensing the pervasive Immortal Spiritual Energy between heaven and earth, the Ultimate Dissolution Disc trembled uncontrollably. It was like a cultivator seeing the essence of heaven and earth, filled with greed and desire.

The situation with the Little 'bá' beast was similar to that of the Dissolution Disc.

This little creature's appetite was truly terrifying. After devouring four Immortal Realm chess pieces in a row, it finally stopped eating.

But it seemed to have eaten to its fill. The 'bá' beast, however, did not undergo metamorphosis and evolution. It only fell into a deep slumber for a long time.

After some investigation and brief communication with the 'bá' beast, Li Fan speculated that the Immortal Realm chess pieces it swallowed were only fragments of laws. This kind of unhealthily processed food caused the 'bá' beast to have indigestion. It needed pure Immortal Spiritual Energy as a catalyst to aid digestion.

Both of them were on the verge of a breakthrough.

Yet, they needed the addition of Immortal Spiritual Energy to undergo a qualitative change!

The Immortal Spiritual Energy pervading heaven and earth grew increasingly dense.

The greed of the Dissolution Disc and the Little 'bá' beast grew even stronger, almost uncontrollable, threatening to break free from Li Fan.

However, through Li Fan's communication and assurances, even though it was somewhat reluctant, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao still detached two extremely small but absolutely pure wisps of Immortal Spiritual Energy.

It transported them to Li Fan's side.

The moment Li Fan received the Immortal Spiritual Energy from the Great Celestial Venerable's legacy, he sensed that the Xuanhuang Realm's favorability towards him had dropped significantly.

He snorted coldly, temporarily ignoring it. Li Fan suppressed his urge to investigate further and separately infused these two wisps of Immortal Spiritual Energy into the Dissolution Disc and the Little 'bá' beast.

Brilliant, crystalline light gradually enveloped the two objects.

Even Li Fan, their master, lost the ability to sense them.

Furthermore, the surge of might emanating from the two light clusters forced him to retreat.

The two immortal artifacts seemed to be in the process of formation.

Li Fan also sensed that the interception formation he had set up in the center of the Star Sea had been triggered.

Chapter 1399: Turning the Tide

In the heaven and earth of the Xuanhuang Realm, countless viscous, multicolored liquids instantly materialized out of thin air. They then flowed like trickling streams into the cracks, irrigating them.

Like legendary immortal pills and marvelous medicines, the torn cracks in the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth instantly healed.

Moreover, a considerable amount of multicolored fluid scattered in the air and flowed across the land.

The areas touched and illuminated by these multicolored streams gradually formed a ring of colorful light. A trace of sacred aura emerged from them, existing independently of the world, and incompatible with the surrounding ordinary realms.

Li Fan continuously formed hand seals, maintaining the Xuanhuang Realm's ascension momentum. His eyes, however, narrowed as he surveyed the various light rings and realms that had suddenly appeared throughout the heaven and earth.

To concentrate all power to the greatest extent and promote Xuanhuang's ascension, Li Fan had already destroyed or merged most of the grotto-heavens and small worlds that were a burden, all returning to Xuanhuang.

And now, as Xuanhuang Realm was on the verge of transformation, new grotto-heavens and blessed lands were forming, slightly slowing down Xuanhuang's ascension.

These newly formed grotto-heavens and blessed lands were different from those of the old era. They were not independent entities that separated after blooming and bearing fruit. They were more like new "organs" evolved by heaven and earth!

Li Fan's gaze penetrated the protective light rings of these grotto-heavens and blessed lands, melihat the unique powers of law within each, which were profoundly mysterious.

For example, one nascent grotto-heaven gathered and evolved laws related to "seeing." Li Fan judged that if beings were to be born in this grotto-heaven in the future, or cultivate there for many years, under the influence of the grotto-heaven's unique laws, they would very likely awaken related divine abilities.

There were also a very small number of grotto-heavens that, after a brief appearance in the world, transformed into a rainbow light, chose a target, and directly merged into the sentient beings below. These selected fortunate beings were not the sleepers in the illusion formation, but newly born life forms since the Xuanhuang Realm's mutation. The grotto-heavens thus moved across the land from top to bottom!

The grotto-heavens and blessed lands were not isolated from each other. They were faintly interconnected. Some were close to each other, while others were naturally antagonistic.

But by sensing the underlying connection between them, Li Fan realized that their ultimate destiny was to devour each other and then unify.

Finally, the grotto-heaven and blessed land that unified everything, accumulating the strengths of all, nurturing to the extreme. Then, it would separate from the Xuanhuang Realm.

This process, which might normally take tens of millions, or even hundreds of millions of years to evolve on its own, would still occur, even if it went against Xuanhuang Realm's own will.

"Is this a necessary path for ascending to the Immortal Realm? Embedded in Xuanhuang Realm's fundamental logic?" Li Fan watched as strange and varied grotto-heavens and blessed lands suddenly descended within the Xuanhuang Realm, and a glimmer of enlightenment suddenly emerged in his mind.

This was a change that would only occur when Xuanhuang Realm was pushed to the brink of sublimation and was truly about to ascend to the Immortal Realm.

From the very beginning of Xuanhuang Realm's creation, it had been written into its foundation. Even though Xuanhuang Realm had always existed as a lower-realm Star Sea, an ordinary cultivation world. But when it was about to return to the Immortal Realm, this long-hidden "innate characteristic" finally manifested.

"Xuanhuang Realm was created using methods of forging the Immortal Realm, with materials from the lower realms. In other words, it can be considered a downgraded version of the Immortal Realm to some extent..." Li Fan thought of his method of using Origin Energy Essence to replace Immortal Spiritual Energy and operate immortal formations, his eyes flickering uncertainly.

"Although Xuanhuang Realm possesses the inherent characteristics of 'immortality,' it is limited by its mortal body. Its actual performance is no different from other ordinary cultivation worlds. Only True Immortals can clearly see the clues within."

"No wonder Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao has such a hateful personality. It turns out it was a fallen princess wandering among the common people. No matter how well you treat her, as long as there is the slightest deviation from her will, she will immediately put on a]dark face, and might turn against you at any time. And even if you treated her well before, the moment a new strong being comes to show concern, she is likely to immediately switch allegiance..."

Recalling the interactions Li Fan had with Mr. Bai, the Sacred Master, and Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, Li Fan gradually understood.

At its core, it was due to Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's inherent arrogance. Even ants, no matter how good you were to them, were still ants. They might change their attitude based on their current circumstances, but their innermost thoughts would never change.

Only Immortals, even if only half-immortals, might be able to make Xuanhuang Realm take them seriously.

These innate characteristics of the Xuanhuang Realm caused new changes to suddenly occur at the critical moment of sublimation and ascension.

Li Fan let out a soft snort, observing with a cold eye: "You don't have the 'fate' of a princess, but you have the 'air' of a princess!"

Various strange phenomena unfolded in the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth.

Li Fan committed this dreamlike scene to memory. Then, his gaze was involuntarily drawn to a desolate, isolated blank area in the world that showed no changes.

Yuandao Prefecture!

The illusory Xuanhuang Beings Grand Formation had not covered Yuandao Prefecture, but it had been enveloped by it. The power of the immortal formation had spread, isolating it from the outside world. Later, Li Fan even built a wall around the borders of Yuandao Prefecture, completely sealing off the prefecture.

Naturally, this was to prevent the Great Law Master from suddenly appearing and causing trouble at the critical final moment of sublimation.

In fact, besides the immortal formation and the wall, Li Fan had also meticulously prepared additional surprises for the Great Law Master.

On the border of Yuandao Prefecture, eighteen bronze figures were hidden and stood within the illusory Immortal Formation. Only Li Fan, the creator of these bronze figures, could see the two terrifying killing intents hidden within them.

The Annihilation Wind Tribulation, and the Decaying Greenery.

The Annihilation Wind Tribulation was collected by Li Fan from damaged immortal artifacts in the Xuanhuang Realm. As long as immortal artifacts remained in the world, they would more or less contain something similar to the Infinite Mirror.

As for the Decaying Greenery, it was initially discovered by Li Fan on the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God. It burned the foundation of life for things, and its destructive power was no less than the Annihilation Wind Tribulation.

The Annihilation Wind Tribulation was a special evolution of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation towards immortal artifacts. The Decaying Greenery, however, was a special attack against immortal servants!

Two years ago, the Immortal Boat, which was constantly in internal conflict, gradually descended into madness. The Immortal Shaft Institute, which was in a disadvantageous position and on the verge of being cornered, finally chose to fight desperately and released the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God. The Desolate God wreaked havoc, and Li Fan also sensed the strange aura from this creation of the Immortal Realm. He sent Tian Yang to fight it and gain insights.

Tian Yang did indeed gain some understanding. At the same time, with the substantial support of True Immortal flesh and blood provided by Li Fan, he successfully brought back the corrosive Decaying Greenery that had attached itself.

Li Fan used True Immortal flesh and blood as a breeding ground to cultivate a large amount of Decaying Greenery.

Although the Annihilation Wind Tribulation and the Decaying Greenery were already terrifying calamities for mortals, their destructive effects on beings at the "Immortal" realm were even more significant!
