In the previous life, facing the Annihilation Wind Tribulation. The Sacred Emperor and the Heavenly Physician only felt dread but still made efforts to stop it. As for the Great Law Master, he panicked and fled directly. Judging from the Great Law Master's performance, his fear of the Annihilation Wind Tribulation was evident.

Coupled with the Decaying Greenery...

"Let me see what this Great Law Master is made of."

The mutation of the Xuanhuang Realm gradually calmed down.

Besides evolving numerous grotto-heavens and blessed lands, four great mountains also rose in the four corners of the world.

Among them, the highest peak of the mountain range towered majestically, like a celestial pillar, piercing the clouds.

The four magnificent mountain ranges guarded the Xuanhuang Realm. After they appeared and stabilized, the heaven and earth, which had been trembling due to being at the point of sublimation, seemed to have found support and stabilized on their own!

"Are these the Immortal Heavenly Pillars corresponding to the Immortal Realm?" Li Fan looked at the four mountain peaks, lost in thought.

The various changes within the world seemed to have stirred the ancient memories of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. Li Fan, without actively probing, could vaguely sense its extreme excitement.

At its prompting, the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable, having already released all its Immortal Spiritual Energy, made another move.

The Nameless One extended his left hand, and a golden, dazzling small bell slowly appeared. A strong wind swept through the heaven and earth, slowly lifting this golden bell, ascending into the nine heavens.

As its altitude increased, the golden bell's brilliance grew brighter and brighter. When it reached the sky, level with the sun, the dazzling radiance emitted by the golden bell even enveloped the sun!

"Buzz..."

A crisp bell chime echoed through heaven and earth. The light suddenly contracted, and the Xuanhuang Realm plunged into brief darkness. When the light reappeared, there was only one sun in the sky again, and...

It was not the same as before.

"Great Sun Golden Bell!" Li Fan's eyes suddenly contracted as he recognized the immortal artifact that had replaced the sun in the Xuanhuang Realm's sky.

The Golden Bell transformed into the sun. At this moment, all living beings in the Xuanhuang Realm felt a sense of unease, as if a sword of Damocles was suspended above their heads, ready to fall at any moment.

At the same time, Li Fan felt the "burden" on his shoulders, generated by the appearance of the true Great Celestial Venerable, increase even further.

When he saw that the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable had completed the Golden Bell transformation and was still continuing his actions, Li Fan's expression gradually became solemn.

The second immortal artifact taken out by the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable was a seemingly ordinary round disk.

The moment it left Nameless's hand, it transformed into five colors – white, green, black, red, and yellow – and rapidly surged towards all parts of the heaven and earth, like Immortal Spiritual Energy.

The colors within the Xuanhuang Realm thus became more vibrant. A unique vitality began to emerge, and life began to gestate. In addition to these five colors, Li Fan inexplicably sensed another formless and intangible special power permeating from the round disk towards all parts of the Xuanhuang Realm.

The illusory formation Li Fan had meticulously set up, like a cage, firmly bound the Xuanhuang Realm. Because of the impact of this inexplicable force, it actually loosened somewhat.

Conversely, the burden on Li Fan's shoulders grew even heavier.

"Primordial Five Elements Wheel!" Li Fan squinted his eyes but did not stop Nameless's actions.

When the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable took out the third immortal artifact, Li Fan's ears suddenly heard the sound of a baby crying urgently!

Li Fan instantly recognized the source of the sound.

It was the Carefree Celestial Venerable.

He let out a cold laugh and ignored it. Li Fan waved his hand, dispelling the sound.

Li Fan naturally knew why Carefree, who had been hiding and playing the coward all this time, would appear at this moment.

The power of the Xuanhuang Realm and its cultivators were in a relationship of mutual decline and rise.

Previously, because the overall strength of Xuanhuang Realm cultivators far surpassed that of the Xuanhuang Realm itself. So, even though the true Great Celestial Venerable descended, its impact on the world's cultivators was minimal.

But now, as the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable continuously integrated immortal artifacts into the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth, constantly increasing the stakes, the cultivators had gradually fallen into a disadvantage.

This was because: the weight of one immortal artifact was greater than that of billions of sentient beings!

Even though the immortal artifacts were used countless times and their Immortal Spiritual Energy was nearly depleted, they still exerted such influence.

However, without a doubt, the integration of immortal artifacts brought only benefits, not drawbacks, to Xuanhuang Realm's formal ascension. Therefore, Li Fan continued to allow Nameless to proceed.

At this moment, the third immortal artifact dissolved into heaven and earth, it was the Tai Xu Qing Ming Lamp.

The illusory flames flickered unstably. The flickering frequency gradually increased, finally appearing completely still. At this instant, Li Fan saw the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth also flash. Then the flames gradually extinguished, and the Tai Xu Qing Ming Lamp transformed into specks of lingering embers, scattering with the wind.

"This is..."

Another layer of immortal artifact power was added.

The moment this restriction was generated, Li Fan's figure, standing in the void, uncontrollably sank slightly.

Li Fan paid no mind, relaxing his body, and looked up towards the heavens.

As the Tai Xu Qing Ming Lamp's flames extinguished, or rather, merged into the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan clearly sensed that the suction from the Immortal Ruins had been weakened to a certain extent.

Not only the suction from the Immortal Ruins, but also the effect of the illusory formation acting upon the Xuanhuang Realm was further reduced.

The ascending Xuanhuang Realm seemed like a ferocious beast, slowly breaking free from Li Fan's control.

When the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable took out the last immortal artifact, the Purple Qi Woven Dream Shuttle, Li Fan's ears once again heard the crying of the Carefree Celestial Venerable. However, this time the voice was much weaker than before. It seemed that the impact on cultivators of the Reverse Dao Longevity were far greater than on Li Fan.

Not only in reality, but also in the Carefree Dreamscape, all the cultivators Li Fan had secretly dispatched to explore the dreamscape heard the same voice. Only Hou Mingwu, who had delved into the 8th level of the dream world, was spared.

Li Fan's expression stirred, and after pondering for a moment, he finally began to communicate with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

"Too much is as bad as too little. The nourishment from three immortal artifacts is already sufficient."

"The last one can be left to the Great Celestial Venerable for protection."

"Ascension is imminent, there is no time to digest it."

...

Li Fan appealed to his emotions and reasoned with him.

The Xuanhuang Realm, which was in a state of extreme desire after devouring three immortal artifacts, hesitated at Li Fan's suggestion.

However, the journey of ascension to immortality was like rowing against the current; not progressing meant regressing. In that moment of hesitation, the Xuanhuang Realm's momentum of ascension showed signs of slowly descending.

The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao was instantly jolted awake.

It made the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable stop sacrificing immortal artifacts.

The noisy crying sound in Li Fan's ears also disappeared with the end of Nameless's task.

Nameless's task was complete, and now it was Li Fan's turn to act.

Li Fan had already rehearsed the sublimation process with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao beforehand. Li Fan bowed slightly towards the Xuanhuang sky.

A jade token representing the imperial decree appeared in his hand.

This Imperial Edict Jade Token represented the will of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

Holding the jade token, one could freely command all the power within the Xuanhuang Realm, just like the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

Instead of Li Fan having to pretend to act according to destiny.

Li Fan took a step forward, his figure stretching infinitely upwards against the wind. Within a few breaths, he transformed into a giant that reached the heavens.

He also donned a mysterious black and gold robe, his head adorned with a crown, sparkling with starlight, obscuring Li Fan's facial expression.

Li Fan held the Imperial Edict Jade Token with both hands and gently drew it across the Xuanhuang land below.

The earth rumbled, and mountains trembled.

The areas Li Fan passed through instantly had their spiritual energy boiled and vaporized. A colossal vacuum zone was formed.

Then, with the cooperation of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, the remaining Immortal Spiritual Energy in the world was channeled by the surrounding spiritual energy into this vacuum depression.

Li Fan, using the method of "Heavenly Law and Earthly Manifestation," wrote upon the Xuanhuang Realm with the Imperial Edict Jade Token as his brush: [Creation]!

Although his current cultivation realm was insufficient to mobilize Immortal Spiritual Energy. However, by creating special zones in this manner, Immortal Spiritual Energy could be induced to enter them voluntarily.

This was the most massive True Immortal character script Li Fan had ever written.

And it was only possible to write it by leveraging the power of the super Xuanhuang Realm at the brink of sublimation.

If he relied solely on his own strength, even with the Five Elements Great Grotto-Heaven and the Xuanhuang World Destruction Transformations as his foundation, he would be instantly drained.

But now, the life force from the Star Sea's ground fissure depressions was continuously being extracted.

The Supreme Autumn Water transformed into a blue sword phantom, traversing throughout the Xuanhuang Realm, evenly infusing the boundless power of the Star Sea.

Coupled with the power of various elements previously absorbed by the Xuanhuang Realm but not yet fully digested, such as fragments of remnant realms.

At this moment, all were superimposed together, acting as fuel, igniting the [Creation] character script with a boom!

Creation unfolded within the Xuanhuang Realm.

The four great immortal pillars once again rose, reaching the heavens. The grotto-heavens and blessed lands overflowed with radiant light, their contained laws appearing even more sacred. The living beings on the earth, reaping the benefits; gaining without toil, their divine souls and physiques strengthened day by day...

Amidst the evolution of all sorts of auspicious phenomena, Xuanhuang's momentum of ascension continued to surge upwards, rocketing forward.

So-called creation was happening before their eyes.

Looking at the dramatic changes in the Xuanhuang Realm, which he had orchestrated, and recalling the various differences within Xuanhuang Realm before and after the changes.

And countless details of his communication with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao consciousness at each stage.

Li Fan's expression was slightly stunned.

"Is it Heaven, or Man?"

"Heaven and Man are indistinguishable."

"When Heaven achieves creation, Man can also achieve creation."

"Sitting still can lead to ascension, sitting in the heavens..."

"Can lead to immortality!"

Countless streams of light characters arranged and combined in Li Fan's mind, constantly changing.

Finally, they formed a dazzling cultivation technique.

Sit, Heaven, Art!

Ever since Li Fan evolved the Sit Mountain Art to the Sit Immortal Art, his primary cultivation technique had entered a state of extreme redundancy.

Because what was trapping Li Fan was no longer cultivation realm, but the bottleneck of major realms!

No matter how much cultivation he gained, if he couldn't overcome that hurdle, it was useless!

Therefore, Li Fan had almost forgotten about his primary cultivation technique. This had to be said to be a miraculous aspect of cultivation.

But at this moment, observing the Xuanhuang Realm's transformation and ascension driven by the power of creation, it naturally and effortlessly led to the evolution and perfection of the Sit Mountain Art to its next stage.

The Sit Heaven Art had long been within Li Fan's expectations. At this moment, witnessing the sacred scene and comprehending the divine technique, Li Fan's heart only had a slight ripple of emotion.

After all, for him, the improvement of realm was far more important than the improvement of cultivation. Having witnessed the infinite power of the Star Sea and mastered the Grand Heaven Divine Technique, as long as his realm increased, improving his cultivation would be as easy as flipping a hand.

Li Fan felt neither joy nor sorrow.

The Sit Heaven Art was a technique Li Fan had deduced himself, and he understood it thoroughly. It originated from the same source as the Sit Mountain Art. With a single thought, he had already cultivated it to perfection.

At this moment, as the Xuanhuang Realm surged forward on its path of ascending to the Immortal Domain, the feedback power from the Sit Heaven Art surged like rivers and oceans.

He was already at the peak of Deity Transformation, and the bottleneck had not yet been broken. The surplus cultivation could only be stored for now.

Phantoms of [Calamity Body] from the Supreme Sect appeared within Li Fan's body.

But now, Li Fan vaguely sensed a faint connection between these Calamity Bodies and someone in the Carefree Dreamscape.

"Even if I am willing to bring my chickens and dogs to ascension..."

"You are not among the chickens and dogs."

Li Fan shook his head slightly, his expression indifferent.

The Calamity Bodies in the Dantian shattered inch by inch. Then, under the pouring of seemingly endless feedback power, they transformed from Li Fan's phantom into the appearance of the Xuanhuang Realm!

Through countless reincarnations, Li Fan had, if not stripped the Xuanhuang Realm bare, then at least dug through it with a fine-tooth comb.

Every time the world was destroyed, everything in the Xuanhuang Realm was completely revealed to Li Fan.

In this world, if anyone understood the Xuanhuang Realm more than Li Fan, it would be no one.

Even the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao itself did not know about the methods Li Fan had deeply implanted within the Xuanhuang Realm.

When understanding reached a certain conceptual level.

With a mental rewrite, the phantom Xuanhuang Realm generated within Li Fan's Dantian became identical to the real Xuanhuang Realm!

Except for the absence of sentient beings within the phantom, every other detail could be matched one by one.

What surprised Li Fan even more was that the energy level of the world phantom generated by the feedback power was almost identical to the current Xuanhuang Realm!

In other words, within Li Fan's Dantian, the world phantom formed by the infusion of Xuanhuang's ascension feedback power could be considered another Xuanhuang Realm.

However, this Xuanhuang Realm was purely in the form of energy!

"This... how is this possible?"

"How can the feedback power be so great?"

Even as the creator of the cultivation technique, Li Fan was stunned by the scene before him.

But he was, after all, someone who had seen great things.

He quickly regained his composure, his expression not filled with joy, but gradually becoming solemn.

"The principle of the Sit Heaven Art is similar to the Sit Mountain Art. To sit and reap the rewards; as you progress, I progress too."

"Now that I have exhausted all my methods, and Xuanhuang Realm is only a hair's breadth away from its final qualitative change... It has been sublimating for so long, yet it has not achieved that slight qualitative change..."

"What exactly is needed to achieve this qualitative change?"

Instantly, countless schemes flashed through Li Fan's mind.

"The Immortal-Mortal Transformation characters? Or should I still use the Immortal Realm chess pieces? Or, based on the remnants of the ancient immortal formations, try to repair the Star Crossing Great Formation?"

Each attempt involved endless possibilities. Most existences related to "Immortal" were completely unknown variables, not something Li Fan could deduce now. Li Fan's head ached, but he could not choose the most suitable plan.

It seemed that each method could work, yet each method might also fail.

"Could it be that in this lifetime, I still cannot achieve Dao Integration and ascend to the Immortal Realm?"

"If all else fails, I will try each method one by one. There must be a correct path to ascend the world." Such a dejected thought quietly arose in Li Fan's heart.

Once this thought appeared, it was like a dike bursting, flooding thousands of miles. It completely destroyed Li Fan's psychological defense.

His thoughts became like a storm-ridden mind, chaotic and unceasing.

Li Fan stopped thinking about the conditions required for Xuanhuang's sublimation and ascension. Instead, he began to consider how to end this life and begin the next.

The plan was excellent.

But for some reason, Li Fan felt somewhat uneasy.

Theoretically, everything in the simulation could be reproduced through another simulation. For Li Fan, there was truly nothing that could be "lost" in the world.

Except for Li Fan's own changes.

Every time True Return activated the simulation and returned to the predetermined anchor. Everything in the world was reset.

Even Li Fan's physical strength and cultivation were the same. He needed to rely on True Return's inherited cultivation function to return to the state of the previous simulation.

However, within each reset, there was a variable that constantly moved forward.

That was Li Fan's will!

Specifically reflected on the True Return interface, it was Li Fan's maximum psychological age and the default True Return charging progress.

And these two factors had not changed for a long time...

Li Fan's heart was filled with unprecedented hesitation at this moment.

Time ticked by, and Li Fan could not make a final decision.

There were only ten hours left until Li Fan initiated Xuanhuang's ascension in the branching simulation of the Three-pronged Tree technique. Li Fan's expression was inscrutable. He took a step forward and arrived at the origin of everything.

The humble mortal body of Da Xuan, the house where he lived during his lifetime.

Even though "Li Fan" had mysteriously disappeared, the study remained spotless, just as it had always been. Clearly, that "aunt" still held some hope for "Li Fan's" return.

Li Fan lay on the bed and closed his eyes.

It was as if he had returned to the moment he first transmigrated.

Time seemed to freeze. Then, it flowed quietly, as if ice was breaking.

Having undergone a hundred lifetimes of reincarnation, all his experiences flashed through Li Fan's mind in an instant.

Li Fan attempted to find a way to break through the deadlock in this manner.

Day turned into night, and Li Fan lay quietly on the wooden bed.

It was as if he had fallen into a deep sleep.

Yes, Li Fan could indeed use repeated True Return simulations, and through elimination, determine one by one the key factors for achieving qualitative change.

This was also the most stable approach.

Theoretically, there were no problems.

But every time Li Fan decided to do so, inexplicable images would flash through his mind.

It was the persistence of Mo Rubin, who, despite the flaws in the High Wall, disregarded his own life to investigate; and the Heavenly Physician in the illusion formation, who ultimately gave up on comprehending the High Wall for the sake of the Heavenly Law Realm.

"Once lost is forever lost."

In the darkness, Li Fan's eyes suddenly opened.

He softly whispered these four words.

With True Return around, there was indeed nothing in the world that could be "forever lost" to him. Unless that item's rank was even higher than True Return.

Obviously, mere transformation from mortal to immortal was not enough to achieve that.

"True 'loss is forever loss' exists within my heart."

"True Return can influence everything in the world, but it cannot reverse my changes."

As if understanding something, Li Fan's gaze seemed to penetrate the darkness, gradually brightening.

"The loss of this unknown characteristic might not affect my advancement to the True Immortal realm. But for the path beyond True Immortal, it might have profound implications!"

After a long period of contemplation, as a ray of sunlight appeared on the earth, dispelling the darkness, Li Fan finally understood completely.

Where the unease in his heart originated.

"Why is it like this?"

"Is it due to over-reliance on [True Return]?"

"Or something else?"

"The path beyond True Immortal is too distant for me. Moreover, with my understanding, the Nameless True Immortal realm seems to only require complete mastery and refinement of a certain Great Dao. It doesn't seem related..." Li Fan frowned tightly, filled with confusion.

"But it seems I have no better option than exhaustive trials."

...

Li Fan walked out of the house, looking at the rising sun on the horizon.

While continuing to ponder, he stepped away from the Great Xuan Small World.

He paced around within the Xuanhuang Realm.

The surrounding scenery jumped and changed incessantly, as Li Fan's mind reflected everything around him.

Starting from the Sea of Eastern Clouds, heading west.

As his thoughts churned, the frequency of the surrounding scenery's changes seemed to accelerate.

Li Fan, immersed in a state of meditation akin to enlightenment, did not alter his outward output.

The reason he "walked" faster and faster.

It was precisely because of the special relationship between Li Fan and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. Like a reborn parent, its favorability was extremely high.

Therefore, without Li Fan's prompting, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao proactively helped Li Fan lighten the burden of travel.

Even though the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao did not know why Li Fan was randomly moving around the world inexplicably.

Perhaps it mistakenly believed that Li Fan was making final preparations for the sublimation and ascension.

Li Fan naturally noticed the favor shown by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

But he didn't pay much attention.

Previously, when the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable traveled throughout the land to repair various damages to the Xuanhuang Realm, the Xuanhuang Realm had also provided such convenience.

With one step, the distance between heaven and earth transformed, as if shrinking the ground into inches.

However, now that the anomalies in various places had been resolved, the Xuanhuang Realm had not actively done so for a long time.

"What a servant!" In the branching simulation, upon seeing the true face of the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan cursed inwardly.

"I possess supreme escape techniques, why would I need your rudimentary convenience?"

With a thought, the phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed and appeared at Li Fan's side.

Just as he was about to fly away, escape the entanglement of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, and seize the last moment to calmly ponder.

But Li Fan's movement suddenly halted.

He looked at the phantom of the wooden sword beside him.

His mind recalled the performance of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao when it provided convenience.

A subtle expression gradually appeared on Li Fan's face.

"My supreme escape technique is the fusion of my understanding of the unwavering pursuit of the sword path, the transformation of truth and falsehood, and..."

"The teachings of Xuan Tian King, from the soul memory of Dharma King Ji Yuzhen of the Xuan Tian Sect."

"The core of the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!"

"The Horizon Instantaneous Formation was also obtained by Xuan Tian King from the Immortal Realm..."

Li Fan rapidly recalled his past experiences.

Xuan Tian King said gently to Ji Yuzhen: "The Golden Lock Dangling Formation spans across all heavens. Even if the target is at the far end of the star sea, as long as it is locked, the chain can arrive instantly and capture it. I told you before that the reason this effect can be achieved is because it is embedded with the [Horizon Instantaneous] Formation. This formation was originally inscribed on the Ascension Platform in the Immortal Realm. When I escaped, I moved the entire immortal formation down..."

Boom!

Xuan Tian King's voice, like thunderclaps, traversed the ancient past, piercing the mist, illuminating Li Fan's mind.

"Wait! Could it be..."

A flash of brilliance appeared in Li Fan's eyes.

He waved his hand, dispersing the phantom of the wooden sword beside him.

He continued to pace slowly through the Xuanhuang Realm.

As expected, soon after sensing Li Fan's actions, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao began its act of showing favor.

Li Fan exerted no effort of his own; it acted on its own.

The surrounding scenery changed rapidly. Li Fan closed his eyes, sensing the changes occurring in the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth around him.

"This feeling..."

"It's correct!"

"It's the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!"

Li Fan's figure suddenly stopped.

His heart was uncontrollably excited.

His thoughts raced: "As part of the Star Crossing Great Formation, the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, though damaged..."

"But each time this formation is used, it consumes a great deal. Xuan Tian King, who was planning for unforeseen circumstances, had long ago replicated three copies as a backup."

"The Horizon Instantaneous Formation is not critical. The key is..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he scanned the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth.

"Ascension Platform! Inscribed! Complete!"

Li Fan's body trembled slightly with excitement due to this guess.

"The Ascension Platform must have been the place where the Immortal Realm received cultivators from the lower realms."

"Being named Ascension, besides the Horizon Instantaneous Formation, there must be other powers inscribed within."

"At that time, Xuan Tian King was also fleeing in a panic, and he had only just entered the Immortal Realm. He was completely incapable of separating the Horizon Instantaneous Formation alone in such a short time."

"Therefore, it is highly likely that the three copies of the inscription left by Xuan Tian King were the complete inscriptions on the Immortal Realm's Ascension Platform!"

"This might be the key!"

Even without one hundred percent certainty, Li Fan had undoubtedly found the most likely factor to achieve the final qualitative leap.

From his experiences over so many years, Li Fan had never dared to underestimate anything from the Immortal Realm.

"Now, the most critical question is, where are the three copies of the inscription left by Xuan Tian King back then?"

Li Fan had destroyed the Xuanhuang Realm more than once, and the objects remaining in the World Destruction Formation did not include these inscriptions.

This suggested that these inscriptions might not be within the Xuanhuang Realm.

If the Xuanhuang Realm had not proactively shown favor, indirectly alerting Li Fan.

Then Li Fan might have gone to search for clues within the Qilin beast's eyes in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, or even within the remnant Great Wall outside the High Wall.

But now, the unintentional actions of the Xuanhuang Realm indicated a possibility to Li Fan.

"The Ascension Platform inscriptions might be within the Xuanhuang Realm!"

"Due to the influence of the inscriptions, the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth, subtlety by subtlety, learned the Horizon Instantaneous Formation."

"Even, as I guessed in the branching illusion, some of Xuanhuang Realm's innate characteristics from the Immortal Realm were also influenced by this Ascension Platform!"

Li Fan suppressed the urge to dig up the Xuanhuang Realm inch by inch.

Calming his state of mind, as if intentionally, as if unintentionally, he communicated with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

He brought up the matter of its proactive showing of favor.

The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao seemed somewhat proud of its actions.

Soon, it fell into Li Fan's trap.

It recounted everything it knew in detail.

"Just as I expected!"

"It learned it spontaneously, without knowing how!"

Li Fan patiently continued to inquire about further details.

The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, through Li Fan's continuous strengthening, had reached an unprecedented peak of self-mastery.

Therefore, under Li Fan's guidance, it slowly discovered the source of this "unprompted learning."

Li Fan followed the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's hint and flashed away, arriving at his destination.

It seemed to be a million miles deep beneath the Xuanhuang land.

Even the flowing earth veins had vanished here; the surroundings were merely a accumulation of pure Xuanhuang power.

Li Fan looked at the somewhat familiar architectural style of the surroundings, like an ancient magic formation.

A stone slab was embedded in the center of the formation.

Chapter 1400: The Cause Was the Effect of That Year

"In this additional simulation, I seem to not have the treasure True Return. Other than that, there is no difference from experiencing everything myself."

Recalling the myriad images that suddenly flashed through his mind, Li Fan's expression was grave.

When the Dao Annihilation black energy engulfed the falling Xuanhuang Realm, unable to escape, he made no attempt to activate True Return, simply waiting for death with resignation.

"But in the simulation, my simulated self did not feel any abnormality at the disappearance of True Return, as if my simulated self had never possessed this treasure. From the moment I activated the additional simulation, a branch was created that excluded True Return..."

"This is interesting. Even in the simulation of True Return, as long as it is an additional one, existing alongside the main simulation, can the branching simulation not simulate oneself?" Li Fan's thought moved, and a flash of inspiration suddenly crossed his mind, as if he had understood something.

But this inspiration was like a candle in the darkness, instantly swallowed by the surrounding boundless darkness. When Li Fan tried to recall it later, he could not remember it no matter how hard he tried.

Knowing that he might have missed the secret of True Return, Li Fan's expression froze, and he felt a momentary sense of loss.

But soon, he recovered.

Li Fan believed that as his comprehension of [True-False Transformation] continued to improve, and his compatibility with True Return deepened, he would eventually uncover the secret of [True Return] completely and thoroughly.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan composed himself and carefully pondered the experiences in the branching simulation.

"Xuanhuang's sublimation plan proceeded almost as I anticipated. There were no major flaws in the preparations, and no unexpected enemies appeared."

"The only obstacle to Xuanhuang's ascension was that it was always a hair's breadth away from the final qualitative transformation. This is the starting point of the heaven-and-earth difference between Immortal and Mortal."

"What exactly can achieve this qualitative change?"

Instantly, countless schemes flashed through Li Fan's mind.

"The Immortal-Mortal Transformation characters? Or should I still use the Immortal Realm chess pieces? Or, based on the remnants of the ancient immortal formations, try to repair the Star Crossing Great Formation?"

Each attempt involved endless possibilities. Most existences related to "Immortal" were completely unknown variables, not something Li Fan could deduce now. Li Fan's head ached, but he could not choose the most suitable plan.

It seemed that each method could work, yet each method might also fail.

"Could it be that in this lifetime, I still cannot achieve Dao Integration and ascend to the Immortal Realm?"

"If all else fails, I will try each method one by one. There must be a correct path to ascend the world." Such a dejected thought quietly arose in Li Fan's heart.

Once this thought appeared, it was like a dike bursting, flooding thousands of miles. It completely destroyed Li Fan's psychological defense.

His thoughts became like a storm-ridden mind, chaotic and unceasing.

Li Fan stopped thinking about the conditions required for Xuanhuang's sublimation and ascension. Instead, he began to consider how to end this life and begin the next.

The plan was excellent.

But for some reason, Li Fan felt somewhat uneasy.

Theoretically, everything in the simulation could be reproduced through another simulation. For Li Fan, there was truly nothing that could be "lost" in the world.

Except for Li Fan's own changes.

Every time True Return activated the simulation and returned to the predetermined anchor. Everything in the world was reset.

Even Li Fan's physical strength and cultivation were the same. He needed to rely on True Return's inherited cultivation function to return to the state of the previous simulation.

However, within each reset, there was a variable that constantly moved forward.

That was Li Fan's will!

Specifically reflected on the True Return interface, it was Li Fan's maximum psychological age and the default True Return charging progress.

And these two factors had not changed for a long time...

Li Fan's heart was filled with unprecedented hesitation at this moment.

Time ticked by, and Li Fan could not make a final decision.

There were only ten hours left until Li Fan initiated Xuanhuang's ascension in the branching simulation of the Three-pronged Tree technique. Li Fan's expression was inscrutable. He took a step forward and arrived at the origin of everything.

The humble mortal body of Da Xuan, the house where he lived during his lifetime.

Even though "Li Fan" had mysteriously disappeared, the study remained spotless, just as it had always been. Clearly, that "aunt" still held some hope for "Li Fan's" return.

Li Fan lay on the bed and closed his eyes.

It was as if he had returned to the moment he first transmigrated.

Time seemed to freeze. Then, it flowed quietly, as if ice was breaking.

Having undergone a hundred lifetimes of reincarnation, all his experiences flashed through Li Fan's mind in an instant.

Li Fan attempted to find a way to break through the deadlock in this manner.

Day turned into night, and Li Fan lay quietly on the wooden bed.

It was as if he had fallen into a deep sleep.

Yes, Li Fan could indeed use repeated True Return simulations, and through elimination, determine one by one the key factors for achieving qualitative change.

This was also the most stable approach.

Theoretically, there were no problems.

But every time Li Fan decided to do so, inexplicable images would flash through his mind.

It was the persistence of Mo Rubin, who, despite the flaws in the High Wall, disregarded his own life to investigate; and the Heavenly Physician in the illusion formation, who ultimately gave up on comprehending the High Wall for the sake of the Heavenly Law Realm.

"Once lost is forever lost."

In the darkness, Li Fan's eyes suddenly opened.

He softly whispered these four words.

With True Return around, there was indeed nothing in the world that could be "forever lost" to him. Unless that item's rank was even higher than True Return.

Obviously, mere transformation from mortal to immortal was not enough to achieve that.
