Chapter 1401: The Heavenly Beast Achieves a Feat (Revision Complete)

The ancient stone tablet, enshrined at the center of the formation, was like the Nine-Star Red Pearl that Li Fan had seen before in the ruins of the Xuanhuang World-Guarding Immortal Formation.

However, unlike the missing Nine-Star Red Pearl, this ancient stone tablet remained stubbornly in place.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, attempting to discern the content carved on the stone tablet within the formation.

The stone tablet remained motionless, yet the lines upon it seemed to shift constantly, appearing blurry and indistinct.

This instantly reminded Li Fan of the ancient Immortal Realm coins he had seen previously.

"It seems to be a unique recording method of the Immortal Realm. However, the content carved on this stone tablet…"

"Is even more complex!"

Li Fan's heart stirred, but he did not rush to investigate further. He keenly sensed that the formation before him appeared to possess a misleading effect. What could be glimpsed through the formation might not be the truth.

With the help of the Dissolution Disc, Li Fan began to analyze the formation before him.

"There is no Immortal Spiritual Qi. For the sake of its concealment, it seems to even lack the most basic spiritual energy. Then what exactly is supporting this formation to operate for so many years?" After some research, Li Fan became intrigued.

Li Fan’s current mastery of formations was undoubtedly that of a grandmaster. He could even merge and deduce immortal formations according to his own needs. Yet, a formation of this type was something Li Fan had never encountered before.

"It is not that the energy consumption for the formation's operation is too small, allowing it to be sustained by a single item. The power of this formation…" Li Fan pondered, tentatively transforming his spiritual energy into a small bird, intending to breach the formation.

He encountered no obstruction whatsoever.

However, the moment it crossed the boundary of the formation, the spiritual bird vanished without a trace, as if it had been evaporated.

Li Fan's pupils contracted sharply.

Because he was utterly unable to perceive the form in which the bird he controlled had disappeared.

Li Fan snapped his fingers, and then thousands of birds, like an overwhelming dark cloud, charged towards the formation.

Under Li Fan's precise control, the total amount of spiritual energy contained in all the birds was minuscule. Below a certain threshold, it ensured that the formation's stronger defensive reactions would not be triggered.

Their fate was all the same, without exception.

Li Fan carefully savored the process of the birds' disappearance.

"The spiritual energy was not 'consumed.' Instead, the very foundation that maintained the spiritual energy's existence was drained…"

As all the birds vanished, Li Fan vaguely sensed something.

This formation actually gave him a feeling of familiarity.

Li Fan then used concrete physical objects for experimentation.

Stones, magical artifacts, as well as plants and flying creatures.

The outcomes were largely similar.

Anything that entered the formation vanished without exception.

Li Fan's expression gradually turned solemn. "Everything I've tested before were all 'mortal' objects. What about those related to 'immortals'?"

Golden Primordial Origin Essence transformed into a tiny dragon, impacting the formation. The air seemed to be scorched by flames, distorting. Then the golden light gradually faded, and the end result was the same!

Following this, Li Fan took out a mass of True Immortal flesh and blood. Golden threads were inserted into the flesh and blood. The True Immortal flesh and blood, like a puppet controlled by strings, swayed and slowly entered the formation.

The golden threads that Li Fan used to control it snapped midway. However, the True Immortal flesh and blood that entered the formation underwent a different change than the mortal objects before.

The stone tablet, lying quietly within the formation, its originally flickering patterns suddenly stilled for a moment.

In this instant, Li Fan vaguely saw a lightning bolt illuminate on the stone tablet, striking the True Immortal flesh and blood that had entered the formation.

The strange and mysterious aura of the True Immortal flesh and blood vanished abruptly. It was no longer considered immortal and instantly transformed into a mortal object.

Then it dissipated within the formation!

This sudden change occurred in the blink of an eye. At first glance, it appeared as though the True Immortal flesh and blood, like all the mortal objects used in the experiment before, could not last even a moment within the formation.

But Li Fan keenly perceived something else.

Li Fan repeated the previous operation, continuously probing with True Immortal flesh and blood. He hoped to seize that fleeting opportunity to see the lightning strike from across the void.

"The light that illuminated on the stone tablet seemed to be one of the patterns from the Ascension Platform, engraved by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao? It can actually turn immortals into mortals!"

Li Fan was utterly shocked.

However, he also understood that what he was using for the experiment was not true "immortals," but merely flesh and blood revived from the corpses of True Immortals, devoid of consciousness. It could not be compared to a True Immortal.

But regardless, the terrifying regenerative and defensive capabilities of True Immortal flesh and blood had already been verified on the Immortal Puppet Tian Yang. It could ignore almost all mortal attack methods and even had a certain degree of immunity to True Immortal script influences.

Yet, such a transcendent and terrifying existence had no power to resist before the lightning pattern on the stone tablet.

"If it can turn immortals into mortals, why can't it turn mortals into immortals?"

"Ascension Platform, Ascension Platform…"

His previous conjecture seemed to be validated. Li Fan looked at the stone tablet not far away, his mood gradually becoming excited.

After another period of experimentation, having consumed nearly one-tenth of his stored True Immortal flesh and blood without any success, Li Fan finally had to give up this arduous method.

The lightning-like pattern on the stone tablet appeared for too short a duration. Moreover, what was seen through the formation was subject to a certain degree of distortion. To see it clearly like this was like dreaming.

"In my previous several world-destroying calamities, the Xuanhuang Realm completely turned into nothingness. But I did not detect the existence of this formation and stone tablet."

"This formation should not be fixed in this location. It is like a living creature; if it encounters an insurmountable situation, it can strategically transfer itself."

"It requires no power source, yet can transfer itself at critical moments. This formation is truly wondrous!" Li Fan marveled.

"Since it cannot be forcibly broken, it seems only the Little Turtle can be called upon."

Li Fan's heart moved. Blue light flashed beside him.

Supreme Autumn Water appeared beside Li Fan, carrying the Little Turtle.

"Greetings, Great Master." Autumn Water was still extremely respectful.

Upon seeing the Little Turtle bare its teeth at Li Fan, Autumn Water directly slapped its head.

Energy surged from the blow; it was not merely a gesture but a full-powered strike!

The Little Turtle was instantly stunned.

In its normal state, even if it had transformed from an Immortal Realm jade pendant, enduring such a blow would have undoubtedly caused serious injury.

But this lifetime, the Little Turtle had consecutively devoured four Immortal Realm chess pieces. Empowered by Immortal Realm laws, its physique had already grown to an unimaginable extent.

It merely let out a mournful cry, and the Little Turtle recovered.

Under Autumn Water's coercion, it shrunk its head towards Li Fan, bowing in a show of deference.

"Indeed, one thing conquers another." Li Fan secretly nodded.

Perhaps due to being manifested from a living being's form, after prolonged closeness, the Little Turtle actually regarded the Autumn Water Taoist boy as a parental figure.

And Autumn Water, under Li Fan's orders, had been continuously feeding it Immortal Realm chess pieces and taking it around the Star Sea hoping its sensitive instincts might gain some insights, further solidifying this "parental" identity.

Consequently, the Little Turtle was almost completely obedient to Autumn Water.

With a thought, Li Fan, through Autumn Water, commanded the Little Turtle to crawl towards the stone tablet surrounded by the formation.

Before this formation, the Little Turtle's sensitive perception seemed to have lost its effect.

It was like a blind person, and had not even detected the existence of that strange formation before this. Only when it slowly crawled to the boundary of the formation did it suddenly become alert, and stopped.

It looked ahead with confusion, its eyes filled with vigilance.

The Little Turtle was unwilling to move forward, but Autumn Water urged it on.

After a moment of hesitation, the Little Turtle's eyes emitted a faint, mysterious silver starlight.

After observing for a long time, the Little Turtle unwillingly continued to advance.

"As expected, just as I predicted, the Little Turtle was originally an Immortal Realm item transformed. It possesses a certain resistance to this formation. Furthermore, having consumed four Immortal Realm chess pieces, its physique has undergone a qualitative change. It should be able to withstand the formation's attack!" Li Fan's eyes gleamed.

The Little Turtle crawled very slowly.

It stared at the stone tablet not far ahead, and a trace of doubt flickered in its eyes. It seemed to feel a strange sense of familiarity with this stone tablet.

Therefore, it became even more resistant.

It was only when Autumn Water intervened, appealing to its emotions and offering benefits, that the Little Turtle reluctantly continued to move forward.

Li Fan waited patiently for the Little Turtle to retrieve the stone tablet.

Simultaneously, he continued to examine the strange formation before him.

After such a long time, Li Fan had vaguely recalled the origin of this feeling of familiarity.

It originated from the formation's mechanism of cutting off the foundation of an object's existence!

In the earth fissure depressions scattered throughout the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, life force flowed in dark rivers, enveloped by a layer that siphoned away life force. This cut off the foundation of an object's existence, and this siphoning of life force was the reason for the accumulation of life force in the fissures; the corrosive green energy wrapped around the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God on the Mystic Immortal Boat also devoured the existence principles of whatever it touched.

And even…

The formless High Wall encircling the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Could also be seen as directly erasing the foundation of the concept of "before" existing.

"All of these can be seen as the absence of elements of existence."

"It is remarkably similar to this formation!" Li Fan's eyes glittered, a storm of thoughts churning in his mind, bringing forth many realizations.

"These should all be methods from the former Immortal Realm."

"It is even possible that those outside the High Wall have also mastered such divine abilities."

"Based on the clues I've obtained so far, when Xuan Tian King laid these hidden traps, he was likely only a half-immortal. Without Immortal Spiritual Qi, how did he achieve all this?"

The Little Turtle was within the formation the entire time.

Continuously stimulated, the formation's operation allowed Li Fan to observe it more clearly.

Even the symbols within the stone tablet in the center of the formation were becoming more and more visible.

Among the numerous patterns that flashed, Li Fan surprisingly captured patterns extremely similar to the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!

"Because I was peeking through the formation, the sight was distorted, so it wasn't a perfect match. But it further confirms my conjecture!"

"This stone tablet, replicated by Xuan Tian King, indeed contains the complete inscriptions from the Immortal Realm's Ascension Platform."

"This inscription encompasses almost everything. Each one corresponds to a certain power originally belonging to the Immortal Realm."

"Such as the Horizon Instantaneous Formation. And also, the transformation of Immortals into mortals, and mortals into Immortals!"

Li Fan's emotions surged. The farther the Little Turtle crawled, the greater the pressure it seemed to bear, and its movements became slower and slower, almost stagnant!

It was only one step away from the stone tablet, but the Little Turtle's efforts were futile.

The Little Turtle's eyes flashed with a trace of ferocity. It kept growling, expressing its immense rage.

However, it was completely unable to break free from Li Fan's control technique.

This technique was precisely something Li Fan had covertly learned from Mo Rubin's method of controlling the Qilin beast's eyes.

Whether it was the ancient guardian beast of the Xuan Tian Sect, or the Little Turtle born not long ago.

Their original forms were jade pendants brought from the Immortal Realm by Xuan Tian King.

In essence, they could be considered the same being.

Control methods that were effective for the Xuan Tian Sect's Qilin beast would naturally be effective for the Little Turtle before him.

Li Fan had also secretly experimented with this before.

Otherwise, he would not have allowed the Little Turtle to directly devour four Immortal Realm chess pieces.

Under Li Fan's ruthless compulsion, despite its increasingly severe injuries, the Little Turtle finally crawled to the front of the stone tablet.

Using its comparatively slender body, it bore the stone tablet on its back.

Carrying it on its back, it then let out a low roar and slowly retreated.

On the stone tablet, countless patterns shifted unpredictably.

The Little Turtle's flesh and blood were also shaved away bit by bit, disappearing unseen.

In the end, only a hollow shell remained, along with the Little Turtle's eyes, protected by silver starlight, and shining.

Carrying the stone tablet on its back, it moved forward slowly but with unwavering determination.

After an unknown amount of time, it finally crawled out of the range covered by the strange formation.

The moment it left the formation, the Little Turtle completely lost its strength and could no longer move.

Autumn Water quickly stepped forward to assist it.

Li Fan, however, gazed at the stone tablet on the Little Turtle's back. The patterns on it had all extinguished. The sacred and solemn aura had also disappeared simultaneously.

It was like a mundane object, ordinary and unremarkable.

Li Fan casually threw an Immortal Realm chess piece, handing it to the Little Turtle, which had performed a great service but was now on its last legs.

He himself levitated the stone tablet, examining it carefully.

Chapter 1402: Xuanhuang Ascends to the Immortal Realm

In the additional simulation, I seem to not possess the treasure True Return. Other than that, there is no difference from experiencing everything myself.

Recalling the myriad images that suddenly flashed through his mind, Li Fan's expression was grave. When the Dao Annihilation black energy engulfed the falling Xuanhuang Realm, unable to escape, he made no attempt to activate True Return, simply waiting for death with resignation.

But in the simulation, my simulated self did not feel any abnormality at the disappearance of True Return, as if my simulated self had never possessed this treasure. From the moment I activated the additional simulation, a branch was created that excluded True Return...

This is interesting. Even in the simulation of True Return, as long as it is an additional one, existing alongside the main simulation, can the branching simulation not simulate oneself?

Li Fan's thought moved, and a flash of inspiration suddenly crossed his mind, as if he had understood something. But this inspiration was like a candle in the darkness, instantly swallowed by the surrounding boundless darkness. When Li Fan tried to recall it later, he could not remember it no matter how hard he tried.

Knowing that he might have missed the secret of True Return, Li Fan's expression froze, and he felt a momentary sense of loss. But soon, he recovered.

Li Fan believed that as his comprehension of [True-False Transformation] continued to improve, and his compatibility with True Return deepened, he would eventually uncover the secret of [True Return] completely and thoroughly.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan composed himself and carefully pondered the experiences in the branching simulation. Xuanhuang's sublimation plan proceeded almost as I anticipated. There were no major flaws in the preparations, and no unexpected enemies appeared. The only obstacle to Xuanhuang's ascension was that it was always a hair's breadth away from the final qualitative transformation. This is the starting point of the heaven-and-earth difference between Immortal and Mortal.

What exactly can achieve this qualitative change?

Instantly, countless schemes flashed through Li Fan's mind. The Immortal-Mortal Transformation characters? Or should I still use the Immortal Realm chess pieces? Or, based on the remnants of the ancient immortal formations, try to repair the Star Crossing Great Formation?

Each attempt involved endless possibilities. Most existences related to 'Immortal' were completely unknown variables, not something Li Fan could deduce now. Li Fan's head ached, but he could not choose the most suitable plan. It seemed that each method could work, yet each method might also fail.

Could it be that in this lifetime, I still cannot achieve Dao Integration and ascend to the Immortal Realm?

If all else fails, I will try each method one by one. There must be a correct path to ascend the world.

Such a dejected thought quietly arose in Li Fan's heart. Once this thought appeared, it was like a dike bursting, flooding thousands of miles. It completely destroyed Li Fan's psychological defense. His thoughts became like a storm-ridden mind, chaotic and unceasing.

Li Fan stopped thinking about the conditions required for Xuanhuang's sublimation and ascension. Instead, he began to consider how to end this life and begin the next. The plan was excellent. But for some reason, Li Fan felt somewhat uneasy.

Theoretically, everything in the simulation could be reproduced through another simulation. For Li Fan, there was truly nothing that could be 'lost' in the world. Except for Li Fan's own changes.

Every time True Return activated the simulation and returned to the predetermined anchor. Everything in the world was reset. Even Li Fan's physical strength and cultivation were the same. He needed to rely on True Return's inherited cultivation function to return to the state of the previous simulation.

However, within each reset, there was a variable that constantly moved forward. That was Li Fan's will! Specifically reflected on the True Return interface, it was Li Fan's maximum psychological age and the default True Return charging progress. And these two factors had not changed for a long time...

Li Fan's heart was filled with unprecedented hesitation at this moment. Time ticked by, and Li Fan could not make a final decision. There were only ten hours left until Li Fan initiated Xuanhuang's ascension in the branching simulation of the Three-pronged Tree technique.

Li Fan's expression was inscrutable. He took a step forward and arrived at the origin of everything. The humble mortal body of Da Xuan, the house where he lived during his lifetime. Even though 'Li Fan' had mysteriously disappeared, the study remained spotless, just as it had always been. Clearly, that 'aunt' still held some hope for 'Li Fan's' return.

Li Fan lay on the bed and closed his eyes. It was as if he had returned to the moment he first transmigrated. Time seemed to freeze. Then, it flowed quietly, as if ice was breaking. Having undergone a hundred lifetimes of reincarnation, all his experiences flashed through Li Fan's mind in an instant. Li Fan attempted to find a way to break through the deadlock in this manner.

Day turned into night, and Li Fan lay quietly on the wooden bed. It was as if he had fallen into a deep sleep. Yes, Li Fan could indeed use repeated True Return simulations, and through elimination, determine one by one the key factors for achieving qualitative change. This was also the most stable approach. Theoretically, there were no problems.

But every time Li Fan decided to do so, inexplicable images would flash through his mind. It was the persistence of Mo Rubin, who, despite the flaws in the High Wall, disregarded his own life to investigate; and the Heavenly Physician in the illusion formation, who ultimately gave up on comprehending the High Wall for the sake of the Heavenly Law Realm.

"Once lost is forever lost."

In the darkness, Li Fan's eyes suddenly opened. He softly whispered these four words. With True Return around, there was indeed nothing in the world that could be 'forever lost' to him. Unless that item's rank was even higher than True Return. Obviously, mere transformation from mortal to immortal was not enough to achieve that.

"True 'loss is forever loss' exists within my heart."

"True Return can influence everything in the world, but it cannot reverse my changes."

As if understanding something, Li Fan's gaze seemed to penetrate the darkness, gradually brightening. "The loss of this unknown characteristic might not affect my advancement to the True Immortal realm. But for the path beyond True Immortal, it might have profound implications!"

After a long period of contemplation, as a ray of sunlight appeared on the earth, dispelling the darkness, Li Fan finally understood completely. Where the unease in his heart originated.

"Why is it like this?"

"Is it due to over-reliance on [True Return]?"

"Or something else?"

"The path beyond True Immortal is too distant for me. Moreover, with my understanding, the Nameless True Immortal realm seems to only require complete mastery and refinement of a certain Great Dao. It doesn't seem related..."

Li Fan frowned tightly, filled with confusion. "But it seems I have no better option than exhaustive trials."

...

Li Fan walked out of the house, looking at the rising sun on the horizon. While continuing to ponder, he stepped away from the Great Xuan Small World.

He paced around within the Xuanhuang Realm. The surrounding scenery jumped and changed incessantly, as Li Fan's mind reflected everything around him. Starting from the Sea of Eastern Clouds, heading west. As his thoughts churned, the frequency of the surrounding scenery's changes seemed to accelerate.

Li Fan, immersed in a state of meditation akin to enlightenment, did not alter his outward output. The reason he 'walked' faster and faster. It was precisely because of the special relationship between Li Fan and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. Like a reborn parent, its favorability was extremely high. Therefore, without Li Fan's prompting, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao proactively helped Li Fan lighten the burden of travel. Even though the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao did not know why Li Fan was randomly moving around the world inexplicably. Perhaps it mistakenly believed that Li Fan was making final preparations for the sublimation and ascension.

Li Fan naturally noticed the favor shown by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. But he didn't pay much attention. Previously, when the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable traveled throughout the land to repair various damages to the Xuanhuang Realm, the Xuanhuang Realm had also provided such convenience.

With one step, the distance between heaven and earth transformed, as if shrinking the ground into inches. However, now that the anomalies in various places had been resolved, the Xuanhuang Realm had not actively done so for a long time.

"What a servant!"

In the branching simulation, upon seeing the true face of the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan cursed inwardly. "I possess supreme escape techniques, why would I need your rudimentary convenience?"

With a thought, the phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed and appeared at Li Fan's side. Just as he was about to fly away, escape the entanglement of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, and seize the last moment to calmly ponder. But Li Fan's movement suddenly halted. He looked at the phantom of the wooden sword beside him. His mind recalled the performance of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao when it provided convenience. A subtle expression gradually appeared on Li Fan's face.

"My supreme escape technique is the fusion of my understanding of the unwavering pursuit of the sword path, the transformation of truth and falsehood, and..."

"The teachings of Xuan Tian King, from the soul memory of Dharma King Ji Yuzhen of the Xuan Tian Sect."

"The core of the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!"

"The Horizon Instantaneous Formation was also obtained by Xuan Tian King from the Immortal Realm..."

Li Fan rapidly recalled his past experiences. Xuan Tian King said gently to Ji Yuzhen: "The Golden Lock Dangling Formation spans across all heavens. Even if the target is at the far end of the star sea, as long as it is locked, the chain can arrive instantly and capture it. I told you before that the reason this effect can be achieved is because it is embedded with the [Horizon Instantaneous] Formation. This formation was originally inscribed on the Ascension Platform in the Immortal Realm. When I escaped, I moved the entire immortal formation down..."

Boom! Xuan Tian King's voice, like thunderclaps, traversed the ancient past, piercing the mist, illuminating Li Fan's mind.

"Wait! Could it be..."

A flash of brilliance appeared in Li Fan's eyes. He waved his hand, dispersing the phantom of the wooden sword beside him. He continued to pace slowly through the Xuanhuang Realm. As expected, soon after sensing Li Fan's actions, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao began its act of showing favor. Li Fan exerted no effort of his own; it acted on its own. The surrounding scenery changed rapidly.

Li Fan closed his eyes, sensing the changes occurring in the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth around him. "This feeling..."

"It's correct!"

"It's the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!"

Li Fan's figure suddenly stopped. His heart was uncontrollably excited. His thoughts raced: "As part of the Star Crossing Great Formation, the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, though damaged..."

"But each time this formation is used, it consumes a great deal. Xuan Tian King, who was planning for unforeseen circumstances, had long ago replicated three copies as a backup."

"The Horizon Instantaneous Formation is not critical. The key is..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he scanned the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth. "Ascension Platform! Inscribed! Complete!"

Li Fan's body trembled slightly with excitement due to this guess. "The Ascension Platform must have been the place where the Immortal Realm received cultivators from the lower realms."

"Being named Ascension, besides the Horizon Instantaneous Formation, there must be other powers inscribed within."

"At that time, Xuan Tian King was also fleeing in a panic, and he had only just entered the Immortal Realm. He was completely incapable of separating the Horizon Instantaneous Formation alone in such a short time."

"Therefore, it is highly likely that the three copies of the inscription left by Xuan Tian King were the complete inscriptions on the Immortal Realm's Ascension Platform!"

"This might be the key!"

Even without one hundred percent certainty, Li Fan had undoubtedly found the most likely factor to achieve the final qualitative leap. From his experiences over so many years, Li Fan had never dared to underestimate anything from the Immortal Realm.

Chapter 1403: Proving Half-Immortal Through Dao Integration

The ancient stone tablet, enshrined at the center of the formation, was like the Nine-Star Red Pearl that Li Fan had seen before in the ruins of the Xuanhuang World-Guarding Immortal Formation. However, unlike the missing Nine-Star Red Pearl, this ancient stone tablet remained stubbornly in place.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, attempting to discern the content carved on the stone tablet within the formation. The stone tablet remained motionless, yet the lines upon it seemed to shift constantly, appearing blurry and indistinct. This instantly reminded Li Fan of the ancient Immortal Realm coins he had seen previously.

"It seems to be a unique recording method of the Immortal Realm. However, the content carved on this stone tablet… is even more complex!"

Li Fan's heart stirred, but he did not rush to investigate further. He keenly sensed that the formation before him appeared to possess a misleading effect. What could be glimpsed through the formation might not be the truth.

With the help of the Dissolution Disc, Li Fan began to analyze the formation before him. "There is no Immortal Spiritual Qi. For the sake of its concealment, it seems to even lack the most basic spiritual energy. Then what exactly is supporting this formation to operate for so many years?" After some research, Li Fan became intrigued.

Li Fan’s current mastery of formations was undoubtedly that of a grandmaster. He could even merge and deduce immortal formations according to his own needs. Yet, a formation of this type was something Li Fan had never encountered before.

"It is not that the energy consumption for the formation's operation is too small, allowing it to be sustained by a single item. The power of this formation…" Li Fan pondered, tentatively transforming his spiritual energy into a small bird, intending to breach the formation. He encountered no obstruction whatsoever. However, the moment it crossed the boundary of the formation, the spiritual bird vanished without a trace, as if it had been evaporated.

Li Fan's pupils contracted sharply. Because he was utterly unable to perceive the form in which the bird he controlled had disappeared.

Li Fan snapped his fingers, and then thousands of birds, like an overwhelming dark cloud, charged towards the formation. Under Li Fan's precise control, the total amount of spiritual energy contained in all the birds was minuscule. Below a certain threshold, it ensured that the formation's stronger defensive reactions would not be triggered.

Their fate was all the same, without exception. Li Fan carefully savored the process of the birds' disappearance. "The spiritual energy was not 'consumed.' Instead, the very foundation that maintained the spiritual energy's existence was drained…"

As all the birds vanished, Li Fan vaguely sensed something. This formation actually gave him a feeling of familiarity. Li Fan then used concrete physical objects for experimentation. Stones, magical artifacts, as well as plants and flying creatures. The outcomes were largely similar. Anything that entered the formation vanished without exception.

Li Fan's expression gradually turned solemn. "Everything I've tested before were all 'mortal' objects. What about those related to 'immortals'?"

Golden Primordial Origin Essence transformed into a tiny dragon, impacting the formation. The air seemed to be scorched by flames, distorting. Then the golden light gradually faded, and the end result was the same! Following this, Li Fan took out a mass of True Immortal flesh and blood. Golden threads were inserted into the flesh and blood. The True Immortal flesh and blood, like a puppet controlled by strings, swayed and slowly entered the formation.

The golden threads that Li Fan used to control it snapped midway. However, the True Immortal flesh and blood that entered the formation underwent a different change than the mortal objects before. The stone tablet, lying quietly within the formation, its originally flickering patterns suddenly stilled for a moment. In this instant, Li Fan vaguely saw a lightning bolt illuminate on the stone tablet, striking the True Immortal flesh and blood that had entered the formation.

The strange and mysterious aura of the True Immortal flesh and blood vanished abruptly. It was no longer considered immortal and instantly transformed into a mortal object. Then it dissipated within the formation!

This sudden change occurred in the blink of an eye. At first glance, it appeared as though the True Immortal flesh and blood, like all the mortal objects used in the experiment before, could not last even a moment within the formation. But Li Fan keenly perceived something else.

Li Fan repeated the previous operation, continuously probing with True Immortal flesh and blood. He hoped to seize that fleeting opportunity to see the lightning strike from across the void. "The light that illuminated on the stone tablet seemed to be one of the patterns from the Ascension Platform, engraved by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao? It can actually turn immortals into mortals!"

Li Fan was utterly shocked. However, he also understood that what he was using for the experiment was not true 'immortals,' but merely flesh and blood revived from the corpses of True Immortals, devoid of consciousness. It could not be compared to a True Immortal. But regardless, the terrifying regenerative and defensive capabilities of True Immortal flesh and blood had already been verified on the Immortal Puppet Tian Yang. It could ignore almost all mortal attack methods and even had a certain degree of immunity to True Immortal script influences. Yet, such a transcendent and terrifying existence had no power to resist before the lightning pattern on the stone tablet.

"If it can turn immortals into mortals, why can't it turn mortals into immortals?"

"Ascension Platform, Ascension Platform…" His previous conjecture seemed to be validated. Li Fan looked at the stone tablet not far away, his mood gradually becoming excited.

After another period of experimentation, having consumed nearly one-tenth of his stored True Immortal flesh and blood without any success, Li Fan finally had to give up this arduous method. The lightning-like pattern on the stone tablet appeared for too short a duration. Moreover, what was seen through the formation was subject to a certain degree of distortion. To see it clearly like this was like dreaming.

"In my previous several world-destroying calamities, the Xuanhuang Realm completely turned into nothingness. But I did not detect the existence of this formation and stone tablet."

"This formation should not be fixed in this location. It is like a living creature; if it encounters an insurmountable situation, it can strategically transfer itself."

"It requires no power source, yet can transfer itself at critical moments. This formation is truly wondrous!" Li Fan marveled.

"Since it cannot be forcibly broken, it seems only the Little Turtle can be called upon."

Li Fan's heart moved. Blue light flashed beside him. Supreme Autumn Water appeared beside Li Fan, carrying the Little Turtle.

"Greetings, Great Master." Autumn Water was still extremely respectful.

Upon seeing the Little Turtle bare its teeth at Li Fan, Autumn Water directly slapped its head. Energy surged from the blow; it was not merely a gesture but a full-powered strike! The Little Turtle was instantly stunned. In its normal state, even if it had transformed from an Immortal Realm jade pendant, enduring such a blow would have undoubtedly caused serious injury. But this lifetime, the Little Turtle had consecutively devoured four Immortal Realm chess pieces. Empowered by Immortal Realm laws, its physique had already grown to an unimaginable extent. It merely let out a mournful cry, and the Little Turtle recovered.

Under Autumn Water's coercion, it shrunk its head towards Li Fan, bowing in a show of deference. "Indeed, one thing conquers another." Li Fan secretly nodded. Perhaps due to being manifested from a living being's form, after prolonged closeness, the Little Turtle actually regarded the Autumn Water Taoist boy as a parental figure. And Autumn Water, under Li Fan's orders, had been continuously feeding it Immortal Realm chess pieces and taking it around the Star Sea hoping its sensitive instincts might gain some insights, further solidifying this 'parental' identity. Consequently, the Little Turtle was almost completely obedient to Autumn Water.

With a thought, Li Fan, through Autumn Water, commanded the Little Turtle to crawl towards the stone tablet surrounded by the formation. Before this formation, the Little Turtle's sensitive perception seemed to have lost its effect. It was like a blind person, and had not even detected the existence of that strange formation before this. Only when it slowly crawled to the boundary of the formation did it suddenly become alert, and stopped. It looked ahead with confusion, its eyes filled with vigilance.

The Little Turtle was unwilling to move forward, but Autumn Water urged it on. After a moment of hesitation, the Little Turtle's eyes emitted a faint, mysterious silver starlight. After observing for a long time, the Little Turtle unwillingly continued to advance.

"As expected, just as I predicted, the Little Turtle was originally an Immortal Realm item transformed. It possesses a certain resistance to this formation. Furthermore, having consumed four Immortal Realm chess pieces, its physique has undergone a qualitative change. It should be able to withstand the formation's attack!" Li Fan's eyes gleamed.

The Little Turtle crawled very slowly. It stared at the stone tablet not far ahead, and a trace of doubt flickered in its eyes. It seemed to feel a strange sense of familiarity with this stone tablet. Therefore, it became even more resistant. It was only when Autumn Water intervened, appealing to its emotions and offering benefits, that the Little Turtle reluctantly continued to move forward.

Li Fan waited patiently for the Little Turtle to retrieve the stone tablet. Simultaneously, he continued to examine the strange formation before him. After such a long time, Li Fan had vaguely recalled the origin of this feeling of familiarity. It originated from the formation's mechanism of cutting off the foundation of an object's existence! In the earth fissure depressions scattered throughout the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, life force flowed in dark rivers, enveloped by a layer that siphoned away life force. This cut off the foundation of an object's existence, and this siphoning of life force was the reason for the accumulation of life force in the fissures; the corrosive green energy wrapped around the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God on the Mystic Immortal Boat also devoured the existence principles of whatever it touched. And even… The formless High Wall encircling the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Could also be seen as directly erasing the foundation of the concept of 'before' existing.

"All of these can be seen as the absence of elements of existence."

"It is remarkably similar to this formation!" Li Fan's eyes glittered, a storm of thoughts churning in his mind, bringing forth many realizations. "These should all be methods from the former Immortal Realm."

"It is even possible that those outside the High Wall have also mastered such divine abilities."

"Based on the clues I've obtained so far, when Xuan Tian King laid these hidden traps, he was likely only a half-immortal. Without Immortal Spiritual Qi, how did he achieve all this?"

The Little Turtle was within the formation the entire time. Continuously stimulated, the formation's operation allowed Li Fan to observe it more clearly. Even the symbols within the stone tablet in the center of the formation were becoming more and more visible. Among the numerous patterns that flashed, Li Fan surprisingly captured patterns extremely similar to the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!

"Because I was peeking through the formation, the sight was distorted, so it wasn't a perfect match. But it further confirms my conjecture!"

"This stone tablet, replicated by Xuan Tian King, indeed contains the complete inscriptions from the Immortal Realm's Ascension Platform."

"This inscription encompasses almost everything. Each one corresponds to a certain power originally belonging to the Immortal Realm."

"Such as the Horizon Instantaneous Formation. And also, the transformation of Immortals into mortals, and mortals into Immortals!"

Li Fan's emotions surged. The farther the Little Turtle crawled, the greater the pressure it seemed to bear, and its movements became slower and slower, almost stagnant! It was only one step away from the stone tablet, but the Little Turtle's efforts were futile. The Little Turtle's eyes flashed with a trace of ferocity. It kept growling, expressing its immense rage. However, it was completely unable to break free from Li Fan's control technique. This technique was precisely something Li Fan had covertly learned from Mo Rubin's method of controlling the Qilin beast's eyes. Whether it was the ancient guardian beast of the Xuan Tian Sect, or the Little Turtle born not long ago. Their original forms were jade pendants brought from the Immortal Realm by Xuan Tian King.

In essence, they could be considered the same being. Control methods that were effective for the Xuan Tian Sect's Qilin beast would naturally be effective for the Little Turtle before him. Li Fan had also secretly experimented with this before. Otherwise, he would not have allowed the Little Turtle to directly devour four Immortal Realm chess pieces. Under Li Fan's ruthless compulsion, despite its increasingly severe injuries, the Little Turtle finally crawled to the front of the stone tablet. Using its comparatively slender body, it bore the stone tablet on its back. Carrying it on its back, it then let out a low roar and slowly retreated.

On the stone tablet, countless patterns shifted unpredictably. The Little Turtle's flesh and blood were also shaved away bit by bit, disappearing unseen. In the end, only a hollow shell remained, along with the Little Turtle's eyes, protected by silver starlight, and shining. Carrying the stone tablet on its back, it moved forward slowly but with unwavering determination. After an unknown amount of time, it finally crawled out of the range covered by the strange formation. The moment it left the formation, the Little Turtle completely lost its strength and could no longer move. Autumn Water quickly stepped forward to assist it.

Li Fan, however, gazed at the stone tablet on the Little Turtle's back. The patterns on it had all extinguished. The sacred and solemn aura had also disappeared simultaneously. It was like a mundane object, ordinary and unremarkable. Li Fan casually threw an Immortal Realm chess piece, handing it to the Little Turtle, which had performed a great service but was now on its last legs. He himself levitated the stone tablet, examining it carefully.

Chapter 1404: Dao Hidden Pause

When Li Fan's consciousness reawakened, he had returned to the predetermined anchor point.

And now...

As Li Fan silently recited the incantation for 'True Return,' instead of a curtain of mist enveloping the surroundings, the entire world entered a state of stillness at Li Fan's whim. The vibrant colors shifted into a monotonous black and white.

Li Fan had never observed the world from such a perspective. He stared blankly at the shattered Great Array of Return to Void, the residual winds seemingly frozen in mid-air. Countless Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth surrounded him, each with its unique form. Further in the distance, a gaunt figure could be vaguely seen descending upon the land—it was the Star Sea Hunger Immortal, seeking enlightenment.

Everything before him appeared unchanged from before the 'True Return' was activated, with the sole difference being that they were trapped in a black and white, frozen state. Li Fan observed cautiously for a long time, then felt a stir in his heart. His form flickered, and he actually began to move within this frozen world!

This was undoubtedly a novel experience. Li Fan narrowed his eyes, attempting to touch a nearby Celestial Soul of Heaven and Earth. Even in its black and white form, Li Fan recognized it instantly as an old acquaintance, Chi Yan. Compared to its previous form as a Celestial Soul, Chi Yan's expression was now more vivid, almost indistinguishable from a real person. However, its eyes remained tightly shut, and its illusory clothing was tattered, making it seem somewhat out of place amongst the other Celestial Souls.

The moment Li Fan touched Chi Yan, its body flashed, transforming into countless particles of light that scattered with the wind. Li Fan also sensed that the range of this frozen world had significantly shrunk.

Temporarily disregarding the distant figure, Li Fan narrowed his eyes, replaying the images that had appeared in his mind. Besides fragments of pure Chi Yan's laws, there were also scattered memory fragments. These were the past experiences of a blind cultivator who achieved reverence through fire. The power displayed by this blind cultivator in the memory made Li Fan's blood run cold.

In a desolate, ice-cold starfield with no discernible end, the blind cultivator sat in contemplation. After an unknown number of years, specks of fire began to gather around the cultivator. The frigid starfield gradually grew warm, then intensely hot. Finally, the entire starfield was incinerated by an incorporeal flame, becoming a void of nothingness where even cold ceased to exist. In the final scene, the blind cultivator seemed to vanish from existence.

Li Fan, who had now achieved Dao integration with the Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth, possessed the strength of a half-immortal despite being merely in the Dao integration realm. Therefore, he could truly appreciate the immense power displayed by the blind cultivator in the memory. "Merely the phenomenon caused by his enlightenment was so terrifying." "A True Immortal... it must have been a True Immortal!" Li Fan was profoundly shaken.

But soon, he realized something even more astonishing. "Wait, what I just saw..." "A True Immortal's enlightenment, vanishing from existence." "Was this the moment he achieved the state of a Nameless True Immortal?" Li Fan was once again terrified, his body trembling uncontrollably. His thoughts raced. Within moments, Li Fan vaguely deduced the reason behind this.

"The Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth are the manifestations of the Xuanhuang Realm's laws, generated from the imprints left by cultivators throughout history." "Even after the Xuanhuang Realm ascended to the Immortal Realm, this characteristic was retained. The Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth are also the laws of the Xuanhuang Immortal Realm, manifested through deeper imprints in heaven and earth." "They resonate with the Dao, or even merge with it. Those who resonate most deeply with various laws would naturally be the Nameless True Immortal who once 'achieved Dao through Dao'!" "Once they enter the state of being 'Nameless,' they vanish from existence. All the Xuanhuang Immortal Realm could perceive was his final moments before achieving Dao..." Li Fan's expression grew solemn. After achieving enlightenment, the Nameless True Immortal *became* the Great Dao itself. He knew that if his guess was correct, what he had just absorbed was the enlightenment of a Nameless True Immortal from his past journey of achieving Dao! Even if it was just a trace among the scattered light particles. For Li Fan, who had just stepped into the Immortal Realm, it was undoubtedly a tremendous benefit.

Carefully replaying the thoughts in his mind, after a brief moment of excitement, Li Fan suddenly felt something was amiss. "Beyond True Immortal, achieving the state of 'Nameless' through Dao. Each path is different. The Dao of Fire is already occupied. What use is it to me?" "Unless..." "That blind Nameless True Immortal is already dead." The more Li Fan thought about it, the more likely it seemed. He quickly scanned the surrounding Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth. It was extremely rare for them to evolve into human-like cultivators, like Chi Yan; there were only three such instances. "If I absorb them, I should also be able to perceive the visions of the corresponding Nameless True Immortal achieving reverence in the past!" As Li Fan was about to act, his expression suddenly changed. In the time it took him to ponder, the effect of the frozen black and white world had shrunk again. It was now reduced to a spherical area with a radius of only ninety-nine feet around him. Coincidentally, there were no Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth within this area. A sense of helplessness surged through Li Fan. "So, besides absorbing objects within the frozen world accelerating its collapse, lingering for too long also..." "This reserved area after activating 'True Return' does not last indefinitely. It seems the duration is very short." Li Fan now understood the new changes that had occurred with 'True Return' after he had achieved Dao integration, or rather, reached the half-immortal realm. That is, after activating 'True Return,' everything in the world would not immediately become illusory. Instead, a large area centered on Li Fan would remain in a black and white, frozen state. As for how large this area was, Li Fan hadn't had time to verify. However, it should be extremely vast; at least the entire Xuanhuang Immortal Realm, as far as Li Fan could see, was covered by it. Li Fan also speculated that the effective range and duration of the black and white frozen area might be directly correlated with his strength. He had only just entered the Immortal Realm, so the effects he could maintain were naturally very limited. "Let's temporarily call this black and white frozen area the 'Hidden Dao' zone." "Within the Hidden Dao zone, all things except me seem to be in a superimposed state of 'both true and false.' Maintaining the Hidden Dao zone also requires certain energy related to 'True Return.' When I touch or perceive things within the Hidden Dao zone, it is equivalent to dragging them from the 'both true and false' state to the 'true' state, like myself. The energy to maintain the Hidden Dao zone is then consumed in large quantities, causing the Hidden Dao zone to shrink significantly..." Even though he was left with no room to maneuver, Li Fan did not immediately leave the Hidden Dao zone. He had already realized that being in the Hidden Dao zone made it easier to comprehend the 'Transformation of Truth and Falsehood.' It was tens of thousands of times easier than in the normal world. Every extra moment spent there was of infinite benefit to him. "When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth." Li Fan pondered and comprehended the essence of 'True Return.' At the same time, he looked around at the boundary of the Hidden Dao zone, ninety-nine feet away. Like the previous 'True Return,' it was now enveloped by layers of mist. "Truth is falsehood. Falsehood is truth." Li Fan's brow furrowed, desperately trying to decipher the most ethereal and profound principles in the world. After a while, the range of the Hidden Dao zone shrunk again. Rolling mist engulfed everything except Li Fan. Li Fan's consciousness slowly descended into darkness. However, this time, Li Fan did not fall into a complete coma, losing all consciousness. He remained half-awake, half-asleep, and in a daze, he seemed to see a boundless bright light erupting from the darkness. In the blinding white light, countless things, people, and objects appeared. When Li Fan's consciousness fully cleared... Anchor point: 1 year, Mount Solitude! Li Fan's expression was somewhat dazed. He stretched out his hands, examining them carefully. Everything that had happened from 'True Return' until now felt extremely unreal. His thoughts were still immersed in comprehending the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. A full day and night passed before Li Fan finally ceased his contemplation, unable to catch any more sparks of inspiration. Li Fan's attention then focused on the 'True Return' prompt.

[Simulation ended.]

[Choose one option to retain from the following:]

[1. One item currently held in this simulation.]

[2. One's own cultivation realm from this simulation.]

[3. Simulated memory of a person closely related to oneself. This memory can be inherited by that person.]

[4. Abandon the above choices and speed up the recharge progress.]

"I have already achieved half-immortal status, yet there is no additional prompt for inheriting an extra option." "It seems my attainment of half-immortal status was well within 'True Return's' predictions." Li Fan said with a touch of self-deprecation. "However, the newly born Xuanhuang Immortal Realm does not count as an extra variable, but descending from beyond the High Wall... does?" Li Fan fell into a period of contemplation. Then, he shook his head and came to his senses. "Overthinking is useless. Since I have achieved half-immortal status, I am invincible in the Star Sea." "This lifetime, I must look beyond the High Wall." "Whatever mysteries exist, I will explore them!" After overcoming many challenges, he finally achieved Dao integration and the half-immortal realm. Although far from perfect, he was nevertheless an immortal, superior to all mortals. For the four options of 'True Return,' he would definitely choose to retain his cultivation. However...

Walking slowly to the edge of the cliff on Mount Solitude, he looked up at the weak Great Xuan Small World, and even the Xuanhuang Realm. Li Fan couldn't help but sigh. "If I were to inherit my cultivation here, the Great Xuan Small World would probably be torn apart by the ascension phenomena immediately." "Even the Xuanhuang Realm, stitched together from various realms, would shatter and fall into the Immortal Ruins due to the immense shock." "Forget it!" "There is still a use for them." Li Fan's expression turned solemn, and he softly chanted, "Falsehood is truth." Instantly, the feeling of peak half-immortal cultivation from his previous life, after achieving half-immortal status, descended upon Li Fan's body. Due to the prolonged contemplation in the Hidden Dao zone, Li Fan's understanding of the 'Transformation of Truth and Falsehood' had significantly advanced. Compared to the past, when the visualized cultivation could only last for a fleeting moment, it could now persist for three full breaths. As he chanted, Li Fan had fully regained his peak half-immortal strength from his previous life. Within the first breath, Li Fan drew his wooden sword and had already arrived in the depths of the vast, empty Star Sea. Within the second breath, Li Fan chose the option to inherit his cultivation through 'True Return.' In the Star Sea, winds surged and waves roared like a tempest! Centered around Li Fan, who descended like an immortal, the remnants of True Immortal script power formed a terrifying storm that shook the entire Star Sea. As if being drawn, the remnants of True Immortal script power, dormant in various parts of the Star Sea, converged towards the eye of the storm like a hundred rivers returning to the sea. The situation seemed to be escalating. The third breath passed, and Li Fan had completely inherited the cultivation from his Dao integration with the Celestial Souls of Heaven and Earth. In this lifetime, since Xuan Tian King achieved Dao tens of thousands of years ago, he was finally the second half-immortal! "It truly is 'True Return.'" Li Fan marveled as he felt the infinite power surging within him, deep and profound. Unlike the visualized cultivation derived from his understanding of truth and falsehood, which was like a rootless duckweed and could dissipate at any moment, 'True Return' made the false truly real. Half-immortal Li Fan looked at the increasingly powerful storm of True Immortal remnants in the surroundings and slowly extended his left hand. The surging, expanding storm instantly halted, then was continuously drawn into Li Fan's hand. In just a few breaths, this terrifying calamity, capable of plunging the Star Sea into further ruin, was completely nullified by Li Fan. Li Fan curled his lips, looking at the collection of True Immortal remnants in his hand, like a wad of paper scrawled with countless different characters. Even without deliberately shielding himself with power, these ancient calamities, which Li Fan had previously viewed as formidable dangers and needed to be constantly wary of, could not harm him in the slightest. "It's not that these remnants have lost their effectiveness." "It's that the laws they constructed cannot affect me, who have already become an 'Immortal.'" "After all, they are just residual echoes of True Immortal scripts." Li Fan was quite satisfied with his strength after his advancement. "In fact, aside from lacking Immortal Spiritual Energy, I am no different from True Immortals of the past. At the very least, in terms of status, we are equal." "Immortal Spiritual Energy..." Li Fan's attention shifted to the Bound Object he had bound: the Dissolution Disc. Normally, bound objects, regardless of any changes in reincarnation, damage, or sublimation, would not affect the binding space of 'True Return.' Once 'True Return' was activated, they would revert to their initial bound state. But now... Li Fan willed it, and the Dissolution Disc was summoned. In his sea of consciousness, countless stars seemed to rise, dazzling and bright. [Dissolution Disc, Immortal Rank], had returned to the present along with Li Fan! "Just like the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone from before." Li Fan looked at the '[...] leg bone' in 'True Return's' binding space, lost in thought. "Perhaps only beings like True Immortals are qualified to be brought along by me through the transformation of truth and falsehood."

Chapter 1405: Ominous Signs

Li Fan carefully examined the [Dissolution Disc, Immortal Tier].

In his previous life, Li Fan had already deeply experienced the terrifying power of the Dissolution Disc after it was officially promoted to an immortal artifact. With a single thought, Immortal Formations could be formed. Once an Immortal Formation was formed, it could slay gods and destroy immortals!

Mo Sha, among all the Heavenly and Earthly Spirits, was one of the most powerful. When it completed the transformation from mortal to immortal along with the Xuanhuang Realm, its strength in the Heavenly and Earthly Spirit state was imaginable.

A dark ink-like substance obscured Li Fan's eyes. His right fingertip also surged with countless wriggling black dots. Li Fan extended his right hand, gently pressing the wisp of ink onto the True Immortal residual energy conglomerate held in his left hand. The True Immortal residual energy, which was ravaging the Star Sea, could not resist under the erosion of Mo Sha's power and was completely annihilated by the dense ink, disappearing from the world.

The ink tide surged ceaselessly, and when it receded, Li Fan's hands were empty.

"It can annihilate True Immortal residual energy, and even against True Immortals, it wouldn't be too far behind. The benefits of promotion through the new method are evident. As long as it consumes enough Heavenly and Earthly Spirit energy, it can be instantly transformed into its own use."

"With Mo Sha's protection, even I, a 'half-immortal,' despite lacking Immortal Spiritual Energy and other means befitting an immortal, can still roam and crush the Star Sea."

"But my true trump card is still the [All-Tiers Dissolution Disc]!"

In Li Fan's mind, countless Dissolution Discs shone brightly. Silver-white starlight emanated from each star, flowing and converging. It appeared in Li Fan's palm.

"Mo Sha's power as a Heavenly and Earthly Spirit is already so formidable. Yet, before the Dissolution Disc, capable of forming true Immortal Formations, it was instantly reduced to nothing like an ant!"

Li Fan, who had just achieved Dao Integration, was actually not much stronger than Mo Sha as a Heavenly and Earthly Spirit without upgrading his other divine abilities to the half-immortal level. Facing the Immortal Formation he set up himself, it was equally defenseless.

"Like a toddler holding an immortal treasure, its offensive and defensive capabilities are completely disproportionate."

"And the reason for this absurd situation..."

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, attempting to draw the silver starlight in his palm into his body. However, it remained unmoved.

"Immortal Spiritual Energy. But I cannot use it?"

The Dissolution Disc exhibited performance beyond Li Fan's imagination because, in his previous life, at the critical moment of his Dao Integration, Li Fan had drawn a wisp of Immortal Spiritual Energy obtained from the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable's legacy and gave it to the Dissolution Disc. After obtaining Immortal Spiritual Energy, the Dissolution Disc underwent a true transformation. Moreover, this transformation seemed more thorough than that of the Xuanhuang Realm and Li Fan.

To verify his conjecture, Li Fan's thoughts stirred slightly, and the Dissolution Disc's countless stars shone. Immortal Spiritual Energy flowed, instantly forming a miniature Immortal Formation before Li Fan. It appeared as a palm-sized silver ring, but it was actually based on the [Bewilderment, Xuanhuang All Beings] Great Formation, with the laws of the [Detain] Script integrated within.

One ring would fly out and easily suppress all existences below the immortal level.

The Dissolution Disc continued to shine, and one silver ring after another appeared. They were arranged in a row before Li Fan, totaling ninety-nine rings, before the Dissolution Disc could no longer sustain itself and was forced to stop. The energy contained within each silver ring was far greater than the mortal Bewilderment Great Formation that Li Fan had painstakingly set up to cover the entire Xuanhuang Realm in his previous life. After all, the gap between Immortal and Mortal was immeasurable. Even after being promoted to an immortal artifact, forming ninety-nine Immortal Formations at once seemed to have reached its limit.

Li Fan stared at the Dissolution Disc, which seemed to have depleted its Immortal Spiritual Energy. He saw new Immortal Spiritual Energy slowly regenerating within the countless star-like sub-discs! Li Fan was certain that during this process of depletion and regeneration, the Dissolution Disc did not absorb any energy from the outside.

"In a sense, it's infinite." Li Fan pondered.

At the same time, he felt a hint of regret and profound confusion.

"After Nameless succeeded the Great Celestial Venerable, I once used the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao to observe and inspect the remaining four Immortal Artifacts."

"There was indeed Immortal Spiritual Energy within them, but it depleted with use. They could not be like the Immortal Tier Dissolution Disc, with inexhaustible Immortal Spiritual Energy!"

"What exactly is the reason for this?" Li Fan's eyes flickered, his thoughts churning.

After a long period of contemplation, he tentatively concluded: "Perhaps it was a deliberate restriction placed by the Immortal Realm when gifting the Xuanhuang Immortal Artifact."

"However, now that the Immortal Realm is destroyed, and the newly born Immortal Artifacts are free from the constraints of the upper realm, they have reverted to their original properties."

"But..." Li Fan felt something was still wrong. If it were simply a matter of regenerating Immortal Spiritual Energy, then the Great Celestial Venerates of Xuanhuang in previous generations should have destroyed all the old Immortal Artifacts and forged new ones.

"Perhaps it has something to do with the Dissolution Disc itself."

After a long while, Li Fan suddenly understood something.

"The Ultimate Dissolution Disc was formed by the fusion of the Ultimate Disc and the Dissolution Disc. Both of these are secondary products of the Tianxuan Realm."

"The Tianxuan Mirror was one of the Immortal Artifacts brought back by Xuan Tian King from the Immortal Realm."

"In a sense, the Dissolution Disc itself is a descendant of an immortal artifact."

"Moreover..." Li Fan's mind recalled the process of obtaining the Dissolution Disc. Gu Xinghan, the disciple of the Medicine King Sect who possessed Li Fan's transformed body as the Dissolution Disc, coincidentally obtained the Ultimate Disc. The two approached and gradually merged. After Gu Xinghan's death, this item was buried deep underground with him, enduring thousands of years. It could be said that the birth of the Dissolution Disc was an event with an extremely low probability and immense difficulty.

"Perhaps the simple fusion of two secondary products is not enough. It also requires the tempering of time, and even the destruction and rebirth of a realm, to be qualified for promotion to an immortal artifact..."

Li Fan only then truly understood how fortunate it was to have obtained the Dissolution Disc back then. Although he couldn't grasp the principle, Li Fan now possessed this immortal artifact anyway.

Li Fan was very satisfied with the Dissolution Disc's power, but his only frustration was that he, personally, could not absorb or utilize the Immortal Spiritual Energy generated within the immortal artifact. Li Fan made further attempts to channel the Immortal Spiritual Energy from the Dissolution Disc into other items, such as the Myriad Beast Crystal Condensate and the Dao Transformation Stone, and so on. But without exception, the silver starlight passed straight through, with no lingering effect. Furthermore, the items that received the infusion seemed to not even perceive the presence of Immortal Spiritual Energy.

"It seems this inexhaustible Immortal Spiritual Energy can only be used by the Dissolution Disc itself."

"It's not that I can't, but that no one can." Li Fan shook his head slightly, pondering inwardly.

"No wonder Xuan Tian King, despite gathering so many treasures from the Immortal Realm, still found it so difficult to advance from the half-immortal realm."

"Between artifacts, and between artifacts and Immortals, are vastly different."

"Perhaps even the True Immortal Nameless, and the True Immortal's body, could not transfer their Immortal Spiritual Energy to Xuan Tian King. Otherwise, given their relationship, and the inexhaustible nature of Immortal Spiritual Energy, Nameless Immortal would not have been stingy with helping him."

Suddenly, Li Fan recalled a past event concerning Xuan Tian King, learned from Ji Yuzhen's memories: "But I heard that Xuan Tian King could extract and refine Immortal Spiritual Energy from the Great Celestial Master Tiandu? What's the explanation for that?"

"The fragments of the Heavenly King of the Xuan Tian Sect's memory, while not entirely trustworthy."

"However, it serves as a reminder. When I return to Xuanhuang in this life, I must be wary of that enigmatic Great Celestial Master..."

Li Fan stood amidst the Star Sea, his thoughts calming down after a long time. Only then did he open the [True Return] interface to check the specific changes after his promotion to Dao Integration, reaching the half-immortal realm.

Name: Li Fan

Realm: Immortal

Physiological Age: ...

Psychological Age: ...

Void Transformation Charging Progress: 50%

Anchor Charging Progress: 0%

Current Anchors: 3

Usable Anchors: 1

Bound Items: [Nameless True Immortal's Leg Bone], [Falling Mortal], [Dissolution Disc, Immortal Tier], Dao Transformation Stone, Origin of Xuan Tian Mirror (Fragment), Tai Yan Boat, Myriad Beast Crystal Condensate, Ten Thousand Man Essence Blood.

...

When Li Fan saw the single word [Immortal] under his 'Realm' on the [True Return] panel, his eyebrows couldn't help but raise slightly.

"It seems that in the eyes of [True Return], half-immortal and immortal are essentially the same."

Li Fan gazed lovingly at the word 'Immortal' for a long time before continuing. Once one had transcended from mortal to immortal, the physiological age was no longer a constraint for Li Fan. And the psychological age limit, which had long been his only cause for concern, had also vanished. Li Fan's expression became somewhat dazed.

"It can be considered a temporary achievement of 'longevity' in the general sense." A phased goal had been achieved. As for the true 'longevity' he desired and sought, it still seemed quite distant. However, it was no longer an illusionary, unattainable prospect.

Li Fan found it strange that the physiological and psychological ages displayed on the [True Return] panel were not infinite, nor a fixed number. Instead, like the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone or the Immortal Realm copper coins he had seen before, they presented as constantly changing scenarios. Li Fan's eyes narrowed, trying to decipher what these numbers were trying to convey. He had to admit that after ascending to immortality, his status had elevated. Things that were almost impossible to achieve previously, even with great effort and facing backlash, were now easily accomplished.

"Seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand eight hundred sixty-four years, thirteen days, and seven hours..."

After seeing his lifespan limit on True Return, Li Fan's brows furrowed. Seven million three hundred thousand years was far less than he had imagined! How could it be worthy of the legendary immortals? Moreover, according to Li Fan's observation, this constantly fluctuating number did not change at a uniform rate. Most of the time, it would drop significantly after a period. Only rarely would it increase.

Li Fan stared intently at this profound number. Suddenly, an inexplicable sense of understanding surged into his heart.

"The lifespan of an immortal cannot possibly be only a few million years."

"But in [True Return]'s judgment, I can only live this long..." A golden light suddenly flashed in his eyes, and Li Fan instantly realized: "This is the lifespan within the 'mortal world,' not mine!"

As if discovering a world-shattering secret, even though Li Fan had now become a half-immortal, his heart couldn't help but pound violently.

"When that constantly fluctuating number reaches zero, the entire mortal world will face its end simultaneously."

"All living beings within it will perish together, facing eternal damnation!"

"If I were within it, and hadn't activated [True Return], the same fate would befall me!"

"No?!" Li Fan's thoughts raced, and his heart began to beat even faster.

"Previously, my psychological age did not change with True Return's state. It was only related to my own experiences."

"Then, when the psychological age merges with this number and disappears..." Li Fan's expression turned grim.

"Even if I constantly activate [True Return], this 'countdown to the end of the mortal world' cannot be altered?"

"The arrival of this true doomsday is not something I can avert through [True Return]!"

Just after ascending to immortality and before he could fully savor the joy, Li Fan was immediately confronted with the terrifying end revealed by True Return. Even with Li Fan's extraordinarily resilient spirit, he felt overwhelmed at this moment. The only good news was that there was still ample time before the true doomsday arrived. Furthermore, the number displayed by True Return was not immutable.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan gradually calmed down.

"Looking at it now, True Return is actually predicting and forecasting the lifespan of the 'mortal world'."

"It must have encountered a major problem. Perhaps even the destruction of the Immortal Realm is related to this doomsday!"

"It's not that I can't live that long, but that the world itself cannot exist that long!"

A thick cloud of gloom seemed to descend upon Li Fan's heart. The joy of ascending to immortality vanished instantly. Regardless of the fate of the mortal world's inhabitants, Li Fan, for the sake of his own pursuit of longevity, had to try and resolve this doomsday crisis.

"Perhaps, in True Return's view, only Immortals can make a difference in changing the fate of this doomsday."

"Below the Immortal level, no matter how much they struggle, they cannot alter their destiny."

"Even if it were displayed, it would be useless and only add to the worry."

Li Fan looked at the pitch-black Star Sea before him.

"Perhaps to understand the truth of the doomsday, I need to start from the Dao Annihilation Tribulation."

...

Li Fan continued to examine the remaining parts of the True Return panel. After ascending to immortality, the void transformation charging progress also saw a qualitative leap. It seemed that True Return's own abilities had been strengthened. After activating True Return and returning, it no longer required accumulating charging progress from scratch but directly completed 50% of the charging.

Chapter 1406: The Illusory Array Tricks Heavenly Doctor

In the additional simulation, I seem to not possess the True Return treasure. Aside from that, there is no difference from experiencing everything myself." Recalling the myriad images that suddenly flashed through his mind, Li Fan's expression was grave. When the Dao Annihilation black energy engulfed the falling Xuanhuang Realm, unable to escape, he made no attempt to activate True Return, simply waiting for death with resignation.

"But in the simulation, my simulated self did not feel any abnormality at the disappearance of True Return, as if my simulated self had never possessed this treasure. From the moment I activated the additional simulation, a branch was created that excluded True Return..."

"This is interesting. Even in the simulation of True Return, as long as it is an additional one, existing alongside the main simulation, can the branching simulation not simulate oneself?" Li Fan's thought moved, and a flash of inspiration suddenly crossed his mind, as if he had understood something. But this inspiration was like a candle in the darkness, instantly swallowed by the surrounding boundless darkness. When Li Fan tried to recall it later, he could not remember it no matter how hard he tried.

Knowing that he might have missed the secret of True Return, Li Fan's expression froze, and he felt a momentary sense of loss. But soon, he recovered.

Li Fan believed that as his comprehension of [True-False Transformation] continued to improve, and his compatibility with True Return deepened, he would eventually uncover the secret of [True Return] completely and thoroughly.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan composed himself and carefully pondered the experiences in the branching simulation. "Xuanhuang's sublimation plan proceeded almost as I anticipated. There were no major flaws in the preparations, and no unexpected enemies appeared. The only obstacle to Xuanhuang's ascension was that it was always a hair's breadth away from the final qualitative transformation. This is the starting point of the heaven-and-earth difference between Immortal and Mortal."

Or should I still use the Immortal Realm chess pieces? Or, based on the remnants of the ancient immortal formations, try to repair the Star Crossing Great Formation?"

Each attempt involved endless possibilities. Most existences related to 'Immortal' were completely unknown variables, not something Li Fan could deduce now. Li Fan's head ached, but he could not choose the most suitable plan. It seemed that each method could work, yet each method might also fail.

Li Fan stopped thinking about the conditions required for Xuanhuang's sublimation and ascension. Instead, he began to consider how to end this life and begin the next. The plan was excellent. But for some reason, Li Fan felt somewhat uneasy. Theoretically, everything in the simulation could be reproduced through another simulation. For Li Fan, there was truly nothing that could be 'lost' in the world. Except for Li Fan's own changes.

Every time True Return activated the simulation and returned to the predetermined anchor. Everything in the world was reset. Even Li Fan's physical strength and cultivation were the same. He needed to rely on True Return's inherited cultivation function to return to the state of the previous simulation.

However, within each reset, there was a variable that constantly moved forward. That was Li Fan's will! Specifically reflected on the True Return interface, it was Li Fan's maximum psychological age and the default True Return charging progress. And these two factors had not changed for a long time...

Li Fan's heart was filled with unprecedented hesitation at this moment. Time ticked by, and Li Fan could not make a final decision. There were only ten hours left until Li Fan initiated Xuanhuang's ascension in the branching simulation of the Three-pronged Tree technique.

Li Fan's expression was inscrutable. He took a step forward and arrived at the origin of everything. The humble mortal body of Da Xuan, the house where he lived during his lifetime. Even though "Li Fan" had mysteriously disappeared, the study remained spotless, just as it had always been. Clearly, that "aunt" still held some hope for "Li Fan's" return.

Li Fan lay on the bed and closed his eyes. It was as if he had returned to the moment he first transmigrated. Time seemed to freeze. Then, it flowed quietly, as if ice was breaking.

Having undergone a hundred lifetimes of reincarnation, all his experiences flashed through Li Fan's mind in an instant. Li Fan attempted to find a way to break through the deadlock in this manner. Day turned into night, and Li Fan lay quietly on the wooden bed. It was as if he had fallen into a deep sleep.

Yes, Li Fan could indeed use repeated True Return simulations, and through elimination, determine one by one the key factors for achieving qualitative change. This was also the most stable approach. Theoretically, there were no problems. But every time Li Fan decided to do so, inexplicable images would flash through his mind. It was the persistence of Mo Rubin, who, despite the flaws in the High Wall, disregarded his own life to investigate; and the Heavenly Physician in the illusion formation, who ultimately gave up on comprehending the High Wall for the sake of the Heavenly Law Realm.

With True Return around, there was indeed nothing in the world that could be "forever lost" to him. Unless that item's rank was even higher than True Return. Obviously, mere transformation from mortal to immortal was not enough to achieve that.

"True 'loss is forever loss' exists within my heart."

"True Return can influence everything in the world, but it cannot reverse my changes." As if understanding something, Li Fan's gaze seemed to penetrate the darkness, gradually brightening.

"The loss of this unknown characteristic might not affect my advancement to the True Immortal realm. But for the path beyond True Immortal, it might have profound implications!"

After a long period of contemplation, as a ray of sunlight appeared on the earth, dispelling the darkness, Li Fan finally understood completely. Where the unease in his heart originated.

"Why is it like this?"

"Is it due to over-reliance on [True Return]?"

"Or something else?"

"The path beyond True Immortal is too distant for me. Moreover, with my understanding, the Nameless True Immortal realm seems to only require complete mastery and refinement of a certain Great Dao. It doesn't seem related..." Li Fan frowned tightly, filled with confusion.
