"But it seems I have no better option than exhaustive trials."

...

Li Fan walked out of the house, looking at the rising sun on the horizon. While continuing to ponder, he stepped away from the Great Xuan Small World. He paced around within the Xuanhuang Realm. The surrounding scenery jumped and changed incessantly, as Li Fan's mind reflected everything around him. Starting from the Sea of Eastern Clouds, heading west. As his thoughts churned, the frequency of the surrounding scenery's changes seemed to accelerate.

Li Fan, immersed in a state of meditation akin to enlightenment, did not alter his outward output. The reason he "walked" faster and faster. It was precisely because of the special relationship between Li Fan and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. Like a reborn parent, its favorability was extremely high. Therefore, without Li Fan's prompting, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao proactively helped Li Fan lighten the burden of travel. Even though the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao did not know why Li Fan was randomly moving around the world inexplicably. Perhaps it mistakenly believed that Li Fan was making final preparations for the sublimation and ascension.

Li Fan naturally noticed the favor shown by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. But he didn't pay much attention. Previously, when the Nameless Great Celestial Venerable traveled throughout the land to repair various damages to the Xuanhuang Realm, the Xuanhuang Realm had also provided such convenience. With one step, the distance between heaven and earth transformed, as if shrinking the ground into inches. However, now that the anomalies in various places had been resolved, the Xuanhuang Realm had not actively done so for a long time.

"What a servant!" In the branching simulation, upon seeing the true face of the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan cursed inwardly. "I possess supreme escape techniques, why would I need your rudimentary convenience?"

With a thought, the phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed and appeared at Li Fan's side. Just as he was about to fly away, escape the entanglement of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, and seize the last moment to calmly ponder. But Li Fan's movement suddenly halted. He looked at the phantom of the wooden sword beside him. His mind recalled the performance of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao when it provided convenience. A subtle expression gradually appeared on Li Fan's face.

"My supreme escape technique is the fusion of my understanding of the unwavering pursuit of the sword path, the transformation of truth and falsehood, and..."

"The teachings of Xuan Tian King, from the soul memory of Dharma King Ji Yuzhen of the Xuan Tian Sect."

"The core of the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!"

"The Horizon Instantaneous Formation was also obtained by Xuan Tian King from the Immortal Realm..." Li Fan rapidly recalled his past experiences.

Xuan Tian King said gently to Ji Yuzhen: "The Golden Lock Dangling Formation spans across all heavens. Even if the target is at the far end of the star sea, as long as it is locked, the chain can arrive instantly and capture it. I told you before that the reason this effect can be achieved is because it is embedded with the [Horizon Instantaneous] Formation. This formation was originally inscribed on the Ascension Platform in the Immortal Realm. When I escaped, I moved the entire immortal formation down..."

Boom! Xuan Tian King's voice, like thunderclaps, traversed the ancient past, piercing the mist, illuminating Li Fan's mind.

"Wait! Could it be..." A flash of brilliance appeared in Li Fan's eyes. He waved his hand, dispersing the phantom of the wooden sword beside him. He continued to pace slowly through the Xuanhuang Realm.

As expected, soon after sensing Li Fan's actions, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao began its act of showing favor. Li Fan exerted no effort of his own; it acted on its own. The surrounding scenery changed rapidly. Li Fan closed his eyes, sensing the changes occurring in the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth around him.

"This feeling..."

"It's correct!"

"It's the Horizon Instantaneous Formation!" Li Fan's figure suddenly stopped. His heart was uncontrollably excited.

His thoughts raced: "As part of the Star Crossing Great Formation, the Golden Lock Dangling Formation, though damaged..."

"But each time this formation is used, it consumes a great deal. Xuan Tian King, who was planning for unforeseen circumstances, had long ago replicated three copies as a backup."

"The Horizon Instantaneous Formation is not critical. The key is..." A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he scanned the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth.

"Ascension Platform! Inscribed! Complete!" Li Fan's body trembled slightly with excitement due to this guess.

"The Ascension Platform must have been the place where the Immortal Realm received cultivators from the lower realms."

"Being named Ascension, besides the Horizon Instantaneous Formation, there must be other powers inscribed within."

"At that time, Xuan Tian King was also fleeing in a panic, and he had only just entered the Immortal Realm. He was completely incapable of separating the Horizon Instantaneous Formation alone in such a short time."

"Therefore, it is highly likely that the three copies of the inscription left by Xuan Tian King were the complete inscriptions on the Immortal Realm's Ascension Platform!"

"This might be the key!" Even without one hundred percent certainty, Li Fan had undoubtedly found the most likely factor to achieve the final qualitative leap. From his experiences over so many years, Li Fan had never dared to underestimate anything from the Immortal Realm.

Chapter 1407: Xuanhuang is Sliced

"Moreover, after True Return's upgrade, the Void Transformation charging progress directly jumped to 50%. Its charging speed also greatly increased. It will only take less than a year to complete the remaining 50% charge. Even..."

"'The charging upper limit has also doubled from 200% to 400%. This is the value that was previously only achievable after absorbing the Dangling Puppet of the Hanging Hand for the first time. Now, it is normal for me. Furthermore, the defensive strength of True Return is also incomparably superior to before. It will no longer be like paper in front of True Immortals, as it was in the past.'"

"'As expected, the strength True Return can exhibit is directly related to my own strength. Once I step into the Immortal realm, the changes in True Return will follow accordingly. This is what can be observed on the surface.'"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, carefully sensing. He nodded slightly, very satisfied.

At the end of the [True Return] panel are the anchors and bound items. Three predetermined anchors. The first is the moment Li Fan first entered this world. It was set the moment he transmigrated, a complete mortal. The second anchor was at the summit of Solitude Mountain, with the Canghai Pearl as the foundation building spiritual object, at the late Foundation Establishment stage. The third anchor was also at the summit of Solitude Mountain, at the late Foundation Establishment stage. However, [True Return] served as the foundation building spiritual object.

"'The display order of True Return's bound items has also changed subtly. It is no longer arranged as it was in the past, by binding order. Instead, it seems to be arranged according to their 'rank'?'"

Li Fan looked at the bound item list where '[Nameless True Immortal's Leg Bone]' was at the forefront and '[Myriad Man Essence Blood]' was at the end, pondering.

After a moment, Li Fan closed the panel. Without much hesitation, he dropped the last empty anchor at this point in time. True Return's fourth anchor was thus set.

Location: The center of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Cultivation: Half-immortal!

"'After stepping into the Half-immortal realm, it's like starting from a new stage. The Immortal Realm has long been destroyed. Finding the path after Half-immortal is not easy. My strength will not increase significantly for the time being. It is expected that new reincarnation will start from this anchor for a long time to come...'"

"'The main goal of this life is to collect and integrate all usable resources within the High Wall. And begin to explore outside the High Wall.'"

"'Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable, Heavenly Physician, Great Law Master, Hungering Immortal...'"

"'Hmph.'"

Li Fan sneered coldly.

"'Oh, and the Xuanhuang Realm and the Xuanxian Boat. These two places, which I couldn't obtain before due to insufficient strength, can finally be completely scoured now.'"

"'After ascending to the Immortal realm, my perspective will naturally be different. Perhaps in this life, I will discover more interesting things from the Xuanxian Boat. And the true secret of Sun Piaomiao's 遗物.'"

Li Fan's expression was inscrutable, his gaze flickered towards the location of the Xuanxian Boat at the other end of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. The 'Immortal's Momentum' was already fixed at the highest point of the Star Sea. Looking down from above, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, which formerly seemed vast and boundless, now appeared like a pond to Li Fan, visible at a glance.

"'However, I must not become too arrogant.'"

"'I will act after True Return is fully charged.'"

Li Fan slowly withdrew his gaze after a long time, thinking in his heart.

"'Anyway, True Return's charging speed has become extremely fast now.'"

Having said that, Li Fan did not return to the Xuanhuang Realm. Instead, he stayed in the center of the Star Sea. While waiting for True Return to finish charging, Li Fan did not idle around. He used this spare time to sort out his past learning and knowledge, especially the True Immortal Script. When he was mortal, through countless reincarnations, Li Fan felt he had already studied the True Immortal Script to its limit. Even though there was still a gap between it and the characters representing the Great Dao itself, it wouldn't be too far off.

But now, from the 'Immortal's' perspective, when he revisited it, he realized he was completely wrong! Although he saw the same patterns, the perspective of an immortal and a mortal were indeed different. There were too many details that were ignored and overlooked when he was mortal. Recalling the True Immortal Scripts he had written in the past, Li Fan couldn't help but shake his head repeatedly.

"'It's simply like a child's scribbles!'"

"'Speaking of which, those True Immortal Scripts that caused the calamity in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, seemingly originating from the imitation brush of a certain Immortal, don't seem very aesthetically pleasing either. If I study them for a while longer, it wouldn't be difficult to surpass them.'"

Li Fan scoffed.

"'Currently, the True Immortal characters I know, setting aside their specific powers, are divided into three tiers in terms of authenticity. The first tier is the imitation brush from a certain Immortal, such as '[Ancient]' and '[Chaos]', all falling into this category. The second tier is the genuine True Immortal Scripts from the Immortal Realm, such as '[Hunger]' and '[Return]', all belonging to this category. In terms of both aesthetics and practicality, they are superior to the brushstrokes of that certain Immortal.'"

"'As for the third tier, which is closest to the Great Dao itself, it is manifested through the leg bone of the Nameless True Immortal, such as '[Detain]', '[Innate]', and '[Immortal-Mortal Transformation]...'"

In Li Fan's mind, the greatest contributor to his advancement to the Half-immortal realm resurfaced. Even though he had ascended to immortality, he still felt that this character contained endless mysteries. He was so immersed that he couldn't extricate himself.

A year passed in the blink of an eye. Two years for the anchor. After True Return was fully charged, Li Fan also woke up from his seclusion. A year was not enough for him to completely sort out his learning. Fortunately, he could multitask, organizing and improving himself while not neglecting important matters.

After achieving Half-immortal status, the first thing Li Fan had to do was to meet his old acquaintances: the Heavenly Physician and the Law-Transmitting Celestial Venerable. Li Fan had already vaguely pinpointed the locations of these two Supremes of the Grand Void in the Star Sea. Indeed, they were diligently lingering in the ruined Great Wall beneath the High Wall, collecting resources for the revival of the Heavenly Law Realm.

Li Fan's gaze flickered, and with a single step, he crossed half the Star Sea. First, he arrived before the Heavenly Physician. Without letting the Heavenly Physician notice, a silver halo was directly cast upon him. It was one of the ninety-nine Immortal Formation rings that Li Fan had refined using the Dissolution Disc!

While the Heavenly Physician was searching for suitable materials among the numerous ruined realms, he suddenly felt a flicker of illusion before his eyes. When he recovered, the vast, dead, ruined Great Wall surrounding him had inexplicably disappeared.

Before the Heavenly Physician's eyes appeared a vibrant world, one that he was extremely familiar with. The Heavenly Law Realm! Cloud Water Celestial Palace, Heavenly Law Pavilion, Heavenly Sword Valley... Seeing his homeland, which he yearned for but had been separated from by life and death long ago, the Heavenly Physician was stunned. He landed on the ground and personally touched every blade of grass and tree. His cloudy eyes were filled with nostalgia and disbelief.

But being the Heavenly Physician, he quickly woke up from the beautiful dream Li Fan had woven for him. Or rather, Li Fan had intentionally left loopholes. Because at this moment, in the Heavenly Law Realm before the Heavenly Physician, there was no one! Only the newly born "world" itself existed. Besides that, there was nothing else!

The Heavenly Physician's expression gradually turned solemn. Thousands of golden threads shot out from him, attempting to comprehend the truth behind the strange phenomenon that had suddenly appeared before him. But to his shock, the golden threads, which had always been effective, all dimmed and dissipated in mid-air shortly after leaving his body.

The Heavenly Physician took a deep breath, suppressing the shock in his heart. While slowly flying, he carefully searched the Heavenly Law Realm. But he could find no flaws whatsoever. Moreover, besides himself, there were no other living beings. After such a search three times, the Heavenly Physician was finally convinced of his predicament. The look of shock on his face could no longer be suppressed. The Heavenly Physician's aura began to become somewhat chaotic.

The scene before his eyes, although it was what he had always longed for, the Heavenly Physician understood that it could not possibly be real. It was merely a false image created to trap and delude him. The Heavenly Physician attempted to break out of this illusion. But after an unknown amount of time, it was still in vain.

The Heavenly Physician looked up at the sky, opened his mouth, seeming to want to say something. But ultimately, he did not speak. On his aged face, there was no expression of resignation or despair. His eyes became even more resolute. This time, he did not wander aimlessly. Instead, he stood in the void and meticulously observed the surrounding "illusion."

The Heavenly Physician's mind immersed itself in the contemplation of the "world" before his eyes. At times, he frowned deeply; at others, he seemed to come to a sudden realization. After an unknown amount of time, a voice suddenly rang in his ears.

"Can you understand it?"

It seemed to be a question, or perhaps a mockery. Like a thunderclap, it jolted the Heavenly Physician awake. A figure in white clothes appeared beside him at some unknown time. A lean young man looked at him with a half-smile. No aura was revealed from his body, but his eyes were like the boundless, vast Star Sea, unfathomable. Even the Heavenly Physician, who was at the peak of the Star Sea's capacity, felt a frantic alarm within his heart as this young man appeared.

Suppressing the shock in his heart, the Heavenly Physician clasped his hands and said neither servilely nor arrogantly, "Reporting to senior, I can understand one or two points."

The young man, who was merely a projection of Li Fan within the formation, smiled slightly, "Not bad. I didn't expect that in such a barren lower realm, someone like you could emerge."

"Very good!"

Li Fan clapped his hands, seeming extremely appreciative. "After I woke up, I found my seclusion grounds suddenly surrounded by a High Wall. I originally intended to investigate here, but unexpectedly discovered the two of you..."

"Is this world created for you? How is it, does it meet your desires?"

The few words spoken contained an immense amount of information. The Heavenly Physician's thoughts raced, analyzing the unfathomable young man before him. The Heavenly Physician naturally could not guess the other party's strength based on his apparent age.

"To be able to trap me silently, and that formless imposing aura..."

"Lower realm, woke up."

"He must be a True Immortal."

"Not the one in the Immortal Ruins who achieved enlightenment."

"When did another True Immortal appear in this Star Sea?"

The Heavenly Physician was filled with doubt.

Chapter 1408: The Mystery of the Final Transmission of Dharma

A thin young boy, appearing no older than seven or eight years old, lay on the thatched roof, gazing at the sky.

Upon hearing his mother's call, he was about to get up when he lost his footing and fell directly from the roof.

Fortunately, he landed on a haystack below, avoiding injury.

Gou Dan seemed accustomed to this, patting himself down and straightening his clothes. He then ran home.

At the dinner table, his mother, while serving Gou Dan food, admonished him, "You went to the village head's east end to play again? I told you to stay away from that madman!"

Gou Dan ate voraciously, carelessly replying, "I think Uncle Madman is a good person. He's not as scary as you say."

Gou Dan's father, who had always been taciturn and had remained silent since the meal began, put down his chopsticks upon hearing Gou Dan's words and slapped him on the head.

"What do you know! How many people in the village didn't believe in that evil and what happened to them in the end? I told you to stay away from him, so stay away from him!"

Under the iron fist, Gou Dan dared not retort. However, he remained unconvinced in his heart and continued to eat in silence.

After this, although Gou Dan outwardly stopped going to Mad Uncle's house,

he would secretly bring some good food to visit Mad Uncle whenever he had the chance.

Mad Uncle was Gou Dan's own name for him. The villagers simply called him a madman.

He was also a member of the village, orphaned from childhood and raised by the community. He was somewhat normal when he was young, but as he entered middle age, he became somewhat eccentric.

He often muttered strange things.

Such as, "I've seen multiple versions of myself," "I'm not me at all." Sometimes he would even point at someone in the village and shout in terror, "Didn't you die already?"

And most of the villagers he cursed would indeed die suddenly shortly thereafter.

Immortals and gods indeed existed in this world. The villagers were convinced that the madman must be connected to those mysterious, unfathomable powers. To avoid further trouble, the villagers decided to unite and expel the madman.

However, it seemed there was something he cared deeply about in the village. Sensing the villagers' malice, the madman suddenly erupted and attacked them.

Gou Dan didn't know how many people died that day, but ever since then, the villagers chose to avoid and keep their distance from the madman.

Only the innocent and fearless, like Gou Dan, dared to approach the madman.

Mad Uncle always stayed in his ancestral dilapidated house, where no sunlight penetrated, and it was extremely dark. He would curl up in a corner, constantly repeating something under his breath.

Initially, Gou Dan stumbled upon it accidentally while playing a game of hide-and-seek with his friends. He was startled by the eerie and terrifying atmosphere inside the house.

However, when he heard the madman's murmurs, although he didn't understand the meaning of the syllables, Gou Dan was involuntarily captivated by them.

It was only when the increasingly urgent shouts of his playmates from outside kept coming that Gou Dan reluctantly left. Ever since then, whenever Gou Dan felt lost, he would hear Mad Uncle's murmurs in his ears.

Finally, one day, Gou Dan could no longer resist the temptation and returned to Mad Uncle's dark room.

He politely brought a roast duck.

Perhaps the aroma of the food briefly awakened Mad Uncle's sanity. He stopped mumbling, unceremoniously snatched the roast duck, and devoured it.

After a full meal, Mad Uncle, in his lucid state, only warned Gou Dan to stay away from him.

Did Gou Dan, who had been deceived into giving up a roast duck, just let it go? Naturally, he refused to leave. He even asked Mad Uncle about the phrases he had been constantly muttering.

Mad Uncle remained silent at first.

Then, he rummaged through a pile of wooden tablets in the ruined house and said that these were all ancestral tablets.

He didn't know what he was saying when he was delirious. However, this strange illness had plagued their Xuanyuan clan since ancient times.

Fortunately, only one person in each generation suffered from this peculiar illness. As the Xuanyuan clan gradually spread its branches, not many people remembered this genetic disease.

"Let this curse end here." Mad Uncle arranged the tablets in order on the ground. When it came to his turn, he only placed an empty wooden tablet.

Then, to Gou Dan's shocked eyes, all the tablets spontaneously combusted, turning into ashes in the small wooden room in an instant.

Gou Dan also asked about the inexplicable deaths of the villagers.

Mad Uncle revealed a pale smile. "Fixed deaths have nothing to do with me. The rooster crows, and the world turns white. Does the great sun in the sky really come from the rooster's crow?"

"Gou Dan, you must know that everything in the world has already happened countless times. This is just another rehearsal. Just like you..."

Mad Uncle stared intently at Gou Dan, then his expression slowly turned extremely terrified. After the fear subsided, he became delirious again. Before completely losing his mind, he casually flung Gou Dan out the door.

From that day on, Gou Dan vaguely believed that this Mad Uncle must be hiding some great secret.

Although the young Gou Dan couldn't understand Mad Uncle's words, he firmly believed that the secret hidden within Mad Uncle was likely related to the legendary immortals!

For this reason, Gou Dan racked his brains and learned Mad Uncle's real name from his father.

Xuanyuan Sheng.

Even though everyone in the village, including Gou Dan, was surnamed Xuanyuan, Gou Dan felt Mad Uncle's name was exceptionally good.

In the days that followed, Mad Uncle's madness worsened. Even Gou Dan's attempts to comfort him with food were no longer effective.

Gou Dan could only climb onto Mad Uncle's roof and close his eyes, listening to Mad Uncle's increasingly bizarre sounds from below.

Every time he listened to Mad Uncle's outwardly creepy tone, Gou Dan slept exceptionally soundly.

This continued until Gou Dan was nine years old.

One night, a tremendous noise suddenly erupted from the village. When the villagers were awakened, they discovered the explosion came from Xuanyuan Sheng's house.

By the time they rushed over, they found that for some reason, the place had been razed to the ground.

Mad Uncle's death did not cause much of a stir. In the eyes of most of the Xuanyuan clan, the disappearance of the scourge Xuanyuan Sheng was actually a good thing.

Only Gou Dan felt immense grief over Mad Uncle's death. He even took the opportunity to search the accident site carefully when no one was around. Unfortunately, he found nothing but a charred wooden tablet.

This wooden tablet was burned, with only the last corner remaining. Gou Dan, being illiterate, took it to a literate elder in the village to inquire, only to discover it was the character "Hong."

"Xuanyuan Hong."

Gou Dan had a very good memory. He vaguely remembered that when Mad Uncle arranged the tablets on the ground in order, this tablet seemed to be placed in the first position by Mad Uncle with great solemnity.

Knowing it was his ancestor's tablet, Gou Dan dared not keep it for himself.

After respectfully kowtowing, Gou Dan burned the remaining wooden tablet clean.

Xuanyuan Village, peaceful and secluded since ancient times.

After Xuanyuan Sheng's death, the village returned to its former peaceful life. Gou Dan gradually grew up, and the villagers no longer called him "Gou Dan."

Instead, they called him by his name, Xuanyuan Tuo.

Xuanyuan Tuo's life trajectory was like that of the other villagers.

Sowing, plowing, harvesting. Getting married, taking a wife, having children.

However, in his leisure time, Xuanyuan Tuo's mind would still vaguely recall Mad Uncle's murmurs from back then.

As time passed, that mystical melody remained in his mind, never fading.

As Xuanyuan Tuo grew older, his life also seemed destined.

Until, when Xuanyuan Tuo was fifty years old.

Xuanyuan Tuo's son died of illness. His wife, unable to bear the pain of a parent outliving their child, followed him in death shortly after.

Within less than half a year, Xuanyuan Tuo lost two loved ones in succession. He was heartbroken.

Feeling that life was meaningless, he always wanted to end his own life.

But at the critical moment, the mystical melody that had accompanied him since childhood sounded again, dispelling the dark thoughts in his mind.

Xuanyuan Tuo sat motionless for several days. The grief in his heart slowly subsided.

He no longer intended to remarry or have children.

Instead, a thought ignited in his heart like a flame and then spread uncontrollably.

Witnessing the passing of loved ones one by one, Xuanyuan Tuo deeply understood the fragility of life.

Thinking that he was already nearing fifty years old and would likely follow the deceased soon, Xuanyuan Tuo felt immense fear.

He neither ate nor drank, sitting motionless for two days.

Xuanyuan Tuo finally decided to cultivate the immortal path, seeking eternal life!

For an old farmer nearing fifty, the pursuit of immortality seemed like a complete joke.

Xuanyuan Tuo also knew how absurd his decision was.

So he did not announce it, but quietly packed his bags and left Xuanyuan Village.

Alone, he embarked on the path of seeking immortality.

Fortunately, the immortal path was prosperous in this era, and immortals were not reclusive. Instead, the figures of immortals flying through the void could be seen occasionally in almost every major town.

After enduring endless ridicule, Xuanyuan Tuo finally found out the location of the nearest immortal cultivation sect.

The Sect of Returning Origin!

After a thousand hardships, Xuanyuan Tuo finally arrived outside the Sect of Returning Origin.

He was shocked to find several hundred others like him gathered there. Most of them were children accompanied by attendants. Someone like him, with one foot in the grave, aspiring to cultivate, was unique.

After some inquiries, Xuanyuan Tuo finally understood why everyone was gathered outside the sect's gate. It was because it was not yet time for the Sect of Returning Origin to recruit disciples, and the sect's protective formation was activated, enveloping the mountains. This immortal blessed land was inaccessible to mortals.

Xuanyuan Tuo inquired about when the next disciple recruitment ceremony would be held. He was told it would be in three years.

He had intended to wait obediently outside the sect gate like these people. But for some reason, as Xuanyuan Tuo looked at the sect's protective formation, which everyone else feared like a tiger, he inexplicably didn't find it particularly terrifying.

Feeling a restless urge, the usually bold Xuanyuan Tuo decided to take a risk.

As a result, just as he expected, he encountered no danger and inexplicably walked all the way to the main gate of the Sect of Returning Origin!

He was overjoyed to meet an immortal elder and wanted to join the sect, but was mercilessly ridiculed by the other party.

Fortunately, just as he was about to be forcibly expelled, an elder surnamed Xu, perhaps out of pity, gave him an introductory immortal manual. He promised that if Xuanyuan Tuo could cultivate spiritual energy within a year, he could return to see him.

Although he did not officially join the sect this time, he had obtained an immortal manual. Xuanyuan Tuo treasured the book closely and bypassed the crowd still waiting at the sect gate. For safety, he also traveled a long distance to a more remote mortal town.

Xuanyuan Tuo himself was illiterate. To cultivate the manual, he sought help from others whenever he had the chance.

Although he was old, his mind was still sharp. After safely reaching his destination, Xuanyuan Tuo could already recognize most of the characters in the introductory immortal manual.

Without a master to guide him, Xuanyuan Tuo studied it himself.

The immortal manual was profound. Even an introductory cultivation technique was not something a worldly old farmer could cultivate alone.

Moreover, Xuanyuan Tuo was already past his prime. The best period for cultivation had long passed.

In addition, he had to work during the day to make a living...

In the blink of an eye, the year was almost up, and Xuanyuan Tuo, holding the immortal manual in vain, had achieved nothing.

"Even if I cultivate spiritual energy, I won't have time to go back."

Xuanyuan Tuo was almost utterly disheartened.

"Cultivation is too difficult for ordinary people like us."

He suddenly remembered the young immortal master he had seen in the city a few days ago. Barely twenty years old, he could already roam freely through the wind.

How unfair was the Heavenly Dao!

Despair, jealousy, fear...

Xuanyuan Tuo collapsed on the ground, looking up at the sky.

"Why can't everyone cultivate in this world?"

"Why is there such a restriction between heaven and earth?"

"This damned Heavenly Dao!"

Such curses were commonplace. They were happening constantly everywhere in the world, day and night.

But while Xuanyuan Tuo cursed in his heart, he again heard the familiar murmuring chant of his Mad Uncle, Xuanyuan Sheng, in his ears.

However, this time, it did not disappear quickly.

It looped over and over again, completely filling his mind!

In a trance, Xuanyuan Tuo seemed to return to his childhood.

In that eerie dark room, Mad Uncle stood among the Xuanyuan ancestor tablets filling the room, his face contorted.

"It's appearing again! Unable to be extinguished, the vengeful spirits linger!"

"Then let's all die together!"

A raging fire suddenly erupted from Xuanyuan Sheng's body.

Then he lunged towards the menacing rows of tablets.

The dark flames, from Xuanyuan Sheng's body, gradually transferred to those tablets.

Amidst Xuanyuan Sheng's frenzied laughter, the fire gradually consumed everything.

In the end, only the corner of the one with "Xuanyuan Hong" written on it remained.

Then, it was found by Xuanyuan Tuo!

【Xuanyuan Hong】!

Three large characters appeared spookily in his mind, gradually seeping bloodstain by bloodstain from a gilded color.

Then it exploded with a bang!

Xuanyuan Tuo fainted from it.

When he woke up, he stared blankly at the sky. Then he looked at himself in the mirror.

Something seemed to have changed.

Looking back at the introductory immortal manual given by the immortal elder of the Sect of Returning Origin, Xuanyuan Tuo found it incredibly easy to understand.

Even...

It was somewhat too simplistic.

Xuanyuan Tuo was no longer eager to achieve cultivation and return to join the Sect of Returning Origin.

Instead, he began to contemplate the question he had previously pondered.

"Why can't everyone cultivate in this world?"

Xuanyuan Tuo naturally knew that all living things were born with differences, and each person was unique.

But was there any way for all beings to disregard talent differences and cultivate?

The murmurs that had always accompanied him no longer sounded, and Xuanyuan Tuo felt unaccustomed to it for a moment.

But at the same time, various scenes began to continuously appear in his mind.

Some were scenes of countless plants and animals.

Some were faces both familiar and unfamiliar.

Some were scenes of conversations with unclear meanings.

"Going forth, what confidence do you have?"

"Do your best, and leave the rest to fate."

"That doesn't sound like you."

"The disparity in strength is too great; only by risking our lives can we fight."

"Fine, go then. Whether it's a blessing or a curse, who knows."

...

Xuanyuan Tuo pressed his temples.

He seemed to have forgotten some extremely important mission.

The scattered memories did not affect Xuanyuan Tuo's resolve.

Instead, with the help of these sudden fragments of memory in his mind,

Xuanyuan Tuo continued to delve deeper into the previous question.

How can everyone cultivate?

The images in his mind became more and more numerous and chaotic.

Gradually, they pieced together the life of another powerful cultivator named [Heavenly Physician Venerable].

But Xuanyuan Tuo, relying on the obsession in his heart, temporarily suppressed everything.

He continued to think mechanically.

He sat motionless in the courtyard for thirty-three days.

On this day, Xuanyuan Tuo, who had become extremely emaciated, with only a thin layer of skin clinging to his bones like a skeleton, suddenly stood up.

His eyes were as bright and dazzling as the stars in the sky.

He looked up at the heavens and whispered to himself.

"I wish to become an immortal, why seek heaven? If heaven does not grant it, I shall take it myself!"

"Following heaven leads to mortality, defying heaven..."

"Leads to immortality!"

Xuanyuan Tuo's previously hunched chest straightened instantly.

With his mortal body, he met the gaze of the heavens.

Although no special aura emanated from him, he seemed to be on equal footing.

He continued to chant, "Therefore, the path of immortality is..."

"Absorb the spiritual energy of heaven and earth, and control its flow;

Borrow the wonders of heaven and earth, to build the foundation of the Dao;

Peer into the laws of heaven and earth, to refine the Golden Core;

Seize the essence of heaven and earth, to achieve the Nascent Soul;

Extract the marrow of heaven and earth, to attain its spirit;

Sacrifice the soul of heaven and earth, to merge the body with the Dao;

Defy the principles of heaven and earth, to prove eternal life!"

Xuanyuan Tuo spoke faster and faster until, with the last sentence, he collapsed from exhaustion, laughing wildly on the ground.

Too weak, Xuanyuan Tuo, who had obtained the dao he desired, fell into a deep slumber.

The spiritual energy of heaven and earth was spontaneously drawn, rolling in like a whirlwind, lifting and encircling Xuanyuan Tuo from the ground.

After a long while, the phenomenon of spiritual energy infusion into his body gradually disappeared.

Xuanyuan Tuo slowly descended to the ground. His seventy-year-old body was filled with vitality. Although his appearance remained old, he contained boundless vitality within.

And then, after an unknown amount of time...

Xuanyuan Tuo's face, while sleeping, suddenly twitched violently.

He abruptly opened his eyes.

But there were no pupils, only eyeballs filled with whites, an eerie appearance.

His voice also became more aged and low.

"Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao is more troublesome than I thought."

"I almost completely lost myself and couldn't restore my original consciousness."

"Cough, cough, I miscalculated."

Chapter 1409: Tampering with Strength

"The Xuanhuang Realm is worthy of being a great realm with immortal lineage. The Heavenly Dao's power is far superior to the Heavenly Law Realm."

"This [Heavenly Soul Rebirth] technique completely severs the connection with the former realm, leaving only a wisp of remnant consciousness to be reborn. I have already experimented with it tens of thousands of times in the Heavenly Law Realm without failure."

"Although I anticipated some unexpected situations when dealing with the Xuanhuang Realm, the actual danger level still far exceeded my expectations."

"It took a full fifty years to awaken..."

After spending some time, the ancient voice finally spoke again, filled with disbelief.

"Strange! Heavenly Soul Rebirth uses the [Heavenly Soul] Great Dao of the Heavenly Law Realm as a sacrifice to be reborn and enter the Xuanhuang Realm, becoming a creature within the realm. This is to deceive the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao."

"The original plan was for me to awaken, then diagnose the Xuanhuang Realm, and then create a new method to sow chaos from within. But now, before my true consciousness has awakened, this body has already created the new method?!"

"To reverse the laws of heaven and earth to prove longevity..."

The Heavenly Physician became increasingly bewildered.

"This cultivation method is exactly in line with my thoughts, and even more exquisite in many details!"

Just then, as if sensing the Heavenly Physician's words, Xuanyuan Tuo's eyelids twitched violently.

The Heavenly Physician's voice began to weaken.

"No! Heavenly Soul Rebirth is superior to the soul-snatching technique. I have awakened, why does this body's consciousness still exist?"

"Xuanyuan Clan?!"

Amidst the Heavenly Physician's exclamations, Xuanyuan Tuo completely awoke from his coma.

The Heavenly Physician lost all traces of sound.

And the awakened Xuanyuan Tuo seemed completely unaware of the Heavenly Physician's existence within him. He joyfully examined his cultivation, which had already reached the Qi Refining realm.

After a while, Xuanyuan Tuo took to the air and, amidst the exclamations of the mortals in the city, soared into the sky.

Within the Immortal Formation, light and shadow shifted.

Next, Xuanyuan Tuo, relying on a vague sense in his mind, continuously searched for spiritual treasures of cultivation within the Xuanhuang Realm.

In just half a year, he established his Dao foundation with [Xuanhuang Myriad Spirits], achieved Golden Core with [Heavenly Evolution Method], and advanced to Nascent Soul with [Primal Chaos Grotto-Heaven]. He then entered the Void Transformation stage with the change of [Myriad Phenomena of Heaven and Earth]. He advanced all the way, unstoppable!

Until the peak of Void Transformation, he stopped at the step of [Sacrificing the Soul of Heaven and Earth to Integrate with the Dao].

The Xuanhuang Realm was filled with innumerable souls of heaven and earth. How to choose became Xuanyuan Tuo's dilemma.

Before the creation of the new method, the souls of heaven and earth were often seen by cultivators as projections of the will of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, the most suitable path for comprehending heavenly laws. Although some cultivators had attempted to capture the souls of heaven and earth, at best they could only use them for enlightenment. There was no method to refine and convert the power of the souls of heaven and earth into their own cultivation.

"The souls of heaven and earth are born with heavenly duties. Although they appear as independent entities after being born as human phantoms, they are still connected to the network of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth. The new method I envisioned is precisely to steal the power of heaven and earth through this connection."

"Each soul of heaven and earth corresponds to a corresponding heavenly law. My goal is..."

Xuanyuan Tuo looked at the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth. The scenes within the realm all turned illusory, forming a vast network of interlacing lines. Xuanyuan Tuo scanned the giant network, carefully searching for his target.

After an unknown amount of time...

Xuanyuan Tuo's gaze suddenly focused. Then, a complex expression flashed across his face. Full of doubt, full of joy.

"I don't know why, but I feel an inexplicable familiarity."

"Moreover, the law corresponding to that soul of heaven and earth does not seem to be inherent to the Xuanhuang Realm. Compared to other laws, it seems somewhat out of place..."

"From the upper realm?"

Xuanyuan Tuo pondered for a long time, and finally made up his mind.

It took another half a year, using all his skills, to finally lure out this unique soul of heaven and earth!

Enveloped in golden light, its aura was sacred and inviolable, like an ant looking down at Xuanyuan Tuo below.

"Even though you originated from the Immortal Realm, you have merged into the Xuanhuang Realm and descended into the mortal world. Yet, at the brink of death, you are still unaware!"

A year ago, Xuanyuan Tuo was still a farmer nearing fifty, with the mentality of a farmer. But with his cultivation and realm increasing over the past year, and the memories in his mind continuously emerging, Xuanyuan Tuo's disposition had changed drastically. He no longer regarded even those with deep connections to the upper realm as something to be feared, treating them merely as prey.

Xuanyuan Tuo struck down with his palm, and the space around the golden soul of heaven and earth was instantly frozen. Countless scenes from the Xuanhuang Realm transformed into ferocious phantoms, swarming forward. It was as if a world was created around the golden soul of heaven and earth, and then various souls of heaven and earth were evolved to attack it.

Xuanyuan Tuo seemed like a commander of three armies, sitting unmoved in the central command. Letting his subordinates fight. Although the golden soul of heaven and earth was powerful, after Xuanyuan Tuo isolated its connection with the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth through unfathomable means, it was ultimately just a tree without roots and water without a source. It was eventually worn down and killed, transforming into a golden light that Xuanyuan Tuo devoured.

"Soul of Heaven and Earth, [Gold Keeper]!"

The brilliant golden light receded, and Xuanyuan Tuo exhaled deeply. The Gold Keeper had existed since the creation of the Xuanhuang Realm. Created by an Immortal, it possessed the ability to manage and create all things in Xuanhuang. It was originally hidden deep within the Xuanhuang Realm, undetectable by mortals. But with the destruction of the Immortal Realm, the Gold Keeper's law, which relied on ancient formations for effect, had also been shattered. Only then did Xuanyuan Tuo discover its traces.

By merging with the [Gold Keeper], Xuanyuan Tuo's strength took a qualitative leap. Ordinary Longevity cultivators were no match for him. Only the sect leaders of the Immortal Dao's ten great sects, with their deep foundations, could perhaps pose a threat to him.

Xuanyuan Tuo knew it was time to begin his path of preaching the Dharma, and it was also the final step.

"Using human momentum to seize heavenly momentum."

"Using the human way to define the heavenly way."

"When the number of cultivators practicing my new law increases, and eventually reverses the universe, making this the only method of cultivation, that will be the day I achieve Dao."

"From today onwards, I will turn the Xuanhuang Realm upside down!"

With this belief, Xuanyuan Tuo arrived at Congyun Marsh on the desolate border of the Xuanhuang Realm. He began his first transmission of the Dharma.

When he transformed into a celestial being and announced to the world, "Reversing the laws of heaven and earth to prove longevity," it did not cause much of a stir. Because the new law was too shocking, few cultivators were willing to believe him and switch to re-cultivation.

But Xuanyuan Tuo did not mind, and continued to spread the new law across the Xuanhuang land. And when the first batch of mortals who couldn't cultivate were promoted to cultivators, they became Xuanyuan Tuo's most fervent believers. They did not know Xuanyuan Tuo's name, and only respectfully referred to him as [Law-Transmitting Immortal Venerable].

The believers spontaneously formed the Myriad Immortals Alliance, helping each other and spreading the new Dharma. In just a few years, the new Dharma had spread like wildfire, sweeping across the world!

This anomaly naturally attracted the attention of the celestial Dao ten great sects high above. Slaughter descended. The Myriad Immortals Alliance had only just taken shape, how could it contend with the ten great immortal sects that had dominated the Xuanhuang Realm for millennia? Even without the ten great immortal sects acting personally, their affiliated sects alone were enough to inflict heavy losses on the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

But the new Dharma cultivators had an advantage that the old Dharma cultivators could not match. Firstly, the cultivation speed of the new Dharma was incredibly fast. Even if they were annihilated, a large number of new Dharma cultivators would reappear within a short period. Secondly, once they reached the Nascent Soul stage, the survival ability of new Dharma cultivators was incredibly strong. As long as their souls were not fatally injured, their physical bodies could instantly recover from any severe injuries. With these two factors combined, although many new Dharma cultivators died, most of them were in the Qi Refining to Golden Core stages. As for those at Nascent Soul and above, they often managed to survive. Through continuous struggle, their experience became richer. In contrast, the old Dharma cultivators required a large amount of time and resources to cultivate a qualified combatant. One less was one less. With this shift in power, the situation began to gradually reverse.

Furthermore, Xuanyuan Tuo could sense that even within the ten sects, some individuals had begun to switch to the new Dharma. They were no longer a monolithic entity, so how could they possibly eradicate external enemies in one fell swoop?

Just as everything was developing favorably according to his plan. An ominous premonition grew stronger in Xuanyuan Tuo's heart, as if disaster was imminent at any moment! Even though Xuanyuan Tuo had carefully concealed his whereabouts and no longer openly preached the Dharma in broad daylight, this sense of crisis did not diminish. Xuanyuan Tuo knew that he must have been targeted by the big figures of the ten sects.

Only by facing them directly could he truly understand the despair of confronting behemoths like the ten sects. Xuanyuan Tuo tried every means possible, but he always seemed to face only one outcome: death.

But Xuanyuan Tuo did not want to die. Just as despair was about to engulf him, that ethereal chanting voice that had accompanied him since childhood, after many years, reappeared! Since embarking on the path of cultivation, this voice had disappeared from Xuanyuan Tuo's life. Now that it had returned, it brought back all the experiences Xuanyuan Tuo had gone through over the years!

Amidst the hazy and mystical chanting, Xuanyuan Tuo seemed to relive his past experiences. What's more, he could observe everything around him from a third-person perspective. Xuanyuan Tuo even felt an inexplicable intuition that he could, to some extent, manipulate and alter these people's thoughts!

When he saw a young cultivator standing beside him, listening to his lectures in his memory, Xuanyuan Tuo suddenly felt an inexplicable surge of great joy. He knew that this young man was his only hope of survival!

His soul rejoiced and leaped, and with the sound of the chanting, Xuanyuan Tuo approached, touched, and invaded... Even though it was just an illusion from memory, with the power of the chanting, Xuanyuan Tuo seemed to have truly entered the other person's soul! He knew everything about him.

Chen Tianhai! The foremost direct disciple of the Grand Tai Yan Sect! The Nine Scrolls of Heavenly Evolution, the Primordial Dao Stone Mother!

"There is actually such a divine object in the world?" Xuanyuan Tuo's heart churned, almost waking him up from the mystical realm. The Dao Stone Mother was something Xuanyuan Tuo had never heard of, even in the countless scenes that constantly appeared in his mind!

"If I could borrow the power of the Dao Stone Mother for deduction, it would surely guide me to a glimmer of hope for survival!" Xuanyuan Tuo's heart reignited with hope.

But the Dao Stone Mother was something that even Chen Tianhai, the foremost direct disciple of the Grand Tai Yan Sect, was not qualified to use. As an outsider, and an enemy of the ten Immortal Sects, how could he possibly mobilize it... It was sheer fantasy!

"Perhaps, I can manipulate and influence Chen Tianhai to accomplish this." Xuanyuan Tuo suddenly enlightened. To pry into the thoughts of illusions from past memories was already an unimaginable feat. To influence reality in the future through illusions of the past was even more unheard of.

But for some reason, Xuanyuan Tuo inexplicably felt confident. If he could use the chanting voice in his mind... This matter would not be difficult. Xuanyuan Tuo was indeed a heaven-blessed prodigy. Even though he didn't understand the principle of the chanting voice at all, it didn't prevent him from instinctively studying its practical use.

In a daze, he established a connection with the real Chen Tianhai. He could vaguely perceive Chen Tianhai's thoughts and feelings at every moment. Thus, Chen Tianhai's memories were subtly altered. It seemed that when he was observing the preaching and lecturing years ago, the preacher had looked at him for some reason. In the years that followed, that gaze from the preacher had followed him all along. It became his inner demon, causing him to lose sleep and peace.

Chen Tianhai, being chosen as the foremost direct disciple of the Tai Yan Sect, naturally had impeccable talent and disposition, making him an absolute celestial prodigy. Chen Tianhai, with great perseverance, forcefully suppressed the unease in his heart.

Xuanyuan Tuo did not become arrogant, but patiently waited for the opportune moment indicated by his senses. The seed had been sown; it would eventually blossom and bear fruit.

As expected. Not long after, Fang Dingge, the sect master of the Great Dao Sect, entrusted Xingji Daoist, the sect master of the Tai Yan Sect, to use the Dao Stone Mother for deduction regarding the matter of six Longevity cultivators encircling and suppressing the preacher. Xingji Daoist deduced five hundred million times, and all deductions ended with the preacher's death. Upon receiving the reply, Fang Dingge set off to search for and hunt down the preacher.

"Six Longevity cultivators, what a grand gesture." Xuanyuan Tuo's heart turned cold. Sensing death approaching, Xuanyuan Tuo, though startled, remained calm. He used the mystical power of the chanting voice to continue corrupting and influencing Chen Tianhai's state of mind.

It was also Xuanyuan Tuo's destiny not to perish. Xingji Daoist, due to suppressing the unrest in the Uncertain Prison, temporarily left the Tai Yan Sect. Chen Tianhai, in the end, could not resist the temptation from within and unilaterally activated the Dao Stone Mother for deduction. After countless deductions, he finally found the only glimmer of hope amidst all the impossibilities!

Chen Tianhai seemed to have foreseen the demise of the six Great Longevity cultivators, his mind shaken, and he became utterly dispirited. Xuanyuan Tuo, however, seized the final opportunity and rushed towards the small world deduced by the Dao Stone Mother. Just before being surrounded by the six Great Longevity cultivators of the Immortal Sect, he reached his destination.

The six Great Longevity cultivators arrived one after another. Even with his heaven-defying divine abilities, under the siege of the six Great Longevity cultivators, Xuanyuan Tuo was quickly heavily injured. Just as he was about to perish.

Affected by their battle, the alien races in the small world, who had suffered heavy casualties, launched an unexpected counterattack. Those beings, whom the six Great Longevity cultivators regarded as ants and paid no heed to, chanted and summoned a gate. It enveloped all seven of them, including Xuanyuan Tuo.

The portal opened, and endless darkness engulfed everyone.

In the sea of darkness, relying on the scenario deduced by the Dao Stone Mother, Xuanyuan Tuo used the surviving will to survive from the resurrected True Immortal to kill the six Great Longevity cultivators one by one. He himself, due to his severe injuries, eventually fell into a coma in the sea of darkness.

During this period, the Heavenly Physician, who had been lurking and waiting for the opportunity, finally regained control of the body.

"What is that chanting sound?" The Heavenly Physician, who had been observing all along, was also shocked by the mysterious and unfathomable power.

The Heavenly Physician thought this body was doomed. He never expected that Xuanyuan Tuo would actually find a glimmer of hope of survival amidst the impossible. To influence reality in the future by relying on past memories. This ability did not exist in the mortal world!

"More importantly, Xuanyuan Tuo and I are essentially one soul. But that chanting sound only exists in his memory."

"Although I know of its existence, I cannot recall or perceive it specifically..."

The Heavenly Physician's mind was greatly shaken and could not calm down for a long time.

Chapter 1410: The Demon Carving Sound of Heavenly Profound

At the same time as being shocked by this unknown great power, the Heavenly Physician also felt a sense of fear towards the original owner of this body.

Thus, the Heavenly Physician took advantage of Xuanyuan Tuo's injury and coma to gradually tamper with the body. The Heavenly Physician knew that Xuanyuan Tuo was protected by that mystical chanting sound. Therefore, he did not use conventional methods, but solely relied on the connection between him and Xuanyuan Tuo, formed by the [Heavenly Soul Rebirth] technique, to slowly infiltrate, using himself as medicine.

In a sense, he was Xuanyuan Tuo, and Xuanyuan Tuo was him.

However, due to the mystical power that enveloped the Xuanyuan Clan's bloodline, Xuanyuan Tuo, who should have lost his independent consciousness, could still maintain control of his body. The stronger Xuanyuan Tuo became, the stronger the Heavenly Physician also became.

As his injuries gradually healed, Xuanyuan Tuo slowly awoke and escaped from the sea of darkness. The mysterious disappearance of the six Longevity Realm powerhouses naturally caused a huge uproar. However, the ten great sects had deep foundations. Although this loss was considerable, it was not enough to cripple them.

Xuanyuan Tuo had a vague premonition that he would face the ten great sects' true trump cards next. However, inexplicably, Xuanyuan Tuo seemed to have overestimated the ten great sects. Until he achieved Longevity Heavenly Venerate, the ten great sects had not organized any effective counterattacks.

They only contracted their forces and consolidated their sect territories. They allowed the Myriad Immortals Alliance to nibble away at the smaller sects on the periphery of the ten great sects.

And when Xuanyuan Tuo finally attained Longevity, the laws of the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth were forever changed. The old methods no longer existed, and the new method became the only viable path for cultivators in the world. Xuanyuan Tuo's long-held ideals and ambitions were finally realized.

Anyone willing to cultivate in the world could do so without hindrance. Although he foresaw that as the number of cultivators practicing the new method increased, the resources required for their cultivation would become a bottleneck for cultivators. But Xuanyuan Tuo already had a plan to deal with this.

He absorbed the power of the [Gold Keeper], allowing him to manipulate the Xuanhuang Realm to constantly generate various rare treasures, grotto-heavens, and even souls of heaven and earth. Internally, the Xuanhuang Realm constantly evolved, self-sustaining. Externally, it annexed and absorbed surviving cultivation worlds in the Star Sea to supplement resources.

As the number of new Dharma cultivators grew, Xuanyuan Tuo's strength would also constantly increase. Even if the path to Immortality was severed, he could reach the peak of the Star Sea.

At that time, he would repair the ancient formation left by the Xuan Tian Sect, lead the Xuanhuang Realm to first escape the coverage of the Immortal Ruins. After reaching a relatively safe area for a period of time, he would then use the power of reversing the laws of heaven and earth during the Dao Integration of a Longevity Heavenly Venerate to continuously transform the Xuanhuang Realm.

According to Xuanyuan Tuo's calculations, only the coordinated efforts of two or more Longevity Heavenly Venerates in constructing the Xuanhuang Realm, coupled with the activation of the ancient formation's power, might allow them to cross the High Wall!

Xuanyuan Tuo, also known as the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, while continuously accumulating and improving his own strength, was also secretly evaluating cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm who could shoulder great responsibility. He did not focus on their aptitude, but only on their character and integrity!

If they passed the test, the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate would secretly act to help them comprehend the laws of reversal and directly achieve the Longevity realm!

Xuanyuan Tuo had indeed identified several young people worthy of entrustment. But before he could act, a catastrophe befell the Xuanhuang Realm: the inability to cultivate multiple laws!

This anomaly in heaven and earth was somewhat unexpected for Xuanyuan Tuo. He controlled the Dao of [Gold Keeper], and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao should have been under his control. However, such a change occurred inexplicably. Xuanyuan Tuo understood that the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao must have been inadvertently stimulated to unleash a power capable of countering the Dao of Gold Keeper.

The Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable! This name instantly appeared in Xuanyuan Tuo's mind.

He held no malice towards this newly promoted Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable. He even wanted to seek him out for a conversation. But unfortunately, this Great Celestial Venerable, using the power of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, had been well-hidden.

Furthermore, Xuanyuan Tuo had to divert his attention to deal with the mess left behind by the Myriad Immortals Alliance after the calamity of cultivating multiple laws. The ten great sects had deep foundations, and their disciples practiced diverse cultivation methods. Order was maintained, and they would not collapse completely in an instant.

However, the Myriad Immortals Alliance, although it had expanded rapidly in numbers, mostly practiced the [Heavenly Net Divine Technique] preached by Xuanyuan Tuo. This technique, personally deduced by Xuanyuan Tuo, was all-encompassing and allowed for eventual mastery, but it became a death sentence for the Myriad Immortals Alliance during the calamity!

The Myriad Immortals Alliance, having been established for a short time and being a loose alliance of new Dharma cultivators, had few leaders with absolute authority besides Xuanyuan Tuo's high prestige. Under the calamity, the Myriad Immortals Alliance descended into horrific mutual slaughter. The Myriad Immortals Alliance, which the ten great sects considered a major threat, thus collapsed before the ten great sects even acted!

Through this incident, Xuanyuan Tuo deeply understood the importance of a strong foundation. Although the Myriad Immortals Alliance appeared grand and powerful during its uprising, its accumulation was insufficient, and its ability to withstand risks was too poor. It was easily broken by any slight disturbance.

Xuanyuan Tuo tried to rescue and preserve the Myriad Immortals Alliance's strength while also trying to find the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable. However, after establishing the new law, coupled with the power of the [Gold Keeper], he was in a state of irreconcilable opposition with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. The Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable, naturally, bore an irreconcilable hatred towards him.

"You misunderstand me profoundly. This is judging by actions, not intentions." Xuanyuan Tuo felt a slight regret. However, as a supreme expert, his pride would not allow him to offer an explanation.

Even the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable could not stop the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, who had successfully reversed the laws. However, not long after, two unexpected events occurred that Xuanyuan Tuo had not anticipated.

The first was that Xuanyuan Tuo, the strongest person of this era, would occasionally feel a sense of heart palpitations. His inner premonition carried unease and sadness. After careful investigation, Xuanyuan Tuo was shocked to discover that this emotion did not originate from himself but from another existence within his body! An existence he had never discovered for a long time – another consciousness!

The second event was that the calamity of not being able to cultivate multiple laws had not yet passed, and the disaster known as the Immortal-Mortal Miasma had quietly descended upon heaven and earth. The arrival of the Immortal-Mortal Miasma was accompanied by the death of the nameless Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable!

This event was even more bewildering to Xuanyuan Tuo than discovering another consciousness within him. Because Xuanyuan Tuo understood that this was the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable, at the cost of his own life, initiating a reversal of the laws. By becoming both the new and old Heavenly Venerates simultaneously, he had suffered a backlash and perished.

Xuanyuan Tuo could not understand the other party's actions at all. However, Xuanyuan Tuo knew that anyone who could bear both new and old Heavenly Venerates simultaneously could not be an incompetent fool. He must have had his reasons for doing so.

Xuanyuan Tuo pondered endlessly but could not understand. Until later, he discovered that even after cultivators expelled and overcame the Immortal-Mortal Miasma, it still remained in the bloodline of their descendants. As part of the laws of heaven and earth, it prevented mortals from cultivating.

But if mortals could overcome this inhibitory force and embark on the path of cultivation, it would be equivalent to completing a small-scale reversal of the laws. Although it did not reach the level of affecting the laws of heaven and earth, over a long period, with countless mortals constantly embarking on the path of cultivation. The birth of each cultivator was equivalent to shaking the foundation of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate.

"Although they cannot kill me, they have offset a large part of the accumulation I gained from each cultivator practicing the new Dharma."

"Originally, in the new Dharma system, each cultivator born would become a part of my cultivation foundation. With continuous accumulation, one day, it would push me to an unknown divine realm!"

"But now..."

"It is destroying my path!"

Even a mud person has some fire. Upon realizing this, Xuanyuan Tuo could not help but become furious. But the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable was already dead, and Xuanyuan Tuo had nowhere to vent his anger!

Just as Xuanyuan Tuo's state of mind was unprecedentedly unstable, his consciousness was suddenly pulled into a pitch-black space. He lost control of his body.

Facing him floated a vicissitudinous old man with white hair. Although their faces were not the same, looking at the other party, Xuanyuan Tuo felt as if he were looking in a mirror!

"Heavenly Physician!" For some reason, Xuanyuan Tuo called out the other party's name.

The Heavenly Physician did not waste words with him. Instead, tears of blood flowed from his eyes. He just repeatedly chanted as if possessed, "Quickly return to the Heavenly Law Realm, quickly return to the Heavenly Law Realm!"

Xuanyuan Tuo immediately understood that this was the reason for his persistent unease in recent times. The Heavenly Physician, preoccupied with returning to the Heavenly Law Realm, could not hear anything Xuanyuan Tuo said.

Xuanyuan Tuo tried to suppress him, but was horrified to find that the other party was almost like a copy of himself, with almost identical strength. What's more, with the addition of an extremely strong desire to return home, he was even stronger than Xuanyuan Tuo! Gradually gaining control of the body! The appearance of the illusory transmitter also slowly transformed into the Heavenly Physician's original appearance!

As if sealed in a small dark room, Xuanyuan Tuo could only vaguely sense what was happening outside. He saw that when the Heavenly Physician finally returned to the Heavenly Law Realm after immense hardship, the inhabitants of the Heavenly Law Realm had all been slaughtered. The tragic scene was almost unbearable even for Xuanyuan Tuo. His homeland had suffered a great catastrophe, and the Heavenly Physician fell into madness. His heart was like a terrifying storm, severing Xuanyuan Tuo's connection with him.

Xuanyuan Tuo gathered his strength, trying to regain control of his body. After an unknown amount of time, a transparent figure, other than the Heavenly Physician, also appeared in this space. What caused Xuanyuan Tuo's infinite sense of crisis was that this transparent figure seemed to be ignorant, yet it could attach itself and erode his consciousness. This was a bizarre power that Xuanyuan Tuo had never encountered before.

Despite his strenuous resistance, he could not stop its gradual erosion. Just before this transparent figure completely occupied Xuanyuan Tuo, in his mind, the ethereal chanting voice reappeared. With the help of this miraculous power, Xuanyuan Tuo managed to maintain his consciousness.

In the dark space, time flowed by. After an unknown period, Xuanyuan Tuo finally sensed that the opportune moment had arrived. This body seemed to have entered a peculiar space. And in this place, the mystical chanting sound became unprecedentedly clear.

Xuanyuan Tuo, relying on his accumulated power, made a full counterattack, and surprisingly gained temporary control of the body for an instant. Although it was only for a moment, after understanding his current situation, Xuanyuan Tuo came up with a plan to deal with it.

The space the body was currently in seemed to be the interior of an immortal artifact. It was precisely because of this that it resonated with the chanting sound of the immortal-tier power. Xuanyuan Tuo softly murmured and left the chanting sound inside the immortal artifact's spatial interior. Relying on this mystical chanting power, which could influence reality through past memories, Xuanyuan Tuo was confident that by utilizing the later comers who would continuously enter this immortal artifact space, he could find a way to escape.

After branding the chanting sound, Xuanyuan Tuo lost control of his body again and was sealed in the boundless darkness. Time flowed by, unknown. During this period, he tried to counterattack several times, but the power suppressing and sealing him inexplicably grew stronger. It seemed he had no chance of turning the tables. But Xuanyuan Tuo never gave up. Because the chanting sound he had planted was constantly gathering energy for his counterattack. It was only a matter of time before he could completely break free.

...

Returning to the present.

When Li Fan looked at the scene evolved from the transmitter's body memory within the illusion formation, his expression shifted slightly. Even though he believed he already had a thorough understanding of the stories of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate and the Heavenly Physician, he did not expect the truth to be so convoluted, and... the twists of fate.

However, what bothered Li Fan the most were the various strange phenomena of the Xuanyuan Clan. Not only the extremely mystical chanting sound. But also the madman Xuanyuan Sheng that Xuanyuan Tuo saw in his childhood.

"Dog Egg, you must know that everything in the world has already happened countless times..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, carefully pondering this sentence. "Is it the madman's meaningless ramblings, or does it have a deeper meaning?"

The description in the words made it difficult for Li Fan not to associate it with [True Return]. And in Xuanyuan Tuo's memory, it was not certain whether Xuanyuan Sheng had truly died that night.

"The Xuanyuan Clan worships the tablet of Xuanyuan Hong. It should be Xuan Tian King's backup plan."

"Xuan Tian King actually mastered such a heaven-defying technique as the chanting sound?"

"Or is that the true power of a Half-immortal?"

Although Li Fan had ascended to Half-immortality, his methods were limited to formations. Other than that, there was no qualitative difference from his mortal stage.

"Imprinted in the Heavenly Profound Realm?" Li Fan's gaze pierced through the Utmost Darkness Star Sea and focused on the Xuanhuang Realm. He had entered the Heavenly Profound Memorial Hall multiple times before and experienced various illusory transmissions of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate.

"It seems to be experiencing the past of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate."

"In reality, he is being eroded by the chanting sound..."

Chapter 1411: Two Profound Sounds from the Immortal Realm

"The murmuring sound appears in the sea of consciousness of all cultivators who have entered the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters."

"Although it only exists in memory and seems unlikely to cause any ripples, the accumulated power in the dark could be enough to allow Xuanyuan Tuo to escape. With a sudden outburst, with its peculiar nature, perhaps most cultivators would be completely drained by a memory from their past." Li Fan's gaze flickered.

The Immortal Formation miniaturized into a point of light, bringing the still-sleeping Xuanyuan Tuo and the illusory demon into Li Fan's palm, suppressing them within his body.

Then, towards the direction of the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan's expression became indifferent, and he slowly extended his right hand.

The might of a True Immortal, looking down from above.

A palm descended upon the mortal world, spanning the Star Sea.

Located at the fringes of the Star Sea, Li Fan, gazing from afar at the Xuanhuang Realm, unleashed a palm strike.

He did not employ immortal-level techniques, merely using the difference in stature to strike from above.

The True Immortal of the Immortal Ruins was deeply engrossed in comprehending the Dao. In past reincarnations, Li Fan had verified multiple times that as long as it wasn't an energy fluctuation at the True Immortal level, or the appearance of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, it would not disturb him.

Even facing the world-ending Immortal Formation of "Immortal Descent, All Things Return to Ruins," she merely sent out a strand of divine sense to observe.

Li Fan's palm strike landed precisely on the Central Four Prefectures of the Myriad Immortals Alliance in the Xuanhuang Realm.

The target was not the Immortal Ruins, nor was there any external energy overflow or diffusion.

The True Immortal of the Immortal Ruins remained completely unaware. Li Fan's colossal palm descended stealthily.

Not even the slightest anomaly appeared on the firmament of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Only in the Central Four Prefectures of the Immortal Alliance did an intense, apocalyptic tremor occur without any warning.

Li Fan's fingers traversed the Star Sea and made contact and perception.

The Central Four Prefectures of the Immortal Alliance were an extension of the internal space of the Tianxuan Mirror within the Xuanhuang Realm.

When Li Fan first entered the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, he had witnessed the miraculous scene within the Tianxuan Mirror: countless black and white lines, crisscrossing. The black and white lines collided, the two colors continuously intertwined, eventually forming a void point. Innumerable points flickered, intermittently appearing and disappearing, constantly extending outwards in the void, ultimately turning colorful.

At that time, Li Fan was still puzzled by such a wondrous scene in the Tianxuan Mirror. Now, Li Fan understood. This was the Tianxuan Mirror deconstructing the Xuanhuang Realm in its own way.

A flash of brilliance flickered in his eyes. Li Fan's five fingers became like knives, instantly severing the connection between the Tianxuan Mirror and the Xuanhuang Realm.

Then, with a flick of his finger, he clenched his fist fiercely!

Feeling a slight repulsive force, Li Fan exerted a little more strength and pulled.

His palm instantly traversed space and time, returning from the Xuanhuang Realm to the fringes of the Star Sea.

It was as if he were reaching into the water to retrieve something.

Li Fan looked at his palm, where a faint light flickered. An ancient bronze mirror struggled within it.

Squinting his eyes, Li Fan sensed faint, ethereal lines extending from the本体 of the Tianxuan Mirror towards the Xuanhuang Realm.

"These are the various restrictions originally set up by Chuán Fǎ, and the connection between the Tianxuan Mirror, his human clone, and the many Tianxuan sub-mirrors."

"As expected of a former immortal artifact, able to maintain such stable connections even after traversing the entire Star Sea in an instant."

Li Fan praised inwardly.

He described it as a former immortal artifact because Li Fan did not sense any fluctuation of immortal spiritual energy from the本体 of the Tianxuan Mirror.

Even though the immortal artifacts preserved in the legacy of the Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang had been consumed over generations of use in the Xuanhuang Realm, there was still some residual immortal spiritual energy.

However, the Tianxuan Mirror seemed to have completely severed its connection with immortal spiritual energy.

"In a sense, transforming immortal to mortal."

"Incomplete cutting is no cutting at all. Perhaps only in this way can the blow of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation be truly avoided." Reflecting on the obliteration by wind and calamity seen in the remaining immortal artifacts of the Xuanhuang Realm like the Boundless Mirror, Li Fan pondered thoughtfully.

With a slight movement of his thoughts, a white ring flew out, firmly binding the本体 of the Tianxuan Mirror.

Li Fan separated a strand of divine sense and entered it.

Given that he already knew the murmuring demonic sound was imprinted within the Tianxuan Mirror, he had to proceed cautiously.

Having already ascended to the immortal realm, even a strand of divine sense surpassed the mortal realm.

The Tianxuan Mirror had been suppressed and forcefully taken by a mysterious palm from beyond the heavens. At this moment, the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters had fallen into unprecedented chaos. When Chuán Fǎ originally established the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters within the Tianxuan Mirror, it was to guarantee its safety to the greatest extent.

He never expected that after many years, this seemingly unbreakable defense would be instantly destroyed by an unknown existence!

Even knowing that they were facing an unimaginably terrifying existence.

All the Chuán Fǎ practitioners gathered together.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters activated all formations and restrictions, entering the highest emergency state.

However...

All these measures, in Li Fan's current view, were like a child playing house.

If he wished, Li Fan could destroy all of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's defensive measures with just a single strand of divine sense.

But he did not do so.

The divine sense that stealthily infiltrated, no one could detect.

The divine sense evolved into a body, standing within the Tianxuan Mirror, sensing the faint, mysterious forces all around, attempting to pull him into the illusion of Chuán Fǎ's memories.

Although the murmuring sound was the work of a True Immortal, it was ultimately cast through Chuán Fǎ Heavenly Venerable as the medium. It might be invincible against mortal existences.

But to deal with Li Fan, who was already a half-immortal, it was somewhat lacking.

With just a thought of resistance, the murmuring sound could no longer drag Li Fan.

Contact is mutual.

During the time it was attempting to erode Li Fan, Li Fan also "saw and heard" it on some level.

In Xuanyuan Tuo's lasting impression, it was meaningless, void murmuring.

But in Li Fan's perception...

It was a solemn, sacred scripture chant!

"... vain words, birth, birth. Intent, spirit, body, soul, born of chaos, return to chaos."

"One exists eternally. Both lost and existing."

Perhaps because Xuanyuan Tuo had relayed it, Li Fan tried his best to discern it, but could only clearly hear one passage.

The rest were indistinct, rapidly chanted sounds.

This sacred, bizarre chanting voice was not emitted by any single person, but seemed to be sung by countless beings together.

What made Li Fan feel slightly startled was that he could even faintly hear the voices of some acquaintances.

Not just the timbre.

But words they had spoken during their encounters with him.

"Dao Xuanzi, you bully me too much!"

"Nascent Soul late stage at twenty-nine years old..."

"Young friend, what are you anticipating?"

"Tian Yang's whole life, never inferior to anyone!"

...

And so on.

Not only in this life, but tracing back to Li Fan's past reincarnations.

Accompanying these voices, indistinct figures also appeared in Li Fan's sea of consciousness.

Even without faces, Li Fan could easily distinguish their identities.

Under the influence of this chanting, Li Fan even vaguely felt the same sensation as Xuanyuan Tuo of the past.

He seemed to be able to influence the real them in the present through these memory phantoms!

Within the Tianxuan Mirror, the divine sense clone stood silently, eyes closed, comprehending.

Outside the Tianxuan Mirror, Li Fan's main body was already on high alert.

This profound chanting sound could reflect past reincarnation scenes from his soul memory, proving its extraordinary nature.

While it might not necessarily mean it had discovered the secret of True Return's continuous reincarnation.

However, Li Fan could not afford to be careless.

Immortals Formation rings were already in place, guarding him, ready for True Return at any moment.

But fortunately, the worst-case scenario Li Fan had anticipated did not occur.

Li Fan did not relax his vigilance, synchronizing with his divine sense clone's knowledge and feelings.

As he listened, Li Fan inexplicably felt a faint sense of familiarity.

After a moment of thought, a vague sound resembling the truth, accompanied by memories, emerged in his mind.

"Dao, proceeds from the ancient. Xin, is extinguished."

"Xing nian xiu, tong yi, wang shen."

"Thousand lines soul shift, hundred bends soul turns."

"No blame."

...

This sound, coexisted with the profound chanting sound.

The two resonated, not only influencing each other but also making their respective sounds clearer!

Before Li Fan, it was as if two figures appeared, one on the left and one on the right, explaining some supreme principle of the world to him.
