After a moment of stunned silence, Li Fan quickly realized the source of these sounds.

It was an Immortal Art chanted by the Great Master Tiandu when facing the obliteration by wind calamity during the Holy Emperor's era.

In the previous life, when the nameless tablet appeared, intending to turn everything into text on the tablet.

Before the stream of light like a waterfall, the Great Master had also chanted this Immortal Art to avert disaster.

At that time, Li Fan heard it and had tried to record it.

But he was met with the Great Master's contempt and ridicule.

At that time, Li Fan did not understand why. Now, listening again after ascending to immortality, Li Fan realized that just like the profound chanting sound, although immortals and mortals heard the same passage.

There was a crucial difference.

"Dao is born, proceeds from the ancient. Sorrow and 'xin,' Dao is extinguished."

"Xing hun nian xiu, tong dao yi, wang shen shen."

"Thousand lines soul shift, hundred bends soul turns."

"Infinite, boundless, no blame."

...

The difference between immortal and mortal hearing was like heaven and earth!

Li Fan's heart trembled violently, immersing himself in this true Immortal Art of averting disaster.

"It seems my body has undergone no change."

"But it has been able to a certain extent to erase the 'erosion' of the profound chanting sound on me..."

A brilliant light flashed in his eyes. Li Fan, as if divinely inspired, began to chant this Immortal Art of averting disaster as well.

Enveloped by the profound chanting sound, the lingering sense of unease and dread in his heart slowly receded.

Li Fan himself had barely noticed this slight fear.

Only after it truly dissipated, and the significant change between before and after, did Li Fan realize its existence.

"If I were only influenced by any one of the profound sounds, even as a half-immortal, I would inevitably fall into it. But now, with both profound sounds appearing simultaneously, it seems to have formed a balance."

"They are vying with each other, yet I remain unharmed."

Li Fan let out a long sigh.

The power of a True Immortal was indeed extremely bizarre. When interacting with it, one could not be careless.

"Great Master Dao's sound is the Immortal Art of Averting Disaster."

"Perhaps it is precisely because of this Immortal Art that it has been able to safely hide in the Xuanhuang Realm all along without any disturbance."

Having personally experienced the miraculous power of the Immortal Art of Averting Disaster, Li Fan looked at the profound chanting sound again.

"Influencing and altering reality through phantoms of past memories..."

Looking at the countless illusory figures standing in his sea of consciousness.

Li Fan's gaze fell upon one of them.

Focusing his intent...

There was no fluctuation of immortal spiritual energy, not even any mortal energy was generated.

Yet, a miraculous thing happened in an instant.

In the Xuanhuang Realm, on Glazed Island.

He Zheng Hao was staring intently at the small Tianxuan Mirror. Because of the shocking event of Li Fan's palm strike and the disappearance of the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, the prices of all goods had skyrocketed like a roller coaster, completely out of control.

"Damn it, they won't even let me sell it."

"This is the culmination of my life's hard work!"

He Zheng Hao's eyes were bloodshot, already on the verge of madness.

But suddenly, his face turned deathly pale.

His mind felt as if it had been split open by a blow, and he collapsed to the ground.

After an unknown amount of time, he finally recovered.

As if he had lost half his life, he was drenched in sweat.

"Spirit Mist Grass?"

"My contribution points are all intact?"

"Mountain River Hidden Dragon Technique?"

...

He Zheng Hao stared blankly at the countless memories that appeared in his mind.

"Am I hallucinating from the shock?"

The memories appearing in his mind were too complex and chaotic, and it took He Zheng Hao a long time to barely organize them.

"This... is too real. It's as if I personally experienced it. What on earth is going on?"

The more he sorted them out, the more his heart pounded and disbelief grew.

"However, the Mountain River Hidden Dragon Technique? Isn't this the cultivation method I've been yearning for and dreaming of?"

Suddenly, he seemed to realize something, and his expression changed drastically.

"This, could it be real?"

He Zheng Hao cautiously wrote down the characters that appeared in his memory.

He had only written the beginning when his body involuntarily stiffened.

"There's absolutely no mistake, this is the genuine Mountain River Hidden Dragon Technique."

"It actually appeared in my mind on its own. Doesn't that mean I've saved hundreds of thousands of contribution points in one go?!"

He Zheng Hao's heart pounded wildly.

But soon, thinking of the strict Law Enforcement Hall of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, he became dejected again, like a eggplant beaten by frost.

"No, the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters has all disappeared. The Myriad Immortals Alliance is in dire straits itself, who cares about the leakage of cultivation techniques..."

"In times of chaos, dragons and snakes rise to power. Perhaps this is an opportunity for people like us."

Unaware of what he was thinking, a dangerous glint appeared in He Zheng Hao's eyes.

"Xuantian Sealing Spirit Formation?"

Next, He Zheng Hao continued to sort through his memories, with continuous gains and pleasant surprises.

...

At the fringes of the Star Sea, after Li Fan used the power of the profound chanting sound to alter He Zheng Hao's memories, Li Fan himself underwent wondrous changes in response.

Li Fan keenly sensed that several wisps of spiritual energy had inexplicably appeared within him.

Chapter 1412: Heavenly Venerate Skull Secret

These wisps of spiritual energy, compared to Li Fan's current half-immortal cultivation, were indeed negligible.

But they appeared so abruptly, without any warning. Li Fan had to take them seriously.

After careful discernment, Li Fan gradually understood. These inexplicably appearing spiritual energies were due to the changes that occurred to He Zheng Hao in this lifetime as a result of his activation of the profound chanting sound.

"The generation of spiritual energy originates from the feedback of the [Sitting Heaven Technique]. And the feedback force only originates from He Zheng Hao's strength improvement."

"But He Zheng Hao only awakened memories; his cultivation has not seen any substantive progress so far..."

Through the inexplicable connection established by the profound chanting sound, Li Fan's gaze seemed to instantly pierce through time and space, falling upon He Zheng Hao.

It could be said that Li Fan's understanding of He Zheng Hao surpassed He Zheng Hao's own.

With just a glance, Li Fan could see the difference between He Zheng Hao in this life and in the past.

"Originally, He Zheng Hao was only somewhat accomplished in formations. Whether in cultivation talent or state of mind, neither was considered top-tier."

"But now..."

An inexplicable expression appeared on Li Fan's face.

He Zheng Hao's talent in this life was among the best in the entire Xuanhuang Realm.

Moreover, his state of mind had also undergone a subtle transformation.

The former He Zheng Hao, after experiencing various hardships in life, was dominated by a strong "contentment with mediocrity" mindset. His greatest lifelong aspiration was to return to the Heng family in Tianyu Prefecture after achieving fame and fortune, and to hold his head high in front of Heng Ruoshui.

But in this life, in this era of great contention where dragons and snakes rise to power...

If Li Fan had not personally witnessed and caused this change, he would have suspected that another soul had possessed He Zheng Hao.

"What caused this kind of sublime change?"

"Is it just those extra memories?"

Li Fan now had too many methods to achieve a memory infusion that was indistinguishable from reality.

But to instill memories while simultaneously bringing about an effect close to a life sublimation...

This was not an easy task.

"Profound Chanting Sound." Li Fan's expression slowly became serious.

He did not rashly alter the other illusory memories that appeared in his mind. With He Zheng Hao as an observational sample, it was already sufficient for now.

"Whether it is my illusion or a real change that has occurred to you..."

"Allow me to add fuel to the fire!"

With a slight movement of Li Fan's thoughts, the white ring that bound the Tianxuan Mirror outside erupted with brilliant white light.

Analyzing the characteristics of the Tianxuan Mirror, the Immortal Formation underwent related transformations.

After a while...

The Tianxuan Mirror, relying on its own immortal artifact characteristics, and its various connections with the Xuanhuang Realm, were forcefully severed by Li Fan!

The Myriad Immortals Alliance was founded on the Tianxuan Mirror and the Chuán Fǎ Jue.

Now, with the disappearance of these two and the collective disappearance of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's high-ranking officials, the Myriad Immortals Alliance plunged into greater chaos. Any discerning person could see that this colossus, which had once ruled more than half the land of the Xuanhuang Realm, was on the verge of collapse! Perhaps for a short time, out of respect for the former prestige of the Myriad Immortals Alliance and Chuán Fǎ Heavenly Venerable, cultivators could still maintain a certain degree of rationality.

But before long, chaos and slaughter would inevitably descend upon the Xuanhuang land.

The drastic changes in the Myriad Immortals Alliance naturally could not be concealed from the five elders of the Five Elders Council, the Longevity Heavenly Venerates.

However, Li Fan currently had no time to deal with them.

To prevent the Five Elders Council from disrupting his "observation," Li Fan flicked his finger, shooting out a sword shadow.

The sword energy crisscrossed, traversing the Star Sea in an instant, descending into the Xuanhuang Realm.

Along the original dividing line between the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Council, it gently sliced open.

The spiritual energy-devouring white mist barrier at the border of the prefectures disappeared without a trace under the influence of the sword shadow. In its place appeared a bottomless chasm.

Above the chasm, countless sword shadows seemed to drift.

All cultivators who saw this chasm would immediately have the thought:

Those who cross the line die!

This was not a mere bluff. It was the absolute suppression of mortal life by Li Fan, a half-immortal.

Even the five Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Myriad Immortals Alliance would obediently be constrained!

With a casual gesture, he had set up a stage for He Zheng Hao.

Li Fan's attention returned to the murmuring demonic sound that had created all the bizarre changes.

After careful contemplation, Li Fan seemed to grasp something: "If True Immortal script is interpreting the supreme principles of heaven and earth in written form, then the profound murmuring sound originating from King Xuan Tian, and the protective Immortal Art of Great Master Tiandu, are deciphering the Great Dao through [sound]."

"If we make a horizontal comparison at the same level, the actual power displayed by the two..."

Li Fan frowned slightly, unable to make a judgment for the time being.

His understanding of the profound sound system was still too limited.

"Immortal script originates from the creation of the [Dao Inscribing Immortal]."

"Could this profound sound also be the work of some nameless True Immortal?" Li Fan wondered, frowning.

Although his current knowledge of profound sound was only a tiny fraction.

However, the practice on He Zheng Hao had already ignited Li Fan's infinite imagination for this mysterious power.

"Influencing reality through phantoms of past memories."

"This theoretical ultimate realm, couldn't it be achieved by rewriting your own past actions in memory to alter and distort reality?"

"Thus achieving an effect similar to [True Return]."

The more Li Fan thought, the more alarmed he became.

"However, this is only the theoretical limit. This divine ability is by no means easily achievable..."

Li Fan's thoughts were interrupted by the pleasing and communicative intention emanating from the Tianxuan Mirror, bound by the Immortal Formation in his hand.

"Junior [Mirror Xuan] greets the Upper Immortal."

The voice of the Tianxuan Mirror was exactly the same as the human clone he had interacted with in his memory.

It had to be said, it was worthy of being a former immortal artifact. Even though it had fallen to the mortal world now, its vision remained.

It could discern Li Fan's current realm at a glance.

"Mirror Xuan..."

Li Fan snorted coldly and ignored the Tianxuan Mirror.

The divine sense clone within the Tianxuan Mirror completely disregarded the manifested body and flew directly towards the direction of the Museum of Divine Treasures.

Mirror Xuan showed an embarrassed expression, not knowing where he had offended this Upper Immortal.

However, Mirror Xuan dared not offend this suddenly appearing True Immortal, Li Fan. Since the other party was displeased, he did not follow. He merely observed from afar, in secret.

Everything happening within the Tianxuan Mirror naturally escaped his eyes.

Li Fan's divine sense clone, familiar with the path, traversed the Museum of Divine Treasures. Heading straight for the central location.

Within the Tianxuan Mirror, treasures were innumerable. The Museum of Divine Treasures held hundreds of millions of collections.

But what was worthy of Li Fan's attention was only the skull of Mr. Bai, placed in the center of the Divine Treasures Hall.

As if already knowing Li Fan's objective, a figure stood waiting at the skull.

It was Di San Mo, the curator of the Museum of Divine Treasures.

Since it was only a divine sense clone, Li Fan, standing before the skull, did not feel the urgent desire of True Return to devour it.

Li Fan did not rush to take the skull, but instead looked at Di San Mo with great interest.

This old man's appearance, compared to his image from thousands of years ago in the Fallen Immortal Realm, seemed unchanged.

"You know I'm here for this?"

Di San Mo cupped his hands and said neither servilely nor arrogantly, "For something a True Immortal would go to such lengths for, among the many collections, there is only this one."

Li Fan reached out and took out the skull of Mr. Bai.

He did not feel any restrictions or resistance. It seemed that Di San Mo, before him, had stopped struggling fruitlessly and had silently withdrawn all defensive measures.

"Do you know the uniqueness of this skull?" Li Fan asked, weighing Mr. Bai's skull.

"This humble one does not know. It is merely the remains of an old friend. Seeing it again, my heart is filled with sorrow. Thus, I have preserved it carefully." Di San Mo clearly spoke insincerely.

"Do you not fear me, speaking lies before my face?" Li Fan's divine sense clone narrowed his eyes.

Di San Mo cupped his hands again, "This humble one... will not die. Even a True Immortal cannot truly kill me."

"But I have countless methods to make you wish you were dead, yet unable to die." Li Fan smiled.

Di San Mo's expression remained unchanged, his aged face seeming to have seen through everything, "Pain is meaningless to this humble one. Naturally, I fear nothing, and am afraid of nothing."

The divine sense clone nodded slightly, surprisingly not bothering him further. He merely said faintly, "Give me a tour of this Museum of Divine Treasures."

The skull in his hand had already disappeared.

"If you wish to visit according to the normal visiting order of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, then the first stop should be the Calculation and Creation [Era]. However, this humble one has a different opinion."

"A visit to the Museum of Divine Treasures should begin with a ruin."

The divine sense clone followed Di San Mo, slowly venturing deeper into the Museum of Divine Treasures.

On his last visit, he had not reached the seemingly non-publicly accessible area.

...

Outside the Tianxuan Mirror.

Li Fan's main body held Mr. Bai's skull.

Sensing the intense urge of True Return emanating from it.

It was not the first time he had encountered this, but compared to before, Li Fan, who had now ascended to immortality, felt that True Return's desire was even stronger.

"Eternal Remnant Will..."

"What secrets are hidden within Mr. Bai's skull?"

Flipping his hand, he first suppressed the Tianxuan Mirror, and under the protection of a circle of Immortal Formation white rings, Li Fan began to try and have True Return devour the Eternal Remnant Will.

It was somewhat similar to when he devoured Tian Yang's Eternal Remnant Will.

A faint sense of dizziness filled his mind, and the scene before his eyes suddenly changed.

"Hmm?"

Li Fan quickly regained consciousness and looked around.

"It's not like the previous Tian Yang's Remnant Will, where it replaced Tian Yang's identity in the obsession and acted."

"Instead, it seems to be participating and descending in person?"

He appeared to still be in the void, surrounded by endless darkness.

After flying forward for a while, Li Fan suddenly stopped, his eyes narrowing.

Not far away, a figure stood tall.

Li Fan was not unfamiliar with him.

His appearance was exactly like Su Bai, Mr. Bai.

But the moment he saw the other party, Li Fan's heart began to pound violently.

It was like a self-warning that only appeared when facing a life-or-death crisis.

As if encountering an extremely dangerous and terrifying existence, even though the other party had made no move from beginning to end, Li Fan's sense of unease continued to escalate.

"What is going on?"

Li Fan was bewildered.

Su Bai was merely a Longevity Heavenly Venerate.

Let alone that the opponent had already perished, even at his peak, Li Fan, who was already a half-immortal, was confident he would not lose to him.

Why, then, in the illusory realm created by Su Bai's Eternal Remnant Will, would such a sense of crisis arise inexplicably?

He silently invoked True Return, but there was no reaction. Instead, his divine sense clone also sensed that his main body was still hovering in the void of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Only a strand of his divine soul entered Su Bai's Eternal Remnant Will, and it would not truly affect his life or death in reality.

Even though he had confirmed this point, Li Fan's heart-pounding sensation could not be stopped.

Gradually, Li Fan finally came to his senses.

The strangeness in his heart was not due to a premonition of a life-or-death crisis. It was because...

He felt an instinctive fear when facing a high-ranking predator.

It urged Li Fan to flee as quickly as possible.

"High-ranking? Fear?" Li Fan was stunned at first, then found it inexplicably absurd.

He was now a half-immortal!

Su Bai was merely a Longevity Heavenly Venerate of Xuanhuang!

How could he possibly feel fear towards him?

With endless confusion and unwillingness, Li Fan once again carefully observed the "Mr. Bai" before him.

Only then did he vaguely notice something amiss.

Although they shared the same face, Mr. Bai in his memory, even though his eyes were filled with compassion, just as Xu Ke and the orphans in the small temple in Ningyuan City had said. Mr. Bai was the best and most beautiful person in the world, possessing all the best qualities in the world.

But this one before him...

Was inexplicably sinister and bizarre.

Even though the opponent's eyes were closed, Li Fan seemed to sense the overwhelming killing intent and madness in his eyes.

"What is the difference between them..."

Li Fan was still bewildered in his heart.

Not far away, the sinister Su Bai suddenly opened his eyes!

Without any pain.

The scene before Li Fan's eyes changed, and changed again.

Li Fan seemed to have returned to the moment before he met the sinister Su Bai.

But only he knew...

Just now, he had been instantly killed by the sinister Su Bai!

A cold sweat trickled down Li Fan's forehead.

"Could it be that my cultivation in reality was not brought into this Eternal Remnant Will?"

This was the first thought that came to Li Fan's mind.

But after confirming it, Li Fan immediately dismissed it.

"I am indeed at the half-immortal realm, aren't I?"

"How did I die just now?"

Li Fan was both shocked and enraged.

"No wonder that phantom figure remained motionless for so long; it was reserving preparation time."

He discovered that in this illusory realm, all his knowledge and skills seemed to be usable without obstruction.

So this time, Li Fan chose to strike first.

"Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger!"

A gigantic palm descended from the heavens.

Targeting the sinister Su Bai, he intended to crush him like an ant.

But just as the divine ability was about to land, Su Bai's figure suddenly vanished.

Li Fan was stunned, then suddenly came to his senses and quickly looked up.

At some unknown time, he had become as small as an ant, falling onto the fingertip of the sinister Su Bai!

Chapter 1413: Instant Kill Evil Bai

The sinister Su Bai, in an instant, had emulated Li Fan and similarly unleashed a Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger, and its power was even more potent than Li Fan's by hundreds of thousands of times!

An indescribable colossal force descended. Li Fan did not "die" unconsciously as he had the previous time, but could clearly feel the process of his body and soul being repeatedly crushed inch by inch!

Given the strength the sinister Su Bai had previously displayed, capable of instantly killing Li Fan, it was clear he was deliberately tormenting him!

Li Fan could even faintly see a look of enjoyment on the opponent's face!

"You bastard..."

The scene before his eyes changed again and again!

Li Fan once again found himself back before encountering the sinister Su Bai.

The repeated deaths left Li Fan feeling extremely indignant. However, with his years of reincarnation experience, his state of mind was extraordinary. After only a moment, Li Fan calmed down.

His previous anger and indignation were merely due to the stark contrast between his perceived "Longevity Realm" opponent instantly killing him, a "half-immortal."

But now, Li Fan could be sure that the sinister Su Bai's strength was definitely not as simple as the Longevity Realm.

In the cultivation world, strength is paramount, and the weak are prey to the strong. There is no reason for anger.

"This is not a real world, but an illusory scene constructed by the Eternal Remnant Will."

"The sinister Su Bai appeared here and attacked without a word. Moreover, he even gave the tested party a certain amount of preparation time."

"Even after failing the trial and dying, one can be instantly revived..."

As Li Fan pondered, he had vaguely understood the content of the trial of Su Bai's Eternal Remnant Will.

Defeat the sinister Su Bai!

"In reality, perhaps no one in the entire Xuanhuang Realm or the Utmost Darkness Star Sea could achieve this."

"But this is a phantom space generated by the Eternal Remnant Will, which can be considered an advanced version of the Tianxuan Mirror's [Sit and Discuss the Dao] combat function."

Li Fan suddenly realized.

"Immortal Formation, Profound Origin Beginning Spirit!"

His thoughts raced, and in his mind, the Dissolution Disc suddenly radiated boundless brilliance.

It was as if the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation, which was missing, had been instantly completed!

Black and white colors spun around Li Fan, opening up earth, fire, water, and wind in the void, evolving a world.

Li Fan stood in the center, like a mythical creator god, a progenitor!

He had the illusion that as long as he was within this formation, he could control and reduce everything within the formation's coverage according to his thoughts!

Currently, the Dissolution Disc had not obtained the complete formation diagram of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation.

However, having mastered three parts out of nine, it had a quantitative and qualitative understanding of the complete formation's specific power.

Therefore, with the help of Su Bai's Eternal Remnant Will space, the process of reaching the final result was omitted, and the "conception" of the final result was directly achieved.

In the void, Li Fan sat in the center of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation.

The world he created rapidly spread towards the four prefectures.

Soon, it engulfed the sinister Su Bai standing in situ.

"I am the ruler of the Immortal Realm!" Li Fan mobilized the great power of the Immortal Formation, transforming all the laws of the created world into chains, attempting to bind the sinister Su Bai.

The Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation, the fusion of nine formations, indeed displayed its terrifying power.

Dots of flowing light leached from the sinister Su Bai's body, integrating into the world Li Fan had created.

In the heavens and earth, countless illusory figures of Su Bai appeared simultaneously.

Each of them seemed to possess the strength of the Longevity Realm.

Like countless ants, they swarmed towards the sinister Su Bai.

The Su Bai, increasingly entangled by chains, seemed to have given up struggling, motionless.

He merely allowed the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation to diminish his strength.

But the sinister smile that appeared on his face made Li Fan's heart uneasy!

Soon, Li Fan understood the origin of his unease.

The Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Immortal Formation seemed incapable of reaching the sinister Su Bai's power limit.

Even though it could directly reduce the power to the theoretical maximum allowed by the formation with every breath, and this endless deduction...

It seemed to be inconsequential to the sinister Su Bai!

"How is this possible?!" Li Fan was too shocked, even doubting if this trial was a joke played by Mr. Bai on his descendants before his death.

Theoretically, the complete Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation could transform mortals into immortals and immortals into mortals with every breath.

It was equivalent to continuously reducing the cultivation of a True Immortal, yet the sinister Su Bai remained unmoving like a mountain and deep like an abyss.

"Nameless Realm?" Li Fan became increasingly suspicious.

As for the sinister Su Bai, it seemed he had tired of this boring game.

He even transmitted it proactively, allowing the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation to reduce him to its heart's content.

As if endless True Immortal cultivation poured into the world Li Fan had created.

In the endless void, it expanded infinitely, spanning millions of miles in an instant.

Even the Immortal-ranked Dissolution Disc gradually reached its limit.

Cracks appeared, and finally, it could no longer bear it and disintegrated inch by inch!

Li Fan's created "Immortal Realm" also met its end, accompanied by the collapse of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation.

This time, Li Fan perished in the great calamity of the Immortal Realm's destruction.

...

"Nameless True Immortal Realm."

Not long after, Li Fan, who had come back to life once again, began to ponder in the void about the theoretical means he possessed to counter the Nameless Realm.

"Merge with Dao, become one with Dao..."

As the sinister Su Bai attacked again, a seven-colored paint brush suddenly appeared in Li Fan's hand.

"Detain!" With a thought, a True Immortal script appeared in the void before him.

Like an invisible golden lock, it imprisoned the sinister Su Bai.

"Chaos!"

"Hunger!"

"Confinement!"

"Ancient!"

...

One by one, True Immortal scripts representing the laws of heaven and earth flew towards the sinister Su Bai under Li Fan's furious strokes. At this moment, Li Fan seemed to have transformed into the legendary [Dao Inscribing Immortal].

Exhausting the principles of heaven and earth, using Dao to fight the enemy.

Innumerable mystical characters, from their script form, reverted to their linear appearance.

Weaving into a hazy, wondrous dream, continuously dragging the sinister Su Bai into it.

Li Fan's body was also wrapped by infinite Dao, as if becoming "Dao" itself, becoming indiscernible.

Just as Li Fan saw hope for victory in this battle.

However, Li Fan inadvertently caught a glimpse and still saw a hint of mockery on the face of the sinister Su Bai opposite him.

Li Fan's heart suddenly skipped a beat.

Next, he witnessed a scene that horrified him.

The sinister Su Bai, trapped in the vortex of Dao, slowly extended his right hand.

Endless lines, as if attracted by something, shifted their target and converged towards him.

Within three breaths, all the infinite Dao written by Li Fan disappeared.

It transformed into a crystal-clear candy.

The sinister Su Bai threw it into his mouth, crunched it with a crack, and chewed it to pieces!

This time, Li Fan experienced what it felt like to be refined into candy and swallowed alive by someone.

...

"Even the Dao Inscribing Immortal is not enough?"

Li Fan's heart was now devoid of any anger or indignation, as if numb. He set aside the question of whether the sinister Su Bai's displayed strength was reasonable or not.

He only thought about how to kill or defeat the opponent.

"If ordinary methods don't work, then I'll use what I'm best at!"

He stood on the challenge arena once again.

"Ascend!"

Li Fan roared.

The phantom images of the Xuanhuang Realm's ascended feedback power stored within him consecutively turned into reality.

Even within this illusory space, their numbers were amplified by millions of times.

In an instant, countless Xuanhuang Realms shone like stars.

Ascending to immortality together!

This peculiar phenomenon, even the sinister Su Bai, who had come to execute Li Fan, was momentarily distracted.

The billions of Xuanhuang Realms, just as they were about to reach the critical point of transformation,

At Li Fan's thought, they lost their driving force for sublimation.

Instantly, they plummeted from their highest point.

Like countless colossal stones falling into the deep sea, they instantly stirred up terrifying waves!

Countless black energies drilled out from every rift in space.

Gathering sand to form a pagoda, transforming into ferocious beasts.

The areas where the black energy was most concentrated even spawned humanoid figures!

They bore an eight or nine-tenths resemblance to the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly and Earthly Spirit, [Ink Kill]!

Even Li Fan, the originator, had not anticipated this scene, his pupils contracting sharply as he looked at the spectacle of demons dancing before him.

The Dao Annihilation Tribulation, the black energy taking form.

It surged towards the only two living beings in this space-time.

And the vast majority of the targets were aimed at that sinister Su Bai.

Li Fan, relying on his nameless True Immortal cultivation in the illusion, could barely hold on and maintain his life from perishing.

Observing the sinister Su Bai's performance when facing the attack of this endless swarm of black energy formed beasts.

The sinister Su Bai was no longer as calm and playful as before.

Very cautiously, he avoided letting any of the black energy formed beasts touch his body.

With every movement, large swaths of formed beasts were turned into nothingness.

But the beast tide surged, and for a moment, he was also trapped.

The sinister Su Bai's brow furrowed, seeming to feel disgusted.

Li Fan only saw his body ripple like waves.

With each ripple, a figure of Su Bai simultaneously appeared in this space-time.

Their faces were not as clear as the sinister Su Bai's.

But Li Fan could vaguely discern their expressions.

Some were compassionate, like Mr. Bai of the Xuanhuang Realm. Some were like prodigals, unrestrained.

Some were like scholars, utterly useless and subservient. Some were like butchers, radiating killing intent.

The cultivation of each Mr. Bai was identical to that of the sinister Su Bai.

And all these Su Bais were like the black energy formed beasts,

Endless!

Under the encirclement of the Mr. Bai legion, the world-destroying black tide was also quelled.

But during the encirclement, they deliberately did not attack Li Fan.

As if reserving Li Fan's life for the sinister Su Bai.

Looking at the countless pairs of eyes staring intently at him, filled with mockery, ridicule, and compassion.

Li Fan decisively chose self-destruction.

...

Another new life.

"Even the Dao Annihilation Tribulation's black energy is not enough?"

This time, Li Fan did not resist but calmly pondered in the void.

"Perhaps only the true Dao Annihilation Tribulation can kill it."

Unfortunately, Li Fan had no idea what the Dao Annihilation Tribulation truly looked like.

Illusions without basis would not take effect in this space of eternal remnant will.

Before Li Fan's thoughts could wander, he was instantly killed by the sinister Su Bai again.

In the following long period.

Li Fan unleashed all his techniques, desperately resisting the sinister Su Bai.

While pondering a way to break the stalemate.

Even though each death in the Eternal Remnant Will could be ignored in terms of soul damage.

But once the number reached a certain threshold.

In reality, Li Fan's main body inevitably underwent changes.

"As long as I wish, I can withdraw from this trial at any time."

When the soul's upper limit was reduced by one-third.

The reborn Li Fan sensed the subtle changes.

But he did not choose to escape immediately.

Instead, he solemnly considered and made a decision.

"Actually, I already knew the method to deal with this sinister Su Bai."

"Even if I reincarnate countless more times, this only possible way to win will likely not change."

Li Fan pondered hesitantly.

"Although I can easily kill this sinister Su Bai's figure..."

"But it carries the risk of exposing [True Return]."

"Is it worth taking this risk?"

After an unknown amount of time, having died at the hands of the sinister Su Bai once more.

Just before death, looking at the detestable smile on the opponent's face.

The reborn Li Fan's eyes suddenly became resolute.

"Firstly, I believe in the character of this Mr. Bai of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Willingly sacrificing himself to the Dao for all mortals, he should not have set a trap in his own remains."

"Furthermore..."

A brilliance, unprecedented in Li Fan's eyes, erupted.

"I have ascended to immortality, no longer a mortal."

"Having accompanied [True Return] for so long, how could it be snatched away by a mere bone?"

In the real world, Li Fan's main body was prepared to True Return at any time.

In the Eternal Remnant Will illusory realm, looking at the sinister Su Bai, who was grinning and flying towards him not far away.

Li Fan's expression became arrogant, and he softly chanted.

"True becomes false, and false becomes true."

The flying sinister Su Bai's body suddenly stopped.

A look of disbelief appeared on his face.

Then his body gradually faded and disappeared before Li Fan's eyes.

The supremely arrogant and powerful sinister Su Bai, who could crush a Nameless True Immortal and remain unharmed even in the tide of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

Was so easily killed by Li Fan with a single thought.

"This is..."

"The Dao of True becomes False."

"Not a baseless fantasy."

"But a supreme Dao within reach."

"However, I am still far from mastering it."

In the illusion, after experiencing the taste of wielding supreme authority, Li Fan felt a faint sense of loss and melancholy.

Theoretically, he had successfully killed the sinister Su Bai.

The Eternal Remnant Will space gradually collapsed.

In a daze, he returned to reality.

Li Fan felt the excitement of True Return as if it had a full meal.

"Xuanhuang Heavenly Venerate truly loves all beings."

"Seeking life amidst death, returning with the world to True Return."

A moment later, Li Fan's mind heard the prompt from True Return.

Chapter 1414: Mr. Zhen Shan Bai

"Function [Dao Origin] unlocked."

"[Dao Origin]: When [True Return] can be activated, a designated area can accompany it, returning together to the state of the predetermined anchor."

"Alternatively, abandon this [True Return] opportunity and designate a certain area to negate [Dao Annihilation]."

...

Before Li Fan could carefully ponder the meaning of True Return's prompt, countless memories exploded in his mind like starlight.

Most were fleeting, discontinuous fragments.

But the Eternal Remnant Will skull contained an overwhelming amount of memories. It was as if this eternal remnant will was formed by layers upon layers of countless different intentions.

Even with Li Fan's divine soul and will, which were as firm as a True Immortal, he almost got lost in the overwhelming tide of these memory fragments.

Fortunately, [True Return] stood firm in the torrent like a shining star, unshaken. And among the torrent of consciousness fragments, there were a few extremely rare but largest ones.

Like beacons in white mist, lighthouses on the vast ocean, the North Star surrounded by numerous stars.

They continuously guided and marked the direction for Li Fan, preventing him from getting completely lost.

Boom!

Li Fan's intent slowly merged into Su Bai's remaining memories.

A world of ruins, with the air filled with the pungent smell of blood. Like a purgatory, corpses were piled on the ground.

There was no sound in heaven and earth, only extreme silence.

Blood flowed and gathered into a river.

From the dark red reflection, Li Fan saw the face of this body, it was the Heavenly Physician!

However, the "Heavenly Physician" in the reflection of the river of blood had eyes full of confusion and fear.

His body trembled uncontrollably.

A voice echoed in his mind.

The voice was exactly the same as Su Bai's own.

But it was filled with sinister intent.

"How is it? Satisfied?"

"What you always wanted to do, I've done it for you."

The "Heavenly Physician's" face contorted, trembling. It reverted to Su Bai's original appearance.

"What I always wanted to do?" he questioned desperately, his voice trembling.

The sinister Su Bai's voice was full of flippancy, "Wasn't it? Originally the esteemed one of this world, yet transmigrated to the Xuanhuang Realm via the Heavenly Soul Rebirth, attempting to use the Dao of [Medicine] to sow chaos within Xuanhuang and distract them from the expedition..."

"What I've done for you is no different from that [Heavenly Physician]!"

"Just... more thorough."

"Hahahaha..."

The sinister Su Bai's laughter echoed, filling the consciousness space.

"Oh, oh, the main person has arrived."

"Look at his expression; it's truly delightful!"

Su Bai gritted his teeth and cursed, "You damned beast!"

The anger could no longer be suppressed, erupting like a volcano. His body trembled, and his aura returned to the appearance of Mr. Bai of the Xuanhuang Realm.

The sinister Su Bai continued to shout, but his voice grew weaker and weaker.

"No need to be so angry."

"Even if these ants die a million times more, it's all meaningless. In my life, I've seen far more than..."

"Heh heh heh, it's much more tragic than that. At the very least, I kindly left their corpses behind."

"Besides, I am you, and you are me..."

His voice was like a mosquito's hum, no longer audible.

Sensing the approaching figure of the Heavenly Physician,

Su Bai's face was filled with pain.

But in the end, he gritted his teeth and rapidly fled.

...

In the endless dark void.

Su Bai reached out and touched the High Wall, as if blocked by an invisible barrier, unable to advance further.

"High Wall..."

Urgent, excited, and anxious thoughts continuously surged in his mind.

Su Bai pondered, then took out the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable's legacy, the immortal artifacts bestowed by the Immortal Realm.

One after another, they were arranged in a line.

"With so many immortal artifacts self-destructing, coupled with the Xuanhuang Realm's assistance, I should be able to cross this threshold."

Su Bai hesitated for a long time, then finally detonated the immortal artifacts.

In an instant, the fringes of the Star Sea seemed to simultaneously experience the rise of countless suns, even illuminating the Utmost Darkness Star Sea white.

Only the infinite light and heat were gathered upon Su Bai.

His appearance was obscured, his expression unclear, only a radiant white figure.

The figure stepped forward.

As if disappearing into thin air, a part of his body vanished.

With one foot across the confinement of the High Wall, about to completely escape the Utmost Darkness Star Sea surrounded by the High Wall,

Su Bai still looked back at the Xuanhuang Realm with lingering reluctance.

There were too many things in there that he cared about.

Just as Su Bai was lost in thought for a moment.

Suddenly, countless images inexplicably emerged in his mind.

And the content of these images made the naturally kind Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable's heart tremble violently.

Mountains of corpses and seas of blood, countless worlds successively destroyed, and the perpetrator of this monstrous slaughter was unexpectedly identical to him!

At the same time, Su Bai sensed an unprecedented sense of crisis.

His thoughts raced, and without any hesitation.

He actually retracted the leg that had already crossed the High Wall!

The brilliant light on his body gradually faded.

The shocked Su Bai, ignoring the Xuanhuang Realm's consciousness, which had suddenly gone berserk due to his inexplicable retraction,

"What... was that just now?"

As his expression constantly shifted, his mind suddenly heard his own voice.

The tone and inflection...

Were indescribably strange.

"Oh? There's actually one hidden here."

"Tsk tsk tsk..."

"As expected, they are still this foolish."

The change in tone even affected Su Bai's body.

Hints of sinister and manic aura appeared around his eyes.

Along with it, the Xuanhuang Realm Heavenly Dao consciousness attached to him also gradually lost its reason, spewing out all sorts of malicious words.

...

In the Celestial Sword Sect.

In the Sword Tomb, countless swords were pierced straight into the ground.

On each sword, a phantom floated. These were sword spirits born after countless years of tempering.

And now, these countless sword spirits were fighting against the same person.

It was Su Bai, sitting cross-legged in the center.

Countless sword energies crisscrossed, like surgical scalpels, slicing at Su Bai's divine soul and intent.

Su Bai's face maintained a calm expression throughout.

But he could not avoid occasionally flashing a look of pain.

At the edge of the Sword Tomb, the senior disciple of the Celestial Sword Sect watched this scene with an inexplicable expression.

He drank again and again from his wine gourd.

But this time, what flowed out was no longer wine.

But water.

After an unknown amount of time.

Buzz!

A violent shockwave suddenly erupted from Su Bai's body.

The Sword Tomb was instantly in disarray.

Countless sword spirits dissipated into nothingness.

Situ Yao's brow twitched.

But now was not the time to feel heartache. He flashed beside Su Bai.

"Great Heavenly Venerate, how are things?"

After a long silence.

After a long while, Su Bai's somewhat weak voice finally sounded, "The corrupted parts of my divine soul have been severed. Temporarily suppressed."

"But..."

"As that person said, doing this can only delay the inevitable. He will find me sooner or later."

Situ Yao's expression became solemn.

"So, are you still willing to continue executing that plan? Gambling with the lives of your entire Celestial Sword Sect?" Su Bai asked softly.

Situ Yao took another big gulp of water from his gourd.

"Even if we stay here, destruction is inevitable sooner or later."

"We swordsmen, why should we fear death?"

"Moreover, he is looking for you. We ants might not be targeted." His words indicated that a decision had been made.

Su Bai's expression became solemn, and he shakily stood up. As the Xuanhuang Great Celestial Venerable, he bowed to Situ Yao.

Situ Yao accepted it calmly.

...

In the Xuanhuang Realm.

Ningyuan City.

The vitality of mortals is as tenacious as wild grass.

On the ruins of the past, a bustling city had now re-emerged.

It was even more prosperous than before.

Su Bai walked the streets, his face seemingly filled with relief, yet also with a hint of melancholy.

Finally, he had reached his destination.

His original small house.

Recalling the past events that had happened here, Su Bai was filled with emotion.

Seeing the lovely children he had known in the past, now grown adults, Su Bai's eyes were again filled with joy.

"I shouldn't have deprived them of the hope of life."

"I must die."

He said softly.

"Before I die, let me do one small thing for this world."

Reversing the principles of heaven and earth to prove longevity!

Wondrous changes descended upon the Xuanhuang Realm.

...

In the Immortal Ruins.

A colossal figure resembling a skeleton sat cross-legged on the ground, at the center of mysterious characters.

A figure quietly appeared behind her.

And this True Immortal, who was comprehending the Dao, had no awareness of it.

That figure was Su Bai!

However, at this moment, he was wearing black robes. An indescribable madness flickered in his eyes.

"This is the culprit who created your Xuanhuang Realm, and even this Star Sea's calamity."

"As long as you nod, I will kill her right now."

Su Bai flicked his finger on the head of the Hunger Immortal, producing a clear sound.

However, this Comprehending Dao True Immortal remained completely unaware.

She was always immersed in her own enlightenment.

The answer to the sinister Su Bai was a long silence.

The sinister Su Bai did not urge, but instead, looked at the scenery of the Immortal Ruins with great interest.

"Just a broken character of [Hunger], and you've been comprehending for so long, yet you're still at this level."

"I've killed countless trash like this."

"And yet, trash of this caliber is what brought you millennia of suffering..."

The sinister Su Bai's tone was filled with mockery.

"Kindness? Evil? What meaning do they have in the face of survival?"

The sinister Su Bai raised his foot and continuously ground and trampled on the face of the Hunger Immortal.

He even leaned forward, getting close to observe.

Thinking of something, he occasionally let out faint laughter.

But the Hunger Immortal, from beginning to end, showed no reaction at all.

"See? Do you believe now that I wasn't lying?"

"Those things you saw were not hallucinations."

"But real experiences."

"The cruelty of reality far exceeds your imagination."

"A good person like you simply cannot adapt. Hand it over to me..."

He treated True Immortals like ants, but showed extraordinary patience towards Mr. Bai of the Xuanhuang Realm.

He rambled on, even becoming somewhat verbose in his persuasion.

Mr. Bai of the Xuanhuang Realm suddenly spoke, "You are so powerful..."

"Why were you stopped by a mere High Wall?"

The sinister Su Bai's voice abruptly halted.

With a forceful stomp, he stomped hard.

The Hunger Immortal, who was sitting cross-legged on the ground of the Immortal Ruins, was directly knocked over.

The golden chains binding her body rustled.

...

"That sinister Su Bai, he's not just Mr. Bai's baseless fantasy."

"He actually exists?"

Just as Li Fan's main body's intent was immersed in the Eternal Remnant Will left by Su Bai, feeling utterly horrified.

In the Museum of Divine Treasures, Li Fan's divine sense clone, led by Di San Mo.

Arrived at a seemingly unremarkable architectural ruin deep within the Museum of Divine Treasures.

This architectural ruin, placed alongside other historical ruins of the Xuanhuang Realm, seemed unremarkable.

"Does Upper Immortal recognize this place?"

Because of the earth-shattering scenes Li Fan perceived in the sinister Su Bai's Eternal Remnant Will, he appeared somewhat restless.

After a long while, he finally came to his senses.

"This place..."

After discerning it, Li Fan was slightly taken aback.

"Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain?" he asked the old man beside him, somewhat uncertainly.

"Upper Immortal has sharp eyes." Di San Mo nodded.

"But it's not the Sacred Beast Mountain of the Xuanhuang Realm. I brought this here from my homeland and kept it here for preservation."

"It's been an unknown number of years now." Di San Mo's tone was filled with ancient weariness.

Upon hearing this, Li Fan's expression also became serious.

He pondered the meaning behind Di San Mo's words.

"The Xuanhuang Realm originally had no demonic beasts."

"We fled here from another possibility, seeking refuge."

Di San Mo did not remain a riddle-man for long, stating directly.

Li Fan's expression trembled.

"Infinite futures hold infinite possibilities."

"But not all possibilities can continue indefinitely." Di San Mo sighed softly.

"We have reproduced and multiplied in the Xuanhuang Realm for too long, even forgetting our ancient past."

"We thought we could continue to survive here, but we didn't expect this place would also reach its end."

"So Di Yi once again led the clan on a path of flight, but this time, I decided not to leave." Di San Mo flashed and entered the ruins.

As if returning to his former hometown.

"Why?" Li Fan's clone asked curiously.

"Even with the Immortal Ruins appearing and the Star Sea withering, this might be one of the few relatively safe places." Di San Mo smiled.

Synthesizing Di San Mo's words with what he saw in the Eternal Remnant Will.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, his mind filled with thoughts.

...

In Su Bai's Eternal Remnant Will.

Li Fan's main body's spirit wavered. In the memories of the deceased Mr. Bai, he saw the sinister Su Bai.

Just how powerful he was.

With just a slight corruption, Longevity Realm Su Bai gained the power to crush True Immortals.

And as the corruption intensified, Su Bai also briefly experienced the sinister Su Bai's true power.

The world was no longer singular.

Instead, infinite possibilities arose simultaneously.

Su Bai saw countless possibilities for the Xuanhuang Realm's destiny after his death.

Amidst countless apocalyptic endings, he seemed to see the only path to survival.

Thus, Li Fan vaguely understood the reason for the establishment of this Eternal Remnant Will.

Chapter 1415: The Heavenly Doctor Understands the Dao and Dies

"Outside the High Wall, the existence of the sinister Su Bai is simply too shocking."

"It not only involves the power of the sinister Su Bai but also touches upon the truth of the entire mortal world."

"Infinite possibilities arising simultaneously..."

"No, it's far more complex than that!"

Li Fan looked at the memories of the deceased Mr. Bai of Xuanhuang, which flashed by like shooting stars.

He couldn't help but look at the countdown of seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand eight hundred sixty-four years on his [True Return] panel.

"In the sinister Su Bai's memories, there was not only monstrous slaughter but also scenes of truly terrifying calamities descending."

"Even with the sinister Su Bai's unfathomable power, in the face of that world-ending tribulation, he could only flee in disarray!"

"That was the instantaneous collapse of an entire timeline!"

"The true Dao Annihilation Tribulation!"

With the power of Xuanhuang Mr. Bai's Eternal Remnant Will, and through the eyes of the sinister Su Bai, Li Fan personally experienced the terror of the true Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

From the Xuanhuang Realm, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the Great Void outside the Star Sea, to countless immortal cultivation worlds. Including the Immortal Realm floating on the Infinite Sea.

This unimaginable, ineffable, magnificent world, its existence, collapsed in an instant.

It was annihilated without warning, silently.

Not even the concept of void remained.

Only by crossing to another possibility before the Dao Annihilation Tribulation reached oneself could one possibly survive.

...

"So, this seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand eight hundred sixty-four years is True Return's calculated countdown until all possibilities disappear?"

Li Fan's thoughts churned, his heart unable to calm down for a long time.

"The sinister Su Bai frantically slaughtered his other possible selves. Upon sensing Su Bai's existence within the High Wall, he used all sorts of methods, all to make Mr. Bai leap over the High Wall again and willingly surrender..."

"It seems that for him, his own existence in other possibilities is extremely important."

"In the sinister Su Bai's memories, each time he slaughtered himself, it was accompanied by monstrous slaughter, far more brutal than what he had done in the Heavenly Law Realm. That was a slaughter where not even corpses, blood, or memories were left, filling the world with void."

Compared to the sinister Su Bai's actions, Li Fan's world-destroying deeds were insignificant.

"Is it the sinister Su Bai's inherent nature, or is this the style of strong individuals at this level outside the High Wall?"

Li Fan took a deep breath.

"Regardless, the existence of the sinister Su Bai is more terrifying for the Xuanhuang Realm than the Dao Annihilation Tribulation itself."

"At least the Dao Annihilation Tribulation shows no signs of descending yet, but if the sinister Su Bai from outside the High Wall is attracted, the inside of the High Wall will likely be instantly turned into nothingness."

"Therefore, Mr. Bai willingly sought death, temporarily severing his connection with the sinister Su Bai. He even modified all memories of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao he followed, and all those in the inheritance trials in the Fallen Immortal Realm that involved the sinister Su Bai."

"Only leaving crucial information in his own Eternal Remnant Will."

Countless complex memories slowly faded.

Li Fan returned to reality, the skull in his hand transforming into specks of starlight and disappearing into the heavens and earth.

"During the period of corruption by the sinister Bai, Xuanhuang Mr. Bai's vision transcended a single possibility."

"Although I don't know what he exactly saw, it can be almost certain that this information was left for those who came later."

"No matter what method is used. Those who can pass the trial and theoretically defeat the sinister Su Bai are the only ones worthy of entrustment."

"The secret behind the sinister Su Bai's repeated survival and continued strength during the Dao Annihilation Tribulation!" A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"True Return awakened the [Body Transformation] function by absorbing Tian Yang's Eternal Remnant Will, stemming from Tian Yang cultivating [Transforming oneself into matter] to its extreme."

"And this time, by awakening the [Dao Origin] function, it is also due to the sinister Su Bai's cultivation method."

Li Fan squinted his eyes.

"Dao Annihilation. Dao Origin."

...

Deep within the Museum of Divine Treasures, at the ruins of Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain.

Li Fan's divine sense clone's conversation with Di San Mo continued.

"Our clan is not always so lucky, heading to worlds where the Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain is perfectly preserved."

"If by chance, the energy sealed within the Sacred Beast Mountain there has already been depleted, then it truly is a dead end." Di San Mo said with a chuckle.

Before Li Fan's eyes appeared the scene he saw in the Rift Realm Vortex, where Di Yi used a majestic divine face to extract a large bronze-colored key from within a white serpent, opening the vast energy within the Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain.

"So, it's a consumable item." Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

Di San Mo nodded, "This is also why I, and some other demonic beasts, did not follow. Di Yi allowed it. We were all gambling. After all, with our clan's characteristics, if Di Yi encountered an accident and was wiped out, another Di Yi would be born amongst the remaining group not long after."

"So far, this situation has not occurred. It seems Di Yi has won the gamble again." Di San Mo chuckled.

"But who can guarantee that they will always win?" Li Fan retorted.

Di San Mo remained silent.

"Even after leaping to another possibility, escape is impossible. I truly don't know where such a terrifying calamity originates from." After a moment of silence in the hall, Li Fan sighed softly.

"Upper Immortal, why not listen to a story." Di San Mo suddenly spoke.

"Not long ago... a strand of divine soul escaped from that device called [Era]. To experience billions of reincarnations within the Era, yet remain lucid. Such a divine soul characteristic is unprecedented."

Li Fan had also reincarnated within the Era, and hearing this, he became interested.

"It sounds like good material for creating Eternal Remnant Will." he thought inwardly.

"What is his condition now?" Knowing that Di San Mo would not speak without reason, Li Fan asked.

"He has completely vanished from the world." Di San Mo shook his head gently.

"He chose to hide in this ruin. The residual energy in the ruin could protect his fragile divine soul. But it was ultimately too little, and could not sustain him for long. Moreover, he would rather die than be thrown into the Era again..."

"By the time I discovered him, he had become too weak."

"However, during his final period, I discussed many things with him. Based on my memories, and the narration of the entire clan, he proposed the reason for the arrival of this terrifying world-ending calamity."

"Oh?" Li Fan's spirit was immediately uplifted.

"But it is only speculation, Upper Immortal can take it as entertainment." Di San Mo first reminded him like this, then slowly began to speak.

"The world knows that above True Immortals, there are Nameless True Immortals. Nameless True Immortals merge with the Dao. From then on, their records disappear from the mortal world, and they become ethereal and untraceable. Since ancient times, it is unknown how many have reached the Nameless Realm. But..."

Di San Mo waved his hand, and a phantom appeared in the ruin before him.

Countless thin lines, crisscrossing, supported the entire world.

"Although reaching the Nameless Realm is difficult, and the probability is small, in the face of infinite time, it is not such an illusory prospect."

"And for every Nameless True Immortal that is born..."

Di San Mo tapped his finger repeatedly.

The vertical lines in the phantom before him disappeared one by one.

Repeatedly, after an unknown amount of time.

The net of heaven and earth, due to this constant loss, became incomplete.

Slowly bending.

Li Fan's eyes suddenly narrowed.

Finally, the net of heaven and earth could no longer maintain its form.

With a loud boom, it collapsed!

Heaven and earth, were thus overthrown!

Di San Mo waved his hand, and the phantom before him disappeared.

"This is merely our superficial understanding, not the truth closest to reality."

"Perhaps, every Great Dao in heaven and earth is more important than we imagined. Even the absence of a few Great Daos is enough to cause the collapse of the entire possibility."

"Or, besides Nameless True Immortals merging with the Dao, there might be other unknown factors causing the Great Dao to disappear without reason, leading to an unstoppable world-ending calamity..."

Di San Mo's tone was melancholic.

Before Li Fan's eyes, the Nameless True Immortal's leg bone, used to construct the Southern Immortal Pillar, reappeared.

"Perhaps, this truth is already very close to the facts."

Di San Mo continued, "Precisely because countless possibilities are collapsing in a chain reaction, it has become exceptionally easy for us to act, fleeing from one possibility to another."

"Originally, even burning all the energy of the Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain would not have achieved this."

"To put it simply, it's as if, because of the continuous collapse of countless possibilities, they are becoming closer to each other..."

Li Fan listened intently.

Before his eyes, a picture seemed to emerge.

In the darkness, countless lines of light lit up simultaneously, arranged side by side, endless.

But suddenly, some of them began to disappear into the darkness for no reason.

Slowly, more and more light lines disappeared.

The remaining ones, under the influence of this inexplicable crisis, slowly moved closer.

Thus, inevitably, they became distorted and chaotic.

"Annihilation of the Great Dao."

"Crushing of the Great Dao."

Li Fan connected this with what he saw in the sinister Su Bai's memory, and a chill ran down his spine.

"What is the name of this divine soul? To have such speculation, it is certainly not an ordinary person." Li Fan's spirit wavered.

Di San Mo did not hide anything and casually summoned a phantom.

"This person's name is Qiao Si Dao."

"Half a year ago, he finally couldn't hold on and completely perished."

Li Fan looked at the person before him, the resolute expression in his eyes. He nodded slightly.

"Half a year ago..."

...

At the High Wall in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

The Heavenly Physician seemed to have forgotten Li Fan's threat and was wholeheartedly engrossed in comprehending the High Wall.

His progress was faster than he had anticipated.

Perhaps it was due to the countless attempts made over the years.

Or perhaps, after seeing Li Fan, a True Immortal, and personally witnessing the difference between immortals and mortals, a genuine realization surged in his heart.

In short, the Heavenly Physician had a vague premonition.

Perhaps he was not far from fully comprehending the secret of the High Wall.

Upon realizing this fact, the Heavenly Physician's expression underwent a subtle change.

He even began to doubt his actions over the years.

"Perhaps, what that True Immortal said was right?"

"If I had focused solely on cultivation, perhaps I could have found a way to save the Heavenly Law Realm long ago."

Such a thought flashed by.

The Heavenly Physician cast aside all distracting thoughts and once again immersed himself in comprehending the formless High Wall.

With sufficient accumulation, breakthroughs sometimes occurred in an instant.

A moment passed.

Or perhaps it was as long as ten million years.

The Heavenly Physician suddenly retracted all the golden threads he had emitted.

He seemed to have deciphered the mystery of the High Wall.

But at the same time...

An extreme sense of unease surged in his heart.

This unease was only present when the Heavenly Law Realm was massacred.

He had never experienced such a change even when directly facing that True Immortal.

"What exactly..." He stopped comprehending the High Wall's secret.

The Heavenly Physician instinctively wanted to distance himself from the High Wall.

Suddenly...

He seemed to discover something, his pupils contracting abruptly.

Where the formless High Wall was located in front of him, a place where nothing should have existed.

The scene inexplicably distorted.

His heart pounded again, the premonition of danger reaching its extreme.

A black thread suddenly appeared.

Silently, it pierced through the Heavenly Physician's chest.

One became a thousand, a thousand became ten thousand, ten thousand became a hundred million.

In an instant, it penetrated the Heavenly Physician's body, turning him into a puppet controlled by strings.

The Heavenly Physician's consciousness gradually blurred.

However, sensing the countless threads passing through him, he felt a sense of familiarity.

Perhaps it was an illusion, but shortly after, a figure appeared before him.

The Heavenly Physician seemed to see himself in his youth.

However, he was not wearing his favorite white robes.

But a black robe.

His face was neither happy nor sad.

Creak...

The Heavenly Physician's head twisted unnaturally by 180 degrees.

From the front, it turned to the back.

Streams of light and shadow floated from the Heavenly Physician's body into the mysteriously appearing black figure.

The Heavenly Physician's corpse slowly became ethereal and transparent.

And that black figure...

Or the young Heavenly Physician, frowned slightly.

"Do you understand?"

His gaze looked towards Li Fan's main body, who was not far away!

...

At the same time.

Li Fan, who was immersed in the secret of the sinister Su Bai outside the wall, also felt a sense of impending doom, just like the Heavenly Physician.

And this time, it was more intense than ever before.

"Could it be because I triggered Mr. Bai's Eternal Remnant Will, that the sinister Su Bai outside the wall sensed it?"

Li Fan was extremely terrified.

After only a moment of thought, without any hesitation, Li Fan inwardly invoked True Return.

It was also at this moment that Li Fan noticed something extremely strange.

On his True Return panel, his lifespan limit of over three million years was acting crazily, constantly fluctuating.

Not decreasing.

But increasing!

In the instant Li Fan noticed, it leaped from three million to tens of billions.

And it was increasing at an incredibly terrifying speed!

Chapter 1416: True and False, False and True

"What does this mean?"

"In True Return's deductions, the world-ending tribulation that affects countless possibilities shows signs of being reversed?"

As Li Fan silently chanted True Return at an incredibly rapid pace, the seven characters "When True becomes False, False is also True" exploded forth. Li Fan's heart was filled with astonishment.

"After I attained the realm of a True Immortal, the maximum lifespan displayed on the True Return panel is the estimated lifespan within this mortal world. Now that I face imminent disaster, why is the estimated lifespan of the mortal world not decreasing but increasing?"

In the span of a thousand thoughts,

The Dao Concealment domain descended upon the world.

Centered around Li Fan, within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea as far as the eye could see, everything was engulfed in a static black and white.

But unlike last time,

This time, within the completely still world, besides Li Fan, there was one other person capable of movement!

In the world of perfect stillness, that person was so conspicuous that Li Fan immediately sensed and locked onto their position.

And that person seemed to be looking in Li Fan's direction as well.

Their eyes met!

"Heaven… Physician?"

Although his appearance, clothing, and demeanor were vastly different from the Heavenly Physician Li Fan knew,

Li Fan recognized him at first glance.

Recalling the existence of the sinister Su Bai outside the High Wall, glimpsed in Mr. Bai's eternal remnant will, Li Fan instantly understood the source of the inexplicable sense of crisis in his heart.

"Outside the High Wall, there is not only sinister Su Bai but also a corrupted Heavenly Physician?"

"How did he…?"

Suddenly, Li Fan thought of the thousand-year agreement he had made with the Heavenly Physician within the High Wall. The Heavenly Physician, threatened by Li Fan with his life, had thrown himself entirely into understanding the principles of the High Wall to break through as quickly as possible.

"Sinister Su Bai was only perceived after Mr. Bai had one foot out of the High Wall. Before that, I didn't sense any immortal-level fluctuations. Before even crossing the High Wall, he was already detected by the corrupted Heavenly Physician?"

"Is this person's strength even above sinister Su Bai?"

Countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind.

In the black and white, static Dao Concealment region, the corrupted Heavenly Physician was still flying towards his position.

But it was as if he were trapped in slow motion.

Li Fan also saw that at the edge of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, at the foot of the High Wall, the continuous broken remnants of the Star Sea Great Wall looked like they had been ravaged by a mighty flood, becoming desolate and chaotic.

And the invisible High Wall that encircled the Utmost Darkness Star Sea seemed to have developed a breach.

Through that gap, the scene outside the High Wall was faintly discernible.

Unlike the desolate Utmost Darkness Star Sea, outside the High Wall, there was clearly abundant life gathered in various places. But within this somewhat prosperous life domain, there was a starkly uncoordinated, extremely abrupt blank straight line.

Like an ancient grand dao, leading towards an unknowable realm further away.

And here, at the end of this path, as if created by the rampaging charge of an ancient primordial fierce beast,

Li Fan's vision was inexplicably cut off.

As if covered by a towering shadow, as if blocked by a towering wall!

With no time to think, and neglecting to comprehend the matters within the Dao Concealment region,

Li Fan's thoughts raced, and he activated True Return.

He now understood why the estimated lifespan of the mortal world in True Return's deductions had suddenly soared.

This was a deduction of True Return falling into the hands of the corrupted Heavenly Physician!

"With the corrupted Heavenly Physician's current strength, he could wield True Return to save the mortal world from its great tribulation?"

Li Fan gritted his teeth inwardly.

He did not believe that the corrupted Heavenly Physician would spare his life after seizing True Return.

"The lifespan limit on the True Return panel is both for the mortal world and for me."

"Since it was not separated during the deduction, it means…"

"As the vessel of True Return, I likely cannot be separated. Instead, I would be refined into a magical treasure like the Law-Transmitting Jade."

Li Fan's heart turned ice-cold.

He intensified his activation of True Return, reining in the Dao Concealment domain.

The speed at which the black and white world returned was faster than the corrupted Heavenly Physician's movement speed in the stillness.

But what unsettled Li Fan was that the mist outside the Dao Concealment region was constantly churning and vibrating.

It seemed as if some terrifying existence might emerge from it at any moment.

"True Return!!"

Li Fan's final roar echoed in his heart.

Even if the corrupted Heavenly Physician could save the mortal world's great tribulation after obtaining True Return, Li Fan would never willingly hand over True Return.

Either the mortal world would be completely annihilated.

Or he, Li Fan, would be the sole savior.

If they wanted him to sacrifice himself…

Not a chance!

The rolling white mist eventually engulfed everything.

Li Fan's familiar consciousness plunged into a brief slumber as darkness approached.

…

After an unknown period, or perhaps an instant,

A Heavenly Physician in a black robe looked at his empty hands, a trace of bewilderment flashing in his eyes.

Looking back at the long trail of destruction he had caused, he frowned deeply.

With a single thought, he scanned the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

His divine sense paused slightly as it passed over the True Immortal comprehending the Dao in the Immortal Ruins.

There was a hint of hesitation, and then he reached out and picked up the skull-like Starving Immortal.

Flying out of the High Wall, passing through the long, blank passage.

As he looked up at the end,

The Heavenly Physician's body suddenly stiffened, and his hand holding the Starving Immortal loosened involuntarily.

He stood still on the spot.

…

Surrounded by endless darkness.

Li Fan's consciousness drifted as if floating in water.

In a state between consciousness and unconsciousness.

Li Fan was currently unaware and unknowing, observing his surroundings solely by instinct.

Not far away, a point of light seemed to ignite.

Then, tens of thousands of starlight shone forth sequentially.

Connecting into a line, piercing the darkness.

Li Fan's consciousness plunged towards this line of light.

Faster and faster.

As the light filled Li Fan, it transformed into countless light and shadow, erupting violently.

Anchor year 1, center of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea!

“Hoo!”

Like a drowning person desperately gasping for air from underwater, Li Fan instinctively took huge breaths.

Li Fan was still immersed in the immense pressure brought by the corrupted Heavenly Physician in the previous life.

"Hmm?"

As the fear gradually subsided, a mysterious scene of a white line illuminating in the darkness flashed through Li Fan's mind.

"…"

Every time True Return returned to the initial anchor point, it was the best time to comprehend the [Transformation of True and False].

Li Fan forcefully suppressed all distractions in his heart, experiencing the supreme power of True Return.

However, for some reason, the image of the white line remained imprinted in his mind, lingering for a long time. And by staring at the process of countless light spots connecting in the darkness, Li Fan's comprehension of [Transformation of True and False] was rapidly soaring at an extremely terrifying speed.

Li Fan did not question the origin, simply going with the flow and immersing himself.

After a long while, when the image in his mind faded into dimness.

He suddenly opened his eyes.

"False, is also True."

Li Fan slowly uttered these three words.

After experiencing the Transformation of True and False through repeated True Return simulations and personal experiences,

Li Fan now finally understood the meaning of the seven characters that had always accompanied True Return's appearance.

"When True becomes False…"

"Perhaps it refers to the world-ending tribulation that affects all possibilities. Countless worlds instantly transition from True to False, annihilated and disappearing. Not into a so-called void, but into a state of non-existence conceptually, into [False]."

"False is also True, referring to…"

Li Fan's expression became somewhat dazed for a moment.

"The power of True Return, creates a new possibility out of thin air within the false space-time consumed by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation!"

"This…"

Even though he had speculated about the upper limit of True Return's [Transformation of True and False] many times,

Li Fan was still stunned by his own realization at this moment.

"Wait, perhaps, it's not just that."

Suddenly, Li Fan seemed to remember something and eagerly opened the True Return panel again.

Ignoring the prompt for four inheritance choices, Li Fan stared intently at the lifespan limit column on the True Return panel.

Seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand eight hundred sixty-four years, thirteen days, and seven hours!

Chapter 1417: Saving Qiao Sidao

"Same as seen in the previous life."

"So, True Return's activation not only creates a new possibility out of nothing in false space-time but also resets the time node of the entire mortal world to the predetermined anchor point."

"This kind of power…"

Li Fan felt unprecedented shock.

Especially after witnessing the strength of sinister Su Bai and the corrupted Heavenly Physician, beings whose power seemed to transcend even Nameless True Immortals.

No matter how powerful they appeared, before True Return, they were all illusions! One thought could turn true, one thought could turn false!

According to this inferred power of True Return, theoretically, even the corrupted Heavenly Physician should not have been able to act within the Dao Concealment region after True Return was activated.

The only possible explanation seemed to be that Li Fan, as the vessel, was too weak, affecting True Return's efficacy.

"Weakness…"

Li Fan, who had already ascended to the Half-Immortal realm, felt a pang of discomfort. But he immediately thought that even though countless True Immortals died like ants during the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, being a Half-Immortal's "weakness" was not so difficult to accept.

Recalling how his estimated lifespan had frantically increased when he encountered the corrupted Heavenly Physician in his previous life, Li Fan's heart stirred.

The Transformation of True and False was suddenly activated.

Benefiting from personally witnessing the entire process of True Return creating a new possibility, Li Fan's comprehension of the Transformation of True and False had advanced by leaps and bounds.

Visualizing himself possessing Half-Immortal cultivation in the previous possibility.

As he thought, his cultivation descended upon his current body, layering upon itself.

Unlike before, when it could only last for a very short period, Li Fan could now maintain this illusory cultivation for nearly the time it takes to brew a cup of tea!

Even…

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and, focusing intently, attempted to layer his illusory cultivation once more.

It was indeed possible.

But the mental strain caused by this action instantly magnified more than tenfold.

The duration of layered cultivation also plummeted drastically, with significant fluctuations in stability.

"It's already this difficult to replicate just my own cultivation. It's hard to imagine creating an entire possibility out of nothing…"

Li Fan sighed, looking at the numbers on the panel.

Triple Half-Immortal cultivation, although not quite surpassing True Immortals, was likely close.

But…

Seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand eight hundred sixty-four years, thirteen days, and eight hours!

Such an increase in power, in True Return's deduction, could only delay the mortal world's destructive tribulation by one hour! It was better than nothing!

"It seems my current strength is still insufficient to interfere."

Li Fan's heart suddenly felt heavy.

Indeed, although True Return could reset the entire mortal world over and over again, preventing complete destruction.

But the mortal world's decline was an inevitable trend.

It was like endlessly pushing a stone up a mountain, only to have it inevitably roll back down to the bottom in an eternal cycle.

Only by reaching the level of sinister Su Bai or the corrupted Heavenly Physician did it seem possible to break the stalemate.

However, the appearance of these two individuals was too sudden and unreasonable.

And it completely exceeded Li Fan's expectations.

In Li Fan's original plan, he was supposed to proceed step by step, using the powers of the Xuanhuang Realm and the Xuanxian Boat to slowly explore outside the High Wall. To search for clues about the Nameless Immortal, the Cat Treasure, and even the fishing pond.

But now, the sudden arrival of these two had disrupted Li Fan's plans entirely.

Especially the existence of the corrupted Heavenly Physician, which filled Li Fan with lingering fear.

"Once the Heavenly Physician within the wall is sensed, the corrupted Heavenly Physician will instantly descend."

"Doesn't this mean that the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea has been on the brink of life and death all these years? If the Heavenly Physician hadn't been preoccupied with his homeland and focused most of his energy on reviving the Heavenly Law Realm, he might have summoned the corrupted Heavenly Physician long ago!"

"Even, according to the Heavenly Physician's comprehension progress shown in the previous life, he would not have taken long to fully decipher the secret of the High Wall. It's ironic that after successfully reviving the Heavenly Law Realm, the Heavenly Physician's death would also be imminent…"

Li Fan's thoughts raced.

He suddenly remembered the previous life's cycle when he was the Formation Breaking Jade Disc, experiencing thousands of years.
