Anchor year 2078, the world fell into absolute silence.

Only at anchor year 3024, did the long-awaited sunlight appear.

"It seems that due to the corrupted Heavenly Physician's existence, the Xuanhuang Realm will eventually face a dead end under normal circumstances."

"But with the corrupted Heavenly Physician's intervention, the Xuanhuang Realm, or the newly born Heavenly Law Realm, did not completely turn to dust, and there was still hope for revival after a thousand years…"

"It's likely that the corrupted Heavenly Physician showed mercy out of sentiment."

Li Fan pondered inwardly.

Due to the existence of the corrupted Heavenly Physician and sinister Su Bai within the wall, beings of terrifying strength, Li Fan's plans for this life had to be significantly altered. At the very least, he must prevent the Heavenly Physician from getting close to the High Wall again.

"The situation outside the High Wall is still unclear."

"In the previous life, within the Dao Concealment black and white domain, through the straight blank path created by the corrupted Heavenly Physician's collision, I vaguely glimpsed the scene outside the High Wall."

"It seemed to be a normal Star Sea, with abundant life scattered about. And at the end of my vision, something blocked my sight."

"Is there another High Wall outside the High Wall?" Li Fan couldn't help but doubt.

"To understand the current situation outside the High Wall, perhaps I should start with that descendant of the Heavenly Sword Sect."

Shifting his attention back to the True Return inheritance options, Li Fan pondered for a moment and chose to accelerate the charging speed.

True Return's charging speed had always been closely related to Li Fan's strength.

After ascending to Half-Immortal, this was the first time he chose this option, and Li Fan was pleasantly surprised to notice a difference from before.

After Li Fan's realm changed to Immortal on the True Return panel, upon returning instantly, the Void Transformation charging progress was already 50%. And when Li Fan chose to accelerate charging again, this progress bar jumped again.

It directly reached 99%!

"The required waiting time has been greatly reduced."

"Unfortunately, it's not yet 100%."

"A 1% difference is like heaven and earth!"

If True Return could be fully charged after each acceleration option, it would mean Li Fan could activate True Return continuously.

Even if he encountered enemies who could traverse possibilities in the future, he could calmly escape in an instant.

But this 1% gap meant he still had to wait for at least seven days.

"Before I can achieve 100% charging instantaneously, I must act with extreme caution."

As Li Fan's strength increased, the beings he encountered became increasingly unfathomable.

Especially beings like the corrupted Heavenly Physician, who could pursue across possibilities and act within the Dao Concealment region, posing too great a threat to Li Fan.

"I wonder if ascending to the True Immortal realm can suppress him?"

The corrupted Heavenly Physician's extremely indifferent eyes, so similar to his own, flashed in Li Fan's mind again, and he fell into contemplation.

Seven days later.

True Return was fully charged, and Li Fan's figure flickered, silently teleporting into the Xuanhuang Realm.

His destination was naturally the soul hidden within the Museum of Divine Treasures at the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, named Qiao Sidao.

Having maintained his own consciousness through hundreds of billions of reincarnations, and able to deduce the possible truth of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation based on Di Sanmo's description,

Li Fan was very interested in him.

"If possible, perhaps he can replace me in exploring outside the High Wall."

"But I also need to be wary if there's another Qiao Sidao outside the wall."

Li Fan passed by Mr. Bai's skull, his footsteps pausing.

True Return, having absorbed it once, unsurprisingly provided no further prompts.

As for the trial illusion of sinister Su Bai within Mr. Bai's skull, Li Fan avoided it.

Without paying it any further mind, he headed straight for the ruins of the Southern Nether Sacred Beast Mountain in the Museum of Divine Treasures.

"Speaking of which, even though True Return can create possibilities out of thin air with a single thought, it still needs to 'consume' certain exotic items within those possibilities."

Li Fan's thoughts drifted.

And True Return seemed to sense his thoughts, seeming to send out a mocking sneer, mixed with helplessness.

But afterward, no matter how he sensed it, there were no further fluctuations.

Arriving at the Southern Nether Mountain ruins, Di Sanmo had been waiting for a long time.

Just like in the previous life, he said respectfully, "Greetings, Senior!"

Although Li Fan did not display any actual combat power in this life, being able to silently ignore all the restrictions of the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters and arrive at the Museum of Divine Treasures,

It undoubtedly proved his power.

Li Fan saw from Di Sanmo's change in expression that he did not have the memories from the previous life.

His heart relaxed slightly, and without speaking, he simply nodded and observed the ruins before him.

Indeed, as Di Sanmo had said, there were still faint traces of mysterious energy remaining here.

And within these dwindling remnants of energy, a severely weakened divine soul was hidden.

Under the concealment of the mysterious energy, even Li Fan, who was already a Half-Immortal, would not have easily detected it without Di Sanmo's specific reminder.

The appearance of the divine soul was no different from what Di Sanmo had described in the previous life.

Li Fan reached out, directly taking half of Qiao Sidao's life-saving energy.

As if a wilting pond suddenly received rain, Qiao Sidao's extremely fragile divine soul visibly became somewhat stronger.

After Qiao Sidao completely absorbed the energy sphere, Li Fan's thoughts moved, and he canceled the Transformation of True and False.

His divine sense enveloped Qiao Sidao, observing every subtle change within him.

As Li Fan expected.

Although the buffs from the Transformation of True and False had disappeared, the energy spheres generated out of thin air during its effect, having a carrier, did not completely dissipate.

Instead, a small amount of residual energy remained.

Although this proportion was small, it was still of great significance to Li Fan.

After resting for a short while, Li Fan activated the Transformation of True and False again and produced a second sphere.

When the first energy sphere was produced by Li Fan, Di Sanmo only thought it was the energy Li Fan had just extracted.

But now, seeing Li Fan produce a new one after exhausting the previous one,

Di Sanmo's always calm face could no longer maintain its composure.

And Li Fan also noticed that throughout this process, the other party seemed unaware of the workings of the Transformation of True and False.

Although the fluctuations of the Transformation of True and False were extremely obvious to Li Fan.

"However, I cannot afford to be careless."

"Perhaps besides me as a vessel, there are other powerful beings in the world who can detect the activation of the Transformation of True and False."

"In the future, when using divine abilities, I must always pay attention to my own safety."

While contemplating, through continuous activation of the Transformation of True and False and the relentless infusion of numerous mysterious energy spheres,

Qiao Sidao finally showed signs of improvement.

He awoke from his coma.

"Third Uncle, what is this…" Qiao Sidao quickly realized the unusual scene.

Reacting quickly, despite his weakened state, he expressed his gratitude to Li Fan for saving his life.

Li Fan nodded slightly and continued his actions without stopping.

Using materials from the Museum of Divine Treasures as raw ingredients, he fashioned a temporary body for Qiao Sidao.

After infusing his divine soul into it, Li Fan finally stopped.

Continuously using the Transformation of True and False was also a significant burden for him.

He stood and panted for a moment, not showing the slightest sign of fatigue.

Simultaneously waiting for Qiao Sidao to adapt to this new body.

In just half a day, Qiao Sidao had recovered from his near-death state.

All of Di Sanmo's previous efforts were in vain, but now, with a simple intervention from the senior before him, decay had been transformed into the miraculous…

How could Qiao Sidao not understand the terrifying strength of the person before him?

Bowing slightly, Qiao Sidao sincerely thanked him, "Thank you for saving my life, Senior!"

And Di Sanmo seemed to have not yet recovered from his shock, his body still trembling slightly.

Li Fan extended his right hand and placed it on Qiao Sidao's head.

A strand of divine sense entered Qiao Sidao's divine soul.

Faced with his savior and the absolute difference in strength, Qiao Sidao's expression changed slightly, but ultimately, he did not resist.

He allowed Li Fan to observe the memories within his divine soul.

Chapter 1418: The Ancient Dao Takes Shape

Weakness and power, two contradictory terms, seemed to be unified in Qiao Sidao's personage.

Even though his divine soul was on the verge of dissipation, about to perish at any moment before Li Fan saved him. Yet, his vast and complex memories made even Li Fan slightly change expression.

"If my divine soul's strength were only this much, it would be utterly insufficient to support so many memories…"

Setting aside the peculiarity of Qiao Sidao's divine soul for now, Li Fan first roughly scanned the scenes within Qiao Sidao's countless memories.

Most of the worlds deduced by [Era] did not interest Li Fan. Even the various cultivation techniques and divine abilities that Qiao Sidao had encountered and learned in them were of little use to Li Fan now.

However, the ancient secrets of the Immortal Realm that Qiao Sidao had occasionally gleaned during his multiple entries into the Ten Great Immortal Sects were somewhat more useful.

"I just don't know how much of this information is real. Is it just a setting within the deduced worlds, or are they traces passed down from the destruction of various realms…"

After examining all the worlds Qiao Sidao had experienced in his hundreds of billions of reincarnations, only two were worth Li Fan's extra attention.

One was [Eternal Immortal Realm], and the other was [Turbulent Space-Time].

The Eternal Immortal Realm was a perfect world in the deduction, where cultivation civilization had reached its extreme without a world-ending tribulation. Not only was the average lifespan extremely long, but even without cultivation, one could live for thousands of years. There was also a great existence called the [Immortal Spirit Tower].

The Immortal Spirit Tower permeated every corner of the world, releasing pure spiritual energy outwards day and night. Any knowledge you wished to comprehend, be it cultivation techniques, formations, alchemy, or medicine… could be queried and learned within the Immortal Spirit Tower without restriction.

It was within the Immortal Spirit Tower that Qiao Sidao accumulated enough experience to escape from the [Era] device.

After all, it was merely a theoretical system within a deduction, and could not be entirely applied to reality.

With Li Fan's current insight, he could immediately discern the disharmony in various techniques Qiao Sidao had learned.

"Almost but not quite. It might be effective within the virtual [Era] world, but…"

Li Fan used an extremely powerful formation from Qiao Sidao's memories as an experiment.

The formation was named [Heaven and Earth Reversed]. Although the name was unremarkable, once the formation was complete, it could truly invert the sky and earth of a region. Any being incapable of flight would uncontrollably fall from the ground towards the sky. Either they would starve to death during the fall, or they would crash into the world's boundary and be shattered into pieces.

If it were truly as described, then this formation would indeed be quite interesting. But when Li Fan brought it into the Dissolution Disc for testing…

The result was that this formation could not be formed at all.

"Perhaps in a possibility exactly identical to the deduced world, this formation could operate normally. But in the current reality, where the Great Daos are missing and conflicting, the operating environment is unsuitable."

Although it couldn't be used directly, Li Fan did not feel disappointed.

"It points out a certain possibility, which doesn't match reality, but with appropriate modifications, it can operate."

"Qiao Sidao merely survived within the virtual [Era] device, and his understanding of reality only stemmed from his experiences within Era, so he might not possess such capabilities. But I am different."

In his Sea of Consciousness, the Immortal Formation Dissolution Disc pulsed with brilliant light.

The formation data, like rivers of light, was extracted from Qiao Sidao's memories and transferred to the Dissolution Disc.

Qiao Sidao's divine soul felt like it was being tortured by a thousand knives, and he couldn't help but let out a muffled groan. If Li Fan hadn't stabilized his divine soul, this action alone could have directly scattered his soul.

But Qiao Sidao indeed deserved to be someone who struggled and escaped from endless reincarnation. After that, he remained silent, even gradually getting used to the suffering, his expression gradually returning to normal.

It did not take too much time.

Through the transformation of the Dissolution Disc, countless formations in Qiao Sidao's memory were transformed from false formations into real formations that suited the reality!

Li Fan, with a flip of his hand, sent the conclusions deduced by the Dissolution Disc back to Qiao Sidao.

Qiao Sidao, keenly sensing the difference between the formations conveyed by Li Fan and what he had learned and known, was first stunned, then became uncontrollably excited.

Qiao Sidao could still recall how powerful he was in the Era after experiencing countless reincarnations, capable of deciphering the greatest mysteries of heaven and earth and breaking free from the deadlock. But upon arriving in the real world, the extreme contrast made it difficult for him to accept at first.

So fragile that it seemed any gust of wind could extinguish his divine soul. Qiao Sidao knew this was the difference between [Era] and reality.

But now…

Through the changes between the two formations conveyed by the mysterious senior before him, Qiao Sidao seemed to have a glimpse of the specific nature of this difference.

"When one law is understood, all laws are understood. As long as I am given some time, I should be able to complete the transformation of all my knowledge." Qiao Sidao greedily absorbed the knowledge transmitted by Li Fan, even forgetting to thank Li Fan for a moment.

Li Fan did not mind. He could also see that Qiao Sidao was currently in the process of enlightenment.

This divine soul had indeed not disappointed him.

It was usable!

Li Fan then turned to ask Di Sanmo, continuing the unfinished conversation from the previous life.

"What kind of strength is required to leap across possibilities?"

"What is this energy contained within the Sacred Beast Mountain?"

Li Fan spoke, and simultaneously used the Transformation of True and False to materialize another sphere of ancient bronze-colored energy, tossing it towards Di Sanmo.

Li Fan's two questions had already made this long-lived beast, after being immensely shocked, become somewhat nervous.

And when he greedily absorbed this extremely pure energy, feeling the revitalization in every corner of his body. Di Sanmo confirmed that the person before him had definitely reached that legendary level.

Perhaps this body was already too ancient and decayed. The extremely pure and righteous [Ancient Cang Origin] he swallowed was actually slowly seeping away, leaving only a small residue in the end.

But even this small amount was significant to him. At the very least, it could extend his lifespan by tens of thousands of years.

What was more crucial was that he had personally witnessed the senior before him continuously producing [Ancient Cang Origin] as if performing magic.

This divine item, which was supposed to be consumed one part at a time, if it were inexhaustible…

In an instant, countless thoughts flashed through Di Sanmo's mind.

But in the end, they all coalesced into one firm resolve.

No matter what, he had to stay by this senior's side!

For survival, whether his own or that of his entire clan, Di Sanmo had sided with different individuals multiple times.

First, it was Di Yi, then the Beast Taming Sect, and later the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable.

The hope Di Sanmo saw in all these combined did not equal what he saw in the person before him now.

He was not someone who hesitated.

Once decided, he immediately put it into action.

At this moment, when Li Fan asked, Di Sanmo answered directly and without reservation.

"To let Senior know, according to our clan's ancient memory inheritance. In the vast primordial beginning, even the [Primordial Dao Form], which merged with the Dao, could not easily leap across possibilities."

"If we were to compare the Primordial Dao Form to human cultivators, it could be seen as the [Nameless True Immortal] realm. But compared to human cultivators' enlightenment, the great Primordial Dao Forms were naturally derived and manifested from the Dao itself. In terms of strength and comprehension of the Dao, they were inherently superior. Except for certain supreme experts, most Nameless True Immortals could not compare to Primordial Dao Forms." Even though he intended to completely pledge allegiance to Li Fan, Di Sanmo did not embellish his words, merely recounting according to the inherited memory. Li Fan listened without comment, gesturing for Di Sanmo to continue.

"The existence of Primordial Dao Forms was both an advantage and a disadvantage. Because some powerful Daos among the Great Daos of heaven and earth did not manifest as Dao Forms, and due to innate exclusion, they forever lost the opportunity to comprehend these Daos. However, human cultivators are different. Any inherent Dao of heaven and earth can be refined and mastered by humans." Di Sanmo's tone suddenly became somber.

"This was also the beginning of our clan's catastrophe."

"In our primordial world, the number of human cultivators was far less than ours. Humans were mostly treated as pets and food by us. We monopolized the methods of cultivation, and only obedient humans could cultivate. They became our pawns, helping us suppress other humans…"

Di Sanmo slowly recounted the secrets of the demonic beasts.

Qiao Sidao, who was comprehending nearby, couldn't help but listen in. Even in his countless reincarnations within Era, he had never experienced this history. Hearing that humans were merely food for demonic beasts, he couldn't help but frown slightly. He had been cared for by Di Sanmo for a long time, but he had never heard him speak of this matter.

Only Li Fan's expression remained unchanged.

"We are not a short-sighted or unintelligent race. From the human cultivators who defected to us, we saw the terrifying potential contained within the human body. Thus, we intensified our control over humans."

"According to the normal trajectory of history, theoretically, human cultivators in our homeland had no possibility of rising."

"And in reality, it was indeed so. Because a great variable came from outside the world's possibilities!"

Di Sanmo's tone carried a hint of helplessness as he reached this point.

Li Fan, hearing this, seemed to understand something, a sharp glint flashing in his eyes.

"One day, a great calamity inexplicably descended upon our clan."

"A [Nameless True Immortal] actually crossed possibilities and descended into our space-time. He witnessed the plight of humans and began a frenzied slaughter and revenge."

"Initially, there were thirteen [Primordial Dao Forms] in our clan. However, in the battle with that Nameless True Immortal, more than half of them were killed or injured…"

Although Di Sanmo's tone was calm, Li Fan could sense the deep fear hidden within.

"Although that Nameless True Immortal retreated temporarily due to his injuries, before leaving, he plundered the remains of the five Primordial Dao Forms that were slaughtered by him. If he were to refine the Great Dao contained within these remains, our clan would surely face annihilation."

"The remaining [Dao Forms] exhausted countless possibilities but could not find a way for the clan to win. Thus, in despair, they had no choice but to choose to flee."

"However, as I mentioned before, in the primordial beginning, it was extremely difficult to cross possibilities. Even if the remaining eight [Dao Forms] sacrificed themselves completely, most of the clan could not escape."

"Exhausting everything in the world could only allow one person to escape!"

Li Fan's mind instantly flashed with the image of Di Yi.

"Myriad Manifestations Unification?"

Di Sanmo nodded.

"Our clan is all derived from Primordial Dao Forms. At that time, to maintain a sliver of life, only melting and returning to the ancient was possible."

"To maximize the integrity of the surviving clan in the future."

"Countless clan members, whether voluntarily or by force, entered that massive furnace."

"Finally, they merged to become [Di Yi]," Di Sanmo said calmly.

"It's a pity that the most primal and most powerful Primordial Dao Forms were already missing five."

"And then seven more, contributing themselves and disappearing while crossing possibilities."

"Thirteen Primordial Dao Forms, leaving only one. Our clan, from then on, could no longer achieve the glory of the primordial era." Di Sanmo's tone was somewhat melancholic.

"Seven Primordial Dao Forms are needed to leap across timelines?" Li Fan did not pay attention to Di Sanmo's emotions, his eyes narrowing.

"These are old accounts from the primordial era. Since the great tribulation descended, the upper limit of power required to leap across possibilities has been continuously lowering." Di Sanmo waved his hand, and countless illusions appeared in the Southern Nether Mountain ruins before them.

Exactly the same as what Li Fan had seen in the Fallen Immortal Realm.

"As the saying goes, 'be vigilant in times of peace.' After completing the escape, although temporary safety was achieved. Di Yi also successfully separated the myriad manifestations of the clan. But the terror brought by that Nameless True Immortal still lingered in our hearts."

"Therefore, we have been searching for a way to escape possibilities."

"[Ancient Cang Origin] is our discovery."

Li Fan reached out, and the ancient bronze-colored energy sphere reappeared.

"[Ancient Cang Origin]?" Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

"This is our clan's own name for it. In fact, human cultivators should have another name for it. Because this item was actually discovered by us in the ruins of human cultivators. But I have integrated into human society for tens of thousands of years, yet I have never found any records about this item." Di Sanmo explained in detail.

"The divine mask that seals the Ancient Cang Origin, and the key to unlocking the restriction, were both obtained by us in the ruins."

"This ruin is in the Xuanhuang Realm?" Li Fan's eyes gleamed.

Di Sanmo nodded. "Every possibility has subtle differences in its name and actual location. But at least in the possibilities we have experienced, its existence can be found in this general region."

"It seems you have experienced more than just one escape," Li Fan's eyes narrowed as he stared at Di Sanmo.

"In the face of infinite possibilities, time and number of times have little significance."

Di Sanmo looked towards the now empty Rift Realm Vortex.

Chapter 1419: The Ancient Path Perishes Forward

"Ultimately, whether one survives or not is the most important thing," Di Sanmo said with immense gravity.

In the Rift Realm Vortex, winds and clouds surged, and rain poured down year-round. Any traces of the former Southern Nether Mountain had long since vanished into the river of history.

After a long silence in the air, Di Sanmo spoke again. "Besides evading the pursuit of that Nameless True Immortal, the subsequent world-ending tribulation of heaven and earth also forced us to constantly flee. Although we were fortunate enough to always find Ancient Cang Origin to leap and escape, the facts we discovered also led to inevitable pessimistic emotions arising in our hearts."

"To prevent these emotions from having a fatal impact on the clan. Di Yi chose to fracture and derive these emotions, and then let them self-destruct…"

Li Fan naturally knew about the powerful demonic beasts with various peculiar temperaments within the demonic beast clan. He keenly sensed the key point in Di Sanmo's words: "Facts?"

"Infinite futures hold infinite possibilities. This was our original general perception of all worlds. But through repeated leaps and escapes, we began to doubt this perception. Theoretically, each leap should take us to a completely new possibility. The temporal node of arrival in that possibility should also be random. For example, if our luck were good enough, we might even arrive in a world where the twelve Primordial Dao Forms had not yet been slaughtered and the clan was still powerful."

"Perhaps our luck wasn't good enough, and we never encountered it. If it were only this, it would be fine, but…"

Di Sanmo's expression became extremely solemn. "What terrified us was that with each leap, the temporal node of arrival kept shifting towards the future. Although we leaped across possibilities, it seemed we did not reverse our position in the temporal dimension."

"This is also the fundamental reason why I always use 'possibility' instead of timeline to describe it."

Li Fan and Qiao Sidao immediately understood Di Sanmo's meaning.

Qiao Sidao lowered his head, deep in thought, hiding the fear in his heart.

But Li Fan thought of the fact that every time he activated True Return, the entire mortal world's temporal node was reset.

"The Dao Annihilation Tribulation is not only destroying countless possibilities but also seems to be devouring the entire river of time of the mortal world from its source."

"It's like no matter how I activate True Return, I can never go back to before anchor year 1."

"Thinking further, if the mortal world did not possess a wondrous item like True Return, wouldn't that mean…"

"Escape is impossible?" Li Fan's eyes flickered.

If what Di Sanmo said was true, then the scale and terror of this Dao Annihilation Tribulation, and the importance of True Return, were likely far beyond his imagination.

However, Li Fan had not yet managed to leap across possibilities without the aid of True Return, so he could not confirm the authenticity of the information provided by Di Sanmo.

It was even possible that the demonic beast clan was simply too unlucky, and every leap of possibility just happened to be towards the "future."

Countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind in an instant. However, without the ability to verify it now, aimless speculation was useless. Thus, he shifted the topic back to the ruins where Ancient Cang Origin was discovered in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Li Fan had the location and detailed information of the ruins described by Di Sanmo.

His heart stirred slightly. He drew a map of the original Xuanhuang Realm in the air, pointing to a certain location in the center. "Is it here?"

Di Sanmo carefully discerned for a moment, then nodded.

Li Fan suddenly had a vague answer.

The location of Ancient Cang Origin should be the core hub of the ancient immortal formation in the Xuanhuang Realm. Its age was even older than Xuan Tian King's Star Crossing Great Formation, tracing back to the creation of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"My previous guess was that the Xuanhuang Realm was originally created as a testing ground to study how to resist the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. For example, the high similarity between Mo Sha and the black energy of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. And the countless figures resembling Mo Sha that appeared fleetingly when the Dao Annihilation black energy spread like a tide in the previous life, all indirectly confirmed my guess."

"However, my understanding of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation was previously limited to simple black energy, and I didn't realize that this tribulation could even affect countless possibilities."

"I have only truly encountered the Dao Annihilation Tribulation for a short time. In the previous Immortal Realm, there were even existences at the Nameless True Immortal realm. They must have understood the Dao Annihilation Tribulation even more deeply than the demonic beast clan."

"It is understandable that a testing ground that can leap across timelines would be left behind in the Xuanhuang Realm."

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the scene he saw within the True Immortal's memories in the flesh of True Immortals.

"...Qionglang Star Domain... Annihilation... Guarding..."

"...Target found."

When his understanding of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation reached a certain level, looking back at these words, Li Fan gained a new perception of information that he couldn't grasp before.

"The Immortal Realm was not entirely powerless against the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. The Dao Annihilation Tribulation did not suddenly devour all beings on an entire possibility. Instead, it was a gradual fall of different regions. Perhaps this was the contribution of the Immortal Heavenly Pillar, which was made from the remains of Nameless True Immortals."

"And after hearing the news that Qionglang Star Domain was engulfed by the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, I did not feel any particular panic from the True Immortal's memories. Clearly, the people of the Immortal Realm at that time were not so pessimistic about the Dao Annihilation Tribulation."

"I just don't know what happened later that caused the sudden destruction of the Immortal Realm."

With his thoughts drifting, Li Fan pondered further.

The Dao Annihilation Tribulation completely annihilated possibilities. Even the lofty Immortal Realm had vanished into the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, so under normal circumstances, the lower Star Sea should have also disappeared.

But it had still persisted for tens of thousands of years…

"Perhaps it is related to the civilization with abundant life I saw outside the High Wall in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea."

Li Fan mused deeply.

The situation he faced now was similar to when he was a mortal, leaving Great Xuan and coming to the Xuanhuang Realm, where he immediately learned of the existence of the True Immortal in the Immortal Ruins and even the Formless High Wall.

"Looking too far ahead only confuses the mind."

"It's better to proceed step by step, taking things slowly."

…

Li Fan fell into contemplation, neither Di Sanmo nor Qiao Sidao dared to interrupt.

"First, organize your knowledge and transform it into something usable in reality. Later, I will find a tailored cultivation technique for you…"

Qiao Sidao's expression became serious, and he bowed, "Thank you, Senior."

Li Fan then turned to Di Sanmo and said, "Are you willing to work for me?"

He asked a simple question, yet Di Sanmo had spoken so much, revealing almost all of his clan's secrets. Li Fan, familiar with human nature, naturally understood Di Sanmo's intent.

Clearly, after witnessing the supreme power of True Return displayed by Li Fan, he had the thought of pledging allegiance and dependence. Thus, he directly asked.

Di Sanmo answered directly and with a slight bow, "I am willing to serve Senior wholeheartedly!"

Li Fan nodded slightly. "You have the inheritance memories of the beast race stretching back countless years, your intelligence is extraordinary, your knowledge is vast, and in some aspects, you even surpass me. You are perfect for advising me!"

"At this point, there is nothing left to hide. I have indeed come to this world from another possibility!" Li Fan said solemnly.

Qiao Sidao showed a hint of surprise.

But Di Sanmo seemed to have expected it.

After all, this "True Immortal" who suddenly appeared, and Li Fan's question, "What kind of strength is required to leap across possibilities," undoubtedly indicated his uniqueness.

"However, I did not actively leap across possibilities to come here," Li Fan frowned, seeming to recall.

Overall, its strength was far greater than here. Furthermore, it did not face the danger of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation descending in the short term. Who would have thought…"

Li Fan's expression darkened. "One day, two extremely terrifying powerful beings suddenly descended. Their strength even surpassed mine! With a mere gesture, they destroyed my homeland! Even with True Immortal strength, before these two, we were like ants!"

"But for some reason, these two powerful beings seemed to be on different paths. Soon after, they began to fight each other. Heaven and earth were in turmoil, and I could only flee desperately driven by instinct. In a daze, I arrived here…"

Li Fan's words were thrilling.

He even conjured images from time to time.

The scenes of heaven and earth collapsing and the Star Sea being destroyed made even Qiao Sidao and Di Sanmo's expressions change slightly.

And when Di Sanmo saw the sinister Su Bai and the corrupted Heavenly Physician depicted by Li Fan, his expression couldn't help but show horror.

Li Fan had been waiting for this moment, and his tone suddenly changed. "Hmm? You seem to recognize these two?"

Di Sanmo dared not speak recklessly. After carefully discerning again, he said, "These two should be supreme powerhouses capable of leaping across possibilities using their own strength."

"In the history of this world, these two were also Prodigies of their generation. In fact, one of them is still alive today. And furthermore…"

Di Sanmo paused and continued, "They have a close relationship with the actual controller of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable."

He briefly introduced Su Bai and the Heavenly Physician to Li Fan.

Li Fan frowned upon hearing this. "Come to think of it, my world also seems to have these two figures. However, with countless sects and prominent prodigies emerging, they weren't particularly eye-catching."

"Could it be that those two powerful beings were pursuing their other possible selves?" Li Fan's words caused Di Sanmo and Qiao Sidao to exchange glances, their faces showing shock.

After another long silence.

Li Fan looked towards the outside of the Museum of Divine Treasures. "Without reaching the Immortal realm, all are ants. The Heavenly Physician of this world is not worth mentioning. I am more concerned about whether those two powerful beings might sense it and also arrive here."

This question clearly exceeded Di Sanmo's knowledge.

This wise beast was unable to answer for a time.

"It seems I have no choice but to strike first and kill that Heavenly Physician." Li Fan's voice grew colder.

"I don't really recommend Senior doing that," Qiao Sidao suddenly spoke.

Li Fan looked at him, signaling him to continue.

"Assuming those two powerful beings are constantly hunting down their own counterparts for some reason. And based on your world's experience, they have done this more than once. Clearly, they possess some secret method to sense their existence in other possible worlds…"

Qiao Sidao pondered, organizing his words. "If the time of all possibilities is maintained in a certain degree of consistency, then their hunting behavior must also have a sequential order."

"Our current world is temporarily safe because it has not yet attracted their attention."

"If Senior's killing action were to trigger the Heavenly Physician's counterpart in life and death, it might instead attract powerful enemies from beyond the possibility," Qiao Sidao analyzed systematically.

Li Fan nodded slightly with satisfaction.

He naturally didn't intend to actually kill the Heavenly Physician.

After all, he now had a thousand ways to trap him, so why take the risk of possibly attracting the corrupted Heavenly Physician?

He hadn't even revealed that the Formless High Wall could to some extent block the corrupted Heavenly Physician's senses. Li Fan was testing the usability of Di Sanmo and Qiao Sidao.

So far, they seemed quite satisfactory.

Di Sanmo also chimed in, "Instead of taking risks, it's better to imprison him. Using Ancient Cang Origin as energy, which can cross possibilities. This mysterious energy might be able to block perception from beyond possibilities to some extent…"

This was something Li Fan had not considered before.

Better safe than sorry. Li Fan decided to integrate and apply Ancient Cang Origin into the formation for sealing the Heavenly Physician.

The Dissolution Disc had already begun analyzing Ancient Cang Origin.

Li Fan then turned to Di Sanmo. "What are your thoughts on the existence of the corrupted Heavenly Physician and sinister Su Bai?"

"Why are beings in other possibilities so powerful, even though they are not even True Immortals in this world?"

Di Sanmo gave a wry smile. "Perhaps, in this world, there are no 'whys.' Just like that Nameless True Immortal who destroyed our clan back then."

"An ordinary Nameless one fighting evenly with one of the Primordial Dao Forms is already considered strong. But that one could fight thirteen simultaneously…"

"Before true powerhouses, there is no such thing as reason."

Qiao Sidao echoed the same sentiment. "Since ancient times, those who survive tribulations are either the lucky chosen ones, or absolute powerhouses."

"I believe these two are the latter."

Chapter 1420: Evidence Proving Experimental

"Talent, comprehension, these factors that affect one's actual cultivation might have an upper limit. If one can reach the True Immortal realm, their abilities in these aspects wouldn't be lacking."

Qiao Sidao's difficulty was not an issue for him.

And the appearance of Lu Ya, who had been raised by Mr. Bai in the past.

In Di Sanmo's narrative, Li Fan also learned why First Scroll was named [First].

First Scroll was not originally a separate divine soul.

His name was not accidental, resembling the beast race king [Di Yi]. During the forging of bodies for hundreds of divine souls selected, a rare accident occurred. In a violent explosion, all remaining life materials and divine souls merged together.

Originally, such a mixture of residue was insufficient to give birth to an intelligent being. Yet, from this pile of mud, a genius like First Scroll emerged.

Di Sanmo said with great regret, "Even though I tried my best to hide it, First Scroll's uniqueness did not escape the notice of the Law-Transmitters and Mirror Controllers. To prevent First Scroll from becoming a threat after growing stronger, they jointly suppressed him."

"In the face of the new cultivation law created by the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable, without the necessary resources, no matter how exceptional your talent, you would be restricted. The talent that even I find hard to believe, is currently still stuck at the Nascent Soul stage…" Di Sanmo's tone carried a hint of indignation.

"This is also related to our [Illusionary Sage] lineage's characteristics. Since pledging allegiance to the Law-Transmitter, I made an agreement with him not to interfere in the affairs of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, only to provide assistance at certain critical moments. So I cannot interfere too much," he explained to Li Fan.

Li Fan was also familiar with this First Scroll.

When his strength was still weak, he had already heard tales of "cultivating for three years, mortals forming a core. Golden core slays Nascent Soul, surpassing Void Transformation." Later, when appointed as the Island Master of Myriad Immortals Island, he even received instructions from him to build Congyun Immortal City and suppress the entrance to the Netherworld beneath Myriad Immortals Island.

However, with True Return's advantage of endless reincarnation, Li Fan could gather information with impunity and without consequence in every life. Cultivation resources were not an issue for Li Fan.

After reaching the Nascent Soul stage with the Five Elements Great Cauldron, this so-called "prodigy" was no longer within his sight.

"Speaking of which, this First Scroll could be a suitable test subject."

"To see the richness of the remaining possibilities in the current mortal world."

"Even if there are endless possibilities, and each person has the opportunity to achieve the strongest path, but based on talent, comprehension, and state of mind, those with higher qualities have a greater overall chance of achieving Dao. After the Dao Annihilation Tribulation sweeps through, the number of survivors would also be greater. Like He Zheng Hao, to achieve the Nameless Realm, even within infinity, it is rare."

"I can divide them into different tiers based on their talent and send them to explore outside the High Wall separately…" Li Fan had already made his plan.

Not summoning First Scroll for the time being, Li Fan had Di Sanmo lead him directly to the Law-Transmitter's council.

Under the guise of "extremely urgent matters," as decreed by Di Sanmo, the head of the Illusionary Sage lineage of the Law-Transmitter Heavenly Venerate, most of the Law-Transmitters were gathered in one place.

Li Fan, deeply aware of the corruption of these Law-Transmitters, had no desire to waste words with them and directly descended with his Immortal Formation, suppressing all of them.

After assessment, if they were deemed usable, they would be released. If not, they would be destroyed, and new Law-Transmitters would be created using replicated personalities combined with Di Sanmo's flesh-melting technology.

The flesh-melting techniques of the beast race bore roughly seventy to eighty percent similarity to those developed in the small world of the Empire. However, all the Empire's techniques were based on mutated beasts completely devoid of demonic beast bloodlines, allowing them to further tap into the potential within living organisms. Although the techniques appeared less advanced on the surface, their essence was not inferior.

When Li Fan provided them to Di Sanmo, Di Sanmo was greatly surprised and inspired.

Silently gaining control of the Law-Transmitter council, Li Fan did not immediately confront the Tianxuan Mirror.

Instead, he first went to the Guardian Hall.

When the three guardians of the Tianxuan Mirror, who had achieved the Dao Integration realm, repeatedly confirmed the authenticity of the received order and hastily left the Law-Transmitting Jade space with great surprise, leaving only Yan Fafeng alone.

The listless little girl, who had been slumped on the long wooden table, observed for a long time.

Finally, she couldn't help but peek upwards furtively.

"What's going on?" the little girl muttered to herself.

After thinking for a long time, although she wasn't sure exactly what had happened, she knew for a fact that no one was guarding. Yan Fafeng, the little girl, did not generate the thought of escaping, but instead happily settled down to rest.

After an unknown period.

Until a figure suddenly appeared before her, lightly tapping on the wooden table.

The little girl was suddenly jolted awake from her sweet dream, habitually wiping the drool from the corner of her mouth, her eyes wide open.

She showed no sign of having been asleep just moments ago.

She carefully examined the newcomer, tentatively asking, "Are you the new guardian?"

The newcomer, who was Li Fan, smiled slightly. "Yes and no."

"I hate riddle-tellers like you the most," the little girl puffed out her cheeks, saying with disdain.

Then she lost interest in bothering with Li Fan and started counting on her fingers, seemingly calculating something. Her large eyes looked up at the giant circular character sphere above.

Li Fan did not mind.

He leisurely conjured an identical long wooden table before him.

He laid out paper, ground ink, and picked up his brush.

With a single stroke, he wrote two characters.

The moment these two characters appeared, they uncontrollably captured the little girl's attention.

She first froze for a moment, her eyes filled with confusion.

Then she seemed to recall something and suddenly let out a series of meaningless screams.

Unceasingly.

"You… you… you…" Yan Fafeng trembled, pointing at Li Fan as if she had seen a ghost. She couldn't even speak properly.

Li Fan glanced indifferently at the little girl.

The little girl was startled again, but under Li Fan's gaze, she dared not move recklessly, only looking at Li Fan in terror.

"How much of your Immortal Realm memory remains?"

After Yan Fafeng finally calmed down, Li Fan asked indifferently.

This question further confirmed the guess in the little girl's heart.

Her fear intensified, and she quickly shook her head. "I can't remember anything else!"

"Hmm?" Li Fan narrowed his eyes, his brow furrowed.

The little girl waved her hands anxiously, explaining, "Really, I'm not lying!"

"I'm also a bit confused about this. However, Elder Brother Jing Xuan said that to avoid the influence of the Immortal Realm calamity, most immortal artifacts must sever ties with their past selves to survive…"

"These two characters, I only vaguely recalled them just now after seeing you write them."

Immortal artifacts, immortal puppets, immortal servants, and the like.

They seemed to be in a naturally oppressed position before True Immortals.

With just a simple look, Yan Fafeng, the little girl, spilled out everything she knew.

The Yan Fafeng artifact that accompanied her, although from the Immortal Realm, was incomplete from the start.

After she merged with it, her past memories seemed to dissolve like salt in water, becoming lost.

"Don't move."

Li Fan said calmly and reached out to press the little girl's head, examining her internal state.

The traces of the Yan Fafeng artifact were no longer visible.

It had almost completely merged with her human body.

However, some of her "human" characteristics still remained. She had not been completely absorbed and devoured.

"I can feel the wish in your heart."

"Do you want to live on as [Yan Fafeng], or as a true [human]?" Li Fan asked calmly after withdrawing his hand.

The little girl was startled. Then she seemed to realize something and opened her mouth slightly.

She did not give an immediate answer, but after a period of considerable struggle.

"As [Yan Fafeng], although it means losing freedom, one has endless longevity and no fear of death."

"As [human], although one can break free from the constraints of an artifact, perhaps there is no true freedom in this world." Li Fan stated calmly.

The little girl lowered her head, lost in thought.

But ultimately, as Li Fan had expected, she resolutely chose the latter.

To become [human].

"Alright, since your mind is made up, I will grant your wish."

Ten thousand golden threads erupted instantly, piercing deeply into Yan Fafeng's body.

Under unimaginable pain, the little girl instantly burst into tears.

Li Fan ignored her, instead sensing the exotic item within her body and slowly extracting it.

Chapter 1421: Recreating the Evolved Law Jade

The miraculous Heavenly Evolved Dharma Ring was almost completely integrated with the physical body, making it extremely difficult to separate by ordinary means. However, Li Fan, proficient in medical principles and possessing the Transformed True and False ability, directly adopted the most brutal yet effective approach. Without regard for the consequences, he destructively extracted the flesh and blood attached to the Evolved Dharma Ring. During this process, he had to use Transformed True and False to artificially create flesh and blood to fill the gap, sustaining the little girl's life. The physical body was relatively easier. What was more difficult and dangerous was the soul. Having been integrated with the Evolved Dharma Ring for so long, even the little girl's divine soul was filled with the imprints of the Evolved Dharma Ring's suppression. Li Fan's divine sense acted like a blade, precisely and meticulously cutting and separating it inch by inch. Simultaneously, as Transformed True and False filled the void, he used the Infinite Reciprocity Technique to nurture and infuse wisps of essence soul nourishment. The entire process required absolute precision; even the slightest error could cause the Evolved Dharma Ring to remain unharmed, but the little girl would instantly scatter her soul and perish.

However, Li Fan felt no tension whatsoever, even though this was his first attempt at such "medical surgery." After all, there was no third person in this world who had witnessed his conversation with the Evolved Dharma Ring. If he failed despite his best efforts… then it could only be considered the little girl's misfortune. Li Fan focused his mind, immersed in the task. Slowly, as a piece of blood-red circular jade was removed by Li Fan, the little girl entered a wondrous state between "True and False." She appeared no different from before the "surgery," except for becoming somewhat weaker. But in reality, if Li Fan were to cancel the Transformed True and False effect with a single thought, this adorable creature would instantly collapse into a pool of blood and flesh. "The boundary between True and False…" Li Fan observed carefully, contemplating his own creation of True and False. Having gained practical experience with life, Li Fan felt that his understanding of Transformed True and False had taken another step forward, albeit imperceptibly. He couldn't achieve permanence yet. The artificially created space from Transformed True and False would only leave a tiny remnant, but Li Fan could continuously repeat the process, compensating with quantity.

Even so, after Li Fan completed this exquisite and unparalleled separation surgery, the reborn little girl had shrunk considerably. She had originally looked like a five or six-year-old, but now she appeared only three or four years old. When the little girl awoke and looked at her new body, her eyes widened, her face filled with surprise. Although she had lost the blessing of the Heavenly Evolved Dharma Ring, when Li Fan crafted this body, some spiritual energy from the Xuanhuang Realm's phantom image remained. Though the current little girl had no cultivation, in terms of profound foundation, she likely surpassed all cultivators below the Longevity Realm in the Xuanhuang Realm. "Do you remember your original name?" Li Fan asked slowly, stroking the Evolved Dharma Ring in his left hand. The blood and flesh attached to the Heavenly Evolved Dharma Ring had vanished, revealing its original appearance. The circular jade body had a gap, as if sliced by a sword, occupying almost a tenth of its size. At first glance, it appeared incomplete. The little girl hesitated for a moment, then finally replied crisply, "I don't remember." Li Fan's heaven-defying methods further confirmed her previous thoughts. This person before her must be a True Immortal incarnated! No longer daring to show any hint of playfulness, she became quite reserved.

Li Fan, naturally perceptive of the little girl's obvious demeanor, didn't dwell on it. Seeing that she seemed to want to completely bid farewell to her past, he decided not to fuss: "Since that's the case, from now on, your name shall be Li Ningqing." Although separated from the Evolved Dharma Ring, years of cohabitation and fragmented memories from the Immortal Realm had profoundly influenced her. Li Ningqing subconsciously bowed, her small face filled with seriousness, "Thank you, Master, for bestowing my name." Li Fan nodded slightly and said no more, focusing on studying the Evolved Dharma Ring in his hand. Li Ningqing, however, remained standing by his side, not daring to disturb him. But as the saying goes, old habits die hard. After standing for a short while, Li Ningqing couldn't help but grow restless. She looked up stealthily, covertly observing Li Fan. As Li Ningqing had said, there were indeed few memories of the Immortal Realm left within the Evolved Dharma Ring. Fragments of memories related to "Creation" could still exist, precisely because this True Immortal inscription was exceptionally special. It was imprinted into the memory while also subtly influencing the Evolved Dharma Ring itself, allowing it to endure the erosion of time and remain intact.

But even with only scattered fragments remaining, Li Fan saw scenes of value to him. Shadows flickered and shifted, as if the original owner of the Evolved Dharma Ring had encountered an extremely difficult situation. "Foolish, truly utterly foolish." "To disregard such a calamity…" "No, perhaps they already had other plans and could not bother with us. It seems we must rely on ourselves. Otherwise, the tragedy of the Thousand Illusions Star Domain serves as a stark example…"

After an unknown amount of time, the illusory figure had long since departed, leaving the Evolved Dharma Ring alone. A howling wind began to rise, as if a great terror was descending. A mysterious force suddenly enveloped the Evolved Dharma Ring. The Evolved Dharma Ring flew high into the sky, transforming into a meteor, uncontrollably hurtling in a certain direction. And around it, thousands of beams of light, like the Evolved Dharma Ring, pierced the firmament. However, their positions seemed to be scattered.

In the lower Star Sea. After flying for an unknown duration, a figure suddenly reached out and seized the Evolved Dharma Ring. After a careful look, they shook their head slightly. Then, they tossed the Evolved Dharma Ring into the Xuanhuang Realm. These fragmented memories were deeply hidden within the Evolved Dharma Ring. Even after transforming into a miraculous item and being absorbed by Li Ningqing, they would not be perceived by her without specific triggers or enticements. Only Li Fan, who thoroughly searched it in a somewhat destructive manner, could awaken these ancient remaining memories. "It seems the Evolved Dharma Ring came to Xuanhuang from the Immortal Realm a long time ago, was swallowed and absorbed by heaven and earth." The figure seen intercepting the Evolved Dharma Ring was none other than someone Li Fan was familiar with. It was the same figure he had seen in the True Immortal's flesh and blood memories generated by the Kunqian Bone Hand – the True Immortal from the lower realm! "The Immortal Realm, the harbinger of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation had appeared long ago. Even with the 'official' creation of Immortal Heavenly Pillars to maintain order, it's likely that many True Immortals still chose their own methods to survive the calamity. Whether they succeeded is another matter." "In the face of catastrophe, everyone uses their own cunning. This is not a new phenomenon in Xuanhuang Realm's history," Li Fan mused inwardly. What concerned him even more was the scene of thousands of meteoric lights fleeing in different directions.

"At that time node, for the Xuanhuang Realm, it was still the ancient era. But the Immortal Realm star domain where the Evolved Dharma Ring was located seemed to already be facing the great tribulation." "I wonder what else, besides Immortal artifacts like the Evolved Dharma Ring, was among those meteor lights." "Was it a powerful being's intervention, preserving the 'embers' of the Immortal Realm in this manner?" Beyond the past memories of the Evolved Dharma Ring, there was nothing else of particular note. As for the rest, they were cultivation techniques that the Evolved Dharma Ring had continuously deduced over the years. Li Fan, now a Half-Immortal, found these cultivation techniques of little significance. It took him considerable effort to extract the Evolved Dharma Ring, primarily due to its former status as an Immortal artifact. Within his Sea of Consciousness, the Immortal Formation Dissolution Disc emitted specks of Immortal Spiritual Energy. Li Fan first attempted to absorb this Immortal Spiritual Energy using the Evolved Dharma Ring. However, just like Li Fan, the Evolved Dharma Ring couldn't utilize this miraculous energy; it simply passed through its body and emerged intact. The Dissolution Disc reabsorbed the Immortal Spiritual Energy. "As I expected, Immortal Spiritual Energy should have a unique identification tag." "It can only be used by specific entities." Li Fan recalled the process by which the Dissolution Disc officially ascended to the rank of an Immortal artifact. "It was left by the Great Celestial Venerable of Xuanhuang, transformed and absorbed by the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao, and then forcibly separated before reaching the limit of ascending to the Immortal Realm." "I dimly understand the underlying principle. Perhaps the key lies in the transformation through the Xuanhuang world. The operational mechanism might have existed since the creation of the Xuanhuang Realm, similar to the Ancient Immortal Formation, and perhaps even the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao is unaware of it." "To elevate the Evolved Dharma Ring to the status of an Immortal artifact…" Li Fan had no intention of promoting the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation again. Given his previous experience, it was troublesome, though not insurmountable. With his current strength, there were more convenient methods.

Temporarily setting aside the Evolved Dharma Ring, Li Fan looked at Li Ningqing, who had recovered her senses and had immediately lowered her head. "You haven't been outside for a long time. I'll give you some time to explore. Although you have no cultivation, with this body alone, you can roam the Xuanhuang Realm without worry," Li Fan said calmly. Li Ningqing was overjoyed and quickly bowed in thanks. "One year." "After one year, heed my call," Li Fan added. Li Ningqing didn't pay much attention, already overwhelmed by the prospect of a year's freedom. Heaven forbid, she had never had such a long continuous rest in her life. Compared to that detestable Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, Master was truly a benevolent god! Li Ningqing couldn't help but think. While excitedly anticipating her journey, Li Fan sent her out of the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters. He could faintly hear Li Fan's voice in his ear: "Explore more, see more. Don't miss anything interesting." "Don't worry, Master has your back." Li Ningqing felt reassured, her journey to the Xuanhuang Realm filled with anticipation. "Master is so kind, Mirror Xuan will surely be very happy to meet him, right?" Sensing the little girl's cheerful footsteps, Li Fan nodded slightly. "I hope you can discover some hidden secrets of the Xuanhuang Realm." Li Ningqing had been merged with the Evolved Dharma Ring for too long, developing a unique connection. For ancient items from the Immortal Realm, perhaps a similar connection existed. Just as Li Fan had sensed the Immortal Spiritual Energy the moment he extracted it, she would also have some perception. Even though he had ascended to the Immortal Realm, Li Fan would not be careless regarding the Xuanhuang Realm, once an experimental ground for the Immortal Realm. "However, my main focus now should be outside the Wall. Exploration within the Xuanhuang Realm can be entrusted to others."

Having settled the matter of the Evolved Dharma Ring, Li Fan finally arrived before the Mirror Controllers. Here, Li Fan encountered the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror – an ancient green bronze mirror. Three Mirror Controllers sat cross-legged around the mirror. They looked at Li Fan's sudden appearance, and the presence of the Law-Transmitter representative, Zhou, and Di San Mo standing by Li Fan's side, their expressions changed drastically. Without any preamble, Li Fan waved his hand, suppressing all three of them. Li Fan's figure flickered, arriving before the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. He keenly sensed the restrictions placed upon the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's true form. Clearly, these were the work of the Heavenly Physician. "Mirror Xuan…" Li Fan revealed a knowing smile, then tapped the mirror body three times with his finger. The restrictions shattered one by one. The space within the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters trembled violently in sync. A figure floated out from the ancient mirror, staring at Li Fan with an extremely grave and tense expression. "Greetings, Upper Immortal." Li Fan, who knew everything about the Myriad Immortals Alliance, how could he not know about the earth-shattering events happening at the headquarters at this moment? Stealthily contacting the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, Mirror Xuan's human clone also stopped experiencing the "human" life and began to flee towards the naturally hidden celestial cave from his memory. Mirror Xuan believed his actions were stealthy.

But he didn't know that everything was within Li Fan's control. Li Fan subtly extended his hand, his fingers seeming to traverse space and time, then exerted a slight force. Mirror Xuan's expression changed drastically, as if his throat was being choked, his face turning red. A mortal, millions of miles away, was grasped by Li Fan out of thin air and casually tossed aside. The Law-Transmitter Zhou and Di San Mo were both bewildered. Only Mirror Xuan, and his human clone, were filled with terror. "Disobedient." "Deserves a beating." Li Fan tapped his finger again. This time, with considerable force. Both of Mirror Xuan's bodies collapsed to the ground as if struck by lightning. The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters space shook violently, like the end of days. Most terrifyingly, a crack appeared on the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, as if Li Fan didn't care about the fate of this extraordinarily miraculous Immortal artifact! Mirror Xuan was completely terrified and was about to beg for mercy when he saw Li Fan reach out, grasp him, and then stuff him back into the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. However, Mirror Xuan didn't feel the usual sense of being in his element after returning to his true form. Instead, he keenly sensed that, for some reason, a rift had formed between him and the Heavenly Xuan Mirror! After a thorough investigation, Mirror Xuan discovered the reason. Besides the sealing techniques employed by the True Immortal, another "self" was being generated within the Heavenly Xuan Mirror! From that blurry figure, Mirror Xuan seemed to see himself! "This is…" A chill ran down Mirror Xuan's spine. Mirror Xuan, with his vast knowledge, already understood that the True Immortal seemed to be forging a new artifact spirit, intending to replace him! "It shouldn't have been this easy. But it just so happens that my human body also fell into his hands." Mirror Xuan's heart was filled with both fear and shock, as if he could already see his future fate. He repeatedly cried out, "Senior, spare my life!"

Chapter 1422: Secret of the Mysterious Heaven Saint Envoy

Since Li Fan had already activated the Great Array of Fabricated Myriad Beings, how could he stop so easily just because of Mirror Xuan's pleas? In his past reincarnations, Li Fan had a general understanding of Mirror Xuan's character. Perhaps for the sake of caution, Li Fan might spare his life. But he was certainly not going to let Mirror Xuan remain the artifact spirit of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror! In the past, after obtaining the precious mirror through the Law-Transmission, he still chose to preserve the artifact spirit's existence, only using the Mirror Controllers to restrain it. This was definitely because his strength was insufficient to achieve more. But Li Fan was different. Not only did he have the Immortal Array's blessings, but he also controlled Mirror Xuan's human clone. This human clone was equivalent to a "copy" meticulously crafted by Mirror Xuan himself, free from the shackles of being an Immortal artifact. Mirror Xuan himself had described this body as: "Possessing both the weight of an artifact and the spirit of a human. Flawless, nearing True Immortal." This was Mirror Xuan's carefully devised escape method, or rather, path, during the thousands of years he was confined by the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Its profundity lay not just in this human body; it was in the "principle" of constantly generating human bodies. As long as the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror remained, even if the human body were destroyed, another could be quickly regenerated.

Li Fan's previous conversations with Mirror Xuan had been obscure and enigmatic. Now, upon direct investigation, this method was laid bare. "Broadly speaking, it's similar to the mechanism of Zhang Qianmo's Grand Wish Method. However, Zhang Qianmo's Grand Wish Dharma Body relies on the Great Dao of the Xuanhuang Realm." "While the foundation of Mirror Xuan's clone's existence is solely the Heavenly Xuan Mirror itself!" "The Heavenly Xuan Mirror, though devoid of any Immortal Spiritual Energy, still retains its status as an Immortal artifact. Moreover, it preserved a large amount of knowledge from the Immortal Realm, solidifying this status. The weight of a single artifact, in some ways, surpasses that of a realm, perhaps even exceeding it."

Li Fan's expression remained unchanged, but inwardly, he couldn't help but exclaim. However, admiration was admiration; his hands couldn't stop. To Mirror Xuan's utter horror, Li Fan produced a wisp of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's origin. Di San Mo and Zhou, the Law-Transmitter representative, who observed with unperturbed expressions, wouldn't know what Li Fan had taken out. But how could Mirror Xuan not know?

Seeing the familiar aura swirling around Li Fan's hand, Mirror Xuan's expression was as if he had seen a ghost. He frantically tried to recall when he had separated this wisp of origin. But no matter how hard he thought, he couldn't find an answer. Despair and darkness gradually enveloped him. This gift from the Heavenly Xuan Mirror in the past had now become the final rope that entangled him. Mirror Xuan had once arrogantly declared that no one in the Xuanhuang Realm could truly harm him. While true in the past, Li Fan had now ascended to the Half-Immortal realm! Based on the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Formation of the past, the Dissolution Disc instantly deduced and evolved an Immortal-level advanced version, firmly controlling the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. By attacking from both the artifact spirit and the human clone, Li Fan implemented a dual strategy. The Heavenly Xuan Mirror's origin served as a natural access point, and using the fabrication array, a new "Mirror Xuan" was created, gradually replacing his control over the Heavenly Xuan Mirror.

This meticulous scheme of "stealing the sky and changing the sun" would be unimaginable to ordinary mortals. Even for Heavenly Physicians and Law-Transmitters, who were Supremes of the Star Sea, it might only exist in theory. Yet, Li Fan could achieve it with ease. While the Immortal Array Dissolution Disc certainly played a role, Li Fan's strength as a Half-Immortal, offsetting the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's inherent pressure as an Immortal artifact, was more crucial. They were evenly matched, without an insurmountable gap. No matter how tightly defended, how could it withstand such a comprehensive assault? Even without the Dissolution Disc, Li Fan likely could have achieved his goal with more time. The analysis and replication of Mirror Xuan were ongoing. Li Fan also discovered some residual hidden restrictions within the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, which he easily removed. Even if Mirror Xuan hadn't made any secret moves previously, the current anomaly within the Myriad Immortals Alliance couldn't be concealed.

"Law-Transmitter and Heavenly Physician are already returning to the Xuanhuang Realm. It's a good opportunity to capture them all at once," Li Fan thought casually, glancing upwards. He didn't take it too seriously. After witnessing the Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, his counterparts from another possibility, Li Fan believed it was safest for them to remain in their respective places. Remaining still for the moment. In the time it took for the analysis to complete, Li Fan mused on his recent actions of separating the Evolved Dharma Ring and replicating Mirror Xuan. "With my current methods, it's still somewhat difficult to completely 'replicate' a person." "However, creating a near-perfect copy, about eighty to ninety percent similar, should be achievable. This unavoidable flaw due to insufficient strength, in this era where possibilities are continuously annihilating and converging, might actually be an advantage." "The true Heavenly Physician couldn't cross the High Wall. Then, what about the 'Heavenly Physician' I created…" Li Fan's eyes flickered, formulating his exploration plan.

Within the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's space, time was irrelevant. It took Li Fan a full thirty-six hours to initially create a fabricated Mirror Xuan. Currently, it couldn't fully utilize all the functions of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror like a natural artifact spirit, but basic manipulation, information retrieval, and even combat were all possible. Li Fan's first action after gaining control of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror was to access the complete Grand Array of Profound Origin Beginning Spirit. This complete Immortal-grade Grand Array, capable of reconstructing the elements and creating worlds from void, had been coveted by Li Fan for a long time. "Hmm? What a shame." "The Heavenly Xuan Mirror also doesn't have all nine complete formation diagrams," Li Fan sighed slightly.

Although the investigation yielded some results, besides the three diagrams Li Fan had already mastered – [Profound Pivot, Ten Thousand Spirits Return to Numeration], [Withered Fall, Empty Chamber Blooms], and [Boundless, Primordial Forms Revealed] – the Heavenly Xuan Mirror only contained two other Grand Arrays. [Dao Origin, Endless Generation] and [Feather Transformation, Life and Death Ebbs and Flows]! Li Fan was not greedy. After so many reincarnations, he had only collected three formation diagrams. Now, obtaining two new ones was enough for him to digest for a while. Carefully examining these two formation diagrams. [Dao Origin, Endless Generation] explained the principle of simulating the birth and evolution of life within a formation, and how myriad life forces circulated within the world. "Life arises from nothingness, appearing only when the Dao exists…" "Magnificent." Li Fan's eyes sparkled with enlightenment. After a long time, he reluctantly turned his gaze to the other formation diagram. [Feather Transformation, Life and Death Ebbs and Flows]. "A world with only the evolution of life would be abnormal. Life and death intertwine, coexisting. Only then would it align with the Great Dao. This [Life and Death Ebbs and Flows] Grand Array seems to expound upon the principles of life and death…" Li Fan observed carefully and found that the underlying principles bore some resemblance to the [Life and Death Reversal Grand Array] he had seen before. But it was clear that the exquisiteness of this grand Immortal array was far beyond ordinary formations. "It not only governs the flow of life and death within a world but also extends to the world itself, and perhaps even the Star Sea beyond the world?" The more Li Fan pondered, the more he marveled. Activating the [Feather Transformation, Life and Death Ebbs and Flows] could easily drain the life force of an entire cultivation world, transforming it into a single white feather. Then, it could extract infinite life force from this feather, creating a world from a single feather. The Star Sea was no different.

Li Fan couldn't fully comprehend these two formation diagrams on his own. He only had a partial understanding and was already feeling overwhelmed. The reason was that at the level of the Grand Array of Profound Origin Beginning Spirit, it transcended mere formations, integrating the supreme principles of the Great Dao. Without understanding the Great Dao, it was impossible to master them. Fortunately, Li Fan possessed the Immortal Array Dissolution Disc. "Although I don't understand the mechanics, I can still use it for now." "I will learn and comprehend through practice." With nine formation diagrams in total, Li Fan had now obtained five. Slightly more than half, perhaps the Dissolution Disc itself, with enough time, could deduce the remaining parts. But the calculation was immense. Li Fan needed the Dissolution Disc for his daily activities and couldn't allocate sufficient computational power for this arduous task. Therefore, Li Fan only had the Dissolution Disc make a preliminary attempt, deducing slowly. Perhaps one day, like a cultivator suddenly achieving enlightenment, it would surprise him.

Li Fan attempted to search for clues about the remaining formation diagrams of the Grand Array of Profound Origin Beginning Spirit within the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. "It seems that after several shocks, the Heavenly Xuan Mirror has suffered some memory loss." Li Fan frowned slightly. After careful examination, he confirmed that it wasn't a hidden trick by the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, but genuine damage within its true form. Only then did Li Fan feel at ease. "The first shock occurred when it was still in the Immortal Realm, where the Heavenly Xuan Mirror was also contested and changed hands several times, causing damage during repeated refinements." Li Fan, based on the ancient traces within the Heavenly Xuan Mirror and its own preserved memories, began to reconstruct the past. "The second shock was when Xuan Yuanhong, with his help, voluntarily initiated the process of transforming an immortal into a mortal." Li Fan mused thoughtfully, observing the figure of King Xuan Tian in the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's memories. "The third shock…" The subsequent discovery made Li Fan's spirits soar. It concerned why the Heavenly Xuan Mirror fell into the hands of the Law-Transmitter after the destruction of the Heavenly Xuan Sect. The scenes Li Fan witnessed resolved a long-standing question.

Previously, within the Illusion Array of the One-Heart Heavenly Venerate, Zhao Ruoxi, the sect master of the Great Dao Sect, had mentioned a Heavenly Xuan Envoy who escaped the pursuit of the Ten Great Immortal Sects, taking the Heavenly Xuan Treasure Mirror and disappearing without a trace. The Ten Great Sects had put in immense effort, even offering a "mirror for a lifetime" reward, but still couldn't find the treasure mirror. And Li Fan, in his interactions with Mo Ruobin and the residual soul of Ji Yuzhen, had never heard mention of this Heavenly Xuan Envoy. For a long time, Li Fan had believed that the so-called Heavenly Xuan Envoy was merely a figment of Zhao Ruoxi's dream, existing only in fiction, not reality. But… Li Fan's expression became somewhat nuanced as the images flashed rapidly. The Heavenly Xuan Envoy did exist. However, he was not one of the twelve Dharma Kings of the Heavenly Xuan Sect. In fact, he had never even appeared in any official capacity within the Heavenly Xuan Sect. A familiar village scene. It was a village not far from the Fishing Pond. A middle-aged woman with an unremarkable appearance woke from her sleep and inexplicably found a mirror placed by her bedside. Afterward, receiving some unknown information, she suddenly burst into tears, holding the Heavenly Xuan Mirror and weeping. She vaguely called out "A'hong," the name of King Xuan, Xuan Yuanhong! "No wonder Xuan Yuanhong remained distant from Ji Yuzhen and the other female Dharma Kings, never showing any formal demeanor." "He had a childhood sweetheart all along!" "If it were a normal cultivator, their lifespan would be too long, leading to a separation between immortals and mortals." "But King Xuan's rise was too rapid. And with treasures like the Fishing Pond…" "It would be incredibly easy to protect his childhood sweetheart!"

Images flashed rapidly. When King Xuan handed the Heavenly Xuan Treasure Mirror to the woman, he also seemed to have imparted a method of suppression. One was to prevent the Heavenly Xuan Treasure Mirror from overpowering its master, and the other was to prevent its aura from leaking, thus preventing the woman from incurring disaster. The treasure mirror could sense the outside world, and the images were blurry. It could only clearly perceive that the woman who came into contact with it, her strength rapidly increased in a short period. In just three years, from a mortal, she leaped to the Integration Realm. One day, in a secret chamber at an unknown location, the woman cast a secret technique on the Heavenly Xuan Treasure Mirror. "A'hong told me you are from an extraordinary background, from the Immortal Realm." "But the Immortal Realm has been destroyed. Although you were transformed into a mortal with A'hong's help, the connection, however faint, was not completely severed. If A'hong were still here, it would be fine." "But now A'hong is in grave danger… I must go find him." "This journey is fraught with peril, with little hope of survival. I do not wish to take you to your death." "You shall remain in the Xuanhuang Realm." "Remember, the Immortal Dao is no more. Since you have already been transformed from immortal to mortal, do not attempt to ascend to the Immortal Dao again." "Not returning to your immortal artifact form does not mean there is no future. Your Great Dao lies in Measuring Heaven and Mapping Earth." "This Xuanhuang Realm hides too many mysteries. Even A'hong back then could not fully comprehend them. If you can understand all the secrets of this realm…" "The Great Dao awaits!" "I have shown you the path, and thus I have benefited you." "This journey is perilous, so I need your help!"

That figure gently placed their hand on the treasure mirror. Using some unknown method, in an instant, an identical shadow floated out from the Heavenly Xuan Treasure Mirror! "From now on, your name is [Tian Xuan]." "I have taken Xuan Tian away." The voice faded, disappearing into the unknown. The restrictions imposed on him also vanished simultaneously. The freed Heavenly Xuan began to follow the woman's teachings, measuring heaven and mapping earth, searching for the mysteries within the Xuanhuang Realm. One day, he encountered the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate.

Chapter 1423: Must Kill Nameless Immortal

The encounter between the Heavenly Xuan Mirror and the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate was perhaps inevitable. Just as Li Fan's strength had grown to a certain extent, he was destined to meet with Law-Transmitters, Starvation Immortals, and the like. Although its primary power was not for offense or defense, it was still an Immortal artifact transformed into a mortal. If it were only Law-Transmitter alone, Mirror Xuan might have been able to contend with him for a while. But he hadn't anticipated that behind Law-Transmitter, there was also the Heavenly Physician. The combined strength of these two powerhouses subdued the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. For Mirror Xuan, this was undoubtedly a deeply unpleasant memory. After the blurry shadows quickly flickered past, the Heavenly Xuan Mirror transformed, becoming the foundation and supreme treasure of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. During the time Mirror Xuan was measuring heaven and mapping earth, he did not lack gains.
