As his understanding of the Xuanhuang Realm deepened, the Heavenly Xuan Mirror also evolved several capabilities it didn't possess before. For example, differentiation and secondary generation.

Differentiation referred to the Heavenly Xuan sub-mirrors scattered across various prefectures of the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the small Heavenly Xuan mirrors that individuals could use. They all possessed some of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's functions and were, like the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, extensions of itself. Secondary generation was the opposite of differentiation. If differentiation was replication, then secondary generation was mutation. The various secondary bodies born from the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, such as the Azure Xuan Mirror, the Final Stone Disc, and the Dissolution Disc, although seemingly specialized functions of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, were in fact, as Mirror Xuan himself knew, more capable in their respective fields than his true form. During the process of evolving secondary bodies, Mirror Xuan could also, by studying these secondary bodies, advance his corresponding abilities. This research process was completed the moment the secondary bodies were born, so the current secondary bodies were indeed useless to the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. In addition to differentiation and secondary generation, the most important realization of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror was the supreme path of "Establishing the Dao within the Self, Acting the Dao without." Mirror Xuan firmly believed that he could comprehend such a Great Dao not solely due to measuring the Xuanhuang Realm, but also due to the subtle guidance of the woman before she left.

"Establishing the Dao within the Self" meant continuously strengthening the part of existence reliant on the Dao. The Dao governed all things; all existences relied on the Dao. If one could not pursue the ethereal state of merging with the Dao and achieving the Nameless Realm, then settling for the next best thing, focusing solely on a part of the Dao, was also acceptable. Every being's birth was a fusion of various Daos. To completely control the foundation of one's own existence, even if one's strength was still inferior to a Nameless True Immortal, they might not be significantly weaker. Not to mention that some beings with extraordinary talent, simply by comprehending their own Dao, could rival Nameless True Immortals! And "Acting the Dao without" was transcendence after establishing the Dao. Compared to the infinite Great Dao of heaven and earth, one's own existence was ultimately limited. But if one could cross the boundary between "self" and "other," it would be like a fish leaping through the dragon gate, potentially limitless thereafter. This manifested in the Heavenly Xuan Mirror as the coexistence of the artifact and the human, complementing each other. When unhindered, both the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror and his human clone could forge their own path towards the Great Dao. Moreover, once one achieved success, they could even mutually support the other.

Li Fan was not particularly interested in the gossip about King Xuan and his childhood sweetheart. However, the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's enlightenment methods gave Li Fan much food for thought. "The Primordial Dao Forms of the demonic beast race can be seen as the most extreme form of 'Establishing the Dao within the Self.'" "And this concept is remarkably similar to founding my own cultivation base. Both rely entirely on oneself. However, generally, the difficulty of Establishing the Dao is far greater than that of establishing a cultivation base." "As for 'Acting the Dao without'…" Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and he couldn't help but think of Ji Yuzhen's cultivation method, the "All-Encompassing Heavenly Scripture of Divine Separation." When cultivated to its extreme, using the primordial soul as a catalyst, it could achieve the heaven-defying effect of 'Dao Merging.'" "The Great Dao of Heaven and Earth originates from the primordial beginning. This might be the theoretical foundation for 'Acting the Dao without' and 'Dao Merging.'" "Whether through oneself or external means, the essence is the same: merging with more 'Dao.'"

Li Fan absorbed the knowledge voraciously. The Heavenly Xuan Mirror's insights accumulated over thousands of years instantly became nourishment for Li Fan's future path to enlightenment. Although it offered no immediate help in terms of strength or realm, Li Fan had a premonition that this method would be immensely useful in the current era where the Immortal Dao was in ruins. "King Xuan's childhood sweetheart seems to have inherited his legacy. Not only was her cultivation speed astonishing, but she also possessed insights far beyond ordinary cultivators in a matter of days. Indeed, 'one person attains enlightenment, and their associates are elevated'!" As Li Fan integrated the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's understanding of Establishing the Dao and Acting the Dao without, his replication process of Mirror Xuan also saw a leap. By continuously eroding the Heavenly Xuan Mirror's control over all its functions, Li Fan believed that soon, Mirror Xuan would cease to be a mere artifact spirit in name only. Seeing the figure before him becoming increasingly similar to himself and more fluid, Mirror Xuan's face turned ashen, and he gave up struggling. The methods employed by this suddenly descended True Immortal were too mystical; he couldn't comprehend them! Mirror Xuan even felt that this True Immortal's strength might surpass that of his creator! At this point, Mirror Xuan accepted his fate, completely losing any will to resist.

Meanwhile, Di San Mo and Zhou, the Law-Transmitter representative, who had witnessed the Law-Transmitter Heavenly Venerate's centuries-long struggle to subdue the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, were filled with awe and fear. The Law-Transmitter, the Mirror Controller, and the Illusory Sage – the three de facto rulers of the Myriad Immortals Alliance – had all been subdued by Li Fan. The Myriad Immortals Alliance had, without anyone realizing, changed hands. Sensing Law-Transmitter and Heavenly Physician still speeding through the Star Sea, Li Fan smiled faintly. In the face of absolute power suppression, all schemes and plans were meaningless. Li Fan had no intention of announcing his identity as the new master of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. All affairs within the Alliance would continue as usual. The fabricated Mirror Xuan would systematically maintain the balance of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Li Fan first ordered the capture of the cultivator named Qin Zhuang, who was imprisoned in the deepest part of the Nether Prison. Previously, Li Fan had attempted to probe the secrets in Qin Zhuang's mind using a downgraded Immortal Array but was disrupted by an invisible interference and failed. Now that Li Fan had ascended to the Half-Immortal realm, he decided to try again!

Not long after, the skeletal Qin Zhuang was brought before Li Fan. Initially, Qin Zhuang's expression held a hint of disdain and mockery. But upon seeing Li Fan, it turned to suspicion and unease. Li Fan wasted no words, pointing a finger at Qin Zhuang's forehead. Within the Illusion Array, Qin Zhuang's experiences indeed showed inconsistencies that had not appeared before. Fleeting memories, as if from Qin Zhuang's past, flashed intermittently. "What a joke! Asking me to go into the Annihilation Land? Don't talk about missions or anything, I, Qin Zhuang, would absolutely refuse!" "The Ancestor personally ordered it? Then I'll reconsider." … "Your objective this time is to search for a 'Sacred Merchant' bloodline within the Annihilation Land. According to the information provided by Elder Taishang Ji, the infant's relatives all died in internal power struggles within the Sacred Merchant clan. Their parents sent him back to the Annihilation Land before they died. If you can find him, we will have a legitimate excuse to intervene in the Sacred Merchant's internal affairs." "However, the Annihilation Land is fraught with danger. Beneath the ruins, there seem to be remnants of ancient civilizations. To be safe, your mind will need some minor adjustments. Don't worry, everything will be restored to normal when you return." … Within the Illusion Array, a middle-aged cultivator with a square face spoke sternly to Qin Zhuang. Suddenly, as if sensing something, the middle-aged cultivator's gaze shifted away from Qin Zhuang. Their eyes met across the void with Li Fan outside the Illusion Array. Like being frosted, Qin Zhuang's memories instantly turned pale and blurry. Li Fan sensed that even after enduring countless torments from the Myriad Immortals Alliance, Qin Zhuang, who had always maintained his vitality, began to decline uncontrollably. His divine soul and body alike. "Hmph, the restriction was triggered after all." Li Fan, who had finally found a channel to probe information from outside the Wall, was unwilling to let Qin Zhuang die so easily. He pointed another finger. This time, it wasn't an Illusion Array, but a phantom representing the power of the entire Xuanhuang Realm. Even though the opponent's method of stripping life force was something Li Fan had never seen before, neither a divine ability nor a formation, overwhelming power was still paramount. Under such a torrent of power, it was enough to temporarily sustain Qin Zhuang's life. Within the Illusion Array, although Qin Zhuang's memories shifted from color to intermittent flickering gray-white, they continued to play out. Li Fan frowned and observed closely. After a full seven days and seven nights, all retrievable memories within Qin Zhuang's mind had been extracted. There was no further value, and Li Fan ceased sustaining him. Like ashes left after being burned by fire, Qin Zhuang's skeletal body turned into countless gray powder, drifting in the air. Li Fan keenly sensed that these powders seemed to want to transmit a signal to the outside world. With a flash of his eyes, he sealed them with an Immortal Array. After careful observation to ensure no accidents occurred, he slowly savored the insights he had just gained.

"Perhaps Qin Zhuang's memories were intentionally edited. His living environment from childhood to adulthood was such that he knew nothing about powerful beings arriving from outside possibilities." "In his worldview, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea within the Wall is located in the so-called 'Annihilation Land.'" "The Annihilation Land, the place where the Dao Annihilation Tribulation once descended. Almost all regions have ceased to exist. Those who mistakenly enter are lost forever. Only within small areas supported by ruins do some life remain." "What we see as the Wall is what they call 'ruins.'" Li Fan mused silently. Outside the Wall, in the endless Star Sea, life seemed to flourish. The Annihilation Land, having once experienced the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, was a place all cultivators avoided, let alone explored. If not for the ancestor's personal command, Qin Zhuang would never have risked his life. In Qin Zhuang's memories, Li Fan saw the appearance of that ancestor. "It is indeed Situ Yao of the Heavenly Sword Sect." "And that Elder Taishang Ji…" Li Fan's eyes flickered; this was also an old acquaintance. It was the cultivator Ji Zhaoxuan, whose body he had inhabited in the Fallen Immortal Realm's 'Heavenly Sword Sect Sword Refining' instance. "Outside the Wall, various factions stand side by side." "The place Qin Zhuang lived is no longer called the Heavenly Sword Sect, but has been renamed the 'Sword Domain.' And that Sacred Merchant, which seems to be the hometown of Jiao Xiuyuan…" "Merchant Immortal Boat?" Li Fan wasn't entirely sure. Because in Qin Zhuang's memories, the Sacred Merchant was the most elite force among all the factions outside the Wall. Various miraculous treasures were endlessly produced, and sometimes, just one item could instantly turn the tide of battle between two major powers. But for some unknown reason, the Sacred Merchant's interaction with the outside world became increasingly scarce. They even began recalling treasures previously sold externally. This led other factions, who had long coveted the Sacred Merchant's technology, to start harboring restless thoughts.

… Outside the Wall, although various factions coexisted, there was one consensus. The Immortal Dao of the past had led to the descent of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. To prevent the tribulation from continuing, cultivators abandoned their past cultivation methods. And "Immortal" became a target for universal persecution. "Must Kill Nameless Immortals?" Li Fan mused thoughtfully. In Qin Zhuang's memories, Immortals were feared but not dreaded. This was because the major factions outside the Wall possessed unique methods specifically targeting Immortals. And the 'Cat Treasure' Li Fan had seen before was a creation of the Sacred Merchant! As for the 'White Circle Descending to the Mortal World'… Based on Qin Zhuang's memories, Li Fan deduced that it likely originated from a place called 'Heavenly Secrets.' Although Heavenly Secrets, like the Sacred Merchant, excelled in creation, their methods were more 'traditional,' closer to the artifact refining techniques of ancient cultivators. They speculated that Heavenly Secrets might be a conglomeration of scattered cultivation sects fleeing from various places in the past. However, all Heavenly Secrets cultivators denied this. "Besides relying on external artifacts, the reason why factions outside the Wall could contend with Nameless True Immortals, and even hunt them, was due to a trump card." "Each faction used different methods, but the principle was broadly the same." "Weakened, targeted Dao Annihilation Tribulation…" Nameless True Immortals merged with the Dao. But if their own Great Dao were implanted with this weakened version of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation, it would be like an insidious parasite, extremely difficult to eradicate. Not only would their strength be greatly diminished, but they would also constantly fear being locked onto by the true Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

… "Nameless True Immortal version of the Immortal-Mortal Miasma?" "Or perhaps, a specialized Ink Kill?" Li Fan had a general understanding of the situation outside the Wall. Although not perfectly clear, he had a rough outline. The fact that factions outside the Wall were aware of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation's existence, yet showed no particular concern, even daring to use it as an offensive means, puzzled him. It was as if they were confident that the Dao Annihilation Tribulation would not affect them. "Is this truly the case, or is it a fabricated facade?" Li Fan pondered. Just as people within the Xuanhuang Realm only knew about the Immortal Ruins and the Wall, the memories obtained from Qin Zhuang might not represent the complete truth outside the Wall. It's possible that the supreme experts of the civilization outside the Wall had woven a series of lies to maintain the survival of their civilization. In Li Fan's view, the claims made by the civilization outside the Wall had at least two obvious loopholes regarding the Dao Annihilation Tribulation and True Immortals. Nothing was more trustworthy than [True Return]. The seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand-year countdown to the apocalypse was sufficient proof that the Dao Annihilation Tribulation was still ongoing and could not be resisted by the single possibility of the civilization outside the Wall. Yet, they intentionally or unintentionally downplayed the terrifying nature of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation. As for True Immortals, Li Fan had witnessed the scene of 'Cat Treasure hunting Immortals.' Judging by the recovery level of the character 'Hunger' on the Southern Immortal Pillar, she was not far from the Nameless Realm. Yet, under the hunt of the Cat Treasure, she had almost no power to resist and was forcibly dragged away. However, in Li Fan's past reincarnations, Nameless Immortals and Fishing Immortals still existed. This already indicated something. Although they seemed extremely cautious and never appeared in person, their power could still cross the Wall and influence the Xuanhuang Realm… Li Fan understood. Facing these powerhouses who survived the destruction of the Immortal Realm calamity, the factions outside the Wall might not have the upper hand. But they had indeed acquired the capital to "hunt" them.

To achieve such a leap from mortal to this level, it was truly remarkable! It was precisely because he had reached the Half-Immortal realm that Li Fan keenly understood the vast gulf between Immortals and mortals. Therefore, he was even more curious about the methods employed by the civilization outside the Wall to bridge this gap. "Outside the Wall, there are specialized organizations responsible for hunting True Immortals, referred to as [Immortal Hunters] by all factions. Immortal Hunter members undergo specialized training. The divine abilities they are taught are far beyond the imagination of ordinary people. Qin Zhuang was an Immortal Hunter, but before coming to the Xuanhuang Realm, he was only a newly recruited substitute and had never officially participated in hunting True Immortals." Li Fan attempted to replicate some divine abilities from Qin Zhuang's memories. "It bears some resemblance to the power of True Immortal inscriptions. Both invoke the Great Dao of the mortal world, but the difference lies in…" Li Fan narrowed his eyes, visualizing ninety-nine peculiar symbols in his mind. These symbols were called [Dao Origin] by the civilization outside the Wall. By arranging these ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols in different combinations, they could resonate with the Dao and harness the power of the corresponding Great Dao. "The True Immortal Inscriber personally comprehended and imitated the True Immortal inscriptions, which are the closest to the fundamental nature of the Dao, the most primordial." "These Dao Origins are further simplified and systematized, making them easier to learn and control. Moreover, through some means I have yet to discover, they have achieved the miracle of mutual integration and communication between different Dao powers…" In his Sea of Consciousness, the ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols flashed rapidly. Thirty-six extinguished, and the remaining sixty-three flew out, forming a new symbol. "Qin Zhuang's first divine ability learned from the Immortal Hunter organization was [Summon Sword]." "Theoretically, it can summon all sword techniques that have ever existed in the Dao of the Sword, and with good luck, even new sword divine abilities. The distinction seems to depend on the frequency of resonance during Dao Origin merging, which is related to the resonance between different Great Daos…" Li Fan's first attempt was somewhat strenuous. Even comprehending it was difficult. The main reason was that Qin Zhuang himself was a novice in Dao Origin techniques, possessing only a superficial understanding. For Li Fan to replicate the achievements of the civilization outside the Wall, which had strived for countless years, based on such a fragile foundation, was not easy. After hundreds of persistent attempts, none were successful. Li Fan frowned and stopped. "My method is correct." "It's the environment that's wrong!" After carefully savoring the resonance frequencies between the ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols, Li Fan finally understood.

"The Annihilation Land…" Li Fan gazed towards the outside of the Wall. "According to the explanation from outside the Wall, within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the Great Dao is depleted. The surviving regions after the Dao Annihilation Tribulation have Great Daos that are inherently inactive." Li Fan had never ventured outside the Wall, so he couldn't ascertain the exact meaning of "inactive." But he could make an analogy and imagine. "Perhaps this situation can be seen as the richness of the environment and resources." "In a place where the Great Dao is depleted, sensing the Dao is extremely difficult. However, in such harsh conditions, those who still manage to cultivate successfully, upon leaving and reaching a so-called 'highly active' region…" "While within the environment, one wouldn't notice. But when the external environment drastically changes, one would instantly feel the impact on oneself." "Ordinary cultivators with mediocre talent would already be considered geniuses among geniuses!" As this thought flashed through his mind, Li Fan felt a flicker of excitement. But it was quickly suppressed by Li Fan. "The biggest problem is that the cultivation methods outside the Wall are different from those inside. Moreover, various factions are prevalent, and although there are no large-scale wars, minor conflicts are constant. They are highly wary of outsiders. If one's identity is exposed, instead of infiltration, one might be captured and interrogated…" "Perhaps Qin Zhuang, or Jiao Xiuyuan, would be suitable as an entry point," a glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. "Qin Zhuang was taught the ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols, which are merely the most basic techniques of the Immortal Hunters. It is said that there are even more powerful experts who can skillfully wield nine hundred ninety-nine, nine thousand nine hundred ninety-nine, and even an unlimited number of these symbols." "This is also the capital that allows the civilization outside the Wall to hunt True Immortals." In Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness, two images were displayed side by side. On the left, True Immortal inscriptions. On the right, ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols. Li Fan attempted to correlate the True Immortal inscriptions, whose paths were already known, with these ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols. However, it was clear that these Dao Origin symbols were specially encrypted and did not possess the characteristics of the original paths. Without systematic study, even with Li Fan's prodigious talent, he could not decipher them. Shaking his head slightly, he temporarily dismissed this image from his mind. "True Immortals, Immortal Hunters. Although their realms and forms of power expression are vastly different, at their core, it all comes down to the degree of comprehension of the Great Dao." "It's just that outside the Wall, through these so-called Dao Origin symbols, the power of the Great Dao has been translated, allowing mortals to grasp and utilize it. At the same time, it prevents anyone from merging with the Dao and stealing it." The more he savored it, the more Li Fan marveled: "The creator of these Dao Origin symbols must have understood the Great Dao to a degree comparable to the Dao Inscribing Immortal of the past!" No longer completely ignorant of the outside world, and with the possibility of further advancement beyond the Immortal realm, Li Fan began to re-evaluate his exploration plan in his mind. "However, I must make thorough preparations." "Besides guarding against the factions outside the Wall, I must also be wary of existences from other possibilities." Stepping across possibilities was something that was clearly not within the common knowledge of ordinary people. Qin Zhuang's memories naturally contained no records of it. Li Fan even suspected that only a handful of individuals in the entire civilization outside the Wall might know about it. But one must take things step by step. Compared to Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, Li Fan's current strength was indeed too weak. "I still haven't found Immortal Spiritual Energy that I can use, and my path forward is blocked. Furthermore, given the current situation, ascending to the True Immortal realm might only lead to difficulties outside the Wall, and might not necessarily be a good thing." "First, I will improve my strength through the Dao Origin techniques outside the Wall," Li Fan decided. "Additionally, ensuring my safety, I must personally venture outside the Wall to investigate the so-called 'highly active Dao regions' and understand the situation." Learning the Dao Origin translation technique of the Great Dao did not mean Li Fan had to start from scratch. On the contrary, compared to most people outside the Wall, Li Fan had an immense advantage that they couldn't possess. That was Li Fan's knowledge of numerous True Immortal inscriptions, and even the leg bone of a Nameless True Immortal, allowing him to manifest primordial inscriptions close to the Great Dao itself. Dao Origins were merely translated symbols. No matter how combined, transformed, or resonated, their ultimate goal was to access and utilize the power of the Great Dao. If one did not understand the Great Dao itself, but only studied the Dao Origins, it would be like walking blindfolded, only able to grope around. However, if one already had a deep understanding of the Dao being translated, with the distant destination as a reference, learning would undoubtedly be twice as effective with half the effort. "Even, if I understand enough Dao Origin symbols, I might be able to directly decipher them," Li Fan had a faint premonition. "Of course, the creator of the Dao Origin symbols would not have failed to anticipate this. There should be some restrictions that I am not yet aware of."

… Li Fan had several other important matters to attend to before formally exploring outside the Wall. The Five Elders Council, The Land of Eternal Bliss. The Dao-Transforming Stone Mother. Law-Transmitter Jiang. Including the secrets of the Xuanhuang Realm's Guardian Ancient Immortal Formation. Including the Azure Nether Pearl, still floating in the dark rift of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. … In order of difficulty, Li Fan first went to meet Law-Transmitter Jiang. The mysterious characteristic of "All things are like me" on this person had almost caused Li Fan to stumble in the past. Now, Li Fan was very curious whether this mystical power could still affect him after he had ascended to the Half-Immortal realm. Law-Transmitter Jiang meditated in seclusion in the Void Realm, his true form never leaving. Li Fan flashed into this small world, observing his surroundings with interest. And Law-Transmitter Jiang, meditating with his eyes closed, remained completely unaware. "The Void Realm can continuously 'return to origin,' meaning that no matter what happens, it can be reset to its initial state..." "This is somewhat similar to my True Return, but the level is far inferior. It can only maintain this small world. It cannot even reset time, only the state of matter." However, even so, Li Fan was curious about the principle behind the realization of 'Return to Origin.' Thousands of dark golden threads, like his eyes, like his tentacles, spread out like liquid mercury, analyzing the small world for Li Fan. "Hmm… I see. It's not truly unlimited return to origin. The initial essence of the small world is deeply engraved. It's like carving marks on a stone with a file." "All changes that occur within the small world can be eliminated by directly erasing a layer. The carving remains, and in presentation, it returns to the starting point." After a long while, Li Fan understood. He couldn't help but feel somewhat disappointed. However, it was understandable. Law-Transmitter was only at the Star Sea Supreme realm. Without True Return in hand, it was impossible to achieve true 'Transformed True and False.' To devise such a method was already incredibly ingenious. "Although it's crude and clumsy, it can inspire me." Li Fan's eyes flickered. He took a step forward and arrived before Law-Transmitter Jiang, who was calmly meditating. He bent down, bowing his head. He observed the latter carefully. "All things are like me." Li Fan savored the phrase, a strange feeling welling up within him. It had to be said that Law-Transmitter Jiang, the only one regarded highly by Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, was indeed extraordinary. Even though Li Fan had reached the Half-Immortal realm, he couldn't prevent this feeling from arising in his heart. The longer he stared at Law-Transmitter Jiang, the more familiar and intimate it felt. However, compared to when he was mortal, Li Fan could clearly distinguish the difference between himself and Law-Transmitter Jiang. "Like." "But ultimately not." "Without True Return, False cannot become True." Li Fan extended his right hand, flicked his finger at Law-Transmitter Jiang's forehead. Law-Transmitter Jiang, who was in meditation, suddenly opened his eyes. Upon seeing a completely unfamiliar face, his face was filled with shock. He coldly asked, "Who are you?!" Li Fan smiled, "Me? It's you!" His eyes emanated a magical and disorienting light, as Li Fan quietly deployed an Immortal Array, using the Dissolution Disc to simulate this miraculous characteristic.

Then, he reversed it, applying it to Law-Transmitter Jiang. After all, as the original owner of this characteristic, Law-Transmitter Jiang's mind wasn't easily swayed initially. He stared warily at Li Fan. But slowly, in his eyes, Li Fan's appearance and image began to change inadvertently. Becoming increasingly similar to himself. Finally, truly like one person! As if looking in a mirror, Law-Transmitter Jiang looked at himself not far away, his wariness completely vanishing. "I have a premonition that my current strength is far from my limit." "'All things are like me,' what is the ultimate realm? Wouldn't all Great Daos belong to me?" Law-Transmitter Jiang was profoundly shaken as he heard the figure opposite him say this.

Chapter 1424: The Origin of Dao Derives Ten Thousand Phenomena

As if struck by lightning, Law-Transmitter's long-sealed mind was forcibly torn open. Naturally, he followed Li Fan's guidance in his thoughts. "Precisely! All things are like me, heaven and earth are like me, and the Great Dao is also like me…"

At this moment, Law-Transmitter Jiang seemed possessed, murmuring to himself. As his eyes began to gleam, different light projections flickered within this Void Realm. Li Fan had directly transported a complete small world from the Xuanhuang Realm to this place to facilitate Law-Transmitter Jiang's enlightenment.

Under the influence of the Immortal Array, Law-Transmitter Jiang lost his senses, immersing himself in enlightenment. Indeed, with his "All things are like me" supreme characteristic, he could indeed perceive and assimilate everything in the world. Even the myriad Great Daos of heaven and earth.

But Law-Transmitter Jiang was currently too weak. The gap between him and the Great Dao was even wider than that between an ant and the vast sky. If he wanted to assimilate the Great Dao with himself, even with an endless lifespan, it would be wishful thinking. Because before he could achieve this goal, the Dao Annihilation Tribulation engulfing the mortal world would have already descended.

If Law-Transmitter Jiang's consciousness were still clear, he would never undertake such a foolish endeavor. But now that he was within Li Fan's Immortal Array, he was beyond his control.

Li Fan didn't care whether Law-Transmitter Jiang could achieve enlightenment or not. What he cared about was that Law-Transmitter Jiang was currently "using himself to comprehend the Dao." Through the approximation of the "All things are like me" mystical characteristic exerted by the Immortal Array, Li Fan could faintly synchronize with Law-Transmitter Jiang's thoughts, feelings, and perceptions.

Under normal circumstances, such close resonance between two different beings would inevitably lead to mutual detection and even vigilance. But now, Li Fan had used the Immortal Array to block Law-Transmitter Jiang's perception of him, thus achieving a one-way perception of Law-Transmitter Jiang.

Although there was still a gap between his perception and Law-Transmitter Jiang's true thoughts, for Li Fan, it was equivalent to having a constantly enlightened clone helping him comprehend the Great Dao of the world. Moreover, Li Fan believed that as the Dissolution Disc continued to deduce and iterate the Illusory Immortal Array, the gap in their comprehension could be further narrowed.

As the figure in the Void Realm gradually dimmed, before Li Fan departed, he extended his hand. The vast Void Realm became smaller and smaller compared to Li Fan's body, eventually falling into his palm like a radiant pearl. Although the change was slight, during the time Law-Transmitter Jiang was enlightening, Li Fan clearly perceived that his understanding of the "Dao" was slowly but steadily increasing. He intended to keep this "enlightenment machine" with him for a long time.

"It can be considered a controllable, albeit weakened, version of the Immortal Heavenly Pillar."

"Moreover, although the speed of comprehending the Great Dao is far slower than that of Nameless True Immortals, its accuracy may not be inferior. Perhaps even superior!" Li Fan compared them, realizing something. "Because Law-Transmitter Jiang does not comprehend based on his own talent or cognition, but relies on his innate characteristic – in a sense, it can be considered comprehending through the Dao itself."

"Using Dao to comprehend Dao, truly wondrous!"

After carefully placing the Void Pearl, containing Law-Transmitter Jiang, deep within his body, Li Fan meticulously savored the Illusory Immortal Array deduced by the Dissolution Disc based on Law-Transmitter Jiang's characteristic. "This characteristic definitely originates from an extraordinary Immortal artifact. Once this characteristic is mastered, deciphering the Great Dao from nothing would no longer be an unattainable goal."

"Unfortunately, it has been too long, and it has completely merged with Law-Transmitter Jiang, making it impossible to separate. But I can imitate it through formations, achieving eighty to ninety percent of its effect."

"This array should be named…" After pondering for a moment, Li Fan slowly spoke: "Heaven-Connecting, All things are like me!"

Li Fan keenly sensed that this Heaven-Connecting Array was not only suitable for Law-Transmitter Jiang but could also be used for all beings in the world to assist his enlightenment. "However, careful selection is still necessary."

"Law-Transmitter Jiang's enlightenment of the Dao is closest to the origin of the Dao. But for others, no matter how brilliant their talent appears on the surface, limited by their cultivation and strength, their understanding of the Dao will inevitably deviate. These deviations, conversely, can become 'pollutants' that tarnish my understanding."

While contemplating, the Dissolution Disc had already produced the first iteration of the Heaven-Connecting Array, capable of covering an entire realm. Although the Dissolution Disc possessed infinite Immortal Spiritual Energy, the amount that could be utilized each time had an upper limit. Li Fan had not yet found a way to increase this limit.

Furthermore, setting up this "Heaven-Connecting Array" would require approximately thirty days of preparation. Li Fan personally took charge of setting up the array. Meanwhile, under Li Fan's will, an announcement was quickly disseminated throughout the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

"The Heavenly Venerate shows compassion to all beings, teaching without discrimination. Those who believe they have talent can proceed to the various prefectures of the Immortal Alliance for testing. Those who meet the conditions, regardless of origin, past, age, or gender, can enter the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters for an opportunity to explore the Heavenly Venerate's hidden treasures. They may even have the chance to personally receive a sermon from the Heavenly Venerate."

Upon hearing this, the world was shaken. Everything described in the Myriad Immortals Alliance's announcement was too perfect, impossibly so, leading to suspicions of a conspiracy. However, looking back at the past, while the Immortal Alliance occasionally committed scoundrel acts, they never dared to act recklessly in the name of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate.

Thus, the general populace of the Myriad Immortals Alliance initially adopted a wait-and-see attitude. But there would always be those who couldn't resist temptation and feared no death for profit. And when they truly entered the Heavenly Venerate's hidden treasures, reaped immense rewards, and reappeared before the public – fact spoke louder than words. Greed and temptation completely overwhelmed rationality.

Every day, a large number of cultivators confident in their talent went to the prefecture cities of the Myriad Immortals Alliance to participate in the tests. The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters even designated the number of geniuses recommended annually by each prefecture as the most crucial assessment metric. The City Lords of each prefecture spared no effort and employed all means to find talented individuals within their territories, not sparing even mortals. Some City Lords even resorted to fighting amongst themselves for a promising prospect.

When the entire Myriad Immortals Alliance operated towards a single objective, the efficiency was unimaginable compared to Li Fan acting alone. Wave after wave of prodigies were continuously sent to the "Realm of Drafting" created by Li Fan. Their true bodies, barring unforeseen circumstances, would remain there forever. And the replicas, assembled from fabricated personalities and flesh and blood, would reappear in the public eye, serving as both encouragement and deception.

Li Fan floated in mid-air, slightly nodding as he observed the gradually taking shape "Realm of Drafting." Within the heavens and earth, True Immortal inscriptions floated like jewels. Corresponding to the True Immortal inscriptions were ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols. And before the crowd of prodigies, a phantom of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate sat, imparting knowledge and answering questions. This phantom was, naturally, created by Li Fan.

To reap rewards, one must first sow. And as expected, the rewards these prodigies in the "Realm of Drafting" brought to Li Fan would far exceed his investments, proving to be an incredibly profitable venture. "Currently, the enlightenment gained from the beings in the 'Realm of Drafting' is even less than that from Law-Transmitter Jiang alone. However, I believe as their cognition continuously improves, this gap will quickly shorten."

Satisfied with the efficiency of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's operations, Li Fan decided to offer some rewards. With Li Fan's current foundation, even a small offering would be immensely beneficial to them. However, this time, Li Fan chose the improved version of the Tai Jia Divine Art, which could communicate with the Star Sea.

Instead of directly bestowing the Tai Jia Divine Art, he created a formation that granted the people of the Myriad Immortals Alliance an opportunity to enter the formation, connect their minds with the true essence of the Star Sea, and glimpse its profound meaning. Cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm had never escaped the gravitational pull of the Immortal Ruins, nor had they personally witnessed the true power of the Star Sea. This Tai Jia Divine Art allowed them to perceive the Dao of the Star Sea even while remaining in the Xuanhuang Realm.

In this life, Li Fan had not promoted the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation. Ostensibly, the Xuanhuang Realm remained an ordinary cultivation world within the Star Sea. The intricacies of the Star Sea's laws were far superior to the Xuanhuang Realm's heavenly laws. Even a few breaths of enlightenment in the Star Sea would bring immense benefits to Xuanhuang Realm cultivators. And as Li Fan had predicted, all who experienced this were filled with admiration and longing, yearning for the next opportunity. This, in turn, made them even more dedicated to contributing and earning Li Fan's rewards.

Li Fan, delegating the control of the formation to Di San Mo, decided to adopt a hands-off approach. First, he traveled outside the Void to intercept Law-Transmitter and Heavenly Physician, who were still speeding back to the Xuanhuang Realm, and suppressed and sealed them. Li Fan then drew his wooden sword phantom and entered the dark river beneath the rift below the Wall. Following his previous memories, Li Fan arrived before the Azure Nether Pearl, which was floating quietly.

After ten thousand years of continuously releasing life force, the Azure Nether Pearl was now on the verge of collapse, sustained only by a phantom image. Although it had lost its power as an Immortal artifact, it still held significant meaning for Li Fan. Without approaching, not even extending his divine sense, he observed it carefully from afar.

"A creation from the [Divine Witch Realm]…" Li Fan mused inwardly. "My original plan was to transfer life force to the Azure Nether Pearl in reverse, forcibly pulling it back from the brink of destruction. Then, using Transformed True and False, I would 'repair' it step by step."

"Now, it seems a bit too risky." Li Fan had a premonition that if he made the slightest move, the extremely fragile Azure Nether Pearl would instantly shatter into pieces. "The only method is to directly use Transformed True and False for superposition. First, reverse its state of near-destruction."

But to perform Transformed True and False, one needed sufficient observational samples. At the very least, one needed to fully understand the essence of the target, or at least have a "subject" for the spell. Similar to how Li Fan previously replicated the Primordial Cang Origin. However, the current situation was that the Azure Nether Pearl was too fragile. Li Fan couldn't even observe the process up close, only from a distance.

After a long stalemate, a flash of inspiration suddenly struck Li Fan's mind. "Interference cannot come from external influences. We can only hope for changes within the Azure Nether Pearl itself."

"The cultivation techniques of the twelve Dharma Kings of the Heavenly Xuan Sect originated from this Azure Nether Pearl."

"And there was a secret technique within the Heavenly Xuan Sect capable of stripping away and seizing the cultivation gained by disciples, called [Taking Heaven and Replacing It]."

"I recall Zhao Ruoxi mentioning in her dream that the Great Dao Sect obtained this secret technique after annihilating the Heavenly Xuan Sect."

"…" Li Fan's eyes narrowed. "Perhaps, to obtain the Azure Nether Pearl, I must first visit the Five Elders Council."

"That's fine. There is another Eternal Remnant Will located there. I can retrieve it at the same time."

With his mind made up, Li Fan flew out of the Star Sea Rift, but instead of heading to the Five Elders Council first, he went to Myriad Immortals Island. The Myriad Immortals Island was buried with the remains of countless deceased Law-Transmitters, suppressing the so-called 'Netherworld Passage.' The Netherworld Passage, continuously emitting strange energy, was merely a mutation caused by the Xuanhuang Realm's consumption and integration of other worlds.

The power level of the cultivation world was no longer something Li Fan cared about. What interested him more were the countless remains of the Law-Transmitters. "There is no trace of Eternal Remnant Will here."

"However, within the Soul Grinding Plate of the Five Elders Council, there seems to be a preserved Eternal Remnant Will."

"The Five Elders Council once launched a surprise attack on Myriad Immortals Island, precisely to seize the Law-Transmitter remains buried here..." Past memories flowed through his mind.

With a thought, the Myriad Immortals Island violently trembled. Then, under the terrified gazes of countless cultivators, the island slowly rose into the air. "It seems the key lies in that Soul Grinding Plate."

Li Fan collected the remains of the Law-Transmitters, which exuded a chilling aura, and felt no change in True Return's reaction. He looked towards the location of the Five Elders Council and hurried away. Without Li Fan's empowerment, the Myriad Immortals Island fell back into the sea. However, without its suppression, strange energies began to emanate from the Netherworld Passage below.

As the cultivators on Myriad Immortals Island panicked, they received Li Fan's orders. Teleportation formations flickered continuously, and teams of black-robed cultivators emerged, sealing off the area and handling the aftermath.

Li Fan did not use the Wooden Sword's Evasion technique but deliberately slowed his pace, circling around the territory of the Five Elders Council, where the five Longevity Heavenly Venerates resided. In the past, once he entered, he was beyond his control and was influenced. But now, they could no longer affect him, Li Fan, who had already transcended the bounds of heaven and earth. As if proving the heavens and earth, he had already surpassed them.

Chapter 1425: The Great Heavenly Dao Array

"Just like how the Xuanhuang Realm people only knew about the Immortal Ruins and the High Wall, the memories obtained from Qin Zhuang might not represent the complete truth outside the Wall. It's possible that the supreme experts of the civilization outside the Wall have woven a series of lies to maintain the survival of their civilization."

In Li Fan's opinion, the claims made by the civilization outside the Wall had at least two obvious loopholes regarding the Dao Annihilation Tribulation and True Immortals. Nothing was more trustworthy than [True Return]. The seven million three hundred sixty-five thousand eight hundred sixty-four-year countdown to the apocalypse was sufficient proof that the Dao Annihilation Tribulation was still ongoing and could not be resisted by the single possibility of the civilization outside the Wall. Yet, they intentionally or unintentionally downplayed the terrifying nature of the Dao Annihilation Tribulation.

As for True Immortals, Li Fan had witnessed the scene of 'Cat Treasure hunting Immortals.' Judging by the recovery level of the character 'Hunger' on the Southern Immortal Pillar, she was not far from the Nameless Realm. Yet, under the hunt of the Cat Treasure, she had almost no power to resist and was forcibly dragged away.

However, in Li Fan's past reincarnations, Nameless Immortals and Fishing Immortals still existed. This already indicated something. Although they seemed extremely cautious and never appeared in person, their power could still cross the Wall and influence the Xuanhuang Realm…

Li Fan understood. Facing these powerhouses who survived the destruction of the Immortal Realm calamity, the factions outside the Wall might not have the upper hand. But they had indeed acquired the capital to "hunt" them. To achieve such a leap from mortal to this level, it was truly remarkable! It was precisely because he had reached the Half-Immortal realm that Li Fan keenly understood the vast gulf between Immortals and mortals. Therefore, he was even more curious about the methods employed by the civilization outside the Wall to bridge this gap.

"Outside the Wall, there are specialized organizations responsible for hunting True Immortals, referred to as [Immortal Hunters] by all factions. Immortal Hunter members undergo specialized training. The divine abilities they are taught are far beyond the imagination of ordinary people. Qin Zhuang was an Immortal Hunter, but before coming to the Xuanhuang Realm, he was only a newly recruited substitute and had never officially participated in hunting True Immortals."

Li Fan attempted to replicate some divine abilities from Qin Zhuang's memories.

"It bears some resemblance to the power of True Immortal inscriptions. Both invoke the Great Dao of the mortal world, but the difference lies in…"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, visualizing ninety-nine peculiar symbols in his mind. These symbols were called [Dao Origin] by the civilization outside the Wall. By arranging these ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols in different combinations, they could resonate with the Dao and harness the power of the corresponding Great Dao.

"The True Immortal Inscriber personally comprehended and imitated the True Immortal inscriptions, which are the closest to the fundamental nature of the Dao, the most primordial."

"These Dao Origins are further simplified and systematized, making them easier to learn and control. Moreover, through some means I have yet to discover, they have achieved the miracle of mutual integration and communication between different Dao powers…"

In his Sea of Consciousness, the ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols flashed rapidly. Thirty-six extinguished, and the remaining sixty-three flew out, forming a new symbol.

"Qin Zhuang's first divine ability learned from the Immortal Hunter organization was [Summon Sword]."

"Theoretically, it can summon all sword techniques that have ever existed in the Dao of the Sword, and with good luck, even new sword divine abilities. The distinction seems to depend on the frequency of resonance during Dao Origin merging, which is related to the resonance between different Great Daos…"

Li Fan's first attempt was somewhat strenuous. Even comprehending it was difficult. The main reason was that Qin Zhuang himself was a novice in Dao Origin techniques, possessing only a superficial understanding. For Li Fan to replicate the achievements of the civilization outside the Wall, which had strived for countless years, based on such a fragile foundation, was not easy. After hundreds of persistent attempts, none were successful.

Li Fan frowned and stopped.

"My method is correct."

"It's the environment that's wrong!"

After carefully savoring the resonance frequencies between the ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols, Li Fan finally understood.

"The Annihilation Land…" Li Fan gazed towards the outside of the Wall. "According to the explanation from outside the Wall, within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, the Great Dao is depleted. The surviving regions after the Dao Annihilation Tribulation have Great Daos that are inherently inactive."

Li Fan had never ventured outside the Wall, so he couldn't ascertain the exact meaning of "inactive." But he could make an analogy and imagine.

"Perhaps this situation can be seen as the richness of the environment and resources."

"In a place where the Great Dao is depleted, sensing the Dao is extremely difficult. However, in such harsh conditions, those who still manage to cultivate successfully, upon leaving and reaching a so-called 'highly active' region…"

"While within the environment, one wouldn't notice. But when the external environment drastically changes, one would instantly feel the impact on oneself."

"Ordinary cultivators with mediocre talent would already be considered geniuses among geniuses!"

As this thought flashed through his mind, Li Fan felt a flicker of excitement. But it was quickly suppressed by Li Fan.

"The biggest problem is that the cultivation methods outside the Wall are different from those inside. Moreover, various factions are prevalent, and although there are no large-scale wars, minor conflicts are constant. They are highly wary of outsiders. If one's identity is exposed, instead of infiltration, one might be captured and interrogated…"

"Perhaps Qin Zhuang, or Jiao Xiuyuan, would be suitable as an entry point," a glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"Qin Zhuang was taught the ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols, which are merely the most basic techniques of the Immortal Hunters. It is said that there are even more powerful experts who can skillfully wield nine hundred ninety-nine, nine thousand nine hundred ninety-nine, and even an unlimited number of these symbols."

"This is also the capital that allows the civilization outside the Wall to hunt True Immortals."

In Li Fan's Sea of Consciousness, two images were displayed side by side. On the left, True Immortal inscriptions. On the right, ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols. Li Fan attempted to correlate the True Immortal inscriptions, whose paths were already known, with these ninety-nine Dao Origin symbols. However, it was clear that these Dao Origin symbols were specially encrypted and did not possess the characteristics of the original paths. Without systematic study, even with Li Fan's prodigious talent, he could not decipher them.

Shaking his head slightly, he temporarily dismissed this image from his mind.

"True Immortals, Immortal Hunters. Although their realms and forms of power expression are vastly different, at their core, it all comes down to the degree of comprehension of the Great Dao."

"It's just that outside the Wall, through these so-called Dao Origin symbols, the power of the Great Dao has been translated, allowing mortals to grasp and utilize it. At the same time, it prevents anyone from merging with the Dao and stealing it."

The more he savored it, the more Li Fan marveled: "The creator of these Dao Origin symbols must have understood the Great Dao to a degree comparable to the Dao Inscribing Immortal of the past!"

No longer completely ignorant of the outside world, and with the possibility of further advancement beyond the Immortal realm, Li Fan began to re-evaluate his exploration plan in his mind.

"However, I must make thorough preparations."

"Besides guarding against the factions outside the Wall, I must also be wary of existences from other possibilities."

Stepping across possibilities was something that was clearly not within the common knowledge of ordinary people. Qin Zhuang's memories naturally contained no records of it. Li Fan even suspected that only a handful of individuals in the entire civilization outside the Wall might know about it.

But one must take things step by step. Compared to Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, Li Fan's current strength was indeed too weak.

"I still haven't found Immortal Spiritual Energy that I can use, and my path forward is blocked. Furthermore, given the current situation, ascending to the True Immortal realm might only lead to difficulties outside the Wall, and might not necessarily be a good thing."

"First, I will improve my strength through the Dao Origin techniques outside the Wall," Li Fan decided.

"Additionally, ensuring my safety, I must personally venture outside the Wall to investigate the so-called 'highly active Dao regions' and understand the situation."

Learning the Dao Origin translation technique of the Great Dao did not mean Li Fan had to start from scratch. On the contrary, compared to most people outside the Wall, Li Fan had an immense advantage that they couldn't possess. That was Li Fan's knowledge of numerous True Immortal inscriptions, and even the leg bone of a Nameless True Immortal, allowing him to manifest primordial inscriptions close to the Great Dao itself.

Dao Origins were merely translated symbols. No matter how combined, transformed, or resonated, their ultimate goal was to access and utilize the power of the Great Dao. If one did not understand the Great Dao itself, but only studied the Dao Origins, it would be like walking blindfolded, only able to grope around. However, if one already had a deep understanding of the Dao being translated, with the distant destination as a reference, learning would undoubtedly be twice as effective with half the effort.

"Even, if I understand enough Dao Origin symbols, I might be able to directly decipher them," Li Fan had a faint premonition. "Of course, the creator of the Dao Origin symbols would not have failed to anticipate this. There should be some restrictions that I am not yet aware of."

…

With several important matters to attend to before formally exploring outside the Wall, Li Fan had other crucial tasks. The Five Elders Council, The Land of Eternal Bliss. The Dao-Transforming Stone Mother. Law-Transmitter Jiang. Including the secrets of the Xuanhuang Realm's Guardian Ancient Immortal Formation. Including the Azure Nether Pearl, still floating in the dark rift of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

…

In order of difficulty, Li Fan first went to meet Law-Transmitter Jiang. The mysterious characteristic of "All things are like me" on this person had almost caused Li Fan to stumble in the past. Now, Li Fan was very curious whether this mystical power could still affect him after he had ascended to the Half-Immortal realm.

Law-Transmitter Jiang meditated in seclusion in the Void Realm, his true form never leaving. Li Fan flashed into this small world, observing his surroundings with interest. And Law-Transmitter Jiang, meditating with his eyes closed, remained completely unaware.

"The Void Realm can continuously 'return to origin,' meaning that no matter what happens, it can be reset to its initial state…"

"This is somewhat similar to my True Return, but the level is far inferior. It can only maintain this small world. It cannot even reset time, only the state of matter."

However, even so, Li Fan was curious about the principle behind the realization of 'Return to Origin.' Thousands of dark golden threads, like his eyes, like his tentacles, spread out like liquid mercury, analyzing the small world for Li Fan.

"Hmm… I see. It's not truly unlimited return to origin. The initial essence of the small world is deeply engraved. It's like carving marks on a stone with a file."

"All changes that occur within the small world can be eliminated by directly erasing a layer. The carving remains, and in presentation, it returns to the starting point."

After a long while, Li Fan understood. He couldn't help but feel somewhat disappointed. However, it was understandable. Law-Transmitter was only at the Star Sea Supreme realm. Without True Return in hand, it was impossible to achieve true 'Transformed True and False.' To devise such a method was already incredibly ingenious.

"Although it's crude and clumsy, it can inspire me." Li Fan's eyes flickered.

He took a step forward and arrived before Law-Transmitter Jiang, who was calmly meditating. He bent down, bowing his head. He observed the latter carefully.

"All things are like me." Li Fan savored the phrase, a strange feeling welling up within him. It had to be said that Law-Transmitter Jiang, the only one regarded highly by Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, was indeed extraordinary. Even though Li Fan had reached the Half-Immortal realm, he couldn't prevent this feeling from arising in his heart. The longer he stared at Law-Transmitter Jiang, the more familiar and intimate it felt. However, compared to when he was mortal, Li Fan could clearly distinguish the difference between himself and Law-Transmitter Jiang.

"Like."

"But ultimately not."

"Without True Return, False cannot become True."

Li Fan extended his right hand, flicked his finger at Law-Transmitter Jiang's forehead. Law-Transmitter Jiang, who was in meditation, suddenly opened his eyes. Upon seeing a completely unfamiliar face, his face was filled with shock. He coldly asked, "Who are you?!"

Li Fan smiled, "Me? It's you!"

His eyes emanated a magical and disorienting light, as Li Fan quietly deployed an Immortal Array, using the Dissolution Disc to simulate this mystical characteristic. Then, he reversed it, applying it to Law-Transmitter Jiang.

After all, as the original owner of this characteristic, Law-Transmitter Jiang's mind wasn't easily swayed initially. He stared warily at Li Fan. But slowly, in his eyes, Li Fan's appearance and image began to change inadvertently. Becoming increasingly similar to himself. Finally, truly like one person! As if looking in a mirror, Law-Transmitter Jiang looked at himself not far away, his wariness completely vanishing.

"I have a premonition that my current strength is far from my limit."

"'All things are like me,' what is the ultimate realm? Wouldn't all Great Daos belong to me?"

Law-Transmitter Jiang was profoundly shaken as he heard the figure opposite him say this.

Chapter 1426: Ink Kill Dao Annihilation

As Li Fan stepped into the Land of Utmost Bliss, unlike ordinary people, he was not directly pulled into an illusory dream. Instead, he witnessed the reality of the Land of Utmost Bliss. At the edges of the real utopia, there were still traces of human activity. However, the deeper he ventured into the core region, the fewer traces of human life there were.

After flying for some time, he arrived at the center of the utopia. The entrance led to a primeval natural landscape completely devoid of human presence. Sunlight shone brightly, and the climate was humid. Numerous rivers meandered through the endless rainforest. The vitality here was incredibly rich, perhaps the most so in the Xuanhuang Realm. Many species seemed to have evolved later, never appearing in other regions of the Xuanhuang Realm. Li Fan also acutely sensed a force subtly maintaining the ecological balance of this natural utopia.

"Utmost Bliss..." Li Fan's gaze was like lightning. He sent a wisp of his divine sense directly towards this power within the rainforest. The moment it was broken through, Li Fan vaguely heard a faint baby's cry in his ears.

The surrounding rainforest scene instantly disappeared. In a trance, it was as if he had arrived at a small mountain village, and the continuous crying was coming from one of the houses. Li Fan looked around with interest; he had seen this mountain village scene before. It was from a painting titled "The Tale of the Demon Infant Who Swallowed Father and Mother and Forgot Worries."

Following the source of the sound, Li Fan pushed open the door. A thick smell of blood assaulted his nostrils, and the scene inside the room was quite gruesome. He saw an infant lying in a swaddling cloth on a bed. By the bedside, a man and a woman were mangled beyond recognition. However, there was no hint of pain on their faces; instead, they were still grinning foolishly. As if they couldn't feel pain at all, they chipped off a piece from their own flesh and bone, revealing their white bones, and fed it to the infant on the bed.

"Nanny, eat more, eat till you're full. Hahaha." They babbled like madmen while coughing up large amounts of blood. This blood seemed to be something extremely precious. Their faces immediately showed a look of heartache as they hurriedly collected every drop of spilled blood, mixed it with shredded tissue, and stuffed it into the infant's mouth. The infant had no way to stop it and could only cry weakly.

...

Even Li Fan frowned slightly at this somewhat sinister scene. Without a doubt, this was the past of Wuyou. But Li Fan, an accomplished formation master, could see at a glance that this was very different from ordinary illusory formations. "At the very least, this man and woman, who are Wuyou's parents, were they real?"

Li Fan's divine sense manifested, and he slowly walked up to them. Under Li Fan's intervention, their actions were forcibly stopped. As if returning from a dream to reality, the dazed and joyful expressions disappeared from the couple. Although their bodies were unable to move, they seemed to understand their predicament upon regaining consciousness. Infinite despair and madness surged in their eyes. "Ahhhh..." They wanted to say something, but they couldn't open their mouths. They could only emit meaningless sounds.

Dissatisfied with Li Fan's meddling, that force forcibly regained control of the couple. They began their nightmarish actions again, digging out flesh and bones, and feeding the infant.

"This is what they insisted upon; why should Senior interfere?" "Isn't it good to fulfill their wishes?"

A smiling voice suddenly appeared, echoing in the small room. "Putting on a show." Li Fan snorted coldly and was about to react. Suddenly, a figure appeared, bowing gracefully. And in her mouth, she softly called, "Senior, spare my life!"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and examined the other person. She was unclothed, her body frail, with no discernible curves. Her long hair seemed as if it hadn't been cut since birth, covering the ground like a winding black river. Wuyou, with her naked body, showed no hint of embarrassment under Li Fan's gaze, as if this were her natural state.

"Senior, do you know what happened afterwards?" Wuyou pointed at the man and woman in the room feeding the infant with their own flesh and blood and asked expectantly.

Li Fan did not reply, so Wuyou answered herself: "These two, from an unknown Immortal Master, heard of a secret method to defy fate. By feeding the newly born infant with the parents' vital essence and blood, and after eighty-one days, if the infant is then swallowed, one can soar to become an Immortal."

"Hehe..."

The scene in front of Li Fan rapidly shifted. As the infant, nourished by flesh and blood, grew up at an incredible rate, her crying grew louder and louder. Slowly, the sound spread from the small room to other parts of the village. This sound seemed to possess a magical quality; anyone who heard it lost their minds, walking like zombies, slowly approaching, and then "offering their bodies to the demon"!

In just a few days, the entire village had turned into indistinct flesh and blood in the room. The infant's cries slowly spread throughout the entire mountain. Birds and beasts in the mountains, like humans, walked into the room without fear of death. Towering bloody energy blocked the house, as if even sunlight could not penetrate it. In the darkness, accompanied by the incessant crying of the infant, was the heart-stopping sound of chewing. In the end, all living beings in the entire mountain range were swallowed by the demonic infant. Silence reigned. Only the infant's cries echoed.

...

For Li Fan, this level of carnage was already insignificant. He looked towards a corner of the illusion. "As expected of Senior!" Wuyou's voice of admiration sounded at the same time.

Li Fan's gaze fell, and the blurry figure, which had been indistinct, became clear. "Wonderful, wonderful! The Holy Infant is growing faster than planned!" "In a few more days, this spiritual pill will be completely refined. The parents' sincere love, the innate desire for survival, plus the innate instincts of all beasts..." "Old Ancestor will definitely be very satisfied with this Holy Infant." "Seven tries were wasted, but this time it's finally successful."

The figure muttered to himself, happily calculating the time. He flew down, with a heart full of anticipation, and slowly walked into the small room. "To harvest the Holy Infant is what he has always dreamed of. Let him remain in his dream." "Fulfilling his wish, isn't it good?"

Li Fan, however, saw that after the cultivator entered the small dark room, his expression suddenly changed greatly. Confusion and terror intermingled in his eyes. He wanted to break free from his uncontrollable state. But step by step, irresistibly, he approached the infant. And then, completely succumbed, like countless beings already buried in the infant's belly, he dug out his own flesh and bones piece by piece!

"Does Senior find it satisfactory?" The scene suddenly shattered, and Wuyou, with a pure expression, asked expectantly.

Li Fan did not answer, only watching as the countless specks of light that shattered surged towards him. These specks of light, as vast as the starry sky, each represented an illusory dream. Perhaps from mortals, perhaps from birds and beasts. It was like an endless river of memories, washing over Li Fan's divine sense. It wasn't just the visual records; it also contained various insights of different levels. There were the beings who had fallen into this illusion, and... Wuyou herself. Reflections and understandings of the principles of the Xuanhuang Realm!

A mere wisp of divine sense was originally not enough to withstand the baptism of such a vast amount of information. Just as it was about to be assimilated and become part of the fallen illusion, the last part of this wisp of divine soul, however, refused to dissipate. No matter how much Wuyou tried to wash it away with her will, she couldn't touch it in the slightest. Wuyou's eyes couldn't help but show a hint of curiosity. But with her strength, she couldn't see through the residual divine sense at all. This only fueled Wuyou's curiosity further.

After the starry sky, more light spots ignited, like a galaxy falling from high heaven, like a waterfall impacting the last diamond-like residual divine sense. "Are you sure you really want to see?"

After persistently trying, just as she was about to succeed, Li Fan's voice, like a ghost, suddenly echoed in Wuyou's ears, "Are you sure you really want to see?"

After a moment of hesitation, Wuyou continued her actions. The brilliant silver divine sense exploded. What appeared before Wuyou was... Floods surging, heavenly fire raining down, black clouds covering the sun, the world freezing over. Visions of the end of the world erupted simultaneously. And this was just an appetizer. The destruction of worlds was just the beginning. A monstrous tide of black energy descended upon the world, devouring everything. In the rolling sea of black energy, entire star seas vanished. It was like a bright house gradually falling into complete darkness. The existence of the entire world collapsed in an instant. And the terrifying calamity was far from over. The scene illuminated in the darkness, in an instant, expanded countless times. As if in an endless sea, every splash was a complete world. And at this moment, a terrifying darkness from the depths of the sea was constantly devouring. Every apocalyptic scene imaginable played out in this sea. Utter immersion and despair. As the darkness gradually enveloped oneself and eroded slowly. When this sea completely fell into dead silence. After a brief pause, all that could be seen were countless parallel threads. The endless ocean just seen was merely an insignificant speck in one of these threads. And now, these bright threads began to annihilate in large numbers. With the disappearance of each beam of light, corresponding scenes of world destruction flooded into Wuyou's mind. The Great Dao Annihilation Tribulation, affecting countless possibilities, was drawn from Li Fan's personal experiences and the memories of sinister Su Bai from the eternal remnant will.

Such a terrifying spectacle, yet so real, was far beyond Wuyou's tolerance. Even from a mental perspective, her strength was not much weaker than that of the Law-Transmitter or the Heavenly Physician. But now... Dark clouds representing doom, terror, and despair descended through Wuyou into the Land of Utmost Bliss.

Boom! Dream worlds collapsed one after another, plunging into the apocalypse without warning. The very foundation of the dreamland was severely impacted, inevitably experiencing violent turbulence.

"Ahhh!" Wuyou screamed and woke up from the nightmare. Her body trembled uncontrollably, covered in cold sweat. She tried to stop the spread of the terrifying calamity within the dreamland. But the tribulation spread too fast. And even she couldn't protect herself, let alone the myriad beings in the dream?

"Senior, spare my life!" Wuyou left the dream and entered reality. Kneeling before Li Fan, her body trembling. Even though she had previously learned through various channels that this suddenly descended Senior True Immortal's strength was terrifying and even incomprehensible. But to survive such a terrifying great tribulation without dying... far exceeded Wuyou's imagination. All her plans were in vain; Wuyou's only thought now was instinctual survival!

"Worry, worry." "The great tribulation has arrived, how to relieve sorrow?" Li Fan said meaningfully.

The calamity that was violently affecting countless dreams within Wuyou's dreamland suddenly froze. Then, just as it had arrived, it vanished without a trace, silently. A black dot, emanating immense murderous intent, appeared in Li Fan's palm. Then, with a gentle wave of Li Fan's hand, it floated towards Wuyou's forehead. Wuyou's body trembled slightly, instinctively wanting to dodge. But this light spot, radiating rolling black energy, seemed to carry the weight of countless superimposed worlds. She couldn't dodge at all and could only let it enter her divine soul. As if a shadow, it started from the top and then hid in the heart, disappearing without a trace.

After a long while, Wuyou, still shaken, vaguely regained consciousness. Looking at the figure in front of her, she felt how ridiculous and absurd her earlier thoughts of playing tricks and testing were. "Senior, spare my life!" Wuyou lowered her head and took instructions.

Li Fan stood with his hands behind his back, his figure seemingly illuminated by a layer of silver light around his edges, obscuring his face, making it impossible to look directly at him. "Let Senior take me to see the other four." Wuyou respectfully obeyed.

The surrounding scene shifted again. This time, Li Fan felt the power of the dreamland swirling around him. However, he had already implanted countermeasures in Wuyou's mind. With a single thought from him, Wuyou's dream would collapse, so Li Fan let her pull him into the illusion as she wished.

"Ink Kill, Heavenly Immortal Soul, integrated into the phenomenon of Dao Annihilation." "The power is not bad." Li Fan thought this, observing his surroundings. Wuyou, awestruck by Li Fan's methods, was indeed highly efficient. Zhao Ruoxi, the One-Heart Heavenly Venerate, appeared before Li Fan first. She was also naked, as if she had been lying on a beach basking in the sun. Alarmed by the inexplicable great tribulation, she suddenly got up to observe, her expression filled with surprise and uncertainty. And now, the sudden arrival of Wuyou and Li Fan startled her even more. Li Fan had seen this delicate body countless times before. No matter how alluring it was, it couldn't stir Li Fan in the slightest. Zhao Ruoxi also understood the situation through a brief exchange of glances with Wuyou. While deeply shaken internally, she changed into a white robe. "Greetings, Upper Immortal." She bowed gracefully to Li Fan. Li Fan nodded slightly. Just then, fluctuations were felt from the surroundings. Wuyou's form flickered, returning to the appearance of an infant in swaddling clothes. The other three Longevity Heavenly Venerates arrived a moment later.

Chapter 1427: Descent into Samsara

A man in a Taoist robe, and a scholar-like man in white. Li Fan had seen the illusory figures of these two before; they were the True Heavenly Venerate and the Human Dao Heavenly Venerate, respectively.

Within the True Kingdom, no lies existed. And in the Human Dao Heavenly Realm, anyone, regardless of their cultivation level, could change heaven and earth as long as their heart was sincere.

As for the last one, he was a young man in his early twenties with an extraordinary and refined aura. Although Li Fan had never met him in person, he had encountered him once during the Fallen Immortal Realm's trial. Ji Wangxian!

Ten thousand years ago, he had personally established the "Myriad Heavens Commerce" that spanned across the Xuanhuang Realm, building a lavish and luxurious heavenly city with spirit stones. "I never expected that the old ancestor of the Ji family, known for his shrewd business dealings, would transform into a representative of contracts."

"However, according to legend, the entire Ji family and the Myriad Heavens Commerce were tools for Ji Wangxian's cultivation. After the great changes in the world, if he still wanted to maintain his longevity by changing his methods, it's understandable."

As Li Fan's thoughts raced, his gaze swept across the three newly arrived Longevity Heavenly Venerates. Clearly, they had already learned from Wuyou about Li Fan's unfathomable cultivation. Although they appeared calm, maintaining the demeanor of Xuanhuang's top powerhouses, Li Fan could still faintly discern their nervousness.

"Hehehe, don't be nervous."

"The Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate has already been suppressed by me." Li Fan said this casually, yet it made the five Heavenly Venerates present's hair stand on end.

When they saw the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, trapped in an infinite illusion, seemingly asleep yet not asleep, neither awake nor asleep, in Li Fan's palm, their faces inevitably turned pale, and they all lowered their heads, not daring to meet Li Fan's gaze.

Especially Wuyou, her body trembled uncontrollably, filled with lingering fear for her earlier impudent and foolish probing.

Before this, although the five Heavenly Venerates knew that this suddenly descended Senior True Immortal's strength was extraordinary, they had no quantitative concept of just how strong he was. But now they knew.

The Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, who had dominated the Xuanhuang Realm for an era and forced the five of them to submit together, was so easily suppressed by the opponent's effortless move. How could such strength not fill the five with dread?

Li Fan seemed to ignore their inner feelings and continued to say indifferently, "The separation between Immortals and mortals is vast; I will not interfere excessively with you. But there are some things that require your humble help."

"Senior, please command us!" Wuyou spoke first. Such eagerness, in stark contrast to her usual indifference to worldly affairs, caused the other four Heavenly Venerates to exchange glances. However, could those who had attained Longevity in the Xuanhuang Realm be foolish? They all expressed their willingness to serve.

"I have come here for one item: the Soul Grinding Disc." As soon as Li Fan said this, Wuyou and the others looked towards the man in the Taoist robe. The True Heavenly Venerate's face twitched, then he cupped his hands and produced a millstone-like object, handing it over.

Li Fan saw that the Soul Grinding Disc seemed to still be rotating slightly. Beneath it, faint cries of tragedy could be heard from countless souls being ground by the massive millstone. And from "Returning to Truth," there indeed came faint signals of activity.

Within the Soul Grinding Disc, there were fifty-six remnant souls and one hundred and three skeletal remains, but the aura of these remnant souls and skeletal remains seemed even more powerful than those of countless lonely ghosts. Li Fan examined them carefully and saw the secret.

The Soul Grinding Disc, like a giant millstone, constantly ground these remnant souls and skeletal remains. Theoretically, no matter how special they were, they couldn't withstand such torment. At most, they would vanish into nothingness within ten years. But they had persisted from ancient times to the present.

This was because, every moment, streams of pure energy emerged from the Soul Grinding Disc, nourishing these remnant souls. Maintaining their life force, they were subjected to another round of grinding by the giant millstone. This cycle, like being in an endless purgatory, had no end. Li Fan finally understood how these existences, suspected to be eternal remnant wills, were formed.

"A decent method." Li Fan commented calmly. The True Heavenly Venerate lowered his head, not daring to reply.

Li Fan's hand exerted a slight force, and the giant millstone instantly vanished into smoke and dust. The remnant souls and skeletal remains were freed and absorbed by "Returning to Truth." And the residual pure energy in the millstone felt somewhat familiar to Li Fan. It was exactly the same as the pure cultivation that formed after converting one's own cultivation with the "Erosion Chapter" of the "Supreme Primordial True Scripture."

"Remnants of the Supreme Ancient Sect." Li Fan glanced at the True Heavenly Venerate, lost in thought. Converting cultivation with the Primordial True Scripture was not that all of it would be inherited; a small portion would disappear into nothingness, lost.
