Now, it seemed it had flowed into the pockets of the Supreme Ancient Sect.

"The life and death of all cultivators are none of my concern. It truly fits the character of the Supreme Ancient." When the great tribulation descended upon the Xuanhuang Realm in the past, a portion of the ten great Immortal Sects had already escaped. Individuals like Yi Xin and True Being might have unexpected uses in exploring beyond the High Wall. Li Fan temporarily ignored them, focusing solely on observing the changes in "Returning to Truth."

Compared to its previous greedy and joyful desire to devour, "Returning to Truth" behaved strangely this time. It was as if it had eaten something extremely difficult to swallow, wanting to spit it out, yet still swallowing it mouthful by mouthful, enduring it. Li Fan's expression became somewhat subtle. He stood still, observing the prompts from "Returning to Truth." The remaining four Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Council also stood by, not daring to move.

Perhaps this time, the eternal remnant will was not formed by a single person, but by numerous remnant souls. Li Fan had not experienced the trial of the actual illusion, and "Returning to Truth" had absorbed it directly.

"Function [Endless Reincarnation] unlocked." There wasn't even a poem recited, just a simple cryptic sentence.

"[Endless Reincarnation]..." However, these four words immediately piqued Li Fan's interest.

"Using a past life experience as a template, create a time period with a beginning and an end."

"Any being that can be thrown into this time period without the ability to resist."

"If there is a corresponding identity for the being thrown in this timeline, they will possess it. If not, they will be randomly possessed."

" The possessed being for the trapped being can be specified."

"The trapped being will lose all memories related to outside of reincarnation."

"During the entire Endless Reincarnation, only the memories of the trapped being will be retained."

"Time continuously cycles from beginning to end, constrained by the fixed template of events to ensure Endless Reincarnation does not deviate from the original trajectory."

"Endless Reincarnation depends on my existence. Each time True Return is activated and returns to the initial anchor point, the created reincarnation will disappear and must be recreated. Alternatively, a certain price can be paid to choose to retain it."

"The time flow of Endless Reincarnation is a thousand times that of the normal space-time I experience, and it can be greatly accelerated according to my needs..."

The functions of Endless Reincarnation were much more complex than the previous [Avatar] and [Dao Origin], but they were actually very easy to understand. It was a constantly repeating history that Li Fan had experienced. It was important to note that every time Li Fan forced "Returning to Truth," a great terror descended. This meant that in Endless Reincarnation, a destructive tribulation would occur every few decades. And due to "Returning to Truth's" active constraint, beings undergoing reincarnation could not achieve incremental progress and ultimately defy fate like Li Fan.

"I can also constantly observe the state of the being thrown into reincarnation..."

"Interesting. Extremely interesting." As if he had found a novel toy, Li Fan felt a surge of curiosity.

"Qiao Sidao escaped from billions of reincarnations within the Era. Then, can anyone escape from the Endless Reincarnation created by Returning to Truth?" According to the explanation from Returning to Truth, only when the outcome of the reincarnation deviated completely could this Endless Reincarnation be terminated. But the trapped being could still not escape. This reincarnation timeline existed in a state between true and false void. Waiting for Li Fan's next command. Whether to release the trapped being, or create a new Endless Reincarnation.

"It truly lives up to its name, 'Endless'!" Li Fan almost slammed the table in amazement, then turned sharply to look at the True Heavenly Venerate. He gave him a meaningful smile and then gently pointed at him. One of the few Longevity Heavenly Venerates in the Xuanhuang Realm, vanished from everyone's sight without a sound. His life and death were unknown.

The remaining Wuyou and others were terrified. But they had no intention of avenging the True Heavenly Venerate; they could only pray in their hearts that this Senior True Immortal would spare their lives. The entire process of the True Immortal suppressing the True Heavenly Venerate occurred without any energy fluctuations, simply vanishing in a way they couldn't comprehend. They couldn't even resist, let alone understand. The gap was so vast that they completely lost the courage to resist.

Li Fan's attention, however, was already focused on the activated Endless Reincarnation. He chose the history where he, as the Holy Embryo, rode the Medicine King True Cauldron and charged towards the Immortal Ruins. The period that caused the Starving Immortal to destroy the world with a single glance.

Chapter 1428: Dream Array Born of the Heart

The True Heavenly Venerate within Endless Reincarnation lost the memory of seeing Li Fan and returned to the anchor year one. A hint of confusion flashed in his eyes. But how could a mere Longevity realm cultivator resist the might of "Returning to Truth"? This thread of doubt soon vanished. Following his past historical trajectory, he continued his life.

...

Li Fan sensed the rapid flickering of light and shadow within Endless Reincarnation. The thousandfold increase in time flow exerted a unique pressure on him. It wasn't like carrying an Immortal Region chess piece, with his body and soul bearing a heavy burden. Instead, it felt as if his entire being was shrouded in a hazy mist. His thoughts, and even his every action, felt as if he were in a dream. Under this influence, Li Fan even vaguely doubted the reality of his own existence in the present world.

It wasn't just Li Fan. Even the other four Heavenly Venerates standing beside Li Fan began to look dazed. They either recalled past memories, or suddenly saw scenes they had never experienced in their minds, or suddenly remembered a fleeting thought they had long forgotten. All were unable to resist this contamination, falling into it, unable to extricate themselves.

It wasn't until Endless Reincarnation's time flowed rapidly forward, experiencing its first conclusion and starting its second cycle, that Li Fan slowly adapted. His mind focused, the mist around him thinned slightly. He still felt a sense of strangeness, but at least his actions were no longer affected.

Only then did Li Fan have the opportunity to observe what was happening within Endless Reincarnation. He ignored the True Heavenly Venerate, who was in a state of shock, joy, and fear due to his "rebirth." The first thing Li Fan did was to search for "himself" within the Xuanhuang Realm of Endless Reincarnation. To his relief, he did not see another self. Replacing him in advancing Endless Reincarnation towards its predetermined end was a cultivator named "Zhang Fan," who looked remarkably similar to him.

"Naturally, there is no other [Returning to Truth]. Zhang Fan only possesses the illusion of being able to be reborn endlessly. When Endless Reincarnation is activated, his memories will be reset without him realizing..."

"He's just a tool created." Li Fan shook his head slightly and turned his attention to the True Heavenly Venerate.

The True Heavenly Venerate firmly believed that his vision of the Xuanhuang Realm being destroyed in his "previous life" was not an illusion. However, he did not rush to tell others about his reborn experience. Instead, he set aside all other matters and focused on investigating the truth behind the world's destruction. As expected of a powerhouse who had attained Longevity, he quickly traced the impending disaster to the mysteriously appearing Heavenly Dao White. Following the clues, he eventually found his way to the Medicine King Valley.

When the "Annihilation Style" was triggered, and the Medicine King True Cauldron containing the Holy Embryo soared into the sky, the True Heavenly Venerate hiding in the dark also keenly sensed its existence. He was about to intervene. But...

After saving the Medicine King Sect disciples, the Heavenly Dao White flashed in front of the True Heavenly Venerate. Although not an opponent of the Law-Transmitter, he was, after all, the manifestation of the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao will, capable of wielding the power of all worldly spirits. For a time, the True Heavenly Venerate could not escape. He could only watch as the Medicine King True Cauldron flew further and further away.

In this life, the outcome did not change; the Xuanhuang Realm was still destroyed by the Starving Immortal's gaze.

...

"Is this what is called the linear constraint of Returning to Truth?" Li Fan mused, then accelerated the time flow of Endless Reincarnation. His mind became hazy, and the pressure he experienced deepened considerably. Fast-forwarding to the True Heavenly Venerate's next attempt to save the world. Even before the Heavenly Dao White descended, the True Heavenly Venerate had already noticed Zhang Fan, who was plotting in the dark. He made a decisive move, intending to apprehend him. But his revealing his aura actually alerted the prohibitions within the Myriad Immortals Alliance. The Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Council infiltrated the territory, and the Myriad Immortals Alliance treated it as a major enemy. The illusory projection of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate descended and, without explanation, severely wounded the True Heavenly Venerate with a single palm. Amidst the chaos, Zhang Fan had already disappeared without a trace. Not long after, the world-ending tribulation descended again.

"Interesting. The Law-Transmitting illusory projection did not actually appear in this life. To activate the Law-Transmitting illusory projection requires the sacrifice of several Immortal selection candidates."

"But this is not a simulation by Endless Reincarnation, where things are fabricated at will..." Li Fan's eyes flashed with a hint of playfulness: "It seems as if it had already foreseen the True Heavenly Venerate's actions. At the beginning of the reincarnation, the Myriad Immortals Alliance began a large-scale selection of Immortal candidates. There were some deviations compared to what happened in previous reincarnations."

"But the True Heavenly Venerate, focused on investigating the true culprit of world destruction, inadvertently overlooked this point."

"It seems that the so-called constraints of Endless Reincarnation only need to ensure that the beginning and the end are consistent with the original. The specific details in between do not matter."

The third reincarnation. This time, the True Heavenly Venerate directly camped at the border of the Xuanhuang Realm, waiting for the Medicine King True Cauldron to appear. But for some reason, this time the Medicine King True Cauldron did not appear for a long time. Even more unexpectedly, on the very day the end of the world arrived according to his memories, the suction from the Immortal Ruins above suddenly strengthened. Caught off guard, he lost control and began to fall towards the Immortal Ruins. Doing his best to survive, he saw a skeleton standing on the ruined earth, surrounded by severed golden chains. The Starving Immortal in the Immortal Ruins grabbed the barely resisting True Heavenly Venerate and absorbed and refined him. Then, with blood-red eyes, still unsatisfied, he looked down at the Xuanhuang Realm below.

...

"Is this what is called the linear constraint of Returning to Truth?" Li Fan mused, then accelerated the time flow of Endless Reincarnation. His mind became hazy, and the pressure he experienced deepened considerably. Fast-forwarding to the True Heavenly Venerate's next attempt to save the world. Even before the Heavenly Dao White descended, the True Heavenly Venerate had already noticed Zhang Fan, who was plotting in the dark. He made a decisive move, intending to apprehend him. But his revealing his aura actually alerted the prohibitions within the Myriad Immortals Alliance. The Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Council infiltrated the territory, and the Myriad Immortals Alliance treated it as a major enemy. The illusory projection of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate descended and, without explanation, severely wounded the True Heavenly Venerate with a single palm. Amidst the chaos, Zhang Fan had already disappeared without a trace. Not long after, the world-ending tribulation descended again.

"Interesting. The Law-Transmitting illusory projection did not actually appear in this life. To activate the Law-Transmitting illusory projection requires the sacrifice of several Immortal selection candidates."

"But this is not a simulation by Endless Reincarnation, where things are fabricated at will..." Li Fan's eyes flashed with a hint of playfulness: "It seems as if it had already foreseen the True Heavenly Venerate's actions. At the beginning of the reincarnation, the Myriad Immortals Alliance began a large-scale selection of Immortal candidates. There were some deviations compared to what happened in previous reincarnations."

"But the True Heavenly Venerate, focused on investigating the true culprit of world destruction, inadvertently overlooked this point."

"It seems that the so-called constraints of Endless Reincarnation only need to ensure that the beginning and the end are consistent with the original. The specific details in between do not matter."

The third reincarnation. This time, the True Heavenly Venerate directly camped at the border of the Xuanhuang Realm, waiting for the Medicine King True Cauldron to appear. But for some reason, this time the Medicine King True Cauldron did not appear for a long time. Even more unexpectedly, on the very day the end of the world arrived according to his memories, the suction from the Immortal Ruins above suddenly strengthened. Caught off guard, he lost control and began to fall towards the Immortal Ruins. Doing his best to survive, he saw a skeleton standing on the ruined earth, surrounded by severed golden chains. The Starving Immortal in the Immortal Ruins grabbed the barely resisting True Heavenly Venerate and absorbed and refined him. Then, with blood-red eyes, still unsatisfied, he looked down at the Xuanhuang Realm below.

...

"Huh? This is a possibility I've never experienced before."

"Did the Starving Immortal come out of seclusion early?"

In reality, looking at the Starving Immortal within Endless Reincarnation from afar. This Starving Immortal, even though he had achieved enlightenment and was close to the Nameless Realm, could still not discover Li Fan's prying gaze. He only had a vague premonition, looking surprised and uncertain.

...

The Starving Immortal's actions after achieving enlightenment made Li Fan's heart jump, and he temporarily stopped the simulation function of Endless Reincarnation. It wasn't that he feared the Starving Immortal.

"Theoretically, Endless Reincarnation is a new possibility created out of thin air by Returning to Truth."

"So, is it possible that terrifyingly powerful beings capable of traversing possibilities discovered the anomaly and leaped out of Endless Reincarnation?"

"For example, if I used my past life experience as a template. Then wouldn't it mean that in this created Endless Reincarnation, there would be another Black Heavenly Physician?"

Just as Li Fan was filled with doubt, Returning to Truth seemed to sense his thoughts and promptly sent a prompt.

"Incomplete timelines created naturally would not include beings who transcend possibilities."

"Variables caused by template experiences will be presented in other ways to ensure the consistency of the original and the ultimate..."

Li Fan silently sensed the fluctuations of Returning to Truth, feeling relieved while also somewhat regretful.

"It's fine as long as nothing goes wrong." He glanced at the True Heavenly Venerate within Endless Reincarnation, who was collapsing and had not moved for more than ten years, Li Fan shook his head slightly.

"I don't know when this Longevity Heavenly Venerate will break free from the destiny of reincarnation."

"I hope you don't disappoint me."

Of course, even if the True Heavenly Venerate completely gave up the idea of escaping, Li Fan would not easily let him go. This was because Li Fan had already sensed that every time Endless Reincarnation restarted, it was equivalent to "Returning to Truth" initiating a change between true and false. It was just that the scale was incomparable to Li Fan's own activation. But it had the advantage of being continuous and did not interfere with Li Fan's actions in reality.

"This is a valuable tool to assist me in comprehending the transformation between true and false."

"It's a pity that with my current strength, I don't seem capable of activating the second Endless Reincarnation yet." Li Fan thought with some regret.

Returning his thoughts to reality. Li Fan looked at Wuyou and the others. The four Longevity Heavenly Venerates were completely subdued by the methods Li Fan employed.

"I can vaguely sense that beyond the High Wall, there is a great terror."

"This is also why I have stopped short of crossing the High Wall, despite being able to." Li Fan's words made Wuyou and the others' expressions change drastically.

"I know your Wuyou Dreamland has already explored near the High Wall."

"It can cooperate with my actions in reality, attacking from both sides. We will probe the reality beyond the High Wall." Li Fan stared intently at Wuyou. The frail Longevity Heavenly Venerate repeatedly assured him, "Being able to serve Senior is Wuyou's greatest fortune."

"As for you three..." Li Fan looked at the Human Dao Heavenly Venerate, Zhao Ruoxi, and Ji Wangxian. He flicked three specks of light from his fingers, flying into the brows of the three. These were miniature formations that used the Ink Kill Dao Annihilation Phenomenon as the core and the Xuanhuang Realm phantom feedback obtained from the Heaven-Establishing Tablet as energy drivers, capable of monitoring and counteracting.

As soon as they entered their bodies, countless array patterns like roots began to grow deep into the divine souls of the three. However, what made Zhao Ruoxi and the other three feel even more horrified was that they never felt the slightest pain from beginning to end. Instead, a supreme sense of satisfaction and joy surged from their hearts. Even as the array patterns gradually covered their entire divine souls, their feelings towards Li Fan transformed from fear to reverence and loyalty. They knew that this nucleating core rooted deep within their divine souls was constantly prying into all their secrets, yet they had no intention of resisting. Instead, they were eager to completely overturn their divine souls and offer them to the other party.

The Human Dao Heavenly Venerate's blood surged, giving him the urge to die for his benefactor. Ji Wangxian knelt on one knee, deeply impressed. Zhao Ruoxi's cheeks flushed, her body softened, and she collapsed to the ground, her eyes fixed on Li Fan, unwilling to look away for a moment.

Through observing Endless Reincarnation from top to bottom, Li Fan gained a deeper understanding of the Longevity Heavenly Venerates before him. Coupled with the tailored array modifications by the Dissolution Disc, they achieved such miraculous effects.

"It's even a hundred times more effective than the True Temptation Fruit back then." Li Fan thought to himself.

...

He turned his head and said to Wuyou, who had witnessed everything with a pale face, "Your dreamland skills are too shallow. Trying to explore beyond the High Wall will likely be insufficient. Seven days later, you will all come to the Myriad Immortals Alliance."

"I will have someone assist you in making some modifications to the dreamland." As his voice still echoed in the air, Li Fan's figure had already faded, disappearing without a trace.

Chapter 1429: Repairing the Azure Pearl

Through the array patterns rooted deep within Zhao Ruoxi's divine soul, Li Fan scanned all her memories in an instant. As expected of the One-Heart Heavenly Venerate who gathered the essence of countless individuals into one, the scenes she experienced were astonishing. However, this was not the point. Li Fan quickly found what he was looking for. "Taking Heaven and Replacing ..." A secret treasure from the Great Dao Sect, one of the rich legacies from the past destruction of the Xuan Tian Sect. It was said to be able to completely strip away the cultivation techniques and cultivation of Xuan Tian Sect disciples, and even transfer the realm and strength gained from cultivating Xuan Tian Sect techniques to the caster. Li Fan was skeptical of the description of this secret technique. After all, figures like the Twelve Dharma Kings should not be so easily controlled by such a secret technique. But regardless, most of the Xuan Tian Sect's cultivation techniques originated from the Azure Nether Pearl. It was not beyond reason for it to be reclaimed by it. What Li Fan needed to do now was to verify whether there was a connection between this "Taking Heaven and Replacing" secret technique and the Azure Nether Pearl.

By feeding cultivation back into the Azure Nether Pearl, it was brought back from the brink of complete collapse. Then, Li Fan would gradually repair it step by step with the Transformation of True and False. As for the cultivation fed into the Azure Nether Pearl... Zhao Ruoxi, who cultivated the "Myriad Ages, My Own Path," was naturally the best source! From Zhao Ruoxi's memories, Li Fan already knew that although she attained enlightenment through the principle of "Myriad Beings into One," the core of her cultivation technique was still based on the "Myriad Ages, My Own Path" set. "Indulging in games, not pursuing progress." "Successfully defying reason relied on the heaven-defying characteristics of this cultivation technique."

Li Fan snorted coldly in his heart, but in the blink of an eye, he returned to the sunken land below the High Wall, where the Azure Nether Pearl was located. The Dissolution Disc had already translated the "Taking Heaven and Replacing" secret technique into an array. Streams of light, carrying the array information, entered Zhao Ruoxi's divine soul invisibly. The light spots spread along the dense array patterns, and as they operated, Zhao Ruoxi's cultivation was slowly extracted. In Li Fan's hand, four drops of strange green liquid were slowly forming.

Zhao Ruoxi could naturally sense the outflow of her cultivation. For someone at the Longevity realm like her, there was nothing more terrifying than reverting to a mortal overnight. Her face turned pale, not knowing where she had offended the capricious True Immortal. The speed at which Zhao Ruoxi's cultivation drained grew faster and faster, but she was helpless, watching her thousands of years of hard-earned essence disappear before her eyes. Moreover, she soon realized something even more terrifying. Since defying reason and becoming a Longevity Heavenly Venerate of the Xuanhuang Realm, she had become a part of the Xuanhuang Realm. Although she was currently in the Longevity realm, as her cultivation drained, her increasingly weak body seemed unable to support the principles of the Xuanhuang she had defied! As if burdened by a heavy object, her divine soul and body began to ache faintly.

"Gnnnh..." Zhao Ruoxi couldn't suppress a muffled groan, and numerous fine bloodstains appeared all over her body. And it wasn't just this body. All of her were on the verge of collapse. With her spiritual energy completely depleted, even less than that of an ordinary Qi Refining stage cultivator, Zhao Ruoxi felt an unprecedented weakness. The feeling of her soul and body being ground and torn apart was magnified a thousandfold as her strength decreased. Blood gushed out from the cracks all over her body, soaking her into a bloodied person, obscuring the flowing tears. She was in so much pain that she couldn't even let out a scream, only emitting hoarse sounds from her throat. The fear of instantly reverting to a mortal, and the ever-increasing, all-pervasive pain in her soul and body, made Zhao Ruoxi's mind drift back to her childhood in Qing Mountain. At that time, bandits were burning and looting in the village, and blood stained the sky. Hiding outside the village, she saw fierce bandits who seemed to have discovered her and were rushing towards her with sinister smiles. Zhao Ruoxi was in a state of panic. She discovered a figure standing motionless not far away, who had been there since she didn't know when. As if grabbing the only possible lifeline, Zhao Ruoxi cried out, begging, "Immortal Master, save me! Immortal Master, save me!"

The roar from her throat seemed to overlap with the past in her memory. However, the figure that Zhao Ruoxi regarded as her savior was no longer Zhang Rong, the fourth-generation disciple of the Yuehua lineage of the Great Dao Sect, whom she had already retaliated against and devoured. It had become Li Fan! The appearance of the blurry figure in Zhao Ruoxi's mind gradually became clear. As if responding to her plea, Li Fan smiled slightly. From the center of the countless array patterns within Zhao Ruoxi's divine soul, wisps of incredibly pure energy emanated from the Xuanhuang Realm phantom. Initially like a trickling stream, it quickly turned into a great river, roaring and surging ceaselessly. In an instant, it filled Zhao Ruoxi's body. This formerly dying One-Heart Heavenly Venerate instantly became full of vigor again. Feeling the immense and seemingly inexhaustible power from the Xuanhuang Realm phantom within her body, Zhao Ruoxi felt even stronger than before. The bloodstains on her fair skin disappeared. Zhao Ruoxi respectfully bowed to the figure standing deep within her divine soul, expressing her gratitude.

... Without paying attention to the minor commotion on Zhao Ruoxi's side, Li Fan's entire focus was on the extremely fragile Azure Nether Pearl before him. Zhao Ruoxi's lifelong cultivation from the Myriad Ages, My Own Path, only resulted in four drops of green liquid. And without Li Fan needing to control it much, with the subtle connection between it and the Azure Nether Pearl, the green liquid slowly seeped towards the nearby Azure Nether Pearl after its appearance. The nearly ten thousand years of hard cultivation by a Longevity Heavenly Venerate finally allowed this Immortal artifact to escape the brink of destruction!

Li Fan's heart rejoiced, and his divine sense followed closely, enveloping the Azure Nether Pearl heavily. The surface of the Azure Nether Pearl, like the vast azure sky, flowed in layers, attempting to block Li Fan's prying gaze. This defense might work against mortals, or perhaps if the Azure Nether Pearl were still in its prime, it might have been able to stop Li Fan. But it had just escaped a state of near-destruction, half-dead. How could it possibly block Li Fan, who possessed a Half-Immortal body? Divine sense acted like a needle, piercing the azure sky and penetrating deep into the Azure Nether Pearl's interior.

Boom! Li Fan's vision violently shook, and in the next moment, he seemed to have entered a strange realm. Twelve solemn palaces stood tall in the sky, distributed in a circle, occupying the firmament of the world. Each palace enshrined a statue. Continuous streams of cultivators came from the earth, kneeling and praying. And on the statues, faces occasionally appeared, seemingly communicating with these kneeling cultivators. ... Divine Witch Realm!

After the scene in his mind dissipated, Li Fan finally understood what he had just seen. That wisp of divine sense had been forcefully expelled by the Azure Nether Pearl. Li Fan did not attempt to invade again. With the contact he just had, and relying on the Azure Nether Pearl's unique aura, he could replicate it in a short period with the Transformation of True and False! But Li Fan did not leave to attempt it. He already had a premonition that creating another Azure Nether Pearl with the Transformation of True and False would bring a burden far exceeding what he had experienced before, requiring thorough preparation. Since the Azure Nether Pearl could not be moved for the time being, Li Fan set up layers of formations around it. Specks of light representing Immortal-grade formations flickered around Li Fan, giving him some peace of mind.

"False becomes True!" Li Fan lightly chanted in his heart, but the target of his divine ability was not the Azure Nether Pearl, but himself! His cultivation, divine soul, and all other power levels simultaneously doubled. Li Fan looked at the Azure Nether Pearl, still feeling it wasn't enough. After a short rest, he once again used the Transformation of True and False. The superposition of triple cultivation could not last long. Li Fan merely waited for his body to adapt to the burden before focusing his attention and locking onto the Azure Nether Pearl. Using the brilliant azure color as a guide, Li Fan recalled the fleeting glimpse of the Divine Witch Realm scene. He visualized the existence of another Azure Nether Pearl. "False..." "Becomes True!"

Li Fan felt that it was dozens of times more strenuous than replicating the Primordial Cang Origin. This was probably because the Primordial Cang Origin was merely a single form of energy, while the Azure Nether Pearl before him was a convergence of numerous laws. Blue veins bulged on his forehead. And in the next moment, he felt as if his body had been drained, experiencing extreme weakness. But seeing that the color on the Azure Nether Pearl seemed to have become more vivid and lively, Li Fan knew his attempt had succeeded. The superimposed cultivation from the Transformation of True and False slowly disappeared, and the fatigue in his body and mind struck like a collapsing mountain.

But Li Fan merely closed his eyes for a short rest before starting the replication of the Azure Nether Pearl again. Each time he used the Transformation of True and False, his comprehension deepened. But like those things created out of thin air, as time passed, most of these insights would slowly dissipate, leaving only a small portion. "The Transformation of True and False is ethereal, yet it is the foundation of my existence." "Relying solely on Returning to Truth each time, and the supplementary comprehension from Endless Reincarnation, is far from enough."

A resolute glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. Forcing himself despite his body and mind being exhausted, he once again used the Transformation of True and False. In the dark river within the sunken land, indescribable wondrous energies repeatedly descended and disappeared. Time slowly flowed by. Although Li Fan's appearance did not change, his aura became more unfathomable. He truly seemed like a transcendent True Immortal of the current era! After the time it takes for an incense stick to burn, Li Fan finally felt that his body and divine soul had reached their limit. He sighed slightly, the tide of exhaustion uncontrollably surging. Without even looking at the Azure Nether Pearl, which had been restored and seemingly reborn beside him, Li Fan first closed his eyes and sat down to rest properly. In his mind, there was neither thought nor feeling, as if he had fallen asleep. However, vaguely, countless light spots seemed to flicker, then return to darkness. This repeated endlessly.

When Li Fan's spirit was rejuvenated, it was already three days later. Through this short period of high-intensity, near-limit attempts at the Transformation of True and False, Li Fan gained insights equivalent to nearly five activations of Returning to Truth. "This is also because this is the first time I have continuously attempted this at my limit." "It's because it reawakened those insights from the past use of the Transformation of True and False that were fading. The effect from such cultivation next time will definitely not be as good." "But it is still of great significance."

With this attempt, Li Fan had already realized that the insights gained from each activation of Returning to Truth regarding the Transformation of True and False were different from those he gained through imitation. Unquestionably, the insights from Returning to Truth were purer and closer to reality. While the insights Li Fan gained through his own attempts were slightly inferior, they were easier to control. "There is still a long way to go from comprehension to practice." "Each activation of Returning to Truth deepens my comprehension progress, but the specific practice still requires me to do it myself."

Li Fan pondered, as if having realized something. And at this moment, Returning to Truth also transmitted a benevolent hint. Li Fan pondered and continued to try to communicate with Returning to Truth. But he only received silence. Li Fan shook his head slightly, temporarily setting this matter aside, and looked at the Azure Nether Pearl not far away. He reached out and took it. Perhaps it was because Li Fan had partially repaired it, but he didn't feel any resistance. This Immortal artifact lightly landed in his hand.

"Although it has barely escaped the state of fragmentation, its power has severely declined." "After all, the life force contained within it was taken out to repair the Utmost Darkness Star Sea." Li Fan thought this as he looked at the abundant life force in the dark river of the sunken land. But what Li Fan valued was not the life force of the Azure Nether Pearl, but its legendary miraculous function. "The Azure Nether Pearl can devour other Immortal artifacts and transfer their functions to itself." "And it can extract the cultivation techniques of cultivators from their corpses."

After Li Fan's careful investigation, he discovered that there was no longer an artifact spirit within the Azure Nether Pearl. If Li Fan hadn't repaired it, it would currently be a completely defunct empty shell. But now... "The functions can still be used." Li Fan's heart stirred, and he returned to the Xuanhuang Realm with the Azure Nether Pearl. To prevent the Starving Immortal in the Immortal Ruins from noticing, the surrounding concealment formations were not dispersed, only transformed into a layer of white mist. This also made Li Fan appear extraordinarily ethereal and immortal.

"Devouring Immortal artifacts..." Li Fan looked towards the Sun family's underground secret chamber, where the Boundless Mirror was located. He reached out, and the Boundless Mirror traversed space and time, arriving in Li Fan's palm. "Who is it!" Disregarding Sun Luyuan's startled cry, Li Fan directly fed it to the Azure Nether Pearl. Although it was also an Immortal artifact and severely damaged, the Boundless Mirror was clearly not on the same level as the Azure Nether Pearl. Furthermore, with Li Fan suppressing it, the Boundless Mirror had no power to resist at all. It merged into the vast azure color of the Azure Nether Pearl. The surface of the Azure Nether Pearl seemed to be experiencing a heavy rain, ripples spreading out. Perhaps it was too weak, and suddenly consuming so much, it couldn't handle it. This digestion by the Azure Nether Pearl took almost half a day. When the heavy rain finally subsided, a different aura was born from the Azure Nether Pearl.

Chapter 1430: Mastered by Corpses

The surface of the Azure Nether Pearl, originally a vast azure color, was now divided into many different regions by lines. Most of these regions had indistinct and unclear boundaries.

Only the region displaying a bright mirror seemed "alive" and emitted fluctuations distinctly different from the Azure Nether Pearl's main body. Li Fan vaguely saw a complete Boundless Mirror emanating from the surging aura.

"These different regions are the different Immortal artifacts that the Azure Nether Pearl has devoured before?"

"It's just that with the Azure Nether Pearl's past fragmentation, these functions could no longer be used. Only the newly opened Boundless Mirror region can barely..." An understanding dawned on Li Fan. Compared to the Azure Nether Pearl, the region developed into the Boundless Mirror was easier to conquer.

Li Fan patiently used the Boundless Mirror region as a breakthrough point and finally succeeded in sending a wisp of divine sense into the Azure Nether Pearl's interior, and this time it was not easily expelled. Instead, it took root and sprouted within the Boundless Mirror region.

Soon, as the formation arose with his thoughts, countless light green array patterns, almost the same color as the Azure Nether Pearl's main body, grew and spread from the Boundless Mirror region. Li Fan attempted to completely refine and control this Immortal artifact using the "Array Refining" technique.

The Immortal Rank Dissolution Disc acted efficiently. In just one day, a strange connection was established between Li Fan and the Azure Nether Pearl.

Li Fan let out a long sigh, playing with the Azure Nether Pearl in his right hand. There was no physical contact, just a cool, smooth, and comfortable sensation. The Azure Nether Pearl, reborn from destruction, was as if newly forged. All its past shackles and restrictions seemed to have vanished.

At the very least, Li Fan had meticulously inspected it inside and out and found no residual energy from any unknown origin. Even so, Li Fan was not entirely at ease, and the Array Refining technique continued to operate. Billions of silver stars gradually appeared on the vast azure surface of the Azure Nether Pearl, traces of the array's operation.

Li Fan first studied the Boundless Mirror function. He had once infiltrated this damaged Immortal artifact for a period and knew it very well.

"The numerous divine abilities of the Boundless Mirror are based on the Immortal-grade Grand Array [Boundless, Vast Square]. Theoretically, it can analyze all things in the world. Even things beyond its own level can be analyzed slowly, like the Foolish Old Man moving mountains."

"But the Boundless Mirror I encountered in the Xuanhuang Realm had its power greatly diminished. Let alone all things in the world, even the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, which is also an Immortal artifact, it could only steal glances through gaps."

"And now..."

Holding the Azure Nether Pearl, Li Fan returned to the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Within the space of the Alliance headquarters, the Azure Nether Pearl rippled like clear water. Suddenly, it transformed into the appearance of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror, emitting a faint glow all around.

Li Fan did not receive any threat reminders from the fabricated Mirror Xuan. But he keenly sensed that a new functional region was being opened within the Azure Nether Pearl. It was also a small mirror, but it was ancient and bronze-green, exactly like the true form of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror!

"The Boundless Mirror it devoured was a weakened version. But the Azure Nether Pearl can replenish the functions of the Boundless Mirror through its own divine abilities!"

"Moreover, judging by the current situation, after devouring the Boundless Mirror, it can actually replicate the functions of other Immortal artifacts just through [Analysis]?" Li Fan was both shocked and delighted.

But this joy did not last long. Perhaps because it was generated through the analysis of the Boundless Mirror, the functional area of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror in the Azure Nether Pearl was adjacent to the functional area of the Boundless Mirror. And this boundary was not very clear.

The Heavenly Xuan Mirror functional area existed independently for only about half a cup of tea's time before it was annexed by the Boundless Mirror functional area. And this merger was beyond Li Fan's control.

After the fusion, the image of a small mirror faintly presented on the Azure Nether Pearl's surface also changed. The bronze-green color faded, and the shape became circular. Within the mirror, it seemed a pair of eyes were hidden, secretly observing everything outside.

Li Fan's heart stirred slightly, and the Azure Nether Pearl transformed at his will, the illusory mirror realistically appearing in his hand. The analysis was not yet complete, but it already possessed many functions of both the Boundless Mirror and the Heavenly Xuan Mirror. In addition to conventional functions such as creating internal space, storage, deduction, and analysis, Li Fan valued the "differentiation and secondary generation" ability of the Heavenly Xuan Mirror even more.

Unfortunately, this seemed to be a skill the Heavenly Xuan Mirror learned later in life, not an innate ability. The Azure Nether Pearl's analysis function could not directly replicate it onto itself.

"The Boundless Immortal Array should have reached a sufficiently high rank. Checking the information on the Heavenly Xuan Mirror analyzed within the Azure Nether Pearl, it is almost identical to what Li Fan read from the fabricated Mirror Xuan."

"The only difference is the absence of an artifact spirit."

Li Fan hesitated slightly, and in the end, he did not rush to use the method of sentient beings to cultivate intelligence for the Azure Nether Pearl. Even the method of fabricating personality was not applied to the Azure Nether Pearl. From the fleeting glimpse of the Divine Witch Realm, the twelve statues standing tall in the sky that Li Fan saw gave him a vague sense of unease.

"For now, it's better to use it purely as an artifact."

After the analysis of the Boundless Mirror and the Heavenly Xuan Mirror was completed, Li Fan next experimented with the Azure Nether Pearl's ability to manifest cultivation techniques. After Emperor Sanmo brought several corpses, Li Fan devoured them with the Azure Nether Pearl.

As the corpses disappeared into the vast azure expanse, several subtle auras emerged from the pearl. They were composed of countless small characters, and one by one, they floated above the azure sky. They corresponded to the cultivation techniques that these death row inmates had practiced during their lives.

Even though their cultivation techniques had been forcibly abolished, the Azure Nether Pearl still revealed them! Comparing them, they were exactly the same!

Li Fan reached out and took one of the scrolls.

"Nine Refinements Wandering Spirit Art..."

Li Fan absorbed these characters into his body. Not only the cultivation technique itself. Even the understanding of the cultivation technique and the insights gained during practice from the corpse's previous life also appeared in Li Fan's mind!

"In this way, with the experience of the 'previous life,' cultivation can become so much faster!"

"The only pity is that there are only insights, no memories." Although Li Fan felt some regret, he knew that being able to achieve this much already made it an unparalleled treasure.

"Learning from corpses as a teacher is far more efficient than ordinary tutoring."

"After all, corpses will not hide anything." But in the current Utmost Darkness Star Sea, there were not many beings who could arouse Li Fan's desire to learn and imitate.

"I wonder if these can still be used." Thinking this, Li Fan tentatively threw the large amount of flying ash powder left by Qin Zhuang, who was silenced outside the High Wall, into the Azure Nether Pearl. The powder was slowly devoured by the azure color.

Even after Qin Zhuang's soul and body were scattered, he still contributed his light and heat. Within the Azure Nether Pearl, it seemed as if a great wind had arisen. Li Fan watched closely, afraid of missing any detail. The Azure Nether Pearl was, after all, a treasure valued by King Xuan Tian. Ordinary means of destroying corpses and evidence did not seem to be able to withstand the Azure Nether light's investigation.

After a period of gestation, a wisp of peculiar colored aura appeared within the boundless azure. It was extremely eye-catching. It was a continuous gradient from black to white, passing through all the colors of time.

Li Fan took this wisp of aura.

"[Thirty Lectures on Dao Origin Basics]..." Sensing this name, Li Fan's expression became somewhat strange. However, he soon immersed himself in Qin Zhuang's practice and understanding of the Dao Origin symbols. The experience was completely incomparable to forcibly probing memories with Immortal Arrays.

Soul-searching and memory extraction, especially with the remnants of many restrictions within Qin Zhuang's divine soul, could not achieve such immersion. He could only perceive what Qin Zhuang had learned and how long he had spent. But with the Azure Nether Pearl, all of Qin Zhuang's thoughts based on these Dao Origin symbols were powerfully recreated in Li Fan's mind. It was as if Li Fan, in Qin Zhuang's identity, relived his life!

When Li Fan's consciousness cleared, he had mastered the "[Thirty Lectures on Dao Origin Basics]." Moreover, integrating Li Fan's own understanding, he was even more proficient than Qin Zhuang, a member of the Immortal Hunter organization. This feeling of gaining without effort was truly addictive. Li Fan couldn't help but smack his lips.

"With such a precious treasure in hand, I can't wait to go outside the High Wall and sweep through it. It would certainly be equivalent to hundreds of years of my hard cultivation." A dangerous glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. But in the end, he resolutely suppressed it.

First, there was the risk factor. More importantly, Li Fan could not yet determine whether this heaven-defying method of gaining insights through the Azure Nether Pearl had any side effects. The changes in Li Fan's divine soul were able to persist to some extent through [Returning to Truth]. If the changes were minor, perhaps they could be ignored. But if they accumulated, and even two or three activations of Returning to Truth couldn't cleanse them, it would be very dangerous and not worth the loss.

"First, let's conduct safety verification with a large number of test subjects."

"Furthermore, theoretically, being able to capture the thoughts of a corpse during its lifetime is definitely not limited to cultivation techniques."

"I wonder if there is any way to restore all the memories and thoughts of a corpse before its death?"

"If so, I could create and replicate a cultivator out of thin air, making them more like their original self." Li Fan played with the Azure Nether Pearl, which had returned to its original form, his thoughts churning.

...

The remaining four Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elder Council arrived on time as summoned. Without alarming anyone else, they were personally received by Di Sanmo and Qiao Sidao and taken to the Realm of Return to Origin, where Law-Transmitter Jiang resided. Due to the blockade of the Heaven-Connecting Grand Array, they naturally could not sense the existence of Law-Transmitter Jiang at the core of the array.

However, Li Fan had intentionally released some of Law-Transmitter Jiang's insights, synchronizing them with them. Therefore, as soon as they entered this small world, they were immersed in the profound enlightenment of "All things are like me."

Especially Zhao Ruoxi. The "Myriad Ages, My Own Path" and "All things are like me" were essentially the same in their core ideology. However, "Myriad Ages, My Own Path" achieved ultimate union with the Dao through continuous devouring. While "All things are like me" directly skipped the intermediate steps and reached the final destination: I am the Dao, and the Dao is me.

Even though she had already undergone Li Fan's rigorous training and her temperament had transformed, Zhao Ruoxi could not help but feel a sense of imbalance and jealousy at this moment. Zhao Ruoxi was like this, and the other three Longevity Heavenly Venerates, as well as Di Sanmo and Qiao Sidao, were no better off.

"I originally thought that Senior's [Great Sun Divine Art] in the Alliance, which could communicate with the Star Sea, was already miraculous. I never expected that facing the Great Dao directly would be..." Qiao Sidao was so shocked he couldn't speak, remaining silent for a long time.

"All things are like me" was the feeling of "talking with the Dao" and gaining insights. But once he returned to reality, it was as if nothing had happened; no trace of understanding the Dao remained. When Li Fan withdrew his merciful "gift," judging by the expressions on their faces, he could tell their inner disappointment.

"How is it?" At this moment, Li Fan appeared and asked. The few of them sobered up, first bowed respectfully, and then spoke, their words overflowing with praise.

"I wish to integrate this enlightenment of the Great Dao into your dreamland." After everyone finished speaking, Li Fan said calmly. His words made everyone's eyelids jump. Especially Wuyou. After the initial uncontrollable surprise, Wuyou's heart was filled with immense fear. Such a fortunate event falling from the sky... Could it be another way for this True Immortal to torment them?

Wuyou had inquired from Zhao Ruoxi about many things recently. Just as Wuyou didn't know how to respond, Li Fan spoke again.

"In dreams, there is no life or death."

"Cultivators who do not fear death are best suited as pawns to explore beyond the High Wall."

"However, there is a drawback: their strength is too weak, and their cultivation speed is too slow." Li Fan smiled.

"If the ants are too weak, even a million of them will not amount to much."

"But if ants become hyenas, it's a different story."

"The manifestation of strength in Wuyou's dreamland is only at the level of consciousness. However, through this method of directly facing the Great Dao, it is almost like a divine decree, capable of raising mortal cultivators to the Longevity realm in a short period."

"And it can be quantitatively controlled." Li Fan spoke lightly, but to the ears of the few present, it was like thunder. They still harbored some doubts in their hearts, but Li Fan's recent display of methods made them have to believe.

"Take this divine soul as an example." Li Fan spread out his palm, and a speck of light floated within it. It was a promising seedling personally selected by him from [Era]. With a thought, the "All things are like me" transformation insights were all poured into this divine soul. Although still extremely weak, this divine soul's theoretical cognition expanded at an unbelievable speed.

Not only were the insights from Law-Transmitter Jiang himself, but also Li Fan's thoughts and reflections over the years. Except for the Transformation of True and False, everything else was recorded in the Heaven-Connecting Array.

Chapter 1431: The Happy Land Arrives at Xuanhuang

Under normal circumstances, ordinary cultivators would not be able to withstand the improvement brought about by such rapid comprehension of the Dao. For them, the saying "to hear the Dao in the morning and die in the evening is acceptable" was their destiny. But at this moment, the Realm of Return to Origin was under Li Fan's complete control. Life and death were not dictated by heaven, but by mortals!

A mysterious and unfathomable power descended, sculpting and strengthening the soul in Li Fan's palm. The speck of light became increasingly crystalline and radiant, and the aura emanating from it grew more astonishing. Unlike the others present, Li Fan's vision showed a string of numbers floating above this soul-speck. It was the Profound Pivot, Ten Thousand Spirits Return to Numeration, one of the Grand Arrays of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit, quantifying the strengthening of the soul. It rapidly climbed from twenty-three and only slowed down after reaching eighty.

"Without the 'Infinite' property of Immortal Spiritual Energy, even with illusions of the Xuanhuang Realm's power within me, it's not enough for me to use the Withered Fall, Empty Chamber Blooms Grand Array without restraint. But with Wan Ling Gui Shu, it's perfectly usable."

"It's just that the strength reaches ninety only when approaching the Longevity Realm." Li Fan couldn't help but glance upwards.

"9999." A hundred times the Longevity Realm. But this was not Li Fan's actual combat power, but the limit strength quantified by the Ten Thousand Spirits Return to Numeration Grand Array. "If a True Immortal were to descend into the array, it would probably temporarily display a line of question marks instead."

The Heaven-Connecting Grand Array, combined with the Ten Thousand Spirits Return to Numeration Grand Array, could measure the strength of cultivators within illusions numerically. It could even infuse the comprehension of the Great Dao into cultivators as "experience points," promoting the birth of a large number of Longevity Realm experts within the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss.

The Dreamland of Utmost Bliss differed from illusions in that illusions could be arbitrarily fabricated and distorted at little cost. However, conversely, it was almost impossible for things within illusions to descend into the real world. The Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, on the other hand, was built on reality. Everything within the dream could be rapidly manifested in reality as long as sufficient energy was provided.

"The True Immortal level, let's not discuss it for now. If Immortal Spiritual Energy from the Infinite Star Sea were forcibly connected, countless Longevity and below-level combat powers could be summoned to reality overnight."

"It's already extremely close to the Fallen Immortal Realm." Within the Fallen Immortal Realm, countless worlds existed that were extremely similar to reality, and some of them contained Longevity cultivators. Since objects from the Fallen Immortal Realm could be brought into reality, theoretically, Fallen Immortal Realm cultivators could also.

However, throughout history, only Xuanhuang Realm cultivators' consciousness had traveled to the Fallen Immortal Realm; there was never a mention of Fallen Immortal Realm cultivators breaking the barrier between reality and illusion to descend into the Xuanhuang Realm. Li Fan believed this was a restriction imposed by the True Immortal who originally created the Fallen Immortal Realm.

"If one were to achieve True Immortal status in the Fallen Immortal Realm, perhaps they could cross this boundary."

"It's just that it's almost an impossible feat." Li Fan, who had painstakingly achieved Half-Immortal status, was well aware of the difficulty. At least for the next few thousand years, no such person would appear in the Xuanhuang Realm's Fallen Immortal Realm.

The Fallen Immortal Realm, formed from the remnants of a True Immortal, the dark sea formed from the corpse of a True Immortal, and the will to survive of a True Immortal slumbering in the depths of the dark sea – all held significant meaning for Li Fan at present. After all, perhaps the opportunity for further transformation and achieving True Immortal status was hidden within.

Although achieving True Immortal status might attract the pursuit of forces outside the Wall, Li Fan would not flinch and give up his progress because of it. Moreover, he had the help of True Return. At worst, he could first prove himself as a True Immortal, experience firsthand what a True Immortal was like, and if the situation was truly critical, and True Immortals were in a precarious position, he could return to the Half-Immortal anchor point and start anew.

Amidst Li Fan's contemplation, the soul in his palm, purely in terms of strength, was already no weaker than Zhao Ruoxi. Such heaven-defying methods naturally deeply impressed everyone present. Wuyou, however, asked with a hint of worry, "If so many powerful beings suddenly appear in the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, I fear I won't be able to maintain it..."

Before she finished speaking, Li Fan interrupted, "No matter, with my assistance, the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss will naturally be kept safe and sound."

Wuyou's heart sank. She knew that from now on, the control of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss would likely no longer be in her hands. But she also knew that this might be a great opportunity for her. Her strength was directly related to the scale of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. Even if the leading role was forcibly transferred, with the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss growing daily under the management of a True Immortal, she would undoubtedly receive a considerable benefit. While her thoughts raced, Wuyou could only thank the True Immortal senior for his grace.

...

The transformation of Wuyou's Dreamland of Utmost Bliss was undoubtedly a monumental undertaking. The most crucial aspect was to ensure the safety of the billions of beings living within the Dreamland. Under Li Fan's command, Di San Mo and the other Longevity Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elders Council entered different regions of the Dreamland, presiding over the connection of the Grand Arrays. Wuyou, on the other hand, opened up her mind, allowing Li Fan to manipulate it.

Following the Ink Kill Dao Annihilation Phenomenon previously implanted, which had silently permeated every corner of the Dreamland, Li Fan integrated the power of the Heaven-Connecting, Great Dao as Me Grand Array and the Profound Pivot, Ten Thousand Spirits Return to Numeration Grand Array into the dream. With the Longevity cultivators as nodes, the power of the Grand Arrays quickly took root within the Dreamland. The gradual infiltration of the Dissolution Disc's Immortal Spiritual Energy, through the parasitic Grand Arrays, began to transform the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. With every part transformed, Li Fan's control over the Dreamland increased.

Wuyou Heavenly Venerate, although the creator of the Dreamland, was now helpless to resist the handover of her creation. She even vaguely felt that her connection to the Dreamland, and the benefits she received from it, were due to the True Immortal senior's benevolence in not completely severing this link. Little did Wuyou know that Li Fan still preserved her connection to the Dreamland because he intended to use Wuyou as a scapegoat at a critical moment. After all, exploring outside the High Wall in this life might attract the attention of ultimate powerhouses. If they traced the origin to the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, with Wuyou as the nominal owner, it would provide a buffer period, allowing Li Fan to escape calmly, rather than being in a desperate situation.

The process of taking over the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss seemed extremely smooth. Through the Dissolution Disc's sensing, Li Fan saw in his vision a layer of illusory light bands drifting in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, intertwining with reality but not overlapping. Occasionally, wisps of light were attracted from reality, flying towards the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. In the light band, a new thread would then be born, representing a new dream being generated.

Sitting in the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan's consciousness traveled rapidly through the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, even faster than the wood sword phantom's escape technique. In an instant, he arrived at the edge of the Star Sea, beneath the High Wall. Unlike the normal, formless view, Li Fan now saw a dark, curved boundary line separating the inside and outside of the High Wall. The boundary line, like an obstruction, still gave an insurmountable feeling. But since it had a tangible form, it seemed possible to cross the High Wall.

"This is the High Wall's blockade, its consciousness interface is relatively weak."

"No wonder the five Elders Council members were determined to escape through Wuyou's Dreamland to the outside of the High Wall." Li Fan observed it up close for a long time before a strange feeling suddenly arose in his heart. Previously, when he spied on the High Wall in reality, he would be subjected to its pressure. More importantly, comprehending the principles of the High Wall came with the characteristic of "losing it forever once lost." But in the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, this characteristic did not exist.

Li Fan pondered for a long time, his gaze fixed on the dark line not far away. A strange thought suddenly appeared in his mind. "Perhaps it's because the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss only contains consciousness and is incomplete."

"The High Wall is like a mirror, reflecting oneself."

"The appearance and feelings when facing the High Wall will also differ depending on one's state." Li Fan thought again of the High Wall, which could isolate the prying eyes of powerful beings like the Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai.

"This realm of the High Wall is still a one-way mirror." Staring at it, Li Fan suppressed the impulse to cross the High Wall within the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. Based on the sentiments of Mo Ruobin and the Heavenly Physician in reality towards the High Wall, Li Fan had already guessed that the High Wall, like a dragon gate, was an insurmountable barrier for beings within the wall. However, for those who could traverse it, it also represented immense benefits.

With a thought, Li Fan instantly returned to the Xuanhuang Realm. The transformation of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss had been preliminarily completed. Next, it was time to open more interfaces. Previously, due to Wuyou's own limitations and the deterrence of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, only beings in a small part of the Five Elders Council's territory could enter the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. But now, under Li Fan's instructions, the illusory light band floating above the Xuanhuang Realm emitted thousands of light tendrils, radiating throughout the Xuanhuang Realm and several affiliated small worlds and cave heavens.

The illusory light was intangible and faint. At this moment, countless beings were drawn into illusions, entering a deep sleep while their real bodies were swallowed by the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss and temporarily stored. Within the Dreamland, new conceptual bodies were created and crafted based on their souls. While there were many cultivators, they were insignificant compared to the vast number of mortals.

The most significant change in the updated Dreamland of Utmost Bliss was the addition of a giant city floating in the sky in each region. It was an enhanced version of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Heavenly City, equipped with functions for training, rest, and trade. It even allowed users to actively choose their dream regions. Newcomers found everything dazzling.

As for the old players of the Dreamland, the biggest surprise in this update was the absence of death penalties. No matter how many times they died in the dream world, they would be reborn in the "main city." Furthermore, compared to the past cultivation methods, which were the same as in reality, the Dreamland now had "Dao Comprehension Points." By completing dream missions and through various other means, one could obtain Dao Comprehension Points, which could be used to directly increase their cultivation and realm.

The growth speed of cultivators in the Dreamland was now incomparable to the past. Moreover, according to the announcement, a batch of brand-new dream worlds would be opened. Those who reaped the rewards first would also receive additional bonuses.

...

With the influx of so many new elements, the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss presented a scene of prosperity. Meanwhile, in reality, Wuyou Heavenly Venerate's condition was not as good. Even with Li Fan's modifications to the dream, which had expanded nearly a hundredfold, it was still an unbearable burden for Wuyou. If not for the protection of the Xuanhuang Realm phantom bestowed by Li Fan, Wuyou would have been crushed by her own creation in an instant. Now, to maintain her sanity, Wuyou had reverted to her infant state and fallen into a deep sleep. However, her furrowed brows and occasional cries indicated her pain.

Everything had its pros and cons. If Wuyou bore the brunt of the hardship in creating the dreamland, Li Fan enjoyed almost all the benefits. As the actual master of the dreamland, Li Fan could observe so many beings up close. Their every move, joy and sorrow, every emotional fluctuation, Li Fan could perceive with clarity.

Li Fan gradually gained a deeper understanding of the "human" species. If before, due to the True Return reincarnation, all beings in the world had gradually become meaningless symbols and codes in Li Fan's eyes. Then now, through the close observation of the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss, these "symbols" had once again become vivid and lifelike in Li Fan's eyes. Although they were still symbols, they were more distinct. Li Fan realized that this more concrete and practical understanding greatly aided him in comprehending the Transformation of True and False.

Ultimately, to transform the false into the true, or the true into the false, one needed at least a complete understanding of the essence of things. Although Li Fan could successfully perform the Transformation of True and False without meeting this prerequisite through the power of True Return, if Li Fan himself could understand the essence of things, it might help him accomplish more with the effort "saved" by True Return.

With this thought, Li Fan split his attention, immersing his consciousness in the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss. Exploring outside the High Wall was not a task for a single day. With the Xuanhuang Realm's current strength, it still needed time to accumulate. The countdown to the great tribulation of world destruction steadily decreased.

In the blink of an eye, ten years later. The existence of "no death" and "Dao Comprehension Points" allowed cultivators in the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss to improve their strength at an incredibly terrifying speed. In just ten years, the Dreamland had collapsed more than thirty times. Li Fan had to personally intervene several times to barely maintain the stability of the dream. After dozens of iterations, the Dreamland of Utmost Bliss was now completely filled, extending beyond the High Wall. Some of its vanguard tendrils had even broken through the High Wall! Although only at the consciousness level, the stark difference between the inside and outside of the High Wall surprised Li Fan.

Simply put, the "Dao Comprehension Points" that could be drawn upon by the Heaven-Connecting Grand Array outside the High Wall were generally five to six times higher than those inside the High Wall!
